-----title
浦城
-----detail

/><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1000&endYear=1000')">1000年</a>　在浦城，追寻旧迹，屡题诗。作品：题张浚所居壁五首。留题南源院。留题黄山院。<div id='poem_129298' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_129298' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/129298?labeling=true' target='_blank'>题张浚所居壁<span class='inlineComment2'>（浚，予之姻，此后自郡归乡）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1000年）</span><span id='poem_sentence_1_129298_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_129298'>分题每日摇鸡距，合宴常时把蟹螯。<div id='poem_sentence_2_129298_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_129250_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_129250'>当昼风雷生洞穴，欲斋猿鸟下庭除。<div id='poem_sentence_2_129250_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_129250_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_129251' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_129251' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/129251?labeling=true' id='poem_sentence_0_129251'>禾黍离离一径通，游人揽辔即过从。<div id='poem_sentence_0_129251_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_129251'>趁斋幽鸟闻疏磬，出定高僧见偃松。<div id='poem_sentence_1_129251_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_129251'>夜静龛灯凝古殿，雨馀岩溜迸前峰。<div id='poem_sentence_2_129251_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_129251'>昔年曾此题名处，素壁攲斜翠藓重。<div id='poem_sentence_3_129251_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_129251'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_129251_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1000&endYear=1000')">1000年</a>　将赴朝，有诗留题张彝宪池亭。<div id='poem_129249' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_129249' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/129249?labeling=true' target='_blank'>留题张彝宪池亭<span class='inlineComment2'>（彝宪昆仲三人，皆好学，季弟逝矣）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1000年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_129249")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_129249_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_129249'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_129249'>潇洒危亭枕碧池，昔年飞盖此追随。<div id='poem_sentence_0_129249_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_129249'>正逢五䌽承颜日，兼是三荆并秀时。<div id='poem_sentence_1_129249_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_129249'>夜坐不知银汉没，春游长诉玉杯迟。<div id='poem_sentence_2_129249_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_129249'>如今罢郡重登赏，喜见扶风旧白眉。<div id='poem_sentence_3_129249_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_129249'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_129249_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1000&endYear=1000')">1000年</a>　罢郡归乡时，聪道人自处州偕送；及秋归处州，以诗送之。作品：别聪道人归缙云。<div id='poem_129126' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_129126' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/129126?labeling=true' target='_blank'>别聪道人归缙云<span class='inlineComment2'>（聪送予至别墅）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1000年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_129126")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_129126_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_129126'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_129126'>二年假守栝苍城，郡榻唯师即送迎。<div id='poem_sentence_0_129126_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_129126'>捣药几怜春漏永，调琴长待夜蟾生。<div id='poem_sentence_1_129126_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_129126'>心猿已伏都无念，海鸟相逢自不惊。<div id='poem_sentence_2_129126_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_129126'>送别秋郊岂成恨，白云青嶂是归程。<div id='poem_sentence_3_129126_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_129126'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_129126_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1000&endYear=1000')">1000年</a>　为撰祖父文逸《神道表》及表叔张仲仁《墓志铭》作品：故信州玉山令府君神道表。故宋陕州芮城令清河张君墓志铭。<div id='poem_1152696' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152696' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152696?labeling=true' target='_blank'>故信州玉山令府君神道表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1000年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152696")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152696_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152696'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152696'>玉山府君，以太平兴国三年六月三十日启手足于长乐里之第，其年十二月八日归葬于南原，凡二十三年矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152696_comment'></div>金石未刻，陵谷将变，嗣孙亿大惧夫祖德之坠于地，考诸谱牒，询于耆艾，追述先美，以表幽垄云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152696_comment'></div>府君讳文逸，字慕贤，华阴弘农人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152696_comment'></div>昔周之伯侨，始启封邑，胙土命氏，实曰杨侯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152696_comment'></div>瓜瓞蝉联，大昌厥绪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152696_comment'></div>在西汉时，重侯累相；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152696_comment'></div>施及魏、晋，世为公卿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152696_comment'></div>永嘉之乱、播迁江表，始占籍于上饶郡，因为郡人焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1152696_comment'></div>安土重迁，凡十馀世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1152696_comment'></div>唐上元中，刘展称乱，吴会弗宁，府君之六代祖，始挈其族人，避地于建安之吴兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1152696_comment'></div>斩木诛茅，筑室治产，以财力雄于州里，以义方训于子孙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1152696_comment'></div>曾王父式，蹈德咏仁，隐居求志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1152696_comment'></div>王父郜，属唐季俶扰，干戈日寻，奕世聚居，群从百口，非用武断，不能亢宗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1152696_comment'></div>于是募乡民之拳勇者数百人，受署于本郡，为义军指挥使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1152696_comment'></div>坚壁要害，以备不虞，一邑赖之，终以无患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1152696_comment'></div>烈考弼，遭时未乂，结发从军，受署义军讨击副使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1152696_comment'></div>府君，即副使之次子也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1152696_comment'></div>始在童丱，遂游胶庠，博习亲师，服膺素业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1152696_comment'></div>家世从戎旅之事，以蒙举闻于郡中，而府君耻事轻肥，雅好学问，被服造次，必于儒者，识者以为秦堇父之生丕兹也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1152696_comment'></div>时王氏偏霸闽隅，府君世父太常君实为邑令，以犹子之爱，推延赏之典，才十馀岁，解褐试秘书省校书郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1152696_comment'></div>未几，丁副使君之忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1152696_comment'></div>泣血执丧，殆于天性；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1152696_comment'></div>纯孝之德，乡党称焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1152696_comment'></div>及王氏乖离，吴人致讨，建安失守，归于金陵，改右千牛卫、胄曹参军、知建州仓事，克遂循陔之欢，靡辞掌庾之贱，就加本卫骑曹参军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1152696_comment'></div>先夫人寝疾弥留，府君即解所职，调品药饵，供视膳羞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1152696_comment'></div>目不交睫，衣不解带，如是者凡历三时，而卒以不起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1152696_comment'></div>府君勺饮不入，呕血数升，柴毁支离，仅成死孝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1152696_comment'></div>服除，调补抚州南丰簿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1152696_comment'></div>视事踰月，化行若神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1152696_comment'></div>先是，邑人常以端午为竞渡之戏，具舟数十艘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1152696_comment'></div>聚群不逞之徒，以较胜负，必先载瓦石，因以相击，每岁死伤者数十百人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1152696_comment'></div>府君前知其然，至期大索，笞其为首者数辈，讫事无变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1152696_comment'></div>狱讼衰少，县政益清。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1152696_comment'></div>秩满，拟常州武进丞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1152696_comment'></div>辞不之任，改大理评事、信州玉山令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1152696_comment'></div>邑有镇兵，兼总军政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1152696_comment'></div>府君宽以御下，明以照奸，流亡悉归，版图增羡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1152696_comment'></div>先甲发令，卒乘畏威；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1152696_comment'></div>泮林革音，寇盗屏迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1152696_comment'></div>境内大治，政声流闻，就加大理司直，示陟明也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1152696_comment'></div>未几，王师渡江，台城蔽垒，调发徵敛，繁于秋荼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1152696_comment'></div>府君夤奉简书，事行愆素，曾未数月，得代而归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1152696_comment'></div>老幼攀辕，易服宵遁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1152696_comment'></div>当是时也，国命将坠，人谋已改，府君杜门称疾，不交世务，静以观变，默而俟时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1152696_comment'></div>俄而黄旗运终，青盖西上，诏旨敦迫，州司临门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1152696_comment'></div>方促星火之期，忽婴霜露之疢，不克上道，因以家居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1152696_comment'></div>恶石无徵，梁木斯坏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1152696_comment'></div>享年六十有五，未跻于寿；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1152696_comment'></div>历试百里之宰，未尽其才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1152696_comment'></div>有折冲制胜之略，值艰虞而不得伸；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1152696_comment'></div>有化民成俗之具，逢承平而不及用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1152696_comment'></div>赍志没地，遗恨终天，行道之人，所共叹息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1152696_comment'></div>府君娶武宁章氏，驾部郎中嵩之女也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1152696_comment'></div>生先君，讳某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1152696_comment'></div>象贤惟肖，禀训无违，宦学四方，名声籍甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1152696_comment'></div>及府君归老别墅，先君终鲜兄弟，烝烝就养，不离左右，被褐怀玉，韬光戢耀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1152696_comment'></div>以至下荼蓼之苦，荷清白之谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1152696_comment'></div>世故纷纶，家徒窘绝，未遑射策，奄兹沦逝，后府君九年而终。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1152696_comment'></div>咸平二年十一月，天子有事南郊，其孤亿任谏官，有司以丙戌诏书，追赠先君为大理评事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1152696_comment'></div>宠被泉壤，庆延里闬，行路叹息，父老荣之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1152696_comment'></div>四女：长适陇西李琼；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1152696_comment'></div>次适清河张仲言，后府君七年而逝；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1152696_comment'></div>次适河间俞简臣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1152696_comment'></div>次适清河张彝宪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1152696_comment'></div>率皆大族，莫非令人，妇德嫔风，表仪宗党。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1152696_comment'></div>府君之任玉山也，其孙亿始生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1152696_comment'></div>亿将生之夕，府君前得吉梦，谓必兴吾门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1152696_comment'></div>躬自抚养，特所钟爱，才免襁褓，教以诗书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1152696_comment'></div>及府君之捐馆舍，亿五岁矣，方在孩抱，永违慈颜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1152696_comment'></div>逮十有一岁，太宗皇帝遂闻其名，徵诣阙下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1152696_comment'></div>试以词赋，官于秘书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1152696_comment'></div>自是入蓬丘，直仙殿，升近署，置周行，为天子从官，成国家大典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1152696_comment'></div>罔非锡羡馀庆，燕翼贻谋，天启毕万之大名，世祚于公之阴德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1152696_comment'></div>不然者，蕞尔亿何以及兹？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1152696_comment'></div>亿自举族还都，再见闰月，叹墓木之已拱，忧堂构之将颓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1152696_comment'></div>前年献封公车，求领郡政，皇上固留不遣，亿恳请而行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1152696_comment'></div>瓯粤之区，封畛相错，伏念昔者府君之归窀穸也，铭志阙如。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1152696_comment'></div>岁月寖深，耆旧犹在，遂用采摭，以备万一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1152696_comment'></div>谨按府君天姿谨厚，宽中多恕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1152696_comment'></div>行有枝叶，心无町畦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1152696_comment'></div>慷慨经纶，博通治体。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1152696_comment'></div>信著朋友，仁洽闺门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1152696_comment'></div>胜冠之年，逮事祖母。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1152696_comment'></div>被疾沉痼，经时伏枕，府君束带奉侍，夙夜匪懈，尝恶浣洗，无所不为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1152696_comment'></div>府君母弟五人，率以豪侠自任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1152696_comment'></div>鲜车怒马，轻裘缓带，出入闾里，持吏短长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1152696_comment'></div>暴虎冯河，使酒难近，私匿亡命，结客执仇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1152696_comment'></div>人胥畏之，莫敢忤视。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1152696_comment'></div>府君戒督备至，槚楚是用，诸弟惕息，刚悍少衰，皆以天年，死于牖下，议者许府君之善教也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1152696_comment'></div>涉猎史传，详明典故；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1152696_comment'></div>锐意风雅，动成篇章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1152696_comment'></div>及试吏方州，尝奏伎记室，巧为书檄，曲畅事情，兵戈之馀，遗槁散落。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1152696_comment'></div>素善草隶，自可名家；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1152696_comment'></div>天纵多能，洞晓钟律。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1152696_comment'></div>新声度曲，精义入神；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1152696_comment'></div>图纬数术，罔不研覈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1152696_comment'></div>棋陆蒲塞，出于馀力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1152696_comment'></div>若乃张仲之孝友，安世之慎密，史鱼之直，伯夷之清，宁俞之忠，石奋之谨，刘文饶之恕，秦巴西之仁，庾亮之风流，山涛之识度，凡是众美，无一阙焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1152696_comment'></div>时方搆屯，位不充量。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1152696_comment'></div>盖仲尼云：「如有用我者，其为东周乎」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1152696_comment'></div>汉文谓李广：「惜不当高祖世，万户侯岂足道哉」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1152696_comment'></div>命之通塞，道之行否，固有冥数矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1152696_comment'></div>夫惟贤者，能论撰其先祖之美，而明著之于后世者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1152696_comment'></div>无美而称之是诬，有善而弗知不明，知而弗传不仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1152696_comment'></div>三者，君子之所耻也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1152696_comment'></div>恭惟府君之德业，章章如是，国史弗载，鼎铭未刊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1152696_comment'></div>春礿秋尝，弥用怵惕；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1152696_comment'></div>冬裘夏葛，靡敢遑宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1152696_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1152696_comment'></div>不见成人，范乔之悲罔极；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1152696_comment'></div>有惭于长，太丘之德未衰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1152696_comment'></div>爰勒贞珉，以永终古。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1152696_comment'></div>肸蚃非远，謦欬如闻，嗣孙之勤，尚或临鉴云耳。</div><div id='poem_sentence_112_1152696_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1152700' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152700' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152700?labeling=true' target='_blank'>故宋陕州芮城令清河张君墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1000年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152700")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152700_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152700'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152700'>君讳仲仁，字子信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152700_comment'></div>其先清河人，后徙建安之吴兴，遂为著姓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152700_comment'></div>当王氏之据有闽越也，曾祖从晟，以州里豪右，材兼文武，仕至浦城制置副使、工部尚书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152700_comment'></div>祖赟，以延赏之典，署建州长史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152700_comment'></div>烈考仁邈，检校左散骑常侍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152700_comment'></div>君即常侍之次子也，与伯氏同生，居上为弟，风格甚类，趣向多同，里巷相疑，家人莫辨，每异其服饰以自别焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152700_comment'></div>君爰自童蒙，服膺儒素，韵宇冲粹，智略纵横。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152700_comment'></div>李氏之平建安也，常侍辞疾家居，累徵不起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1152700_comment'></div>君策杖行在，叫阍上书，朝论奇之，即授太常寺奉礼郎，改秘书省校书郎，调补本州松溪尉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1152700_comment'></div>江表平，入朝，历卫州卫县主簿、青州千乘尉、达州巴渠簿兼令尉事，迁陕州芮城令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1152700_comment'></div>以疾去官，旅寓京师，寻访医药。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1152700_comment'></div>积日弥久，美疹愈滋，肩舁而归，遂成沉痼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1152700_comment'></div>清漳卧病，既十年而未瘳；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1152700_comment'></div>东岳敛魂，俄三号而不返。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1152700_comment'></div>以咸平三年六月十八日，卒于仁风里之私第，享年六十二。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1152700_comment'></div>其年某月日，归葬于里冲源，顺也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1152700_comment'></div>君娶武宁章氏，生子三人：长为舟，举进士；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1152700_comment'></div>次垂象，蚤亡；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1152700_comment'></div>次为式。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1152700_comment'></div>女一人，适进士章覃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1152700_comment'></div>自君之被疾也，为舟等夙夜扶侍，躬亲左右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1152700_comment'></div>靡神不祷，靡药不尝，烝烝服勤，目为至孝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1152700_comment'></div>予从祖兵部，即君之元舅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1152700_comment'></div>君之先夫人，实予之尊姑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1152700_comment'></div>某之与君，犹丈人行也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1152700_comment'></div>平生游处，顾托乘以犹新；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1152700_comment'></div>旧馆过从，嗟脱骖之无益。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1152700_comment'></div>谨铭翠琰，以志佳城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1152700_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_28_1152700'>天之德兮世济美，仕两朝兮宰百里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1152700_comment'></div>政之善兮疹何美，祷之久兮药勿喜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1152700_comment'></div>返九幽兮邻万鬼，人之生兮胡至此？</div><div id='poem_sentence_30_1152700_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1000&endYear=1000')">1000年7？</a>　约七月，自建州赴阙，单车即路。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
开封（汴京）

ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=985&endYear=985')">985年</a>　在京任秘书省正字。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='857a1ea332d94827b669a93427c0a103_label'><a href='javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=990&endYear=990')">990年</a>　诣阙献文，改奉礼郎，读书秘阁。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=991&endYear=991')">991年</a>　有诗贺占城献狮子。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=994&endYear=994')">994年</a>　有诗吟义门胡氏华林书院。作品：咏华林书院。<div id='poem_129339' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_129339' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/129339?labeling=true' target='_blank'>咏华林书院</a><span class='authorDate'>（994年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_129339")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_129339_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_129339'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_129339'>闻说华林院，名将阙里偕。<div id='poem_sentence_0_129339_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_129339'>生徒似东鲁，书籍胜西斋。<div id='poem_sentence_1_129339_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_129339'>俎豆儒风盛，埙篪乐韵谐。<div id='poem_sentence_2_129339_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_129339'>门闾双桂茂，编秩九流排。<div id='poem_sentence_3_129339_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_129339'>讲学搴纱幕，题诗挂粉牌。<div id='poem_sentence_4_129339_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_129339'>荀陈传旧族，游夏结同侪。<div id='poem_sentence_5_129339_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_129339'>红实洲生橘，清阴世种槐。<div id='poem_sentence_6_129339_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_129339'>夜蟾穿户牖，晴瀑泻岩崖。<div id='poem_sentence_7_129339_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_129339'>远客来千里，新恩出两阶。<div id='poem_sentence_8_129339_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_129339'>横经定何日，凭此寄幽怀。<div id='poem_sentence_9_129339_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_129339'></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_129339_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=994&endYear=994')">994年</a>　本年或稍前，聘张洎之女。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=995&endYear=995')">995年10月</a>　太宗命待诏朱文济等弹奏新声，群臣献歌诗颂之，亿词理精惬，受奖谕。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=996&endYear=996')">996年</a>　春，迁著作佐郎，多代公卿为表疏，太宗知其贫，屡有沾赉。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=996&endYear=996')">996年</a>　尝为越王生辰使。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=997&endYear=997')">997年</a>　真宗称亿文理精当，擢左正言，馆职如故。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=997&endYear=997')">997年</a>　秋冬，南安郡乡贡进士陈在中贽文投谒，亿答以书，并为延誉。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=997&endYear=997')">997年11月</a>　判集贤院事钱若水荐引，受诏预修《太宗实录》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=997&endYear=997')">997年</a>　与李宗谔、粱颢、赵况、赵安仁同表请复钱熙旧职，不报。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=997&endYear=997')">997年</a>　本年，娶妻张氏。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=998&endYear=998')">998年</a>　应中书舍人宋湜请，为其唱和诗集作序。作品：广平公唱和集序。<div id='poem_1152661' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152661' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152661?labeling=true' target='_blank'>广平公唱和集序</a><span class='authorDate'>（998年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152661")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152661_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152661'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152661'>昔者郑国名卿，赋诗者七子；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152661_comment'></div>郢中高唱，属和者数人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152661_comment'></div>善歌者必能继其声，不学者何以言其志？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152661_comment'></div>故《雅》《颂》之隆替，本教化之盛衰，傥王泽之下流，必作者之间出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152661_comment'></div>君臣唱和，赓载而成文；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152661_comment'></div>公卿宴集，答赋而为礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152661_comment'></div>废之久矣，行之实难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152661_comment'></div>非多士之盈廷，将斯文之坠地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1152661_comment'></div>皇宋二叶，车书混同，端拱穆清，详延俊乂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1152661_comment'></div>皋、夔、稷、卨，日奉吁俞；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1152661_comment'></div>枚、马、严、徐，并在左右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1152661_comment'></div>礼乐追于三代，文物迈于两汉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1152661_comment'></div>有若翰林主人、大宗伯广平公，以才识兼茂，治行第一，登金门，上玉堂，发挥帝谟，润色大业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1152661_comment'></div>自太平兴国迄于咸平，凡岁星再周于天矣，而望实益峻，体貌弥笃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1152661_comment'></div>入奏武帐，天子冠而后见；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1152661_comment'></div>退食温室，家人问而不言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1152661_comment'></div>挺山甫之将明，推安世之慎密。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1152661_comment'></div>作文章盟主，实朝廷宗工，天其或者殆以公为儒林之木铎也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1152661_comment'></div>而视草之暇，含毫靡倦，形于风什，传于僚友。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1152661_comment'></div>同声相应，发言成章，乃进文昌正卿、宥密元老。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1152661_comment'></div>蓬丘之长，兰台之英，争奇逞妍，更赋迭咏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1152661_comment'></div>铺锦列绣，刻羽引商，烂然成编，观者皆耸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1152661_comment'></div>广平公感交游之畴昔，虑竹素之沦胥，休沐之馀，孜孜缀缉，为之七卷，以传于世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1152661_comment'></div>颂声奋发，爵里森布，著于简牍，垂厥方来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1152661_comment'></div>当使仲尼删诗，取《周南》而居首；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1152661_comment'></div>班固著论，称西京之得人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1152661_comment'></div>盖风化之所系焉，岂徒缘情绮靡而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1152661_comment'></div>猥令纪述，蔑容固辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1152661_comment'></div>狂简孟浪，惭于叙事云耳。</div><div id='poem_sentence_28_1152661_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=998&endYear=998')">998年8月</a>　《太宗实录》八十卷成，奏上，亿独草五十六卷。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=998&endYear=998')">998年8月19日</a>　以修《太宗实录》成，乞外补就养，出知处州。帝称其史才，留不遣。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=998&endYear=998')">998年9月8日</a>　固请出知处州，遣之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=998&endYear=998')">998年9月</a>　朝士钱若水、王禹偁、钱惟演等三十八人以诗赠行，亿集而序之。作品：群公赠行集序。<div id='poem_1152658' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152658' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152658?labeling=true' target='_blank'>群公赠行集序</a><span class='authorDate'>（998年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152658")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152658_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152658'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152658'>予至道三年十一月，受诏修先朝国书，越明年八月，书成奏御。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152658_comment'></div>既而以太夫人有桑梓之恋，求典近郡，因奉甘旨，九月诏领缙云郡事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152658_comment'></div>拜命之翌日，复留不遣，再疏恳激，得请而行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152658_comment'></div>公卿巨儒，台阁髦士，寮寀之际，朋从之间，相率赠言，以宠行迈者，凡三十八人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152658_comment'></div>藻绣纷错，珠璧炫耀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152658_comment'></div>观咸、洛之市，天下之货毕陈；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152658_comment'></div>入宋、鲁之邦，先王之礼尽在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152658_comment'></div>亦以见一时文物之盛，岂独为鄙夫道路之光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1152658_comment'></div>昔者楚丘列诸侯之末，有蘧瑗、史徇、史䲡、公子荆、公叔发、公子朝分掌国政，故吴札叹曰：「卫多君子」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1152658_comment'></div>西京承三代之季，有朱买臣、吾丘寿王、司马相如、主父偃、徐乐、严安、枚皋、胶苍、终军、严葱奇并列左右，故史班称曰：「汉之得人」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1152658_comment'></div>巍巍圣朝，英俊咸集。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1152658_comment'></div>爵里鳞布，颂声奋发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1152658_comment'></div>览之者足以知多士在位，周室以宁，七子赋诗，郑志斯见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1152658_comment'></div>何止金声流于下国，华衮被于薄躯而已哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1152658_comment'></div>既铨次成编，辄敷述其事，盖取夫卜商作序，以冠二《雅》之首，用无愧焉。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1152658_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='71707b01dd7b44c8be38262284649f9c_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("71707b01dd7b44c8be38262284649f9c");'><span id='71707b01dd7b44c8be38262284649f9c_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1000&endYear=1001')">1000-1001年</a>，27-28岁</div><div id='71707b01dd7b44c8be38262284649f9c' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1000&endYear=1000')">1000年9月</a>　九月底，到阙，拜左司谏。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1000&endYear=1000')">1000年</a>　归阙，为宋白以下三十人此前送钱若水出知大名府诗作序。作品：群公饯钱侍郎知大名府诗序。<div id='poem_1152659' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152659' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152659?labeling=true' target='_blank'>群公饯集贤钱侍郎知大名府诗序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1000年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152659")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152659_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152659'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152659'>昔汉宣帝有言曰：「国家不虞，边境有事，左右之臣，皆将帅也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152659_comment'></div>乃知登勇爵者，不必专阃外之政，服儒术者，足以升上将之坛，其所由来旧矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152659_comment'></div>去年冬，銮舆北巡，胡马南牧，乃眷全魏之地，实介两河之间，驻跸以壮其军声，擒俘屡献于行在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152659_comment'></div>既而振旅凯以入，求节制之才，畴庸旧臣，作镇兹壤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152659_comment'></div>廉颇年老，不能用兵；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152659_comment'></div>赵孟语偷，未足为政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152659_comment'></div>于是命大京兆长城公繇冬官贰卿兼书殿史阁之职，出领府事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152659_comment'></div>军中之务，一以咨之，且谓之曰：「倚卿为北道主人，使朕得高枕而卧矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1152659_comment'></div>宠锡异等，禄秩有加。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1152659_comment'></div>十乘启行，百壶出饯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1152659_comment'></div>虬髭列侍，师律载严，鹤盖成阴，送车无数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1152659_comment'></div>于时缙绅大夫，相与言曰：「汲黯卧治，郡政自肃；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1152659_comment'></div>刘琨坐啸，塞垣以清。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1152659_comment'></div>当使朔野无烽燧之惊，生民免杼轴之困。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1152659_comment'></div>偃息谈笑，立销胡尘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1152659_comment'></div>投壶雅歌，益治军簿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1152659_comment'></div>俾天下之人，知敦《诗》阅《礼》，真将帅之具，坐筹决胜，敌百万之师，巍巍皇帝，知人而善任使也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1152659_comment'></div>昔者季布治郡，天子倚为股肱；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1152659_comment'></div>申伯于藩，吉甫形于歌颂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1152659_comment'></div>盍为诗什，以道德美」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1152659_comment'></div>由是学士承旨宋公而下，作者凡三十人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1152659_comment'></div>奇彩彪炳，清词藻缛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1152659_comment'></div>入孔子之宅，金石丝竹以尽闻；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1152659_comment'></div>游和氏之场，琮璧圭璜而皆在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1152659_comment'></div>与夫七子之赋郑志，群公之祖二疏，盖不侔矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1152659_comment'></div>某外领使符，归在秋暮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1152659_comment'></div>辟书始下，不及王粲之从军；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1152659_comment'></div>雅言毕陈，窃比卜商之作序。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1152659_comment'></div>芜陋简略，何足以云！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1152659_comment'></div>谨述。</div><div id='poem_sentence_29_1152659_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1000&endYear=1000')">1000年</a>　李继隆自陈州惠书，推誉亿之文章，亿上启谢之。作品：上陈州李相公启二。<div id='poem_1152592' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152592' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152592?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上陈州李相公启<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1000年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152592")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152592_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152592'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152592'>右，某启：昨者相公荣自藩垣，入朝宸极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152592_comment'></div>昼日三接，载延乃眷之恩；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152592_comment'></div>泰阶六符，式显具瞻之贵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152592_comment'></div>东閤幸伸于趋拜，中堂过沐于延容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152592_comment'></div>听谈柄以忘疲，侍坐隅而甚久。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152592_comment'></div>惭非子夏，敢预于言诗；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152592_comment'></div>窃愧穆生，何胜于置醴？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152592_comment'></div>矧又相如之四壁，两辱千秋之小车。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1152592_comment'></div>时屈丞相之尊，亲顾旅人之次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1152592_comment'></div>一瓢牢落，颜回之巷可哀；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1152592_comment'></div>三日氛氲，荀令之香不散。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1152592_comment'></div>实交游之光宠，固里巷之辉华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1152592_comment'></div>夫何下僚，当此殊奖？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1152592_comment'></div>非木石之无识，摩顶踵以不忘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1152592_comment'></div>伏自节过流虹，礼成荐璧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1152592_comment'></div>在镐锡宴，毕上公九献之仪；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1152592_comment'></div>分陕言归，还天子二老之任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1152592_comment'></div>旌旆将离于阙下，壶浆已拥于道旁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1152592_comment'></div>南阳细民，再得于父母；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1152592_comment'></div>河东近郡，深倚于股肱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1152592_comment'></div>恭惟仙舟，寻达雄阃，戎政甚肃，固卧治之有馀；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1152592_comment'></div>品物向荣，谅行春之非远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1152592_comment'></div>限以匏瓜之系，莫参簪履之微。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1152592_comment'></div>空瞻桂树于小山，深羡鸡鸣之下客。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1152592_comment'></div>攀恋之至，倍万愚衷。</div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1152592_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1000&endYear=1000')">1000年</a>　元道宗、奉宗兄弟举进士下第，李宗谔以诗勉之，亿有和作。作品：次韵和中书李舍人勉元氏道宗奉宗兄弟之什。<div id='poem_129079' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_129079' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/129079?labeling=true' target='_blank'>次韵和中书李舍人勉元氏道宗奉宗兄弟之什</a><span class='authorDate'>（1000年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_129079")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_129079_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_129079'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_129079'>二难文彩少人过，落笔寻常只患多。<div id='poem_sentence_0_129079_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_129079'>兔苑暂游冲霰雪，龙门曾上困风波。<div id='poem_sentence_1_129079_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_129079'>一囊负米犹为客，百步穿杨待决科。<div id='poem_sentence_2_129079_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_129079'>更得词臣赠诗句，机云入洛拟如何。<div id='poem_sentence_3_129079_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_129079'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_129079_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1000&endYear=1000')">1000年</a>　集贤院宿直，有诗抒怀，寄李宗谔、梁颢，时李梁并为知制诰。作品：集贤宿直寄中书李梁二舍人。<div id='poem_129374' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_129374' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/129374?labeling=true' target='_blank'>集贤宿直寄中书李梁二舍人</a><span class='authorDate'>（1000年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_129374")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_129374_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_129374'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_129374'>耿耿银釭照直庐，西风黄叶满庭除。<div id='poem_sentence_0_129374_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_129374'>愁心不忍闻宾雁，病眼犹能拾蠹鱼。<div id='poem_sentence_1_129374_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_129374'>攲枕微吟空展转，绕廊闲步自踌躇。<div id='poem_sentence_2_129374_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_129374'>铜龙漏滴传钩盾，玉兔光芒射绮疏。<div id='poem_sentence_3_129374_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_129374'>薄宦久淹沧海郡，故交多入紫垣居。<div id='poem_sentence_4_129374_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_129374'>洛阳已在拜尘后，宣室那逢膝席初。<div id='poem_sentence_5_129374_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_129374'>投阁寂寥深自愧，抱关憔悴拟何如。<div id='poem_sentence_6_129374_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_129374'>宁思西掖五花判，且补河东三箧书。<div id='poem_sentence_7_129374_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_129374'>桑梓任<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>抛万里外，蓬莱试住十年馀。<div id='poem_sentence_8_129374_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_129374'>释之不调嵇康懒，终待休官学灌蔬。<div id='poem_sentence_9_129374_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_129374'></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_129374_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_129374'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_8_129374_0'>⑴ 明刻本、清抄本作狂，祝刻本作枉</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_129374_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1000&endYear=1000')">1000年</a>　钱惟演造访，以诗赋为赠，亿作启谢之。作品：谢太仆钱少卿启。<div id='poem_1152588' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152588' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152588?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢太仆钱少卿启<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup></a><span class='authorDate'>（1000年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152588")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152588_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_1152588_0'>① 少卿进《咸平圣政录》及诗，自将军改官。</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152588'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152588'>右，某启：数日前，少卿特枉轩车，俯临蓬荜，仍以编缀，曲示颛蒙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152588_comment'></div>颜巷萧条，既迂长者之辙；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152588_comment'></div>赵囊牢落，忽得隋侯之珠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152588_comment'></div>缄縢载披，毛发俱耸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152588_comment'></div>窃以述作之妙，谓之圣明；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152588_comment'></div>赋颂之兴，本乎风化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152588_comment'></div>其有沿袭或异，步骤不同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152588_comment'></div>虞卿穷愁，乃就著书之业；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1152588_comment'></div>扬雄寂寞，始奋草《玄》之名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1152588_comment'></div>灵均放词，初因于憔悴；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1152588_comment'></div>兰成述赋，实主于悲哀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1152588_comment'></div>未有世传带砺之盟，身居环列之尹，敞北阙之甲第，屋瓦生烟；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1152588_comment'></div>乘大宛之名驹，汗血流赭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1152588_comment'></div>列鼎而食，执玉以朝，名亚春、陵，势夺张、霍，而乃贱青紫如拾芥，比富贵于浮云，优游文史之场，躬亲布素之行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1152588_comment'></div>折节待士，多拥彗以先驱；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1152588_comment'></div>焦思穷经，或下帷而终日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1152588_comment'></div>以至学成麟角，才掞天庭，思若涌泉，文类摛锦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1152588_comment'></div>汉宫诵赋，万乘喜生于同时；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1152588_comment'></div>梁苑陪游，群公推食于右席。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1152588_comment'></div>门登龙而比峻，谈挥麈以弥清。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1152588_comment'></div>诸生慕义以益勤，名卿愿交而斯众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1152588_comment'></div>芳猷载洽，雅志将伸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1152588_comment'></div>固已简自天衷，腾于物论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1152588_comment'></div>纪一人之言动，何让策书；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1152588_comment'></div>贡二《雅》之声诗，有裨乐府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1152588_comment'></div>召试鳌山之署，式摇鸡距之毫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1152588_comment'></div>不加点以成章，未旋踵而拜命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1152588_comment'></div>亚卿班列，既参惟月之崇；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1152588_comment'></div>太仆职司，仍预奉车之宠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1152588_comment'></div>昔汉光武之偃革，诸将竞乡学之心；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1152588_comment'></div>唐宪宗之厌兵，近臣有改名之请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1152588_comment'></div>以圭璋特达之质，当干戈载戢之秋，舍兰锜之师，就儒冠之饰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1152588_comment'></div>敦说《诗》《礼》，昔为谋师之资；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1152588_comment'></div>慷慨经纶，今挺致君之志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1152588_comment'></div>羽仪通籍，辉映缙绅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1152588_comment'></div>敢谓下顾蜗庐，特留凤藻！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1152588_comment'></div>享海鸟以九奏，诚非所宜；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1152588_comment'></div>投井蛙以兼金，都不之惜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1152588_comment'></div>退自循省，靡敢遑宁！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1152588_comment'></div>岂圯桥授书，怜其可教；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1152588_comment'></div>将延陵听乐，许以知音？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1152588_comment'></div>唯蹈咏以忘疲，庶传玩之无斁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1152588_comment'></div>愿言厚意，何以克胜？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1152588_comment'></div>其盛制，辄留缮写云云。</div><div id='poem_sentence_43_1152588_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1000&endYear=1000')">1000年10月</a>　有诗送王钦若奉使两川。作品：翰林王学士奉使两川。<div id='poem_129434' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_129434' class='poemTitle class='poemContent' id='poem_content_129324'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_129324'>江夏门风盛，东吴族望高。<div id='poem_sentence_0_129324_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_9_129324_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_129324'>去国踰千里，为郎历几曹。<div id='poem_note_129324_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1000&endYear=1000')">1000年10月</a>　宋湜卒，十月归葬，亿作挽歌三首悼之。又为撰墓志铭。作品：故枢密宋给事挽歌三首。宋故枢密副使正奉大夫行给事中上柱国广平县开国伯食邑八百户食实封二百户赐紫金鱼袋赠尚吏部侍郎宋公神道碑铭。<div id='poem_129205' class='authorDate'>（1000年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_129205")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_129205_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_129205'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_129205'>宸游方扈从，移疾废枢机。<div id='poem_sentence_0_129205_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_129205'>步辇亲临问，肩舁遽告归。<div id='poem_sentence_1_129205_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_129205'>忽闻号左毂，旋见泣中闱。<div id='poem_sentence_2_129205_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_129205'>城郢遗言切，忠魂定有依。<div id='poem_sentence_3_129205_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_129205'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_129205_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_129204' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_129204' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/129204?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1000年10月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_129204_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_129204'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_129204'>六龙初展义，七圣尽陪游。<div id='poem_sentence_0_129204_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_129204'>塞外狼烟起，军中羽檄稠。<div id='poem_sentence_1_129204_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_129204'>汉帷方借箸，庄壑忽沉舟。<div id='poem_sentence_2_129204_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_129204'>不奈良臣死，秦医亦漫求。<div id='poem_sentence_3_129204_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_129204'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_129204_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_129203' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_129203' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/129203?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1000年10月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_129203_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_129203'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_129203'>永辞温室地，长别谏书帷。<div id='poem_sentence_0_129203_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_129203'>玉恨埋黄壤，星愁析紫微。<div id='poem_sentence_1_129203_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_129203'>薤歌偏怨咽，衮敛更光辉。<div id='poem_sentence_2_129203_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_129203'>可惜岑文本，辽阳不共归。<div id='poem_sentence_3_129203_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_129203'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_129203_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1152695' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152695' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152695?labeling=true' target='_blank'>宋故枢密副使正奉大夫行给事中上柱国广平县开国伯食邑八百户食实封二百户赐紫金鱼袋赠尚书吏部侍郎宋公神道碑铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1000年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152695")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152695_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152695'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152695'>昔许穆公卒于师，《春秋》重其死王事，赠公衮以褒德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152695_comment'></div>岑江陵薨于行，天子嘉其尽臣节，罢宵警以申恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152695_comment'></div>皇上巡狩两河，驻跸魏郡，惟枢秘副使宋公典掌机要，务烦伤神，得疾膏肓，终于道路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152695_comment'></div>辍视朝于行阙，申追命于泉扃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152695_comment'></div>痛深股肱，见君臣之同体；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152695_comment'></div>布在方策，实今古之相望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152695_comment'></div>所以旌忠魂于九原，铄休光于百世者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152695_comment'></div>公讳湜，字持正，其先广平人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1152695_comment'></div>自微子归周，商丘启国，胙土命氏，源深流长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1152695_comment'></div>处荆蛮者，才亚于骚人；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1152695_comment'></div>仕东汉者，名参于循吏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1152695_comment'></div>或树勋于代邸，或驰誉于南朝，枝叶扶疏，华实蕃衍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1152695_comment'></div>公之远祖，占籍关中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1152695_comment'></div>隐德未融，重世始大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1152695_comment'></div>曾王父泽，登州牟平令；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1152695_comment'></div>王父赞，雍州万年令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1152695_comment'></div>皆以时命之数，屈于州县，咸有清白之训，遗于子孙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1152695_comment'></div>烈考温故，晋天福中擢进士第，累迁右补阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1152695_comment'></div>文雅之誉，流于京师；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1152695_comment'></div>骨鲠之风，播于台阁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1152695_comment'></div>及公之贵，累赠工部尚书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1152695_comment'></div>公即其次子也，襟韵閒旷，风规爽迈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1152695_comment'></div>凝脂点漆，宛是神仙中人；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1152695_comment'></div>虚受兼容，居然廊庙之器。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1152695_comment'></div>爰自髫龀，卓然不群，了无童心，靡杂儿戏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1152695_comment'></div>初入小学，比及大成，恣阅黄卷圣贤之言，蔑闻青衿城阙之刺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1152695_comment'></div>既而究六经之微旨，通百家之杂说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1152695_comment'></div>服勤学问，日引月长；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1152695_comment'></div>刻意著述，朝成暮传。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1152695_comment'></div>迹在丘樊，名振辇毂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1152695_comment'></div>方随乡老之荐，适丁先君之忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1152695_comment'></div>栾棘伤生，几于灭性；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1152695_comment'></div>苴麻终制，始让干禄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1152695_comment'></div>太平兴国五年春，太宗凡三临轩，亲选多士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1152695_comment'></div>公提笔就试，思若涌泉，焕乎成文，曾不加点。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1152695_comment'></div>诸生方当于燥吻，一人已喜于同时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1152695_comment'></div>贾勇先鸣，拔乎其萃，由是一上登进士甲科，解褐将作丞、通判梓州榷盐院，就拜太子右赞善大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1152695_comment'></div>归朝，改著作郎、直史馆，中谢日，赐绯衣银鱼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1152695_comment'></div>雍熙三年，今工部尚书王公化基，以谏官佐计相，上书北阙，自荐其材。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1152695_comment'></div>太宗方求非常之人，待以不次之位，谓宰相曰：「李沆、宋湜，皆佳士也，可并试之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1152695_comment'></div>即日召试制诰于中书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1152695_comment'></div>明日，除右补阙，知制诰，与二公并命焉，当时朝廷有得贤之议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1152695_comment'></div>就转库部员外郎，兼判尚书刑部，面赐金紫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1152695_comment'></div>会有妖尼诉廷尉断狱不平，公职当详谳，未尝发擿，坐是左迁均州团练副使，公论惜之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1152695_comment'></div>移汝州数月，徵拜礼部员外郎、直昭文馆，复以职方员外郎掌诰命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1152695_comment'></div>踰年入翰林为学士，转兵部郎中、知审刑院银台司封驳事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1152695_comment'></div>皇上嗣位，真拜中书舍人，修国史，并兼内署之职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1152695_comment'></div>俄丁皇妣扶风县太君淳于氏忧，柴毁骨立，杖而后起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1152695_comment'></div>五十而慕，昔人所难；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1152695_comment'></div>七日绝浆，仅成死孝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1152695_comment'></div>才卒哭，诏起复视草禁中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1152695_comment'></div>公泣血抗章，愿终丧纪，优诏敦免，不允其请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1152695_comment'></div>是年冬，改给事中，参贰机务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1152695_comment'></div>明年，犬戎犯边，翠华时迈，枢机之任，一二咨焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1152695_comment'></div>露版羽书，实司其缓急；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1152695_comment'></div>伍符尺籍，专校于耗登。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1152695_comment'></div>乘保鄣险，走集者禀于弛张；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1152695_comment'></div>发号令图，方略者出于规画。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1152695_comment'></div>乃至议将帅之能否，授以指踪；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1152695_comment'></div>揣蕃夷之情状，辩其狙诈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1152695_comment'></div>折冲樽俎之际，制胜帷幄之中，料敌若神，谋事鲜过。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1152695_comment'></div>任重责大，功劳智忧，而公与今襄阳王丞相并掌其职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1152695_comment'></div>公竭才尽瘁，知无不为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1152695_comment'></div>蒙犯风霜，勤劳夙夜，陟降帝右，咫尺天颜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1152695_comment'></div>总领万机，便蕃三接，焦心极虑，外彊中乾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1152695_comment'></div>十二月癸酉，上御武帐，召近臣议边事，公方指画上前，俄疾作仆于地，若大醉状，不能知人，同列竞前扶之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1152695_comment'></div>上命中贵人扶掖以就西序，亟令太医切脉，且曰：「疾不可为也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1152695_comment'></div>上忧形于色，日夕候其安否。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1152695_comment'></div>明年正月乙酉，乘舆亲至卧内存问，公以所疾未愈，恳乞先归，面可其奏，且以御衾褥为赐，仍命中使备肩舁、什器、帷帐、汤药、饮膳，送还京师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1152695_comment'></div>既发，又令近臣慰遣于郊外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1152695_comment'></div>己丑，次澶州，憩于法宝寺，是夕，以不起闻，享年五十有一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1152695_comment'></div>上叹息久之，诏赠吏部侍郎，辍朝一日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1152695_comment'></div>命使者护送灵柩归于上都，缘葬所须，并从官给。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1152695_comment'></div>公比及弥留，且有治命曰：「上遇我厚，必卤簿葬我。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1152695_comment'></div>生无益于国，死岂可烦于人」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1152695_comment'></div>诸弟等表其绪言，上深所嘉美，诏以钱五十万、绢三百匹、米麦百石赐其家，以备襄事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1152695_comment'></div>即以其年十月癸丑，归葬于京兆府长安县义阳乡大郭里，从先尚书之兆域，礼也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1152695_comment'></div>公娶清河张氏，封本郡夫人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1152695_comment'></div>婉錍柔嘉，幽閒令淑，仁洽宗党，教成闺门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1152695_comment'></div>二子：长曰纶，以延赏之恩，解褐太常寺太祝，年甫七岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1152695_comment'></div>次佛奴，尚在襁褓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1152695_comment'></div>三女：长适屯田员外郎杨垣，其二皆幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1152695_comment'></div>公生孝谨之族，负王佐之才，幼能属文，谈必稽古。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1152695_comment'></div>尚书府君之捐馆舍也，季父温舒以左拾遗守华原郡，公实从行府中，笺奏皆令代作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1152695_comment'></div>公口占五吏，应接不休；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1152695_comment'></div>日发百函，亲疏有意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1152695_comment'></div>季父拊背叹曰：「真我家国器，恨吾兄不见也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1152695_comment'></div>至性纯孝，出人远甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1152695_comment'></div>奉养慈母，烝烝膝下，调滫瀡以供膳，衣文䌽以承颜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1152695_comment'></div>左宦方州，单车独任，尽留妻妾，给侍庭闱，杜门端居，曾不屑虑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1152695_comment'></div>及太夫人寒暑遘疾，腠理寝深，公药必先尝，目不交睫，祷神请代，指景悼生，虽曾、闵之行，无以过也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1152695_comment'></div>长兄泌，职方员外郎，越王府记室；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1152695_comment'></div>次兄浣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1152695_comment'></div>皆先公而逝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1152695_comment'></div>弟湛，任大理寺丞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1152695_comment'></div>推以友爱，成乎敦睦，棠棣致美，埙篪相须，天伦之欢，士林耸慕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1152695_comment'></div>耀州富平簿涣，太子中允沆，处士澥，进士洞，殿中丞涛，校书郎澹，皆公之从父弟也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1152695_comment'></div>公承高门之庆，为保家之主，协比诸弟，纠合近亲，人不间言，儿无常父，宦成名立，率繇于公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1152695_comment'></div>游吉之亢宗，张仲之孝友，见于是矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1152695_comment'></div>公自决科筮仕，彯缨登朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1152695_comment'></div>至如羊舌肸习于《春秋》，而公分直东观，裁成国史；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1152695_comment'></div>公孙挥善为辞令，而公入参右掖，发挥王言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1152695_comment'></div>隽不疑之治狱也，多所平反，而公当详刑之任，民以不冤；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1152695_comment'></div>山巨源之荐贤也，密陈启事，而公操审官之柄，下无失职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1152695_comment'></div>严安、徐乐并在左右，而公步武禁林，润色帝载；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1152695_comment'></div>刘放、孙资对掌机密，而公徊翔丹地，秉执国钧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1152695_comment'></div>至于蹇蹇匪躬，岩岩群望，外庭集议，不曲从而诡随，宣室论思，必有犯而无隐，此诗人所称「邦之司直」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1152695_comment'></div>又如恂恂善诱，拳拳好德，博施以济众，功成不居，虚己以待物，事至而应，此仲尼所云「古之遗爱」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1152695_comment'></div>雅性冲澹，留心释老，早岁尝受道箓，晚节颇究禅筌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1152695_comment'></div>悟兹无生，用成达观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1152695_comment'></div>素善持论，酌之不竭；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1152695_comment'></div>多识典训，扣之斯应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1152695_comment'></div>挹量陂者，鄙吝之意自泯；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1152695_comment'></div>窥眉宇者，名利之念都息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1152695_comment'></div>接士在贵而思降，定交弥久而益恭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1152695_comment'></div>德迈种而愈勤，人服媚而无斁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1152695_comment'></div>蹊成桃李，夫又何言？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1152695_comment'></div>室有芝兰，但闻俱化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1152695_comment'></div>非大雅明哲，岂能及是耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1152695_comment'></div>公方以将明之才，辅文思之政，谈弭兵之术，议平戎之策，使单于之首，悬之藁街，辽阳之贡，陈于宰旅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1152695_comment'></div>致君尧舜，为宋伊、周。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1152695_comment'></div>而两楹遘灾，二竖为沴，天不慭遗，人之云亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1152695_comment'></div>召公深仁，徒结甘棠之爱；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1152695_comment'></div>留侯素志，莫遂赤松之游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1152695_comment'></div>藐是诸孤，庶乎有后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1152695_comment'></div>常所著述，遗札颇多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1152695_comment'></div>自掌命书，尤振时誉，累当大手笔之事，皆为士君子所伏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1152695_comment'></div>集二十卷，传之子孙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1152695_comment'></div>诸弟等以繐帐犹悬，宿草将列，忧陵谷之或变，虑德音之不昭，谋建丰碑，以表神道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1152695_comment'></div>以某尝学旧史，曾接生平，得以祖述世家，论次阀阅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1152695_comment'></div>叙大丘之德，谅无愧词；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1152695_comment'></div>非臧孙之言，敢期不朽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1152695_comment'></div>聊摭梗概，以为之铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1152695_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_133_1152695'>火德淳耀，文明诞敷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1152695_comment'></div>凤鸟斯至，神龟负图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1152695_comment'></div>时惟宋公，矫翼云衢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1152695_comment'></div>五百之运，其在兹乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1152695_comment'></div>黄离继明，百度思治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1152695_comment'></div>旰昃临朝，斋居决事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1152695_comment'></div>时惟宋公，将顺其美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1152695_comment'></div>咸平之政，既尽善矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1152695_comment'></div>八柱承天，七圣翊轩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1152695_comment'></div>䌤纶衮职，斟酌化源。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1152695_comment'></div>青蒲伏奏，温树无言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1152695_comment'></div>林父忠荩，康侯锡蕃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1152695_comment'></div>三边屡耸，六龙顺动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1152695_comment'></div>借箸前筹，属鞬景从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1152695_comment'></div>美疹弗瘳，吾谋犹用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_147_1152695_comment'></div>城郢遗言，涉洹占梦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_148_1152695_comment'></div>梁木斯坏，太素收神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_149_1152695_comment'></div>易箦而没，委顺全真。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_150_1152695_comment'></div>精爽何托，上骑星辰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_151_1152695_comment'></div>如可赎兮，人百其身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_152_1152695_comment'></div>行路咨嗟，冕旒悽恻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_153_1152695_comment'></div>股肱或亏，其痛何极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_154_1152695_comment'></div>尸谏犹切，忠魂弥激。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_155_1152695_comment'></div>临死之言，不忘社稷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_156_1152695_comment'></div>卜葬咸阳，蓍蔡弗违。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_157_1152695_comment'></div>封树云毕，閟兹音徽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_158_1152695_comment'></div>自古有死，吾将畴依。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_159_1152695_comment'></div>逝者可作，非公曷归？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_160_1152695_comment'></div>丘垄陵夷，光阴迅驶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_161_1152695_comment'></div>传信方来，孰非文字？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_162_1152695_comment'></div>乃刊贞珉，式表幽隧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_163_1152695_comment'></div>怀公之人，于斯堕泪。</div><div id='poem_sentence_164_1152695_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1001&endYear=1001')">1001年1月15日</a>　上元夜，与朱台符等会于太子詹事慎从吉西斋，分题赋诗。又和慎诗寄诸同舍。作品：上元夜会慎大詹西斋分题得歌字。次韵和主人喜诸客见过之什。坐中朱博士言今荆南张谏议典襄阳日尝留意一妓公颇畏内终不得近及移郡荆渚泣别邮亭乃为歌词流布巴郢予感其事赓而成诗。次韵和慎詹事述上元宵会之欢寄诸同舍之什。<div id='poem_129013' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_129013' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/129013?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上元夜会慎大詹西斋分题得歌字</a><span ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1001&endYear=1001')">1001年2月4日</a>　太仆少卿钱惟演直秘阁，亿以诗并至启贺之。作品：贺太仆钱少卿直秘阁。与秘阁钱少卿启。<div id='poem_129353' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_129353' class='poemTitle class='poemContent' id='poem_content_129353'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_129353'>几年宿卫向周庐，频贡文章白玉除。<div id='poem_sentence_0_129353_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence'
