id='poem_sentence_4_129353'>石渠讲论应重席，翠辇巡游且奉车。<div id='poem_sentence_4_129353_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_129353'>禁籞风光暮春月，彯缨看是缀严徐。<div id='poem_sentence_5_129353_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_129353'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_129353_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1152595' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152595' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152595?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与秘阁钱少卿启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1001年2月4日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152595")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152595_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152595'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152595'>右，某启：伏审光承圣恩，荣升秘府，恭惟庆慰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152595_comment'></div>伏以上帝藏书，是开册府；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152595_comment'></div>近臣待诏，爰设直庐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152595_comment'></div>所以校理秘文，讲求坠典，复石渠之故事，继炎汉之得人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152595_comment'></div>茍非奇才，岂膺是选？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152595_comment'></div>少卿学士家传带砺，身袭龟緺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152595_comment'></div>修仁克昌，吴芮早书于甲令；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152595_comment'></div>积善馀庆，毕万独享于魏封。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1152595_comment'></div>而自更宿周庐，入升环卫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1152595_comment'></div>贞师北落，不倚将军之尊，袭爵东吴，靡恃王孙之贵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1152595_comment'></div>但绝编而嗜学，常闭户以著书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1152595_comment'></div>万里立功，颇轻定远；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1152595_comment'></div>《三都》述赋，高揖太冲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1152595_comment'></div>万乘深喜于同时，九寺俄迁于少列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1152595_comment'></div>以才望之充积，果恩宠之便蕃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1152595_comment'></div>太仆奉车，方钦于贵盛；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1152595_comment'></div>秘书内阁，旋直于深严。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1152595_comment'></div>用旌稽古之功，尤洽当仁之论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1152595_comment'></div>眷惟职业，素所蕴崇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1152595_comment'></div>校石室之遗编，伫分四部；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1152595_comment'></div>侍柏梁之高宴，即赋七言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1152595_comment'></div>然陪清跸之游，更献从臣之颂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1152595_comment'></div>梁园旨酒，居客右以无疑；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1152595_comment'></div>谢砌苍苔，代王言而在即。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1152595_comment'></div>适增欣抃，遽辱缄题。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1152595_comment'></div>仰承谦退之私，何胜勤厚之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1152595_comment'></div>感激惭愧，不任下怀<span class='inlineComment2'>（《武夷新集》卷一九。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1152595_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_27_1152595'>校：原阙，据库本补。</div><div id='poem_sentence_27_1152595_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1001&endYear=1001')">1001年2月</a>　宰相李沆、王化基、向敏中以旱求罢，杨亿代撰《乞罢免表》作品：代中书乞罢免表一。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1001&endYear=1001')">1001年3月</a>　宰相李沆、王化基、向敏中以旱求罢，杨亿再代撰《乞罢免表》作品：代中书乞罢免表二。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1001&endYear=1001')">1001年</a>　二月及稍后，和李维《寒食即事》及《千字诗》作品：次韵和集贤李学士寒食即事之什。和集贤李学士千字诗。<div id='poem_129108' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_129108' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/129108?labeling=true' target='_blank'>次韵和集贤李学士寒食即事之什</a><span class='authorDate'>（1001年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_129108")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_129108_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_129108'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_129108'>九逵初旭满辎軿，寒食东风二月天。<div id='poem_sentence_0_129108_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_129108'>陌上垫巾谁傲睨，江边解佩自婵娟。<div id='poem_sentence_1_129108_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_129108'>新妆几处登墙见，沉醉何人藉草眠。<div id='poem_sentence_2_129108_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_129108'>豪侠追欢殊未足，归蹄躞蹀夕阳前。<div id='poem_sentence_3_129108_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_129108'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_129108_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_129152' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_129152' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/129152?labeling=true' target='_blank'>和集贤李学士千字诗</a><span class='authorDate'>（1001年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_129152")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_129152_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_129152'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_129152'>千仞溪何险，千仓稻已收。<div id='poem_sentence_0_129152_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_129152'>出骑千里马，醉典千金裘。<div id='poem_sentence_1_129152_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_129152'>千年河诞圣，千树橘封侯。<div id='poem_sentence_2_129152_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_129152'>千钟不及乱，千钱坐上头。<div id='poem_sentence_3_129152_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_129152'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_129152_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1001&endYear=1001')">1001年3月17日</a>　与近臣同侍帝后苑宴射，应制赋诗。作品：后苑赏花应制（宫花如锦水连漪）<span class='inlineComment2'>（杨亿《后苑赏花应制》注云：“以时字为韵。咸平四年三月十八日。”侍帝宴射在十七日，诗成于十八日。）</span><div id='poem_129069' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_129069' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/129069?labeling=true' target='_blank'>后苑赏花应制<span class='inlineComment2'>（以时字为韵咸平四年三月十八日）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1001年3月17日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_129069")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_129069_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_129069'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_129069'>宫花如锦水连漪，翠辇寻芳正是时。<div id='poem_sentence_0_129069_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_129069'>禁苑定知人未识，朱栏除有蝶偷窥。<div id='poem_sentence_1_129069_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_129069'>艳烘晓日迷天仗，香逐轻风落酒卮。<div id='poem_sentence_2_129069_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_129069'>何幸微臣陪镐宴，蓬壶春漏正迟迟。<div id='poem_sentence_3_129069_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_129069'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_129069_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1001&endYear=1001')">1001年3月19日</a>　制授王旦参知政事，亿代撰让官表。作品：代参政王侍郎让恩命表。<div id='poem_1152462' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152462' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152462?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代参政王侍郎让恩命表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1001年3月19日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152462")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152462_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152462'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152462'>臣某言：伏奉制命，蒙恩特授尚书工部侍郎、参知政事，馀如故者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152462_comment'></div>文昌六官，骤迁于品秩；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152462_comment'></div>黄枢万务，俾预于吁谟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152462_comment'></div>受宠若惊，循涯自失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152462_comment'></div>臣<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>窃以辅弼之任，实代天工；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152462_comment'></div>简求之时，允资人杰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152462_comment'></div>况岩廊之上，副师尹之具瞻；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152462_comment'></div>车服以庸，下丞相之一等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1152462_comment'></div>岂宜滥处，以累至公？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1152462_comment'></div>如臣者，才不逮人，学非稽古，徒荷鲤庭之训，谬登汉殿之科。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1152462_comment'></div>金闺偶列于姓名，蓬岛获窥于图史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1152462_comment'></div>寻掌纶于右掖，复寓直于北门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1152462_comment'></div>骤蒙振拔之恩，获预枢机之任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1152462_comment'></div>参谋帷幄，曾无前箸之筹；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1152462_comment'></div>受禄水衡，深有素飧之愧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1152462_comment'></div>方忧非据，忽奉殊迁，佐阴阳调燮之权，亚辅相崇高之秩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1152462_comment'></div>斗筲至小，殊觉于满盈；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1152462_comment'></div>鼎铉不任，转虞于倾覆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1152462_comment'></div>茍贪荣宠，靡敢敷陈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1152462_comment'></div>岂惟鬼瞰以堪忧，实亦人言之可畏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1152462_comment'></div>伏望尊号皇帝陛下俯矜短拙，曲赐保全，特诏有司，俾停新命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1152462_comment'></div>既负且乘，微臣免至于疾颠；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1152462_comment'></div>唯器与名，圣代更无于虚授。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1152462_comment'></div>虔切之至，伏候允俞。</div><div id='poem_sentence_23_1152462_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1001&endYear=1001')">1001年3月19日</a>　以亿望实素著，未经中书试，即与薛映、梁鼎并命为知制诰。亿上表、启以谢。作品：谢知制诰表。谢除左司谏知制诰表。<div id='poem_1152463' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152463' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152463?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢知制诰表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1001年3月19日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152463")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152463_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152463'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152463'>臣某言：伏奉制命，蒙恩特授臣左司谏、知制诰，仍面赐金紫者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152463_comment'></div>代言禁掖，允谓难才；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152463_comment'></div>赐服轩墀，荐加异数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152463_comment'></div>实曳娄之非称，但跼蹐以靡遑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152463_comment'></div>臣<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>窃以青琐之闼，地望最崇；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152463_comment'></div>紫微之垣，天文是法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152463_comment'></div>设署位于赤墀之下，开直庐于黄阁之中，草尺一之诏书，预五花之判事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152463_comment'></div>发施号令，用诞告于万邦；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1152463_comment'></div>裁成典谟，必追踪于三代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1152463_comment'></div>自非髦俊，岂副拟抡？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1152463_comment'></div>如臣者生自遐陬，本惟寒士，始从童丱，偶涉艺文，勤虽至于绝编，学未能于睹奥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1152463_comment'></div>先皇帝闻其姓字，召赴京师，试于钩盾之中，署以芸香之职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1152463_comment'></div>犬马之齿尚幼，乌鸟之恋颇增。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1152463_comment'></div>获归省于庭闱，久留连于乡曲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1152463_comment'></div>洎还象阙，复隶麟台，寻奏伎于公车，得阅书于东观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1152463_comment'></div>自尔赐太常之科第，预仙殿之职名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1152463_comment'></div>献颂甘泉，特颁命服；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1152463_comment'></div>赋诗柏殿，屡挹衢樽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1152463_comment'></div>属圣政之维新，荷鸿私而首及，擢厕从臣之列，预修太史之书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1152463_comment'></div>惭无直笔之称，莫述先朝之美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1152463_comment'></div>俄切维桑之念，坚求剖竹之行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1152463_comment'></div>崇文广武圣明仁孝皇帝陛下推从欲之深仁，遂承颜之至恳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1152463_comment'></div>会稽出守，既谐昼锦之荣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1152463_comment'></div>天禄言归，重励草《玄》之业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1152463_comment'></div>唯固穷而守道，常省分以忘怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1152463_comment'></div>一亩之宫，愿栖迟而无闷；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1152463_comment'></div>三千之牍，诚衒鬻以为惭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1152463_comment'></div>公府绝造请之仪，禁掖非觊觎之地，老于削椠，是所甘心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1152463_comment'></div>岂谓皇帝陛下察孤直之无徒，念遭逢之有素，当慎选之际，垂特达之知，拔于群萃之中，霈以殊常之泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1152463_comment'></div>补衮之阙，骤进七人之班；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1152463_comment'></div>演丝成纶，便裁五色之诏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1152463_comment'></div>金印紫绶，诚佩服以非宜；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1152463_comment'></div>珠网绮钱，顾优游而何幸！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1152463_comment'></div>官箴斯在，舆颂是虞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1152463_comment'></div>至如汉马卿之才华，方合视草；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1152463_comment'></div>唐常衮之词学，才善除书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1152463_comment'></div>岂兹短才，可以称职？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1152463_comment'></div>然万乘之知特异，九天之命已行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1152463_comment'></div>譬诸驽骀，亦当鞭策其后；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1152463_comment'></div>至于铅钝，敢不摩厉以须？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1152463_comment'></div>庶罄竭于诚明，免废坠于职业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1152463_comment'></div>退循散拙，弥负忧兢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1152463_comment'></div>仰荷天慈，臣无任云云。</div><div id='poem_sentence_42_1152463_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1152597' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152597' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152597?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢除左司谏知制诰启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1001年3月19日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152597")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152597_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152597'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152597'>右，某启：伏奉制命，蒙恩特授前件官、知制诰，仍改赐章服者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152597_comment'></div>代言之任，实演于丝纶；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152597_comment'></div>赐服之崇，莫过于银艾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152597_comment'></div>仍进东台之秩，便参右掖之荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152597_comment'></div>茍非名流，不在兹选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152597_comment'></div>祗荷成命，若无所容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152597_comment'></div>伏念某才不兼人，学非博物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152597_comment'></div>关西清白，徒袭于素风；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1152597_comment'></div>天禄校雠，偶尘于美仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1152597_comment'></div>久居谏署，莫贡皂囊；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1152597_comment'></div>预草国书，谬刊青简。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1152597_comment'></div>寻一麾而领郡，凡再岁以归朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1152597_comment'></div>宿于交戟之中，惟思幞被；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1152597_comment'></div>班在赤墀之下，深愧彯缨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1152597_comment'></div>盖自知之甚明，亦不能而将止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1152597_comment'></div>衒鬻者千数，岂敢诣于公车；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1152597_comment'></div>谏诤者七人，未尝攀于殿槛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1152597_comment'></div>官守之方既失，食浮之议已喧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1152597_comment'></div>敢冀明恩，并加殊宠？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1152597_comment'></div>补衮增秩，任在于弥缝；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1152597_comment'></div>视草求才，职思于润色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1152597_comment'></div>及奉延英之对，更颁命服之荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1152597_comment'></div>凤阁徊翔，已玷巢阿之地；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1152597_comment'></div>鹈梁忝窃，曷逃濡咮之讥？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1152597_comment'></div>矧惟星垣，上法天象。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1152597_comment'></div>荧煌之座，出处近于三台；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1152597_comment'></div>清切之司，动静尊乎肆禁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1152597_comment'></div>紫宸挥翰，垂作典谟；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1152597_comment'></div>红药裁诗，形于骚雅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1152597_comment'></div>为仕进之极美，顾鄙陋以宁堪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1152597_comment'></div>伏揣器能，深惟职业，尺一之诏书填委，但惧稽留；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1152597_comment'></div>六曹之奏议纷纭，将何平决？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1152597_comment'></div>但省躬而增惕，念奋迹之有因。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1152597_comment'></div>此盖某官钦奉昌图，勤求片善，采虚名于画饼，奖薄技于雕虫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1152597_comment'></div>挥麈尾之谈，曲垂题品；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1152597_comment'></div>借羊角之势，使得抟扶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1152597_comment'></div>敢不磨厉以须，僶俛从事，庶逭假人之谤，用酬知己之私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1152597_comment'></div>过此以还，未知所措。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_37_1152597'></div><div id='poem_sentence_37_1152597_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1001&endYear=1001')">1001年</a>　有诗和李宗谔喜拜命之作，又以诗答谢李源、盛度、宗人安期庆贺新命之作。作品：次韵和阁长李舍人喜薛梁二舍人及予同时拜命之什。<span class='inlineComment2'>（李宗谔原诗已佚。）</span>次韵和宗人安期见贺恩命之作。酬谢光丞四丈见庆新命之什。<span class='inlineComment2'>（李源原诗已佚。）</span>史馆盛学士以诗相贺因而答之。<span class='inlineComment2'>（盛度原诗已佚。）</span><div id='poem_129094' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_129094' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/129094?labeling=true' target='_blank'>次韵和阁长李舍人喜薛梁二舍人及予同时拜命之什</a><span class='authorDate'>（1001年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_129094")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_129094_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_129094'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_129094'>西垣清切本无伦，虚薄将何缀侍臣。<div id='poem_sentence_0_129094_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_129094'>承露盘高云际晓，栖鸡树绿省中春。<div id='poem_sentence_1_129094_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_129094'>言成纶綍终非称，室蔼芝兰幸得亲。<div id='poem_sentence_2_129094_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_129094'>从此烟霄连步武，宸游长奉属车尘。<div id='poem_sentence_3_129094_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_129094'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_129094_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_129089' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_129089' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/129089?labeling=true' target='_blank'>次韵和宗人安期见贺恩命之什</a><span class='authorDate'>（1001年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_129089")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_129089_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_129089'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_129089'>分班晓入翔鸾阙，直阁旁连浴凤池。<div id='poem_sentence_0_129089_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_129089'>彩笔闲批五色诏，好风时动万年枝。<div id='poem_sentence_1_129089_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_129089'>勒移钟阜惭归晚，称疾文园恨思迟。<div id='poem_sentence_2_129089_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_129089'>何事吾宗心倍喜，春塘梦彻寄新诗。<div id='poem_sentence_3_129089_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_129089'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_129089_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_129377' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_129377' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/129377?labeling=true' target='_blank'>酬谢光丞四丈见庆新命之什</a><span class='authorDate'>（1001年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_129377")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_129377_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_129377'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_129377'>武夷归路苦迢遥，延阁官曹正寂寥。<div id='poem_sentence_0_129377_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_129377'>彩凤衔书俄锡命，黄金刻印便悬腰。<div id='poem_sentence_1_129377_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_129377'>紫微署近时当制，建礼门深日趁朝。<div id='poem_sentence_2_129377_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_129377'>咫尺天颜曾赐对，荧煌台座得为僚。<div id='poem_sentence_3_129377_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_129377'>鬼神清问忧前席，松柏深情见后凋。<div id='poem_sentence_4_129377_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_129377'>一曲阳春特相寄，惭将木李报琼瑶。<div id='poem_sentence_5_129377_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_129377'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_129377_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_129052' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_129052' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/129052?labeling=true' target='_blank'>史馆盛学士以诗相贺因而答之</a><span class='authorDate'>（1001年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_129052")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_129052_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_129052'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_129052'>前年出守缙云城，曾枉骊歌慰远行。<div id='poem_sentence_0_129052_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_129052'>今日代言青锁闼，又披郢唱见深情。<div id='poem_sentence_1_129052_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_129052'>侧聆九奏都忘味，连得双金自满籯。<div id='poem_sentence_2_129052_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_129052'>红药阶前试吟嚼，胸中鄙吝一时平。<div id='poem_sentence_3_129052_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_129052'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_129052_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1001&endYear=1001')">1001年</a>　并州王太保超致书，多赞美之词，并征处州赠行诗，亿有答书。作品：答并州王太保书。<div id='poem_1152583' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152583' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152583?labeling=true' target='_blank'>答并州王太保书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1001年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152583")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152583_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152583'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152583'>并州太保麾下：近于集贤石君表臣处得手笔一封，耽玩再三，不能暂舍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152583_comment'></div>文彩焕发，五色以相宣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152583_comment'></div>理道贯通，有条而不紊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152583_comment'></div>薰风拂衽，自然析酲；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152583_comment'></div>箫韶在悬，殊觉忘味。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152583_comment'></div>何厚赐之所及，见久要之不忘，甚善甚善！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152583_comment'></div>窃伏自念江表布衣，材出人下，非山东阀阅之后，无负郭膏腴之产<span class='inlineComment2'>（〔一〕）</span>，徒荷世业，遂忝儒流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152583_comment'></div>龆龀之时，传召诣阙<span class='inlineComment2'>（〔二〕）</span>；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1152583_comment'></div>弱冠之岁，通籍于朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1152583_comment'></div>担簦蹑屩，既周于四方；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1152583_comment'></div>抱椠怀铅，亦几乎十载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1152583_comment'></div>何尝不咨诹先觉，博求同人！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1152583_comment'></div>直谅多闻，必取乎三益；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1152583_comment'></div>谈穷势贿，克慎乎五交，懔懔然唯惧当世之贤豪见拒而不容也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1152583_comment'></div>数年前，石氏西斋邂逅相遇，盱衡扺掌，坐客尽倾；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1152583_comment'></div>枕曲藉糟，羽觞无算。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1152583_comment'></div>亦既卜夜，至于继烛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1152583_comment'></div>剖心析肝，荡无城府；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1152583_comment'></div>讲道论义，芬若椒兰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1152583_comment'></div>倾盖如故，此之谓矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1152583_comment'></div>未几边郡思乂，足下既十乘而启行；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1152583_comment'></div>国书成功，下走亦一麾而出守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1152583_comment'></div>地理辽远，诚马牛之不及；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1152583_comment'></div>官守萦系，同匏瓜之见拘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1152583_comment'></div>无复裁咫尺之书，述固陋之恳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1152583_comment'></div>去年仆祇召西走，来朝帝庭；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1152583_comment'></div>足下方镇并门，式遏戎略。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1152583_comment'></div>引领北望，缅怀故人，恨不得解籍金闺，从军紫塞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1152583_comment'></div>依莲汎水，陪幕府之宾从；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1152583_comment'></div>投壶雅歌，奉郡斋之游宴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1152583_comment'></div>今年肇自书殿，入升纶闱，以雕虫篆刻之才，当典谟训诰之任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1152583_comment'></div>五羖之鞟，不能成虎豹之文；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1152583_comment'></div>一割之刀，固无剸犀兕之利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1152583_comment'></div>方夙夜愧惕，惧忝君命，为知己羞，而足下闻之，欣然以书为贶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1152583_comment'></div>松茂柏悦，情虽后凋；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1152583_comment'></div>玉振金相，词多溢美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1152583_comment'></div>且徵缙云赠行之什，颇有姑尤善祝之言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1152583_comment'></div>虽然戏谑，若合符契。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1152583_comment'></div>窃以古之交道，尝闻之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1152583_comment'></div>盖以闻善相告，爵禄相先，急病让夷，谋事补阙，以引以翼，或推或挽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1152583_comment'></div>故萧何举代，曹参趣装以请行；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1152583_comment'></div>王阳登用，贡禹弹冠而愿仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1152583_comment'></div>伐木求友，颂声载扬；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1152583_comment'></div>远方得朋，名教为乐，益以见足下之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1152583_comment'></div>当仆之领郡也，必欲发挥虚名，稔熟舆听，故群公供帐，发而诗成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1152583_comment'></div>及仆之窃宠也，又欲销弭浮谤，充塞前言，故千里附书，明徵其事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1152583_comment'></div>使鄙夫无暴得之愧，圣朝免虚授之讥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1152583_comment'></div>仁者用心，其利溥矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1152583_comment'></div>足以明杀鸡炊黍，范、张区区于小信；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1152583_comment'></div>缟带纻衣，侨、札拳拳于微物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1152583_comment'></div>以今况古，夫何隘哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1152583_comment'></div>边尘不惊，戎阃自肃，干木高卧，足以作藩，夷甫清谈，未妨为政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1152583_comment'></div>唯节宣吐纳，顺时加爱，副九重推毂之寄，成万里封侯之荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1152583_comment'></div>斯慺慺之诚，所望于明哲也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1152583_comment'></div>某顿首。</div><div id='poem_sentence_54_1152583_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1001&endYear=1001')">1001年3月</a>　代冯拯撰让官表。作品：代枢密冯谏议让官表。<div id='poem_1152460' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152460' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152460?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代枢密冯谏议让表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1001年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152460")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152460_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152460'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152460'>臣某言：伏奉制命，授臣右谏议大夫、同知枢密院事者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152460_comment'></div>任峻枢衡，秩崇谏署，虽荷自天之命，弥增跼地之忧，循省再三，陨越无措<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152460_comment'></div>窃以中枢之设，庶政攸归，地望处于深严，职任推于宥密。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152460_comment'></div>朝夕献替，得预于论思；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152460_comment'></div>军国机宜，并令于参决。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152460_comment'></div>茍非挺生民之秀，负王佐之才，嘉言嘉猷，可陪于汉幄，令问令望，素重于周行，即何以膺兑泽于九天，赞禁庭之万务？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152460_comment'></div>在于授受，须允佥谐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152460_comment'></div>如臣者梼昧无闻，迂疏有素，早服膺于文史，偶被荐于贤能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1152460_comment'></div>东堂谬厕于高科，北省寻尘于近列，曾乏当官之称，果贻窃禄之讥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1152460_comment'></div>俄假一麾，远之五岭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1152460_comment'></div>万里空嗟于日远，莫见长安；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1152460_comment'></div>六龙幸属于天飞，得还魏阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1152460_comment'></div>郎署骤迁于秩序，计司令勾于簿书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1152460_comment'></div>遽承乏于柏台，得触邪于蓂砌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1152460_comment'></div>选愞曷伸于职业？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1152460_comment'></div>因循徒历于岁时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1152460_comment'></div>爰自中司，便参近侍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1152460_comment'></div>奉冕旒于武帐，莫效谋猷；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1152460_comment'></div>提铨管于文昌，岂分流品？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1152460_comment'></div>敢谓便蕃之泽，俾参密勿之司，皂囊秩峻于七人，丹地宠延于三接。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1152460_comment'></div>挈瓶之智，倾觉于满盈，履薄之心，不胜于战慄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1152460_comment'></div>实群言之可畏，亦省分以甚明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1152460_comment'></div>须露至诚，仰干玄造。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1152460_comment'></div>伏望尊号皇帝陛下矜其散拙，察以勤拳，特寝新恩，且仍旧贯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1152460_comment'></div>即微臣展四体以率职，更誓恪居；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1152460_comment'></div>圣朝悬好爵以縻贤，庶无虚授。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1152460_comment'></div>虔切之至，伏待允俞。</div><div id='poem_sentence_26_1152460_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1001&endYear=1001')">1001年3月</a>　代陈尧叟撰让官表。作品：代枢密陈谏议让官表。<div id='poem_1152459' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152459' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152459?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代枢密陈谏议让表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1001年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152459")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152459_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152459'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152459'>臣某言：伏奉诰命，蒙恩特授守右谏议大夫、同知枢密院事，馀如故者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152459_comment'></div>丝纶之命，忽降于九霄；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152459_comment'></div>宥密之司，俾参于万务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152459_comment'></div>抚微躬而战慄，听舆议以喧哗，实出非常，深知不称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152459_comment'></div>某<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>窃以谏诤之官，首冠七人之列；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152459_comment'></div>枢机之地，日蒙三捷之荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152459_comment'></div>运筹帷幄之中，议政岩廊之上，盖号股肱之任，必求柱石之材。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152459_comment'></div>如臣者，器本庸微，识惟蒙鄙，为学仅通于章句，奋身早自于丘园。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1152459_comment'></div>先朝谬中于甲科，初命便尘于史阁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1152459_comment'></div>佐钱刀于会府，投刃靡虚；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1152459_comment'></div>掌漕挽于番禺，扬旌甚远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1152459_comment'></div>归阙荷金章之赐，安边无铜柱之勋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1152459_comment'></div>寻复命于紫庭，遽叨荣于丹地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1152459_comment'></div>奉论思于武帐，謇谔无闻；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1152459_comment'></div>阅章奏于公车，否臧莫辩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1152459_comment'></div>顾官箴而是愧，矧岁律之未周。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1152459_comment'></div>敢期涣汗之恩，遽授丝纶之寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1152459_comment'></div>参决庶务，况国政之所归；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1152459_comment'></div>叨据上流，实人言之可畏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1152459_comment'></div>顾践扬之犹浅，且位望以甚隆，茍徒窃禄以冒居，不敢叫阍而沥恳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1152459_comment'></div>既负且乘，岂致寇以非遥？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1152459_comment'></div>居高必危，亦疾颠而是惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1152459_comment'></div>须披肺腑，仰渎冕旒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1152459_comment'></div>伏望尊号皇帝陛下察以至诚，寝兹新命，职守且仍于旧贯，名器免至于假人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1152459_comment'></div>所希为官择才，圣朝无虚授之宠；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1152459_comment'></div>陈力就列，下臣遂知止之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1152459_comment'></div>干冒宸严，期于得请。</div><div id='poem_sentence_26_1152459_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1001&endYear=1001')">1001年3？</a>　三月或稍后，有书启与梁鼎。作品：与梁舍人启。<div id='poem_1152600' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152600' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152600?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与梁舍人启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1001年3？）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152600")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152600_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152600'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152600'>右：某启：伏自拜恩，已伸面贺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152600_comment'></div>恭惟舍人壶冰峻彩，岩桂标英，禀秀气于岷峨，振雄名于京洛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152600_comment'></div>学惟睹奥，入圣域而已优；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152600_comment'></div>辩可离坚，占议围而无敌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152600_comment'></div>品格素高于月旦，词华早掞于天庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152600_comment'></div>爰自先朝，便升清贯，内佐计相，外剖使符，体宽大以布诏条，用文雅而饰吏事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152600_comment'></div>坐棠听讼，克播于欢谣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152600_comment'></div>视草求才，果膺于急召。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1152600_comment'></div>爰九重而肆觐，见万乘以垂知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1152600_comment'></div>宣室延登，问鬼神于前席；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1152600_comment'></div>禁林试可，给笔札于尚方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1152600_comment'></div>一时之纸价顿高，翌日之丝言荐降。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1152600_comment'></div>南宫卧锦，既改七兵之曹；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1152600_comment'></div>西掖封泥，便裁五色之诏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1152600_comment'></div>将启迪于帝载，实焜耀于儒林。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1152600_comment'></div>平奏议于省中，伫申明于唐制，颁号令于天下，同诞布于尧言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1152600_comment'></div>三代之风，不日而复。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1152600_comment'></div>某声尘无取，名辈相辽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1152600_comment'></div>偶谐附骥之诚，亦在续貂之末。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1152600_comment'></div>幸依先觉，必免至于面墙；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1152600_comment'></div>怯见大巫，已自甘于阁笔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1152600_comment'></div>然得亲于兰室，须强厉于铅刀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1152600_comment'></div>顾函丈之有期，忽尺题而为贶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1152600_comment'></div>仰荷劳谦之旨，愈增反仄之怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1152600_comment'></div>内省庸虚，何以胜克？</div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1152600_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1001&endYear=1001')">1001年3？</a>　三月或稍后，有书启与薛映。作品：与薛舍人启。<div id='poem_1152602' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152602' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152602?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与薛舍人启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1001年3？）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152602")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152602_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152602'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152602'>右：某启：伏自光奉天恩，已伸拜贺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152602_comment'></div>伏以舍人汾阴令族，稷下名流，摛词掞天，聚学成海。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152602_comment'></div>千丈磊砢，材实任于栋梁；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152602_comment'></div>十德瑰琦，器自标于瑚琏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152602_comment'></div>早践扬于近署，久薰灼于大名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152602_comment'></div>群公怀居右之惭，万乘恨相得之晚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152602_comment'></div>调两河之兵食，遂辍輶轩，裁五色之诏书，爰升琐闼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152602_comment'></div>华星列位，既上应于哀乌；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1152602_comment'></div>文石分班，且日趋于翔凤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1152602_comment'></div>固已给北宫之双笔，判西掖之五花，思若涌泉，吏将脱腕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1152602_comment'></div>盘石尚在，念祖德之不忘；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1152602_comment'></div>青纸远颁，见王言之诞布。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1152602_comment'></div>固汤诰、禹谟之可复，岂元和、长庆之足云！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1152602_comment'></div>某品格非高，资望素浅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1152602_comment'></div>慕义不已，徒愿于执鞭；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1152602_comment'></div>受宠若惊，敢希于结绶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1152602_comment'></div>附骐骥之尾，或千里之可期；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1152602_comment'></div>草凤凰之书，忧一词而不措。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1152602_comment'></div>北面永伸于师事，东邱岂吝于诲人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1152602_comment'></div>庶承善诱之恩，少逭旷官之责。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1152602_comment'></div>特蒙殊念，曲示长笺，仰戴重知，无任下恳。</div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1152602_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1001&endYear=1001')">1001年4月</a>　奉敕撰试贤良方正策二道。作品：咸平四年四月试贤良方正科策。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1001&endYear=1001')">1001年4月</a>　查道登咸平四年贤良方正科，以书致谢，亿有启答之。作品：谢贤良登科查正言启。<div id='poem_1152603' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152603' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152603?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢贤良登科查正言启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1001年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152603")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152603_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152603'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152603'>某启：伏睹拜恩，已伸面贺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152603_comment'></div>窃以汉崇儒术，始策问于贤良；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152603_comment'></div>唐设制科，多柬求于将相。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152603_comment'></div>既公卿而表荐，亦郡国之计偕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152603_comment'></div>延见于白虎之庭，召试于紫宸之殿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152603_comment'></div>设以三道，必人事而直言；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152603_comment'></div>宾于四门，咸茂才而异等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152603_comment'></div>由是仲舒、晁错，明精祲相荡之源；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1152603_comment'></div>居易、微之，中才识兼茂之选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1152603_comment'></div>故西京号为得士，贞元谓之尚文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1152603_comment'></div>烈于圣朝，聿修坠典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1152603_comment'></div>万乘端冕，坐于武帐之中；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1152603_comment'></div>群臣彯缨，侍于文石之上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1152603_comment'></div>设帐幕之九张，给简牍之三千，赐盛馔于大官，示温颜于前席。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1152603_comment'></div>束帛加璧，顾未为优；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1152603_comment'></div>筑馆以金，曾何足算？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1152603_comment'></div>而某官钦承清问，奋发雄才，翰动若飞，文不加点。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1152603_comment'></div>吾丘之智略辐凑，自谓少双；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1152603_comment'></div>平津之条对精详，果居第一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1152603_comment'></div>天子屡形于叹息，诸公咸愿于服膺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1152603_comment'></div>足光仄席之求，旋降出纶之命，仍于翌日，复对两阶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1152603_comment'></div>天威不违，独恨相得之晚；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1152603_comment'></div>异人间出，必立非常之功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1152603_comment'></div>方偃伏于下风，忽捧承于华检。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1152603_comment'></div>仰窥谦退，非所克当。</div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1152603_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1001&endYear=1001')">1001年5月17日</a>　王禹偁卒于蕲州，亿闻讣作挽歌五首伤之。作品：故蕲州王刑部阁老挽歌五首。<span class='inlineComment2'>（王禹偁卒于五月十七日，六月十八日讣闻于上，亿作挽歌当在稍后。）</span><div id='poem_129210' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_129210' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/129210?labeling=true' target='_blank'>故蕲州王刑部阁老挽歌五首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1001年5月17日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_129210")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_129210_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_129210'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_129210'>东观未绝笔，西垣俄解龟。<div id='poem_sentence_0_129210_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_129210'>罢裁青纸诏，重入白云司。<div id='poem_sentence_1_129210_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_129210'>流落成三黜，联翩换一麾。<div id='poem_sentence_2_129210_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_129210'>黄岗与滁上，应立去思碑。<div id='poem_sentence_3_129210_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_129210'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_129210_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_129209' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_129209' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/129209?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1001年5月17日）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_129209_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_129209'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_129209'>鸡省曾三入，鳌峰近十旬。<div id='poem_sentence_0_129209_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_129209'>命书批凤尾，谏疏逆龙鳞。<div id='poem_sentence_1_129209_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_129209'>按部朱轓远，悲秋素发新。<div id='poem_sentence_2_129209_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_129209'>茂陵终不起，遗札满埃尘。<div id='poem_sentence_3_129209_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_129209'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_129209_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_129208' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_129208' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_title_129208_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_129208'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_129208'>近署罹官谤，清淮绾郡章。<div id='poem_sentence_0_129208_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_129208'>平生不佞佛，晚岁尚为郎。<div id='poem_sentence_1_129208_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_129208'>得疾因卑湿，为文足感伤。<div id='poem_sentence_2_129208_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_129208'>才蒙宣室召，奄忽叹云亡。<div id='poem_sentence_3_129208_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_129208'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_129208_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_129207' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_129207' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/129207?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其四 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1001年5月17日）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_129207_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_129207'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_129207'>楚客离骚怨，子牟江海心。<div id='poem_sentence_0_129207_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_129207'>积忧偏损寿，多病未妨吟。<div id='poem_sentence_1_129207_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_129207'>野鸟俄窥舍，甘棠已结阴。<div id='poem_sentence_2_129207_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_129207'>郡中应罢市，遗爱在人深。<div id='poem_sentence_3_129207_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_129207'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_129207_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_129206' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_129206' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/129206?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其五 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1001年5月17日）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_129206_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_129206'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_129206'>奏稿应盈箧，藏书复几车。<div id='poem_sentence_0_129206_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_129206'>门人谁渍酒，天子想投瓜。<div id='poem_sentence_1_129206_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_129206'>旅榇关山阔，铭旌道路赊。<div id='poem_sentence_2_129206_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_129206'>趋庭有令子，清白自传家。<div id='poem_sentence_3_129206_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_129206'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_129206_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1001&endYear=1001')">1001年</a>　有诗送卞衮再赴淮南转运。作品：殿院卞侍郎赴淮南转运。<div id='poem_129375' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_129375' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/129375?labeling=true' target='_blank'>殿院卞侍御赴淮南转运<span class='inlineComment2'>（卞近自淮右副运归阙，为计司判官）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1001年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_129375")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_129375_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_129375'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_129375'>莎庭治行推尤异，梁苑声华占上流。<div id='poem_sentence_0_129375_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_129375'>早是都人避骢马，近陪计相运牙筹。<div id='poem_sentence_1_129375_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_129375'>东南转粟承新命，淮海扬旌到旧游。<div id='poem_sentence_2_129375_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_129375'>骑置非时陈密启，壶浆几处望行舟。<div id='poem_sentence_3_129375_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_129375'>黄金刻印大如斗，白简飞霜凛若秋。<div id='poem_sentence_4_129375_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_129375'>岁满功成来会课，多应便拜富人侯。<div id='poem_sentence_5_129375_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_129375'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_129375_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1001&endYear=1001')">1001年</a>　夏，有诗送李维赴歙州，并序。作品：李四赴歙州。送集贤李学士员外知歙州序。<div id='poem_129141' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_129141' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/129141?labeling=true' target='_blank'>李四赴歙州</a><span class='authorDate'>（1001年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_129141")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_129141_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_129141'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_129141'>分直蓬邱未再期，江东去去拥旌麾。<div id='poem_sentence_0_129141_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_129141'>名通南省郎官籍，卷续新安郡政诗<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_129141_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_129141'>虎观清风留汗简，鸰原高韵忆吹篪。<div id='poem_sentence_2_129141_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_129141'>故人别后频南望，想见森森琼树枝。<div id='poem_sentence_3_129141_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_129141'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_129141_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_129141'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_1_129141_0'>⑴ 自注：好事者编新安前后太守所赋诗为三卷，目之曰《新安郡政诗》，见行于世。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_129141_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_1152651' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152651' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152651?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送集贤李学士员外知歙州序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1001年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152651")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152651_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152651'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152651'>昔汉明帝云：「郎官上应列宿，出宰百里」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152651_comment'></div>王坦之亦云：「尚书郎正用第二人，何得以此见拟」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152651_comment'></div>当时虽含香握兰，趋走丹墀，未甚重也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152651_comment'></div>爰暨唐室，稍盛其选，由谏官、御史次补者为美迁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152651_comment'></div>迄于皇朝，地望弥峻，乃有侍讲金华之殿，待诏玉堂之署，典校天禄阁，更直紫薇垣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152651_comment'></div>外之即建行台，刺列郡，持使节，总百城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152651_comment'></div>故台郎之贵，过曩时远甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152651_comment'></div>集贤学士、屯田外郎李君，在兴国、雍熙中，以文雄于场屋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1152651_comment'></div>太宗皇帝凡五临轩，试郡国贡士，君以英才杰出，策名甲科。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1152651_comment'></div>自尔随牒于淮、淝间，为诸侯所宾礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1152651_comment'></div>奏伎记室，檄成而愈风；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1152651_comment'></div>案事邻州，狱决而得雨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1152651_comment'></div>入佐著作，改丞太常，掌礼秩宗，阅书广内。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1152651_comment'></div>既而宰邑吴会，有弦歌之音；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1152651_comment'></div>校文成均，正鲁鱼之谬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1152651_comment'></div>英华外发，名声日闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1152651_comment'></div>天子知其藏器在身，劳谦不伐，特出中旨，召试禁林。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1152651_comment'></div>翰动若飞，文不加点，北门诸公，扺掌叹伏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1152651_comment'></div>翌日，受诏兼直书殿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1152651_comment'></div>君蹈泳亨衢，翱翔近署，诚衡遇物，靡有低昂，量陂虚受，不闻澄挠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1152651_comment'></div>天球擅响，雅、郑洞分；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1152651_comment'></div>水鉴忘情，毛发皆见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1152651_comment'></div>为士林之圭表，亦人伦之蓍蔡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1152651_comment'></div>每太液波渌，汾睢草黄，或御酒百壶，式陈镐宴，或卿云五色，垂示天章，君必沾玉斝之醇醪，联柏梁之高韵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1152651_comment'></div>赐花夺锦，肯让景龙时人；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1152651_comment'></div>桂水空梁，无取南朝之体。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1152651_comment'></div>此外风规蕴藉，不杂尘游，驱放玄虚，善谈名理，求之一时，未易得也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1152651_comment'></div>君屏迹势利，游心虚白。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1152651_comment'></div>践赤墀而登文石，非所晏安；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1152651_comment'></div>拍洪崖而挹浮丘，是其雅素。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1152651_comment'></div>且以新安山水之奇秀，江左人物之瑰玮，严助餍承明之庐，劳于侍从；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1152651_comment'></div>阮籍求东平之守，乐其风土。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1152651_comment'></div>实奉俞诏，欢然惬心，夙兴戒徒，星言行役。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1152651_comment'></div>噫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1152651_comment'></div>锦帐绫被，有中台之礼秩；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1152651_comment'></div>金匮牙签，有延阁之官次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1152651_comment'></div>悬龟曳组，建隼剖符，驿吏驾车而来迎，县令负弩而前引。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1152651_comment'></div>千骑骎骎而挟毂，诸曹冉冉而趋府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1152651_comment'></div>载棨戟以先道，露黻冕以行春。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1152651_comment'></div>四十岁专城而居，虽尽美矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1152651_comment'></div>二千石与我共理，厥惟勉旃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1152651_comment'></div>行矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1152651_comment'></div>火云吐峰，汴流激箭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1152651_comment'></div>仙舟东下，何翅一叶之轻；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1152651_comment'></div>旅雁北徂，勿忘尺书之贶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1152651_comment'></div>其它，即期月报政，朝廷赏劳，幸预代言之末，愿草陟明之诏云耳。</div><div id='poem_sentence_45_1152651_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1001&endYear=1001')">1001年</a>　中伏日省直，七夕，先后有诗。作品：中伏日省中当直。七夕。<div id='poem_129308' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_129308' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/129308?labeling=true' target='_blank'>中伏日省中当直</a><span class='authorDate'>（1001年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_129308")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_129308_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_129308'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_129308'>火云烘赫临中伏，青锁深严直右曹。<div id='poem_sentence_0_129308_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_129308'>吏散阶庭时纵步，诗成几案<span class='inlineComment2'>（明刻本作珠玉）</span>独挥毫。<div id='poem_sentence_1_129308_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_129308'>相乌影转风微起，仙掌阴斜日渐高。<div id='poem_sentence_2_129308_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_129308'>何处赐冰和郢酒，谁人割炙动鸾刀。<div id='poem_sentence_3_129308_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_129308'>紫泥封诏防稽缓，寒水浮瓜散郁陶。<div id='poem_sentence_4_129308_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_129308'>丞相忧边稀出沐，延英三刻岂知劳。<div id='poem_sentence_5_129308_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_129308'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_129308_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1001&endYear=1001')">1001年</a>　秋，预玉津园祖送朱昂致仕宴会，赋诗，又和温仲舒送朱昂之作。作品：致仕朱侍郎归江陵。朱侍郎致仕南归上特锡宴于玉津园仍诏两制三馆并预其会以伸祖送辄赋诗美之。次韵奉和知府温尚书送致政朱侍郎十六韵。<div id='poem_129336' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_129336' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/129336?labeling=true' target='_blank'>致仕朱侍郎归江陵<span class='inlineComment2'>（侍郎自内署休致）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1001年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_129336")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_129336_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_129336'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_129336'>二年分直浴堂门，簪笔垂绅奉至尊。<div id='poem_sentence_0_129336_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_129336'>日过八砖批汉诏，宴开三殿挹尧樽。<div id='poem_sentence_1_129336_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_129336'>忽闻抗表干君父，切要悬车示子孙。<div id='poem_sentence_2_129336_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_129336'>碧落改官旌旧德，黄金加赐见深恩。<div id='poem_sentence_3_129336_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_129336'>群公祖道争飞盖，故吏沾襟亦恋轩。<div id='poem_sentence_4_129336_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_129336'>定是辽东叹城郭，肯同彭泽虑田园。<div id='poem_sentence_5_129336_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_129336'>捧觞莫诉前为寿，上马犹能左属鞬。<div id='poem_sentence_6_129336_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_129336'>临别延英对数刻，已应惇史记嘉言。<div id='poem_sentence_7_129336_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_129336'></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_129336_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_129322' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_129322' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/129322?labeling=true' target='_blank'>朱侍郎致仕南归上特锡宴于玉津园仍诏两制三馆并预其会以伸祖送辄赋诗美之</a><span class='authorDate'>（1001年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_129322")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_129322_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_129322'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_129322'>征轮轧轧出皇都，行路咨嗟贤丈夫。<div id='poem_sentence_0_129322_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_129322'>天子特令供祖帐，国门聊且驻骊驹。<div id='poem_sentence_1_129322_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_129322'>旧僚送别倾三省，御醴分甘倒百壶。<div id='poem_sentence_2_129322_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_129322'>下诏已闻推异礼，乞言犹自渴嘉谟<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_129322_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_129322'>冯公不是沉郎署，贺老缘何归鉴湖。<div id='poem_sentence_4_129322_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_129322'>明主恩深若为舍，梦魂应绕博山炉。<div id='poem_sentence_5_129322_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_129322'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_129322_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_129322'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_3_129322_0'>⑴ 自注：上特诏荆南官吏岁时存问，如有章奏附驿以闻。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_129322_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_129331' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_129331' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/129331?labeling=true' target='_blank'>次韵奉和知府温尚书送致政朱侍郎十六韵</a><span class='authorDate'>（1001年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_129331")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_129331_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_129331'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_129331'>拜章纳禄便归休，秘殿亲辞十二旒。<div id='poem_sentence_0_129331_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_129331'>阁笔罢批丹凤尾，拂衣初下六鳌头。<div id='poem_sentence_1_129331_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_129331'>非缘荆渚依刘表，定欲箕山访许由。<div id='poem_sentence_2_129331_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_129331'>北阙子牟终眷恋，南朝安石本风流。<div id='poem_sentence_3_129331_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_129331'>明庭顾遇违三接，别墅生涯治一邱。<div id='poem_sentence_4_129331_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_129331'>身健宁烦策鸠杖，心闲无复梦刀州。<div id='poem_sentence_5_129331_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_129331'>素风有子堪传遗，禅论将谁共对酬。<div id='poem_sentence_6_129331_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_129331'>白璧赐多应尚在，黄金散尽不须留。<div id='poem_sentence_7_129331_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_129331'>人钦雅誉芝兰馥，帝忆嘉言水石投。<div id='poem_sentence_8_129331_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_129331'>祖帐特令开上苑，归帆那肯待高秋<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_9_129331_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_129331'>几程邮驿经浓暑，千里山川见旧游。<div id='poem_sentence_10_129331_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_129331'>已是抛官玉堂署，尚思陪宴井干楼。<div id='poem_sentence_11_129331_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_129331'>时裁奏牍犹规谏，旋写丹经自校雠。<div id='poem_sentence_12_129331_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_129331'>乡里高门表阴德，国朝惇史纪嘉猷。<div id='poem_sentence_13_129331_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_129331'>枌榆旧业须重葺，香火前缘莫废修。<div id='poem_sentence_14_129331_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_129331'>岁计将何资伏腊，龙阳千树木奴洲。<div id='poem_sentence_15_129331_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_129331'></div><div id='poem_sentence_16_129331_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_129331'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_9_129331_0'>⑴ 自注：侍郎辞日，上令待秋凉即路，坚请便行。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_129331_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1001&endYear=1001')">1001年8月26日</a>　秋，子云堂疡生于颊，庸医误治，八月二十六日殇于京师。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1001&endYear=1001')">1001年</a>　以子云堂殇，悲甚，作《殇子述》，以佛理自遣。<div id='poem_1152716' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152716' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152716?labeling=true' target='_blank'>殇子述</a><span class='authorDate'>（1001年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152716")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152716_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152716'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152716'>予授室之明年，出领缙云郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152716_comment'></div>下车十月，而生一子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152716_comment'></div>既三月，执其左手，欬而名之曰云堂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152716_comment'></div>云堂生七月，予被召归阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152716_comment'></div>前一月，太夫人举族先归建安吴兴之别墅，比玺书至，予亦间道归拜坟墓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152716_comment'></div>云堂颇能识其父，迎门而笑，跃而就予抱焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152716_comment'></div>家居仅五旬，虑稽留诏书，遂单车即路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152716_comment'></div>凡再见朏魄，而至京师，气憀慄以变衰，岁峥嵘而将晚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1152716_comment'></div>明年春，迎版舆自三吴，汎九江，浮淮溯汴，就养于辇毂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1152716_comment'></div>而云堂始踸踔能行，旦暮嬉戏于太夫人之膝下，爰笑爰语，甚足慰祖母之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1152716_comment'></div>涉秋乃病，命医视之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1152716_comment'></div>先是，疡生于颊，善疗者必令外决，使毒气不留藏中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1152716_comment'></div>医，市井徒也，利其有瘳，亟饮以药，不数日而愈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1152716_comment'></div>未浃旬，病腹痛，便利，又呼医视之，医亟以药止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1152716_comment'></div>又数日，下血，复召医，但谩言将愈，利于受直。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1152716_comment'></div>讫五日，有加而无瘳，即召他医，医言疾深矣，殆不可为也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1152716_comment'></div>既而疳气上攻，口中龈腭皆创。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1152716_comment'></div>落两齿，手足掉举，目眩转而死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1152716_comment'></div>噫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1152716_comment'></div>生于己亥十月之己未，死于辛丑八月之乙丑，凡六百六十七日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1152716_comment'></div>其赋命也，何夭促之如是哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1152716_comment'></div>因念万物之内，最灵者人，父子之道，斯惟天性。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1152716_comment'></div>过犹不及，适情之所钟；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1152716_comment'></div>有而归无，亦理之可遣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1152716_comment'></div>然高堂夺抱孙之庆，衰门缠遗体之悲，盖衅积自躬，而祸延于嗣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1152716_comment'></div>夫子所谓「苗而不秀」者，是之谓乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1152716_comment'></div>若其月角对耸，山庭衍斥，眉目疏秀，方口大颐，必兴吾门，终能成器。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1152716_comment'></div>其在襁褓，挺然不群，初生才两月，方呱呱而泣，家人取书册展向之，即熟视其文字，喜且笑，若能识焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1152716_comment'></div>未尝遗屎溺于席褥上，虽夜寒，亦展转而起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1152716_comment'></div>家有奴产子者，亦数岁，颇无赖，虽群萃中，了不怖慑，东西跳梁，歌唫无度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1152716_comment'></div>每远见是子，必惶惧号泣，若无所容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1152716_comment'></div>家人潜抱令近之，必大呼殒绝，不知其所以然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1152716_comment'></div>初，疾愈，东室中北壁有画佛像，每过其门，必引身入焉，视其画而笑，若相对语者，乃喜甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1152716_comment'></div>傥家人拒之，必号哭偃踣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1152716_comment'></div>如是，日三四十往，以至于疾甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1152716_comment'></div>性不好弄，不嗜味，不妄言笑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1152716_comment'></div>太夫人常言：「吾阅孩孺多矣，未有此儿之卓异也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1152716_comment'></div>岂吾宗之薄祐，无复大其门闾耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1152716_comment'></div>而疾夫之不夭，将遂挤于沟壑耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1152716_comment'></div>因念尝读金仙子书，了知大雄氏之旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1152716_comment'></div>识六尘之妄相，见诸行之无常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1152716_comment'></div>聚沫非可撮摩，浮云倏然变灭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1152716_comment'></div>轮回起于爱，必断必除；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1152716_comment'></div>烦恼归于空，何执何著？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1152716_comment'></div>一切虚幻，万化纷纶，又安能触类增悲，缅怀舐犊之爱；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1152716_comment'></div>积毁成疾，自贻丧明之戚哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1152716_comment'></div>予出于儒门，沉迷俗谛，犹或慕圣人之达节，希上士之忘情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1152716_comment'></div>诚知其无可奈何，聊以自遣耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1152716_comment'></div>服名教者，得无罪我乎<span class='inlineComment2'>（《武夷新集》卷一一。）</span>？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1152716_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_49_1152716'>之：原无，据库本补。</div><div id='poem_sentence_49_1152716_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1001&endYear=1001')">1001年</a>　秋，与李宗谔、郑文宝等宴于石氏东斋，分韵赋诗。作品：诸公于石氏东斋宴郑工部分韵得愁秋浮并序。<div id='poem_129255' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_129255' class='poemTitle class='poemContent' id='poem_content_129255'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_129255'>楚客登临处，离怀重隐忧。<div id='poem_sentence_0_129255_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_129255'>二毛初入鬓，一叶早惊秋。<div id='poem_sentence_1_129255_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_129255'>旅雁他乡思，悲笳绝塞愁。<div id='poem_sentence_2_129255_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_129255'>凭何遣羁绪，菊蕊满杯浮。<div id='poem_sentence_3_129255_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_129255'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_129255_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1001&endYear=1001')">1001年8月15日</a>　慎从吉寄诗，和之。作品：次韵和慎大詹中秋待月寄西掖三舍人之什。<div id='poem_129109' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_129109' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a class='poemContent' id='poem_content_129109'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_129109'>凉飙送残暑，秋色望中新。<div id='poem_sentence_0_129109_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_129109_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_129109'>僚友东床客，冰清合许亲<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div
