ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1001&endYear=1001')">1001年8？</a>　八月后，有诗赠开封考城县知县孙仅。作品：孙寺丞知考城县。<div id='poem_129073' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_129073' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/129073?labeling=true' target='_blank'>孙寺丞知考城县<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup></a><span class='authorDate'>（1001年8？）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_129073")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_129073_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_129073_0'>① 府尹温尚书，即孙之座主，又荐举贤良方正</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_129073'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_129073'>早得东堂桂一枝，凌云词赋汉皇知。<div id='poem_sentence_0_129073_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_129073'>从军久在红莲幕，对策曾临白玉墀。<div id='poem_sentence_1_129073_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_129073'>霰雪陪游应不晚，弦歌为政莫嫌卑。<div id='poem_sentence_2_129073_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_129073'>春官宗伯大京兆，喜见门生趋府时。<div id='poem_sentence_3_129073_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_129073'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_129073_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1001&endYear=1001')">1001年</a>　冬，路振出知河中府，亿以诗赠之。作品：路学士知河中府。<div id='poem_129376' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_129376' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/129376?labeling=true' target='_blank'>路学士知河中府</a><span class='authorDate'>（1001年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_129376")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_129376_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_129376'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_129376'>一麾新自海滨还，又佩鱼符入故关。<div id='poem_sentence_0_129376_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_129376'>千里山河临剧郡，九天鸳鹭别通班。<div id='poem_sentence_1_129376_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_129376'>楼经往圣回清跸，路接边夷献白环。<div id='poem_sentence_2_129376_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_129376'>版籍素多田赋错，干戈初息羽书閒。<div id='poem_sentence_3_129376_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_129376'>从军上客彫龙藻，佐酒妖姬堕马鬟。<div id='poem_sentence_4_129376_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_129376'>更遣府公吟思发，中条新霁碧孱颜。<div id='poem_sentence_5_129376_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_129376'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_129376_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1001&endYear=1001')">1001年</a>　上书论职官，建议定官制，裁冗员，丰其禄，责以廉，慎封赏。作品：次对奏状。<div id='poem_1152530' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152530' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152530?labeling=true' target='_blank'>次对奏状</a><span class='authorDate'>（咸平四年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152530")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152530_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152530'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152530'>右，臣位列朝行，次当转对，辄倾鄙见，上渎宸聪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152530_comment'></div>退省狂愚，伏增恐慄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152530_comment'></div>臣窃以朝廷之所贵者，唯班爵是先；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152530_comment'></div>君人之所重者，唯名器为急。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152530_comment'></div>是以笾豆之事，各有司存；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152530_comment'></div>樽俎之间，不相踰越。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152530_comment'></div>思不出位，君子称其守官；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152530_comment'></div>必也正名，先王以之经国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1152530_comment'></div>恭惟国家克遵旧制，并建群司，公卿大夫，表著咸设，台省监寺，曹局毕陈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1152530_comment'></div>然而徒有其名，不举其职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1152530_comment'></div>只如尚书会府，上法文昌，治本是资，政典攸出，条目皆具，可举而行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1152530_comment'></div>今之存者，但吏部铨拟，秋曹详覆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1152530_comment'></div>自馀租庸筦榷，由别使以总领；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1152530_comment'></div>民籍伍符，非奉司而校定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1152530_comment'></div>职守虽在，或事有所分；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1152530_comment'></div>纲领虽存，或政非自出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1152530_comment'></div>丞辖之名空设而无违可纠，端揆之任虽重而无务可亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1152530_comment'></div>周之六官，于是废矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1152530_comment'></div>且如寺、监素有于掌执，台、阁咸著于规程，昭然轨仪，布在方策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1152530_comment'></div>昔者汉行故事，宣帝以之中兴；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1152530_comment'></div>鲁为长府，闵子讥其改作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1152530_comment'></div>臣以为国家虑命拟之未允，故置审官之司；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1152530_comment'></div>忧议谳之或滥，故设审刑之署；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1152530_comment'></div>恐命令之或失，故建封驳之局。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1152530_comment'></div>臣以为在于纪纲之不举，不在于琴瑟之更张。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1152530_comment'></div>若辩论官材归于相府，即审官之司可废矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1152530_comment'></div>详评刑辟属于司寇，即审刑之署可去矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1152530_comment'></div>出纳诏命关于给事中，即封驳之局可罢矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1152530_comment'></div>至于尚书二十四司各扬其职，寺、监、台、阁悉复其旧，按《六典》之制度，振百司之遗坠，在我而已，夫岂为难？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1152530_comment'></div>如此则朝廷益尊，堂陛益峻，典故益举，品流益清，端拱而天下治者，由兹道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1152530_comment'></div>臣又以唐虞之时，建官惟百，夏商官倍，秦汉益繁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1152530_comment'></div>施及有唐，典策咸在，自三公之极贵，九品之至微，著于令文，皆有员数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1152530_comment'></div>《传》云：「官不必备，唯其人」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1152530_comment'></div>盖阙之，斯可矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1152530_comment'></div>若乃员外加置，任非其才，故「灶下」、「羊头」，形于嘲诮，「斗量车载」，播厥风谣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1152530_comment'></div>国体所先，尤须慎重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1152530_comment'></div>臣窃睹班簿，员外郎及二百馀人，郎中亦及百数，自馀太常、国子博士、殿中丞、中舍、洗马，俱不下数百人，率预常参，皆著引籍，不知职业之所守，多由恩泽之序迁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1152530_comment'></div>臣窃以昔馆陶公主为子求郎，以为上应列宿，以至更直建礼，伏奏明光，含香握兰，雍容侍从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1152530_comment'></div>又尝读唐朝故事，益知省郎之贵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1152530_comment'></div>三院御史岁满愿迁者，多拗项以望省署，因而名桥或次补，纶闱或便除；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1152530_comment'></div>给谏出刺大郡，犹谓左迁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1152530_comment'></div>今乃百十为群，殆非为官择人之旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1152530_comment'></div>臣欲乞按唐制，应九品已上官并定员数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1152530_comment'></div>臣又念昔者秦之开郡置守，汉以天下为十三部，命刺史以领之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1152530_comment'></div>自后因郡为州，以太守为刺史，降及唐氏，亦尝变更，曾未数年，又仍旧贯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1152530_comment'></div>今国家多命省署之职出为知州，又设通判之官以为副贰，此权宜之制耳，岂可为经久之训哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1152530_comment'></div>臣欲乞诸州并置刺史，以户口多少制其俸禄，分下、中、上、紧、望、雄之等级，品秩之际率如旧章，与常参官比视阶资，出入更践，省去通判之目，但置从事之员，建廉察之使以统临，按舆地之图而区处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1152530_comment'></div>昔者兴国初，诏废支郡，出于一时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1152530_comment'></div>十国为连，周法斯在；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1152530_comment'></div>一道置使，唐制可寻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1152530_comment'></div>至若号令之行，风教之出，先及于府，府以及州，州以及县，县以及乡里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1152530_comment'></div>自上而下，由近及远，譬如身之使臂，臂之使指，提纲而众目张，振领而群毛理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1152530_comment'></div>由是言之，支郡之不可废也明矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1152530_comment'></div>臣欲乞复置支郡，隶于大府，量地里而分割，如漕运之统临，名分有伦，官业自举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1152530_comment'></div>臣又睹唐制内外官俸钱之外，有禄米、职田，又给防閤、庶仆、亲事、帐内、执衣、白直、门夫，各以官品差定其数，岁收其课以资于家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1152530_comment'></div>本司又有公廨田、食本钱，以给公用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1152530_comment'></div>自唐末离乱，国用不充，百官俸钱并减其半，自馀别给一切权停。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1152530_comment'></div>今群官于半俸之中已是除陌，又于半俸三分之内，其二分以他物给之，鬻于市廛，十才得其一二，曾糊口之不及，岂代耕之足云？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1152530_comment'></div>昔西汉张敞、萧望之上言，以为仓廪实而知礼节，衣食足而知荣辱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1152530_comment'></div>念吏俸不足者，常有忧父母妻子之心，虽欲为廉，其势不能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1152530_comment'></div>于是宣帝下诏云：「吏能勤事而俸禄薄，欲其无侵渔百姓难矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1152530_comment'></div>遂加吏俸，著于策书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1152530_comment'></div>臣窃见今之结发登朝，陈力就列，其俸也不能致九人之饱，不及周之上农；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1152530_comment'></div>其禄也未尝有百石之入，不及汉之小吏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1152530_comment'></div>若乃左、右仆射，百僚之师长，位莫崇焉，月俸所入，不及军中千夫之帅，甚可骇也，岂圣朝稽古之意哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1152530_comment'></div>臣欲乞今后百官俸禄杂给，并循旧制，既丰其稍入，可责以廉隅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1152530_comment'></div>官且限以常员，理当减于旧费，冗食悉罢，周行自清。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1152530_comment'></div>臣又念唐虞之制也，凡预品官，各设资考，课其殿最，归于有司，或历阶以升，或越次而补。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1152530_comment'></div>国朝多以郊祀覃恩，因而稍迁，考工之黜陟不行，士流之清浊无辨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1152530_comment'></div>陛下深鉴其弊，姑务惟新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1152530_comment'></div>昨有事于禋燔，但遍加于阶爵，虽矫前失，未振旧规。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1152530_comment'></div>臣欲乞依旧内外官各立考限，复令考功修举其职，每岁置使校考，以表尽公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1152530_comment'></div>资秩改迁，赏罚惩劝，一遵典故，以振滞淹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1152530_comment'></div>臣又念昔者成周之制也，公、侯、子、男皆列土以建国，大夫卿士并受田而无征。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1152530_comment'></div>西汉已来，用秦武功之爵，唯列侯启封，或踰万户，至关内侯，或有食邑，不过数百家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1152530_comment'></div>自是因循，以至唐室，但食邑者率为虚设，言实封者岁入有差。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1152530_comment'></div>殆及圣朝，并无所给，至于除拜之际，犹名数未移，空有食采之称，真同画饼之妄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1152530_comment'></div>臣欲乞依元和中所定实封条贯支给，削去虚邑，但行实食，以宠勋臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1152530_comment'></div>臣又念国家每属严禋，即覃大庆，叙封追赠，罔限彝章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1152530_comment'></div>乃至太医之微，司历之贱，率荷蓼萧之泽，亦疏石窌之封，恩虽出于殊常，事不循于经制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1152530_comment'></div>臣又以勋、散之设，名器实繁，律文以勋、散为二官，已经删定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1152530_comment'></div>故事，加散官至五品必以上闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1152530_comment'></div>今朝散、银青、犹阙命服；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1152530_comment'></div>护军、柱国，全是虚名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1152530_comment'></div>臣欲乞自今以后，常参官勋、散俱至五品者许封赠，官、阶、勋俱至三品者许立戟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1152530_comment'></div>每遇庆泽，令有司准式施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1152530_comment'></div>既礼秩之昭彰，固名品之分别。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1152530_comment'></div>臣又以五等之爵，施之于今，虽有启封之称，曾无胙土之实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1152530_comment'></div>苴茅建社，固不可以遽行；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1152530_comment'></div>翼子贻孙，亦足徵于旧典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1152530_comment'></div>臣欲乞内外官封至伯、子、男者，许荫子；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1152530_comment'></div>至公、侯者，许荫孙；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1152530_comment'></div>别封国公者，许嫡子、嫡孙一人袭封。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1152530_comment'></div>并令有司考求前制，所冀国朝无虚授之宠，臣下知延赏之恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1152530_comment'></div>臣又以今之加功臣之称，始于唐德宗幸奉天，扈跸将士，并加「奉天定难功臣」之号，因一时之赏典，为万世之通规。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1152530_comment'></div>近代已来，将相大臣有加至十馀字者，尤非经据，不可遵行，所宜削除，以明宪度者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1152530_comment'></div>昔讲求典礼，晋国以清；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1152530_comment'></div>考覈名实，汉朝称治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1152530_comment'></div>当至化诞敷之际，是旧章咸秩之时，跂见太平，正在今日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1152530_comment'></div>臣学术素浅，文理未明，辄述狂言，以塞明诏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1152530_comment'></div>陨越于下，启处不遑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1152530_comment'></div>干冒天聪，臣无任省循战汗、激切屏营之至。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_101_1152530'></div><div id='poem_sentence_101_1152530_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1001&endYear=1001')">1001年12月</a>　诏近臣议灵州弃守事，亿上疏言“直须弃灵州，保环庆，然后以计困之尔”。作品：议灵州事宜状。<div id='poem_1152523' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152523' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152523?labeling=true' target='_blank'>议灵州事宜状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1001年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152523")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152523_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152523'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152523'>右，臣今月十六日中使至、奉御劄子：「朕常览古书，备详边事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152523_comment'></div>得其人，则举无遗策；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152523_comment'></div>失其事，则谋之不臧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152523_comment'></div>朕三复斯文，终期在念。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152523_comment'></div>未尝不察言观行，舍短从长，希勠力于邦家，冀太康于宇县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152523_comment'></div>其如妖氛不息，边塞未宁，北狄虽具于堤防，西鄙尚多于艰阻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152523_comment'></div>灵武是中原巨屏，平夏乃近域小蕃，久兴蛇豕之心，常作疆埸之患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152523_comment'></div>阻绝道路，侵犯军城，狂妖转恣于无厌，大郡翻成于孤垒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1152523_comment'></div>纵之斯终成暴乱，讨之则虑困生灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1152523_comment'></div>两途宜在于咨询，百中须从于筹略。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1152523_comment'></div>卿职当纶綍，位列清华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1152523_comment'></div>披经史之遗文，大资智略；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1152523_comment'></div>观古今之盛事，必蕴机谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1152523_comment'></div>黠虏用何法以剪除？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1152523_comment'></div>灵州以何方而废置？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1152523_comment'></div>弃之则有何利害？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1152523_comment'></div>存之则有何便宜？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1152523_comment'></div>专听必当之谋，无吝酌中之论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1152523_comment'></div>分明擘画，密具奏闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1152523_comment'></div>用符果决之诚，以副荡涤之望」者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1152523_comment'></div>窃以询于刍荛，前王之盛德；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1152523_comment'></div>谋及卿士，载籍之格言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1152523_comment'></div>盖所以竭尽下情，详求中道，使举无失策，动必有成，斯圣皇慎重之至也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1152523_comment'></div>然而狂夫之言，圣人择焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1152523_comment'></div>谋之欲多，断之在独。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1152523_comment'></div>伏惟皇帝陛下清閒之宴，亲纡睿览，言之可用者，行之不疑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1152523_comment'></div>臣某幸甚幸甚！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1152523_comment'></div>臣尝读旧史，见汉武北筑朔方之郡，平津侯谏，以为罢敝中国，以奉无用之地，愿罢之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1152523_comment'></div>上使辩士朱买臣等发十策以难平津，平津不能对。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1152523_comment'></div>臣以为平津侯为汉贤相，深明经术，习知利害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1152523_comment'></div>属武帝以雄侈自任，志在开拓，买臣等以词辩获进，并侍左右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1152523_comment'></div>前史又称平津每朝会议论，但开陈其端，使人主自择，不肯面折廷诤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1152523_comment'></div>由此言之，非不能折买臣之舌，盖所以将顺人君之意耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1152523_comment'></div>即朔方之非便，有自来矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1152523_comment'></div>且其地非《禹贡》九州之内，非《周官》职方所领。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1152523_comment'></div>在要荒之外，固声教不及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1152523_comment'></div>元朔中，大将军卫青攘却匈奴，取其河南地以列置郡县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1152523_comment'></div>今灵州是赫连昌地，后魏置州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1152523_comment'></div>盖朔方之故墟，即匈奴之旧壤，僻介西鄙，悬绝诸华，数百里之间，无有水草，烽火不相应，亭障不相望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1152523_comment'></div>当边境谧宁，羌戎即叙，道路不壅，饟馈无虞，犹足以张大国之威声，为中原之捍蔽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1152523_comment'></div>自胡雏作梗，边邑屡惊，杂虏为其胁从，凶党因而昌炽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1152523_comment'></div>待之以爵赏，颇骄蹇而不恭；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1152523_comment'></div>讨之以甲兵，又遁逃而无获。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1152523_comment'></div>凡有赢粮之役，必兴狙击之谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1152523_comment'></div>每至灵武转输，大须发卒防援。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1152523_comment'></div>离去内地，皆无斗心，经涉畏途，皆有菜色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1152523_comment'></div>自曹光实、白守荣、马绍忠及王荣之败，资粮扉屦，所失最多，将士丁夫，相枕而死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1152523_comment'></div>以至募商人入谷输帛，偿以数倍之价，复于积石之孤壤，别筑清远之一城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1152523_comment'></div>边民绎骚，国帑匮乏，既不能制黠虏之死命，又不能救灵武之急难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1152523_comment'></div>数年之间，凶党逾盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1152523_comment'></div>灵武<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_50_1152523", 1152523, "Clauses/142/Comments/0")'>危堞</span>，岿然仅存；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1152523_comment'></div>河外五城，继闻陷没。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1152523_comment'></div>但坚壁清野，坐食糗粮；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1152523_comment'></div>闭垒枕戈，茍度朝夕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1152523_comment'></div>且使贼迁横行沙漠，俶扰疆陲，击列镇之戍兵，侵属国之蕃部。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1152523_comment'></div>虽有警急，无候望而得知；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1152523_comment'></div>纵或凭陵，但缮完而自保。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1152523_comment'></div>未尝出一兵、驰一骑，敢与虏捔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1152523_comment'></div>此灵武之存，无益明矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1152523_comment'></div>平津所言罢敝中国以奉无用之地，正谓今日也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1152523_comment'></div>臣以为存之有大害，弃之有大利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1152523_comment'></div>且如国家募人入粟，偿以十倍之直；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1152523_comment'></div>发卒转饷，涉兹不毛之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1152523_comment'></div>此古人所谓率三十钟而致一石，驱民于死地者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1152523_comment'></div>今或弃之，即可以岁省戍卒，分守内郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1152523_comment'></div>一卒之费，可给十夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1152523_comment'></div>国家无飞刍挽粟之劳，士卒免暴露流离之苦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1152523_comment'></div>必谓废之，即亏失土地，伤损威重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1152523_comment'></div>且如尧、舜、夏禹，圣之盛者也，地不过数千里，而明德格天，四门穆穆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1152523_comment'></div>武丁、成王，商、周之明主也，然地东不过江、黄，西不过氐、羌，南不过蛮荆，北不过太原，而颂声并作，号为至治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1152523_comment'></div>及秦、汉拓土，穷兵远略，虽疆理益广，而干戈日寻，府库之资财屡空，生灵之肝脑涂地，校功比德，岂可同年而语哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1152523_comment'></div>夫蝮蛇螫手，壮士断腕；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1152523_comment'></div>蚁壤不塞，将漏山河。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1152523_comment'></div>今灵武之存，为害甚于蝮蛇；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1152523_comment'></div>供馈之费，为蠹逾于蚁壤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1152523_comment'></div>无鸿毛之益，有泰山之损。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1152523_comment'></div>岂可忽远大之略，徇悠悠之谈！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1152523_comment'></div>昔西汉贾捐之尝建议弃朱崖，当时公卿，亦有异论，元帝能排众多之说，奋独见之明，下诏废之，人颂其德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1152523_comment'></div>元帝之意，宁欲自弃其地？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1152523_comment'></div>当其内属为郡，固已置吏而拊循；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1152523_comment'></div>及其称兵搆乱，岂可劳民而征戍？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1152523_comment'></div>故其诏书曰：「议者以弃朱崖，羞威不行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1152523_comment'></div>夫通于时变，即忧万民；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1152523_comment'></div>万民之饥饿，危孰大焉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1152523_comment'></div>且宗庙之祭，凶年不备，况乎避不嫌之辱哉」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1152523_comment'></div>臣以为正与今日灵武之事相类。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1152523_comment'></div>当羌夷宁谧，靡有寇孽，可以存而勿论；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1152523_comment'></div>及劳师费财，无益保障，固宜废而不举，何足以伤威重而贻羞辱哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1152523_comment'></div>必以失地为言，即燕蓟八州，河湟五郡，所失多矣，何必此为？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1152523_comment'></div>议者又以西北诸蕃，戎马是产，资其控制，以通贸易；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1152523_comment'></div>环、庆诸州，内附蕃落，藉其屏翰，以免惊骚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1152523_comment'></div>此又迂阔之甚！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1152523_comment'></div>且戎人为利所诱，故互市于边关；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1152523_comment'></div>蕃部之族自强，故能庇其种类。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1152523_comment'></div>必来寇其环、庆，固无隔于藩篱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1152523_comment'></div>百雉危城，千里悬隔，自救不暇，岂及于它？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1152523_comment'></div>议者又以其田沃饶，有汉陂之利，恐贼迁因而播种，益以富强。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1152523_comment'></div>况戎人但以攻剽为能，罔知耕稼之事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1152523_comment'></div>河陇之外，弃地甚多，延袤百城，提封万井，西汉屯田之所，疆畔犹存，傥事力耕，可以积谷，何必独耕灵武，乃能足食？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1152523_comment'></div>若灵武于贼有大利，即是必争之地，当朝夕攻取，岂至于今？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1152523_comment'></div>皆为孟浪之谈，殊非经久之计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1152523_comment'></div>况又岁有调发，动致敚攘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1152523_comment'></div>借寇兵而赍盗粮，竭民力而耗国用，为患之大，无出于斯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1152523_comment'></div>虽庸人竖子，亦知其可弃也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1152523_comment'></div>然自清远沦陷，斥候不通，孤城之人，如釜中之鱼跃，黠虏之势，若昆山之火炎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1152523_comment'></div>朝廷必欲弃之，虽牙璋徵兵，灵旗直指，约赍深入，执殳前驱，鼓行贼中，传于城下，然后合其将卒，迁其人民，隳城复隍，塞井夷灶，乃为弃也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1152523_comment'></div>臣伏料国家物力尚屈，未暇此行，虽曰弃之，亦空言耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1152523_comment'></div>今一城生齿，正在焚溺之中，咸必死以是忧，欲自脱而无路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1152523_comment'></div>若陛下慎选单介，间道而行，赍持诏书，宣布王命，令其尽焚卢舍，自拔而归，丁壮悉令持兵，老幼以之襁负。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1152523_comment'></div>古称归师不可遏，又曰置之死地而后生之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1152523_comment'></div>当此之时，人百其勇，临难思免，其锋莫当。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1152523_comment'></div>国家又须申命偏师，扬言出塞，军声既振，贼势自分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1152523_comment'></div>即灵州东迁之民，不虞邀击之患，虽有剽劫，易为枝梧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1152523_comment'></div>且国家所惜者士民，所急者财用，岂可以骁果之旅，委以饿虎之蹊，府藏之实，填于卢山之壑？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1152523_comment'></div>今若弃去灵武，退守环庆，卒免流于绝域，民思保其室家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1152523_comment'></div>供馈不出于郊圻，恩德自沦于骨髓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1152523_comment'></div>民力不竭，士气益扬，何敌不摧？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1152523_comment'></div>何戎不克？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1152523_comment'></div>恭惟陛下欲康宇县，虑困生灵，求必当之谋，思酌中之论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1152523_comment'></div>臣以灵州之废置，计无出于此，望陛下采之而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1152523_comment'></div>陛下又愤兹黠虏，思欲剪除。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1152523_comment'></div>臣以为不可黩武以穷兵，止可伐谋而制胜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1152523_comment'></div>臣窃料贼迁睢盱边塞之外，倔强沙漠之中，胁制诸羌，啸聚不逞，无耕农之业，无蚕织之工。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1152523_comment'></div>为鼠窃之谋，以资衣食；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1152523_comment'></div>聚乌合之众，以扰塞垣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1152523_comment'></div>致蕃夷之服从，用凶威而驱迫，非有厚利，能诱其人？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1152523_comment'></div>朝廷今废弃灵州，每岁更无馈运，绝其觊望，何所窥图？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1152523_comment'></div>此困贼迁之一也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1152523_comment'></div>平夏之西，池盐斯在，先是贸易粟麦，用资糇粮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1152523_comment'></div>今条禁甚严，法网尤密，无敢踰越，渐致携离，此困贼迁之二也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1152523_comment'></div>严敕疆吏，谨奉国经，辨其非常，禁其阑出，使竹头木屑不遂其求，狗盗鸡鸣无施其巧，游魂空碛，坐抵困穷，此困贼迁之三也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1152523_comment'></div>然须精选锐师，分守边地，慎择名将，授之庙谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1152523_comment'></div>训练骁雄，提防侵轶，险其走集，明其侦候。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1152523_comment'></div>茍鸱张而豕突，必烽举以燧燔，并力剪除，分路驱逐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1152523_comment'></div>如秦人之鹿，犄角以攻；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1152523_comment'></div>譬常山之蛇，首尾相应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1152523_comment'></div>蕞尔凶丑，坐致灭亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1152523_comment'></div>臣窃见太祖朝命姚内斌领庆州，董遵诲领环州，二人所统之兵，才五六千而已，阃外之事，一以付之，军市之租，不从中覆，用能士卒效命，羌夷畏威，朝廷无旰食之忧，疆埸无羽书之警。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1152523_comment'></div>臣欲望陛下于武臣中选有将帅之才、知边鄙之事者三数人，分布诸郡，各量其所将兵多少付之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1152523_comment'></div>除廪禄之外，赐与一大县租赋，恣其犒设；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1152523_comment'></div>令开幕府，辟召髦俊，为之僚佐，咨以策略。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1152523_comment'></div>勇智之士，禀其指踪之用；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1152523_comment'></div>军旅之政，许以便宜而行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1152523_comment'></div>傥贼<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_143_1152523", 1152523, "Clauses/456/Comments/0")'>迁侵</span>边郡军戍，扰内属蕃部，并唇齿相援，腹背夹攻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1152523_comment'></div>或战马正肥，戎士思奋，即徵发内属讨虏之羌，俘获之馀，尽分麾下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1152523_comment'></div>且戎人利于降附，盖迫凶渠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1152523_comment'></div>傥挠之以劲兵，示之以大信，怀荒振远，推亡固存，出金帛以购酋豪，悬爵秩以宠降附，明立赏格，厚答战功，即贼迁之腹心，稍稍奔溃，亲离众叛，事去运乖，茕茕独行，谁与为伍？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1152523_comment'></div>但塞外一胡人耳，安能与大邦为雠哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_147_1152523_comment'></div>陛下若欲成谋庙堂，功在漏刻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_148_1152523_comment'></div>臣以为此虏方黠，其财犹丰，腥膻之群，如臂使指，未可以岁月破也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_149_1152523_comment'></div>直须废弃灵州，退保环、庆，然后以计困之耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_150_1152523_comment'></div>如臣之策，祗得三两骁将，付以一二万精卒，以数县租赋给其用度，令分守边郡，贼迁可以计日成擒，朝廷可以高枕无事矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_151_1152523_comment'></div>臣从事儒学，岂知军旅，耳剽日久，心知其然，辄罄謏闻，仰祇清问。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_152_1152523_comment'></div>谈不稽古，词非据经。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_153_1152523_comment'></div>进思尽忠，盖事君之无隐；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_154_1152523_comment'></div>谋或可用，岂以人而废言！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_155_1152523_comment'></div>干冒宸严，臣无任云云。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_156_1152523'></div><div id='poem_sentence_156_1152523_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1001&endYear=1001')">1001年</a>　冬夕，与同僚宴梅询西斋，分题探韵赋诗，亿得“今夕何夕”题，云字韵。有序。作品：冬夕与诸公宴集贤梅学士西斋分得今夕何夕探得云字并序。<div id='poem_129314' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_129314' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/129314?labeling=true' target='_blank'>冬夕与诸公宴集贤梅学士西斋分得今夕何夕探得云字</a><span class='authorDate'>（1001年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_129314")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_129314_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_129314'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_129314'>今夕知何夕，良交会以文。<div id='poem_sentence_0_129314_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_129314'>烛花寒旋落，漏滴远稀闻。<div id='poem_sentence_1_129314_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_129314'>酒面轻浮蚁，歌喉细遏云。<div id='poem_sentence_2_129314_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_129314'>明河光未没，候管气初分。<div id='poem_sentence_3_129314_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_129314'>玉笛梅花怨，金炉蕙草焚。<div id='poem_sentence_4_129314_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_129314'>唯愁曙光发，搔首叹离群。<div id='poem_sentence_5_129314_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_129314'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_129314_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1001&endYear=1001')">1001年闰12月</a>　章频得解后往游陕府，亿以诗赠之。作品：章频得解后之陕府谒严洪二从事。<div id='poem_129371' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_129371' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/129371?labeling=true' target='_blank'>章频得解后之陜府谒严洪二从事<span class='inlineComment2'>（是年闰十二月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1001年闰12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_129371")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_129371_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_129371'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_129371'>春闱犹隔闰，逆旅苦栖遑。<div id='poem_sentence_0_129371_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_129371'>忽尔游分陜，飘然出大梁。<div id='poem_sentence_1_129371_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_129371'>食贫忧桂玉，策蹇冒风霜。<div id='poem_sentence_2_129371_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_129371'>杏苑归期近，棠郊去路长。<div id='poem_sentence_3_129371_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_129371'>幕中逢旧友，岁晚在他乡。<div id='poem_sentence_4_129371_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_129371'>鸡黍且相对，休嗟鬓发苍。<div id='poem_sentence_5_129371_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_129371'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_129371_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1001&endYear=1001')">1001年</a>　有诗送栾崇吉出知洪州。作品：司农栾少卿知洪州。<div id='poem_129055' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_129055' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/129055?labeling=true' target='_blank'>司农栾少卿知洪州</a><span class='authorDate'>（1001年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_129055")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_129055_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_129055'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_129055'>大农搜粟汉名卿，千里江西拥旆旌。<div id='poem_sentence_0_129055_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_129055'>腰下金龟三品绶，手中铜虎八州兵<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：江西旧管八州。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_129055_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_129055'>属鞬牧伯趋庭见，骑竹儿童塞路迎<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：前任江南转运使。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_2_129055_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_129055'>洪井主人今重士，肯教悬榻有尘生。<div id='poem_sentence_3_129055_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_129055'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_129055_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1001&endYear=1001')">1001年</a>　南康军建昌县洪氏，以孝义传家，至文抚、文举兄弟，就所居雷湖创建书院。今年，文举持兄书谒亿，请为文记其事，亿因作《洪氏雷塘书院记》作品：南康军建昌县义居洪氏雷塘书院记。<div id='poem_1152674' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152674' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152674?labeling=true' target='_blank'>南康军建昌县义居洪氏雷塘书院记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1001年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152674")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152674_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152674'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152674'>三代以还，乡党皆有庠塾；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152674_comment'></div>两汉而下，公卿多自教授。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152674_comment'></div>及五胡猾夏，一马渡江，扬粤之区，衣冠举集，士风文物，雄视中原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152674_comment'></div>盖剑客奇材，昔称荆楚之士；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152674_comment'></div>宽柔以教，今见南方之强。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152674_comment'></div>用是出相不下于山东，明经仅多于邹鲁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152674_comment'></div>街谈俚语，必及《诗》、《书》；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152674_comment'></div>总角弁髦，即游学校。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1152674_comment'></div>由学而礼让著，由让而孝义敦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1152674_comment'></div>斑白相推于道涂，耆艾靡游于市井。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1152674_comment'></div>耕者异畔，贾不求丰，亦犹夫洙泗之滨，龂龂如也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1152674_comment'></div>南康洪氏，杰出其间，以耕凿之勤，厚致资产；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1152674_comment'></div>以孝悌之德，大庇族人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1152674_comment'></div>奕世聚居，期功踰于百口；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1152674_comment'></div>至行内激，风声树于一方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1152674_comment'></div>州闾之内，人无间言；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1152674_comment'></div>闺门之中，衣无常主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1152674_comment'></div>渐渍玄泽，陶甄至和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1152674_comment'></div>彬彬然有万石孝谨之风，熙熙然跻华胥仁寿之域。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1152674_comment'></div>且于所居之侧，崇饰学舍，一日必葺，宾至如归，厨廪益丰，弦诵不辍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1152674_comment'></div>褒衣博带，岂减阙里之徒；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1152674_comment'></div>竹简韦编，将敌秘书之副。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1152674_comment'></div>子弟之秀者，咸肄业于兹，田苏与游，曾晰同志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1152674_comment'></div>列第侔于稷下，鼓箧比于虞庠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1152674_comment'></div>韦贤之一经相传，刘氏之七叶俱盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1152674_comment'></div>岂只游谈之矜式，羁旅之畴依，设驿马于四郊，来远客于千里而已！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1152674_comment'></div>至道中，天子遣美俗使者按行郡国，且以御书百轴下赐其家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1152674_comment'></div>家老文抚以隐居求志，肥遁不仕，即遣其弟文举入谢天阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1152674_comment'></div>特赐清閒之宴，召对赤墀之下，劳问数四，叹息久之，解褐授官，以示光宠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1152674_comment'></div>天子又自署一幅曰「义居人」以赐之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1152674_comment'></div>阅闳增气，闾巷改观，虽古之里称通德，族号高阳，家有赐书，门标六阙者，曾未足拟也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1152674_comment'></div>矧处士君耕于岩穴，名动京师，身在江湖，心悬象魏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1152674_comment'></div>每岁遣其子弟，陈土贡于宰旅，上必蕃锡以答其意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1152674_comment'></div>野芹之意，盖以荐诚；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1152674_comment'></div>园葵之心，特蒙委照。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1152674_comment'></div>自渥恩下及，精庐弥肃，宝玉在笥，芝兰盈庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1152674_comment'></div>去年，处士之兄子待用举进士，得乙科，同时侪流登是选者以十数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1152674_comment'></div>初覆一篑，盖由椎轮，后来之人，贯鱼而进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1152674_comment'></div>以锡羡流光之庆，加讨论博习之资。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1152674_comment'></div>圭组相辉，将珥貂于七叶；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1152674_comment'></div>生徒益盛，必著录者万人，然后臻夫极也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1152674_comment'></div>学馆之南有雷塘焉，因以为名，且志其地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1152674_comment'></div>先是，寻阳陈氏有东佳学堂，豫章胡氏有华林书院，皆聚坟索，以延俊髦，咸有名流为之纪述。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1152674_comment'></div>讲道论义，况力敌以势均；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1152674_comment'></div>好事乐贤，复争驰而并骛，宜乎与二家者鼎峙于江东矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1152674_comment'></div>今年助教来，赍处士书谒予，愿志其事，且嘉其服道淳固，树善深笃，谨守家法，勤接士类。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1152674_comment'></div>高门积德，已容驷马之车；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1152674_comment'></div>上帝藏书，更同群玉之府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1152674_comment'></div>景慕不足，牢让非宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1152674_comment'></div>僶俛成文，聊以塞请而已。</div><div id='poem_sentence_49_1152674_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1001&endYear=1001')">1001年</a>　李寅自豫章以书请为其所居涵虚阁作记，因有作。作品：致政李殿丞豫章东湖所居涵虚阁记。<div id='poem_1152675' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152675' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152675?labeling=true' target='_blank'>致政李殿丞豫章东湖所居涵虚阁记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1001年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152675")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152675_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152675'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152675'>涵虚阁者，致政李公考槃之所也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152675_comment'></div>李公挺生民之秀，负王佐之才，决科广庭，文雅第一，从政剧邑，吏人不欺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152675_comment'></div>以太夫人在喜惧之年，有羸老之疾，拜书北阙，求养南陔，天子嘉之，恩礼尤异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152675_comment'></div>既兰台之进秩，仍水衡而分俸，用致官政，归侍庭闱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152675_comment'></div>始卜居历阳，载离寒暑，会公之令子、今西台御史以尚书郎通守洪井，叔孙必葺，岂复怀安？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152675_comment'></div>元方将车，因以东上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152675_comment'></div>今年御史秩满归阙，公且致书于予，曰：「𡨝东西南北之人也，前年来江西，登临山水，览观风物，恋恋而不能去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152675_comment'></div>且欲占数为是邦之民，买田一廛，筑室百堵，编名户版，输税公上，陶陶然与汉阴丈人携手于羲皇之世矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1152675_comment'></div>兹郡之胜，实惟东湖；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1152675_comment'></div>今之所居，介于湖上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1152675_comment'></div>却视阛阓，前瞻渺㳽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1152675_comment'></div>栋宇轇轕，而世喧自分；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1152675_comment'></div>鱼鸟聱耴，而物态咸见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1152675_comment'></div>澄波万顷，韬映云天；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1152675_comment'></div>崇期八达，络绎冠盖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1152675_comment'></div>此亦古人大隐之迹，不出朝市；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1152675_comment'></div>儒者一亩之宫，仅庇风雨者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1152675_comment'></div>且念嘉宾至止，必宴豆以伸欢；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1152675_comment'></div>诸生来思，乃函丈而请益。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1152675_comment'></div>捧觞拜庆，既以奉北堂之欢心；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1152675_comment'></div>岸帻燕居，亦欲倚南窗而寄傲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1152675_comment'></div>裁择爽垲，累土增崇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1152675_comment'></div>俯瞰漪涟，面势素定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1152675_comment'></div>市山木以朴斲，命梓工而经营。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1152675_comment'></div>作为堂皇，成之不日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1152675_comment'></div>形胜尽萃，轩檐若飞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1152675_comment'></div>春之晨，杂芳被堤，绿波如染，可以临清流而赋诗；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1152675_comment'></div>夏之昼，凉飔拂衽，炎云成峰，可以登高明而逃暑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1152675_comment'></div>潦收水清，群木摇落，可以咏秋气于楚词。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1152675_comment'></div>岁暮天寒，密雪飞舞，可以歌南山于周《雅》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1152675_comment'></div>固足以槛心猿而习静，狎海鸥以忘机。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1152675_comment'></div>宴坐观空，入毗耶之不二；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1152675_comment'></div>谷神反听，味玄元之五千。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1152675_comment'></div>岂徒晨昏调膳之馀，雍容肆体而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1152675_comment'></div>东台舍人董公，昔典是邦，或退食之馀，必命驾以至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1152675_comment'></div>留连觞酌，从容笑语，凭轩旷望，目送飞鸿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1152675_comment'></div>秉烛徘徊，门留驷马，赏心不足，好乐无荒，实由斯阁之成，能回长者之辙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1152675_comment'></div>若夫天宇岑寂，湖光皎鉴，俯见云鸟，毫末靡遁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1152675_comment'></div>其形旁连邑居，嚣哗不接于耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1152675_comment'></div>游氛宿雾，寥廓洞开。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1152675_comment'></div>远水长空，混茫为一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1152675_comment'></div>髣髴其梗槩，目之曰「涵虚」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1152675_comment'></div>优哉游哉，聊以卒岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1152675_comment'></div>愿志其事，式为美谈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1152675_comment'></div>予与公有同郡之情，有忘年之契，亲比耆德，钦闻绪言，是用景行高山，讲求方策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1152675_comment'></div>若虚白之室，庄周得之逍遥；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1152675_comment'></div>通德之门，司农推之鸿博。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1152675_comment'></div>集《文选》于南荆者，层楼尚在；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1152675_comment'></div>草《太玄》于西蜀者，高台未倾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1152675_comment'></div>吴兴有韵海之堂，秣陵有乌衣之舍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1152675_comment'></div>载之图牒，芬若椒兰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1152675_comment'></div>今李公地望门风，仙姿道骨，清白义方之训子，文儒经术之传家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1152675_comment'></div>疏广之挥金，老莱之曳䌽，蕴是全德，无忝先民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1152675_comment'></div>而在家必闻，作事可法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1152675_comment'></div>岿然兹宇，揭于通都，声实飞腾，游居企慕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1152675_comment'></div>缔构得地，风烈在人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1152675_comment'></div>予固知夫异日与滕阁、孺亭鼎峙于钟陵，为不朽矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1152675_comment'></div>承命之辱，叙事靡周，聊述所闻，以抵来请云耳。</div><div id='poem_sentence_57_1152675_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1002&endYear=1002')">1002年1月</a>　有诗送郑文宝赴陕西随军转运。作品：郑工部陕西随军转运。<div id='poem_129414' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_129414' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/129414?labeling=true' target='_blank'>郑工部陜西随军转运</a><span class='authorDate'>（1002年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_129414")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_129414_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_129414'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_129414'>西鄙欃枪未扫除，营中慷慨请行初。<div id='poem_sentence_0_129414_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_129414'>三军粒食资心计，一月星邮待捷书。<div id='poem_sentence_1_129414_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_129414'>宣室喜闻延贾谊，茂陵久叹滞相如。<div id='poem_sentence_2_129414_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_129414'>谤言盈箧亲曾见，反间千金计岂疏。<div id='poem_sentence_3_129414_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_129414'>遗爱道傍喧竹马，先声塞外慑穹庐。<div id='poem_sentence_4_129414_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_129414'>冯唐莫叹淹郎署，博望还忻拥使车。<div id='poem_sentence_5_129414_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_129414'>陇右行收万里地，关中坐致九年储。<div id='poem_sentence_6_129414_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_129414'>牙筹羽檄皆吾事，才刃飘飘两有馀。<div id='poem_sentence_7_129414_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_129414'></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_129414_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1002&endYear=1002')">1002年3月</a>　侍帝后苑赏花，应制赋诗。作品：后苑赏花应制（云罗霞绮媚芳辰）<div id='poem_129068' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_129068' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/129068?labeling=true' target='_blank'>后苑赏花应制<span class='inlineComment2'>（以春字为韵咸平五年三月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1002年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_129068")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_129068_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_129068'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_129068'>云罗霞绮媚芳辰，琼圃花开烂漫春。<div id='poem_sentence_0_129068_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_129068'>风递清香随凤辇，波涵倒影落龙津。<div id='poem_sentence_1_129068_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_129068'>仙葩四照烘初日，浓艳千苞赐近臣。<div id='poem_sentence_2_129068_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_129068'>向晚天街戴归处，游蜂舞蝶自随人。<div id='poem_sentence_3_129068_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_129068'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_129068_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1002&endYear=1002')">1002年</a>　闻灵州陷，代宰相李沆等撰上表待罪。诏慰谕之，又代撰谢表。作品：代中书为灵州陷没待罪表。代中书谢表。<div id='poem_1152465' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152465' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152465?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代中书为灵州陷没待罪表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1002年3月12日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152465")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152465_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152465'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152465'>臣某等言：伏自狂胡作梗，西鄙绎骚，清远一城，去秋陷失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152465_comment'></div>近者又睹奏报，窃知灵州不守，将吏沦胥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152465_comment'></div>百雉金汤，曾无固护；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152465_comment'></div>连甍士庶，俱没腥膻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152465_comment'></div>盖廊庙之乏谋，致凶渠之肆毒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152465_comment'></div>动伤嗟于当宁，贻愧耻于具臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152465_comment'></div>臣某等<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>窃以镇抚四夷，决胜千里，运奇兵于掌上，视黠虏于目中，使顽犷咸怀，疆陲不耸，将帅禀指踪之效，君亲无旰食之忧：此宰辅之任也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152465_comment'></div>若冕旒不减于焦劳，蜂虿尚闻于俶扰，使苍生赤子，陷于匪人，亦尸禄素飧，安用彼相？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1152465_comment'></div>实群言之可畏，谅窃位以何颜！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1152465_comment'></div>伏念臣等皆是常才，谬当重任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1152465_comment'></div>虽揣摩铅钝，策励疲驽，智类挈瓶，终莫图于远大，职司补衮，但常惧于阙遗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1152465_comment'></div>自党项弗宁，灵武孤绝，皇帝陛下临朝日昃，求衣未明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1152465_comment'></div>愤蛇豕之微妖，惜膏腴之旧壤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1152465_comment'></div>虑朔方之生齿，委于饿虎之蹊；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1152465_comment'></div>亟比落以兴师，歼厥渠魁之首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1152465_comment'></div>而帷幄曾无于成算，塞垣几至于舆尸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1152465_comment'></div>去岁救兵逗留，丑类猖炽，积石坚垒，俄陷贼锋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1152465_comment'></div>今春已来，又失灵武。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1152465_comment'></div>北门巨屏，遂至于丘墟；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1152465_comment'></div>比屋生民，俱沦于涂炭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1152465_comment'></div>盖臣等每求咨度，曾乏谋猷，上负倚毗，内怀腼厚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1152465_comment'></div>况安危注意，实在台衡；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1152465_comment'></div>夙夜忧边，诚为职业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1152465_comment'></div>既弥纶之无状，乃咎责之攸归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1152465_comment'></div>茍畏避于简书，且因循于官次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1152465_comment'></div>退思补过，虽慕林父之事君；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1152465_comment'></div>用非其人，亦虑匈奴之轻汉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1152465_comment'></div>须倾丹欸，仰黩宸严。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1152465_comment'></div>伏望陛下责以官箴，俾从吏议，特行黜免，用洽至公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1152465_comment'></div>别选英髦，使代其任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1152465_comment'></div>庶贤能之递进，示宪法之无私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1152465_comment'></div>进退攸宜，既俯全于国体；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1152465_comment'></div>和平可召，固上洽于天心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1152465_comment'></div>仰俟刑书，臣等无任云云。</div><div id='poem_sentence_33_1152465_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1152466' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152466' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152466?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代中书谢表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1002年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152466")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152466_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152466'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152466'>臣等言：近以狂寇陆梁，朔方覆没，盖廊庙素无于成算，致士民俱陷于匪人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152466_comment'></div>至尊深动于悯伤，执政实甘于罪戾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152466_comment'></div>共陈奏牍，方俟刑书，承诏旨以丁宁，仰天威而陨越。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152466_comment'></div>臣某等<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>窃以疆埸之事，爰守在于四夷；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152466_comment'></div>帷幄之筹，固折冲于千里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152466_comment'></div>况处弼谐之任，必资经济之能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152466_comment'></div>料敌伐谋，动询于方略；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152466_comment'></div>忧边思职，克举于官常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1152466_comment'></div>然后塞四海之具瞻，副一人之虚伫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1152466_comment'></div>如臣等皆惟庸昧，莫荷倚毗，徒旷废于天工，岂弥纶于王度？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1152466_comment'></div>自胡雏作梗，灵武阽危，皇帝陛下愤蜂虿之微妖，惜金汤之坚垒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1152466_comment'></div>轸尧心于黄屋，遣汉将于文昌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1152466_comment'></div>大兴虓虎之师，将平狡兔之穴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1152466_comment'></div>庶肃清于氛祲，用申画于封圻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1152466_comment'></div>而灵旗未出于塞垣，巨屏已沦于寇孽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1152466_comment'></div>实臣等早无规画，仰负咨询。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1152466_comment'></div>徵龟玉毁椟之由，抱舟楫济川之愧，既晏安而非据，期策免之是行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1152466_comment'></div>岂谓陛下特降泥书，曲形天旨，尚令备位，未责旷官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1152466_comment'></div>履薄自思，但弥增于怵惕；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1152466_comment'></div>叩阍沥恳，固不敢以再三。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1152466_comment'></div>唯坚尽瘁之心，少赎已然之咎<span class='inlineComment2'>（云云）</span>。</div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1152466_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1002&endYear=1002')">1002年</a>　春，有诗怀寄李源。作品：闻李四光丞频游北园因有怀寄。<div id='poem_129244' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_129244' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/129244?labeling=true' target='_blank'>闻李四光丞频游北园因有怀寄</a><span class='authorDate'>（1002年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_129244")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_129244_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_129244'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_129244'>汉相沙堤连甲第，石家金谷有名园。<div id='poem_sentence_0_129244_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_129244'>雍容陌上临邛骑，潋滟斋中北海樽。<div id='poem_sentence_1_129244_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_129244'>过闰已惊春色早，离城殊少俗尘喧。<div id='poem_sentence_2_129244_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_129244'>无由一寄南窗傲，相望迢迢西掖垣。<div id='poem_sentence_3_129244_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_129244'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_129244_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1002&endYear=1002')">1002年3？</a>　参政王旦久任事，招谤议，先后代王旦撰陈情表和谢表。作品：代参政王谏议陈情表。代参政王侍郎谢为乞陈不允表。<div id='poem_1152464' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152464' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152464?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代参政王谏议陈情表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1002年3？）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152464")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152464_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152464'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152464'>臣某言：臣闻昔者成王疑于姬旦，徂东山者三年，文侯信于乐羊，示谤书之一箧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152464_comment'></div>盖贝锦萋斐者，人臣之共畏；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152464_comment'></div>圭璋特达者，圣哲之攸难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152464_comment'></div>苟非明目达聪，表微索隐，独观于昭旷之道，靡牵于众多之辞，使浸润之说不行，谗慝之口无状。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152464_comment'></div>不然者，三月采葛，徒积隐忧；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152464_comment'></div>十人拔杨，岂遑安处？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152464_comment'></div>徒揣循而自庆，实引喻以为烦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152464_comment'></div>臣某<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>伏念臣出自单平，本非茂异，由丘园而奋迹，偶轩陛以策名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1152464_comment'></div>叨佐幕于近畿，但饮冰而从政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1152464_comment'></div>寻效官于秘府，复结绶以登朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1152464_comment'></div>方司关市之征，遽辱已知之荐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1152464_comment'></div>皇帝陛下误垂采听，远赐徵还，俾釐务于钱刀，直推恩于章服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1152464_comment'></div>僶俛从事，唯尽瘁于公家；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1152464_comment'></div>颠沛不违，誓服勤于官次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1152464_comment'></div>曾未周于岁律，俄擢掌于王言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1152464_comment'></div>已惊物议之喧腾，曲荷天慈之全度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1152464_comment'></div>金紫更光于凡质，丝纶莫润于皇猷，才踰期月之间，忽辱深严之召。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1152464_comment'></div>玉堂待诏，极儒者之光华；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1152464_comment'></div>丹笔详刑，体仁君之钦恤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1152464_comment'></div>振拔之恩尤异，倾输之节弥殚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1152464_comment'></div>裁五色之书，虽发挥之无取；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1152464_comment'></div>评三尺之法，固伏念以惟寅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1152464_comment'></div>旋使巴庸之邦，肃将宽大之诏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1152464_comment'></div>抚两川凋瘵之俗，宣九重煦妪之恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1152464_comment'></div>导德泽于黔黎，察能否于官吏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1152464_comment'></div>适为注意之任，敢辞奔命之勤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1152464_comment'></div>才伏奏于青蒲，便超升于黄阁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1152464_comment'></div>位殊次补，官匪序迁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1152464_comment'></div>昔荀爽十旬，诚非骤进；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1152464_comment'></div>虞卿三见，徒是传闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1152464_comment'></div>如臣，无二子之器能，有一时之际会，曾未数年之内，遽参四辅之班。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1152464_comment'></div>已觉满盈，果招谤议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1152464_comment'></div>一昨讼端斯起，词语旁连，固亦内省于心，反求诸己。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1152464_comment'></div>检生平之履行，念身世之遭逢，未尝有出位之思，安敢造欺天之罪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1152464_comment'></div>坦无忧惧，仰俟辩明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1152464_comment'></div>岂期执宪之司，反恣舞文之弊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1152464_comment'></div>棰楚之下，鍜鍊而成，搆似是之巧词，结沉埋之冤气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1152464_comment'></div>上黩凝旒之听，欲希投杼之疑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1152464_comment'></div>而陛下深虑矫诬，别令讯鞠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1152464_comment'></div>既从阅实，果致平反。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1152464_comment'></div>使覆盆之幽，获被大明之照；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1152464_comment'></div>肺石之侧，免为无告之人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1152464_comment'></div>茍非陛下烛物无私，法天不宰，虑五刑之或滥，恐一物之非辜，即众口铄金，复谁分于枉直？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1152464_comment'></div>匹夫怀璧，谅何免于悔尤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1152464_comment'></div>见圣代之至公，顾群生而何幸！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1152464_comment'></div>臣自念秉孤直之操，荷非常之知，徒励夙夜匪懈之诚，固乏左右为容之助。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1152464_comment'></div>绝无党援，素少交亲，特出宸衷，擢参相府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1152464_comment'></div>常怀激励，仰戴恩私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1152464_comment'></div>况处最灵，岂有同于土木？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1152464_comment'></div>不能致远，亦愿竭于驽骀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1152464_comment'></div>其如旅翮甚危，寒根易动，孑孑孤立，茕茕独行，虽恃明主之恩，不顾党人之议，然而祸机莫测，谗舌难防。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1152464_comment'></div>傥媒孽之复生，恐别白而无路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1152464_comment'></div>即陛下伤知臣之睿鉴，微臣昧量力之格言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1152464_comment'></div>进退之间，傥获于由礼；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1152464_comment'></div>保全之惠，庶遂于克终。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1152464_comment'></div>既无损日月之明，亦曲成蝼蚁之志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1152464_comment'></div>伏望陛下俯矜愚恳，稍霈深仁，俾罢去于台司，获退归于散地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1152464_comment'></div>青蝇止棘，庶免于中伤；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1152464_comment'></div>金鼎和羹，幸无于倾覆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1152464_comment'></div>曲全大体，以庇下臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1152464_comment'></div>慺慺之诚，实在于此。</div><div id='poem_sentence_60_1152464_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1152467' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152467' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152467?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代参政王侍郎谢为陈乞不允表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1002年3？）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152467")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152467_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152467'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152467'>臣某言：臣近者虔拜封章，乞归班列，忽奉手诏，不赐允俞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152467_comment'></div>仰睿旨之丁宁，抚微躬而战慄，欲更披于肝膈，虑有黩于君亲<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152467_comment'></div>伏念臣孤直寡徒，顽疏无取。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152467_comment'></div>章句之学，仅能齿于诸生；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152467_comment'></div>清白之规，固克传于奕世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152467_comment'></div>自策名筮仕，陈力当官，尘右掖之清华，践内庭之严秘，乃至典枢机之务，参弼辅之司，并由旒冕之误知，岂副搢绅之公议？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152467_comment'></div>小器固难于大受，高位唯恐于疾颠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152467_comment'></div>夙夜在公，虽僶俛而从事；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1152467_comment'></div>负乘致寇，亦跼蹐之靡遑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1152467_comment'></div>今者讼起下民，辞连执政，宪府职当于推鞫，狱情遽至于矫诬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1152467_comment'></div>既阅实以平反，爰举直而措枉，已从明辩，式正常刑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1152467_comment'></div>其如中司长官，是臣外舅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1152467_comment'></div>践文昌六卿之贵，昧员扉两造之辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1152467_comment'></div>名挂简书，身系非所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1152467_comment'></div>实朝伦之共耻，在戚属以何颜？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1152467_comment'></div>是用沥恳紫庭，祈恩丹扆，愿退归于散地，庶允洽于至公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1152467_comment'></div>岂谓皇帝陛下推洪覆之深仁，示曲成之玄造，特颁泥检，俯示纶言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1152467_comment'></div>徵《周书》之旧章，以其罪不相及；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1152467_comment'></div>推汉高之大度，且复待之如初。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1152467_comment'></div>仰承雨露之私，内积冰渊之惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1152467_comment'></div>渎尊之罪，固不可以再三；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1152467_comment'></div>许国之心，但益坚于方寸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1152467_comment'></div>誓倾臣节，上答天慈<span class='inlineComment2'>（云云）</span>。</div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1152467_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1002&endYear=1002')">1002年3？</a>　三月及稍后，屡有诗送人落第归乡。作品：妹婿黄补下第归乡。黄觉东游。叶生归缙云。元道宗下第东游。<div id='poem_129161' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_129161' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/129161?labeling=true' target='_blank'>妹婿黄补下第归乡</a><span class='authorDate'>（1002年3？）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_129161")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_129161_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_129161'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_129161'>家风早占无双誉<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：君即江夏之后。）</span>，乡荐曾居第一流。<div id='poem_sentence_0_129161_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_129161'>昆岭本期争片玉，庖刀谁料失全牛。<div id='poem_sentence_1_129161_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_129161'>风尘不住梁王苑，烟水还依楚客舟。<div id='poem_sentence_2_129161_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_129161'>应负男儿四方志，故园归去莫淹留。<div id='poem_sentence_3_129161_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_129161'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_129161_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_129277' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_129277' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/129277?labeling=true' target='_blank'>黄觉东游</a><span class='authorDate'>（1002年3？）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_129277")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_129277_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_129277'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_129277'>乡关迢遰数千里，场屋蹉跎二十年。<div id='poem_sentence_0_129277_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_129277'>三献犹垂卞和泪，几人先著祖生鞭。<div id='poem_sentence_1_129277_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_129277'>风尘漫索长安米，禾黍全荒负郭田。<div id='poem_sentence_2_129277_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_129277'>关外贤豪遍投分，赵囊回日满金钱。<div id='poem_sentence_3_129277_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_129277'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_129277_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_129053' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_129053' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/129053?labeling=true' target='_blank'>叶生归缙云</a><span class='authorDate'>（1002年3？）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_129053")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_129053_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_129053'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_129053'>出门西望长安笑，抱璞来求善价沽。<div id='poem_sentence_0_129053_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_129053'>惟罄囊装买群籍，不持刺字谒当涂。<div id='poem_sentence_1_129053_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_129053'>鲈鱼渐熟思归切，羊酪初尝得味无。<div id='poem_sentence_2_129053_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_129053'>送子东还重销黯，我曾三载守仙都。<div id='poem_sentence_3_129053_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_129053'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_129053_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_129389' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_129389' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/129389?labeling=true' target='_blank'>元道宗下第东游<span class='inlineComment2'>（元氏昆弟子侄五人举进士）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1002年3？）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_129389")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_129389_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_129389'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_129389'>举宗文雅孰能陪，须信菰芦出美才。<div id='poem_sentence_0_129389_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_129389'>失意不劳悲玉璞，投知应得上金台。<div id='poem_sentence_1_129389_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_129389'>晓离村店侵残月，昼歇津亭避疾雷。<div id='poem_sentence_2_129389_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_129389'>东道诸侯多重士，融樽处处为君开。<div id='poem_sentence_3_129389_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_129389'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_129389_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1002&endYear=1002')">1002年5月</a>　温仲舒以知开封府繁剧求罢，亿代撰表。作品：代开封府温尚书求解知府表。<div id='poem_1152469' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152469' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152469?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代开封温尚书求解知府表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1002年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152469")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152469_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152469'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152469'>臣某言：臣闻陈力就列，先儒有知止之言；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152469_comment'></div>任重才微，前史著疾颠之戒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152469_comment'></div>布在方策，皎若丹青。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152469_comment'></div>固大带之攸书，实元龟之斯在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152469_comment'></div>臣某<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>伏念臣声猷素寡，才略无闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152469_comment'></div>徒以遭逢，遍尘清近，每忧官谤，上负圣知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152469_comment'></div>一自掌礼秩宗，预文昌之通显；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152469_comment'></div>牧民天府，总京邑之浩穰，唯坚夙夜之诚，仰奉澄清之寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1152469_comment'></div>幸而辇毂之下，桴鼓稀鸣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1152469_comment'></div>闾井之间，版图增美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1152469_comment'></div>大姓偶无于侵小，庶狱不至于称冤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1152469_comment'></div>盖缘每奉天颜，恭承睿训，俾之弹压豪右，抚字疲羸，且形钦恤之仁，深示招携之旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1152469_comment'></div>顾不畏于强御，并特出于主张。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1152469_comment'></div>挺金石之一心，但依洪覆；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1152469_comment'></div>历星霜之三载，莫中巧言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1152469_comment'></div>苟非当宁之曲成，谅亦倾辀而坐致。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1152469_comment'></div>又伏念负重致远，诚非泛驾之材；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1152469_comment'></div>错节盘根，终乏投虚之刃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1152469_comment'></div>米盐靡密，躬亲而岂敢告劳；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1152469_comment'></div>钩距神明，精力而渐知不逮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1152469_comment'></div>非辄图于避事，实恐至于败官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1152469_comment'></div>伏望尊号皇帝陛下察以虔诚，解兹重任，庶保全于贱质，免戕贼于劳生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1152469_comment'></div>中台职司，顾讲求于故事；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1152469_comment'></div>未央朝会，时瞻望于清光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1152469_comment'></div>筋骸渐及于衰迟，衡泌或希于颐养。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1152469_comment'></div>仰冀始终之惠，少矜恳倒之私。</div><div id='poem_sentence_25_1152469_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1002&endYear=1002')">1002年</a>　处州进士周启明下第归乡后寄长书述怀自嗟，亿以书呈秘阁黄夷简，夷简作诗称美，亿有和作。作品：予以缙云进士周启明长书呈秘阁黄少卿黄颇叹重作诗六韵美之因次韵和酬。<div id='poem_129388' class='_poem'><div
