id='poem_1152472' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152472' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152472?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代集贤向相公待罪表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1002年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152472")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152472_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152472'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152472'>臣某言：窃以辅弼之司，实一人之注意；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152472_comment'></div>举措之际，乃四海之具瞻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152472_comment'></div>苟自辍于悔尤，固不遑于启处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152472_comment'></div>臣某<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>伏念臣本非茂异，谬窃科名，爰遭遇于先朝，屡忝尘于华贯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152472_comment'></div>西垣掌诰，俯及二年；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152472_comment'></div>南海颁条，远踰万里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152472_comment'></div>偶注选于阙下，俄入直于禁中，亟膺奖擢之恩，俾佐枢机之务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152472_comment'></div>但倾驽拙，仰奉忧勤，累换星霜，莫裨尘露。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1152472_comment'></div>崇文广武圣明仁孝皇帝陛下绍膺丕构，褒宠旧臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1152472_comment'></div>以先朝簪履之微，不之遗弃；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1152472_comment'></div>顾微臣斗筲之量，深觉满盈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1152472_comment'></div>遽陪四辅以调元，获从六龙而展义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1152472_comment'></div>殊乏一言而启沃，曷宽万乘之焦劳？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1152472_comment'></div>寻奉简书，远巡边徼，恭承宸算，遐震天威。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1152472_comment'></div>愧无前箸之筹，尚轸宵衣之虑，久尘重位，方积厚颜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1152472_comment'></div>去年陛下特出非常，俾之爰立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1152472_comment'></div>中外颇喧于舆诵，君亲益示于眷怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1152472_comment'></div>俯偻循墙，靡容固让；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1152472_comment'></div>负乘致寇，果出自贻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1152472_comment'></div>今者公相之家，子孙搆讼，事连闺壸，词及钱刀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1152472_comment'></div>盖臣遭逢已来，赐予所得，辄营别墅，有爽素风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1152472_comment'></div>脱粟拔葵，既违于典训；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1152472_comment'></div>鼠牙雀角，遂起于争端。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1152472_comment'></div>致上浼于九重，实先甘于三黜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1152472_comment'></div>况臣位居黄閤，俸入甚优，日侍紫庭，体貌尤异，合敦操履，以厉搢绅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1152472_comment'></div>蔑闻市义之名，乃有营私之谤，横议喧腾于乡校，封章叠委于公车，黩冕旒之听聪，罪诚莫赎；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1152472_comment'></div>玷朝廷之名器，责亦何逃？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1152472_comment'></div>俯伏私门，以俟公宪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1152472_comment'></div>然望陛下推豁达之大度，察方寸之微诚，念臣久冒宠荣，常倾丹赤，固乏代天之业，粗坚许国之心，特霈鸿私，得从轻典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1152472_comment'></div>即臣摩顶至踵，仰衔覆帱之仁；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1152472_comment'></div>虽死犹生，终效糜捐之报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1152472_comment'></div>臣无任<span class='inlineComment2'>（云云）</span>。</div><div id='poem_sentence_31_1152472_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1002&endYear=1002')">1002年11？</a>　集贤学士范贻孙卒葬，十一月或稍前，为撰墓志铭。作品：宋故主客员外郎直集贤院高平范公墓志铭。<div id='poem_1152701' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152701' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152701?labeling=true' target='_blank'>宋故主客员外郎直集贤院高平范公墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1002年11？）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152701")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152701_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152701'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152701'>咸平五年二月戊寅，集贤学士、主客员外郎高平范公暴中风眩，终于上都甘泉坊之私第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152701_comment'></div>上以贤相之后，形于叹息，戚里之懿，优其赗赙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152701_comment'></div>两宫遣使以赴吊，四邻闻丧而辍舂，交游恸哭于寝门，行旅咨嗟于闾巷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152701_comment'></div>非椒兰之德，服媚于人，梁栋之材，中道而夭者，畴能痛惜如是哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152701_comment'></div>公讳贻孙，字馀庆，济南历城人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152701_comment'></div>其先历虞、夏、商、周，寔享世禄，春秋、战国，继出名卿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152701_comment'></div>或以博士显东京，或以词人称南国，或以文雄史策，或以信著友朋，蕃衍流光，非可殚举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152701_comment'></div>及公之大父守愚，占数京辅，随牒方州，为郑州防御判官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1152701_comment'></div>命屈当时，庆钟后嗣，累赠太子太师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1152701_comment'></div>王父，故鲁国公讳质，以伊、管事业，辅翼三朝；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1152701_comment'></div>以燕、许手笔，称量天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1152701_comment'></div>由司徒侍中罢为太子太傅、鲁国公，而闻望益大，恩礼弥渥，将为苍生而再起，遽叹哲人之云亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1152701_comment'></div>然自五代以来，百年之内，号良弼者，不闻他人，累赠至尚书令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1152701_comment'></div>烈考讳旻，以公卿子著籍甚之称，在贵游间有台辅之望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1152701_comment'></div>文章组绣于鞶帨，心计剖析于毛氂，任给事中、三司副使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1152701_comment'></div>公累谪宦，事备国书，由公上言，追复官爵，累赠至工部尚书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1152701_comment'></div>公以岐嶷之姿，荷清白之训，思以学优入仕，耻由父任为郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1152701_comment'></div>不杂尘游，专精坟史，果以乡里之荐，亟预贤能之书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1152701_comment'></div>天子临轩，擢居乙等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1152701_comment'></div>同年生率次补州郡从事、掾属、丞尉，天子以公奕世载德，肯构象贤，欲其起家，不循常调，解褐授大理评事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1152701_comment'></div>雍熙中，林胡犯边，王师致讨，飞挽之役，公寔董之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1152701_comment'></div>祗畏简书，大足兵食，凯旋迁光禄寺丞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1152701_comment'></div>数月，改秘书省著作佐郎，面赐五品服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1152701_comment'></div>公以群玉上帝之册府，蓬莱道家之藏室，贤俊咸集，喜田苏之与游，图史实繁，多黄香之未见，于是削章退食，献赋离宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1152701_comment'></div>即日命公待制文馆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1152701_comment'></div>数月，以本官直集贤院。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1152701_comment'></div>自是䌷书石室，侍宴瑶池。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1152701_comment'></div>歌黄鹄于建章，必陪赓载；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1152701_comment'></div>泛楼船于汾水，即奉豫游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1152701_comment'></div>以冠玉之英标，累闻题柱；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1152701_comment'></div>以燃萁之敏思，几至夺袍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1152701_comment'></div>其风度闲详，才调清婉，士流推慕，时论归之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1152701_comment'></div>登朝为殿中丞，迁太常博士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1152701_comment'></div>上即位，入省为外郎，皆领书殿之职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1152701_comment'></div>公克缵绪业，祗荷门阀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1152701_comment'></div>寝丘遗产，非有膏腴；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1152701_comment'></div>晏子旧居，未更爽垲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1152701_comment'></div>而能孝以睦族，俭以饬躬，即安先人之庐，不违王父之命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1152701_comment'></div>雅好礼法，尤重名节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1152701_comment'></div>奉蒸尝之祀，馨德达于神明；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1152701_comment'></div>事期功之亲，欢心洽于宗党。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1152701_comment'></div>性嗜群籍，家藏万卷，或手自缮写，或亲加校雠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1152701_comment'></div>缃素毕陈，敌秘书之副本；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1152701_comment'></div>签题具列，同吴氏之西斋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1152701_comment'></div>好事之名，流布京毂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1152701_comment'></div>每风庭月榭，萧晨兰夕，必命俦啸侣，衔杯漱醪，凡备三益之交，莫匪一时之隽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1152701_comment'></div>汉庭太史，或奏于聚星；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1152701_comment'></div>齐国客卿，无嫌于卜夜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1152701_comment'></div>此亦冲襟高韵，夐越常伦，尚德好贤，有足多者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1152701_comment'></div>呜呼，不幸今也其亡！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1152701_comment'></div>享年四十三，斯夭也已矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1152701_comment'></div>夫人高邑县君李氏，实淮阳丞相之妹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1152701_comment'></div>洪惟伯姊，母仪万邦，作合先朝，居尊长乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1152701_comment'></div>而夫人处贵思降，在富能贫，周旋礼经，辅佐君子，得中馈之道，彰内助之贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1152701_comment'></div>举案齐眉，方期于偕老；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1152701_comment'></div>帷堂昼哭，遽痛于未亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1152701_comment'></div>一子克勤，年十一岁，天子悯之，特授太常寺奉礼郎，月给俸缗，俾终服纪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1152701_comment'></div>固有奇骨，荷兹高门，虽在童蒙，已知孺慕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1152701_comment'></div>有后之庆，斯言不诬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1152701_comment'></div>一女尚幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1152701_comment'></div>夫人以丧无虑居，礼当即远，毁家襄事，竭力送终。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1152701_comment'></div>伊洛之间，松槚斯在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1152701_comment'></div>日月其吉，龟筮无违。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1152701_comment'></div>即以其年十一月戊申，扶护归葬于河南府洛阳县某乡某里，祔于先茔，礼也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1152701_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1152701_comment'></div>劫烬灰飞，沉碑谷变，非刻金石，曷志桑田？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1152701_comment'></div>以某投分生平，托之铭篆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1152701_comment'></div>巨源尚在，庶嵇绍之不孤；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1152701_comment'></div>伯喈有言，述太丘而无愧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1152701_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_69_1152701'>范氏之先，出于陶唐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1152701_comment'></div>积德储祉，奕叶流光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1152701_comment'></div>赫赫鲁公，蝉緌貂珰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1152701_comment'></div>阴德有后，乃生夕郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1152701_comment'></div>于惟集仙，肯构肯堂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1152701_comment'></div>穆然容辉，焕乎文章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1152701_comment'></div>行归于周，动罔不臧，呜呼难忱，今也即亡！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1152701_comment'></div>洛水滨兮邙山址，波东倾兮树西靡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1152701_comment'></div>从先公兮夜台，启新阡兮蒿里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1152701_comment'></div>传三世兮一身，閟九泉兮万祀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1152701_comment'></div>琢贞石兮志佳城，人之生兮胡至此？</div><div id='poem_sentence_79_1152701_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1002&endYear=1002')">1002年</a>　十一月南郊，此前奉旨撰《太常乐章》，备皇帝行朝飨太庙、南郊礼用。作品：太常乐章三十首。<span class='inlineComment2'>（含《皇帝南郊前一日朝飨太庙奏曲》十四章、《南郊降神奏曲》十六章。）</span><div id='poem_129391' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_129391' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/129391?labeling=true' target='_blank'>太常乐章三十首<span class='inlineComment2'>（奉圣旨撰，咸平五年）</span><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其十四 </span>亚献终献送神并奏理安之曲</a><span class='authorDate'>（1002年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_129391")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_129391_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_129391'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_129391'>神之来兮风肃然，神之去兮升九天。<div id='poem_sentence_0_129391_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_129391'>排凌兢兮还恍惚，羽旄纷兮萧芗燔。<div id='poem_sentence_1_129391_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_129391'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_129391_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_129390' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_129390' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/129390?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二十九 </span>皇帝御楼奏隆安之曲</a><span class='authorDate'>（1002年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_129390_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_129390'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_129390'>圜丘类上帝，六变降天神。<div id='poem_sentence_0_129390_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_129390'>禋燔礼云毕，使卫肃以陈。<div id='poem_sentence_1_129390_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_129390'>天颜瞻咫尺，王泽熙阳春。<div id='poem_sentence_2_129390_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_129390'>玉帛臻禹会，动植沾尧仁。<div id='poem_sentence_3_129390_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_129390'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_129390_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_129442' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_129442' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/129442?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span>皇帝南郊前一日朝飨太庙奏理安曲迎神</a><span class='authorDate'>（1002年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>四言诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_129442_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_129442'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_129442'>肃肃清庙，昭事祖祢。<div id='poem_sentence_0_129442_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_129442'>粢盛苾芬，四海来祭。<div id='poem_sentence_1_129442_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1002&endYear=1002')">1002年11月11日</a>　祀天地于圜丘，礼毕，帝赋五言六韵诗一首，赐朝臣，亿具状谢之，又以诗和之。作品：奉和御制南郊礼毕五言六韵诗。阁下谢赐御制南郊诗状。<div id='poem_129341' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_129341' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/129341?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奉和圣制南郊礼毕五言六韵诗</a><span class='authorDate'>（1002年11月11日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span id='poem_title_129341_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_129341'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_129341'>燔柴就阳位，烟燎达高穹。<div id='poem_sentence_0_129341_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_129341'>扫地铏豋洁，严更鼓角雄。<div id='poem_sentence_1_129341_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_129341_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1152533' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152533' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152533?labeling=true' target='_blank'>阁下谢赐御制南郊诗状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1002年11月11日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152533'>右，臣等今日中使至，伏蒙圣慈，赐臣等《南郊礼毕》五言六韵诗一首，依韵和来者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152533_comment'></div>上帝眷怀，方陈于燔燎；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152533_comment'></div>圣人有作，爰载于声诗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152533_comment'></div>俯示颛蒙，俾祛聋瞆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152533_comment'></div>幸睹昭回之采，得闻正始之音，不觉味忘，几乎手舞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152533_comment'></div>恭惟皇帝陛下恭承正统，寅奉旧章，卜郊兆以就阳，神祇昭格；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152533_comment'></div>奉玉帛而来祭，华夏骏奔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152533_comment'></div>爰扫地以贵诚，乃备物而报本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1152533_comment'></div>銮舆出次，雨足洒途；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1152533_comment'></div>冕服升坛，天光烛野。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1152533_comment'></div>动必䜣合，先而不违，实三灵之交欢，谅百福以申锡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1152533_comment'></div>而陛下允膺玄贶，浚发雅言，曲示近臣，咸令属和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1152533_comment'></div>况大君之发咏，岂下士以能窥？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1152533_comment'></div>虽效冥搜，终成滥吹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1152533_comment'></div>朱弦解愠，已睹于变风；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1152533_comment'></div>良玉匿瑕，式希于藏拙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1152533_comment'></div>勉陈鄙陋，有黩高明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1152533_comment'></div>臣等无任云云。</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1152533_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1002&endYear=1002')">1002年12月</a>　与陈恕同为铨选官，谈艺，恕推亿所作《涵虚阁记》“信一代之雄文也”。<br /><a href="javascript: id='poem_sentence_3_129084_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_129084'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_129084_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1002&endYear=1002')">1002年</a>　冬，有诗送凌策知广州。作品：史馆凌职方知广州。<div id='poem_129317' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_129317' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/129317?labeling=true' target='_blank'>史馆凌职方知广州<span class='inlineComment2'>（曾任岭南转运）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1002年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_129317")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_129317_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_129317'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_129317'>番禺出守重，汉殿拜恩初。<div id='poem_sentence_0_129317_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_129317'>华省郎官宿，名山太史书。<div id='poem_sentence_1_129317_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_129317'>剖符从琐闼，持节上轺车。<div id='poem_sentence_2_129317_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_129317'>左顾金龟印，前驱画隼旟。<div id='poem_sentence_3_129317_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_129317'>由来百粤地，曾督九年储。<div id='poem_sentence_4_129317_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_129317'>卉服要荒外，棠阴惠爱馀。<div id='poem_sentence_5_129317_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_129317'>赍装天子赐，封部岛夷居。<div id='poem_sentence_6_129317_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_129317'>羽檄招溪洞，壶浆慰里闾。<div id='poem_sentence_7_129317_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_129317'>国风今已变，民瘼到应除。<div id='poem_sentence_8_129317_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_129317'>江海思归否，蓬山有直庐。<div id='poem_sentence_9_129317_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_129317'></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_129317_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1002&endYear=1002')">1002年</a>　岁暮，有诗送董温其赴王化基淮南幕。作品：董温其赴淮南幕。<div id='poem_129285' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_129285' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/129285?labeling=true' target='_blank'>董温其赴淮南幕<span class='inlineComment2'>（工部王尚书知扬州）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1002年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_129285")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_129285_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_129285'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_129285'>岁晏梁园密雪飞，出关犹忆弃繻时。<div id='poem_sentence_0_129285_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_129285'>属鞬正是从军乐，插羽那忧草檄迟。<div id='poem_sentence_1_129285_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_129285'>陪宴初筵挥玉柄，从游别墅骋金羁<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：府公维扬有别墅焉。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_2_129285_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_129285'>只应偏啖牛心炙，自此声名汉殿知。<div id='poem_sentence_3_129285_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_129285'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_129285_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1002&endYear=1002')">1002年</a>　田锡以文集惠示，亿上书赞誉之。作品：上田谏议书。<div id='poem_1152631' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152631' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152631?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上田谏议书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1002年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152631")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152631_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152631'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152631'>某伏承谏议学士特以雄文，曲垂嘉惠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152631_comment'></div>启缄縢而郑重，窥刀尺以再三。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152631_comment'></div>耽味不忘，佩服无斁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152631_comment'></div>切以谏议学士钟岷峨之间气，袭淹稷之素风，秉笔擅作者之称，穷经得圣人之旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152631_comment'></div>对策三道，中汉殿之甲科；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152631_comment'></div>搆赋十年，占梁园之右席。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152631_comment'></div>爰自讨论汗简，启迪丝言，藻绘彰施，声猷藉甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152631_comment'></div>盖斯文之先觉，实吾道之悬衡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1152631_comment'></div>元礼门墙，固如登于龙阪；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1152631_comment'></div>乐天诗句，亦远播于鸡林。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1152631_comment'></div>某早自计阶，已深景行，虽云慕蔺，何敢望回？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1152631_comment'></div>切尝博访编联，愿窥阃奥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1152631_comment'></div>然《白雪》、《阳春》之曲，属和几希；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1152631_comment'></div>而辉山媚水之珍，不索何获？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1152631_comment'></div>顾思齐之尤切，辱投闇以爰来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1152631_comment'></div>昔者得荆州之书，顿贤十部；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1152631_comment'></div>市《长门》之赋，无吝百金。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1152631_comment'></div>幸窥风雅之言，尽祛鄙倍之思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1152631_comment'></div>获径尺之宝，论价何止于五城；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1152631_comment'></div>闻《九韶》之音，忘味更期于三月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1152631_comment'></div>庶芬馨之俱化，谅钻仰之弥坚，感愧之诚，造次于是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1152631_comment'></div>其盛制，谨留缮写。</div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1152631_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1002&endYear=1002')">1002年</a>　约于本年，乡里姻亲张彝宪奉本郡计籍至京，出亿昔题其池亭二首诗示朝贤，于是晁迥、李宗谔等相继有作，亿为之序。作品：诸公寄题建州浦城县清河张君所居池亭诗序。<div id='poem_1152666' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152666' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152666?labeling=true' target='_blank'>诸公寄题建州浦城县清河张君所居池亭诗序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1002年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152666")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152666_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152666'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152666'>茂才清河君，于予盖乡先生丈人行也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152666_comment'></div>顷者书轨未同，齿血犹壮，不扫一室，有志四方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152666_comment'></div>薄游九江，讲学庐阜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152666_comment'></div>励精文史，既素业之大成；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152666_comment'></div>归省庭闱，值戒车之适驾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152666_comment'></div>未几青盖西上，先正从行，乔木怀安，族人攸庇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152666_comment'></div>亢宗裕蛊，盖肥家之是图；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152666_comment'></div>委质策名，于观国而何暇？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1152666_comment'></div>雍熙二年，仲氏举进士，中乙科。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1152666_comment'></div>淳化三年，季弟随计偕，列高等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1152666_comment'></div>推让致美，君之志也，俄而先府君捐馆寿阳，犊车归葬；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1152666_comment'></div>先夫人启手故里，驹隙终丧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1152666_comment'></div>商于解印而归，叔庭既冠而逝，实有天伦之戚，无复西笑之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1152666_comment'></div>且欲没齿田园，放怀林壑，与浮丘把袂，为羲皇上人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1152666_comment'></div>其所居也，背山临水，占奇据胜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1152666_comment'></div>累世增葺，极为轮奂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1152666_comment'></div>曲池皎鉴，脩梁横度，虚阁崛起，反宇凌空。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1152666_comment'></div>云山蔽亏，鱼鸟聱耴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1152666_comment'></div>赏心肆体，于焉取斯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1152666_comment'></div>予淳化四年，由书殿得告，归迎版舆，时君膝下承颜，友于欢宴，置酒危榭，酣饮终日，予亦斐然成咏，题于梁屋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1152666_comment'></div>及咸平三年罢郡缙云，复造仙墅，君且永怀罔极，痛深终鲜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1152666_comment'></div>逝者如此，灵光岿然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1152666_comment'></div>予用是追感畴昔，赓载前唱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1152666_comment'></div>今年，君奉本郡计籍，来上中台。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1152666_comment'></div>盖因县次之续食，将与故人而胥遇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1152666_comment'></div>君之爱子，实吾家之宅相，而予之外弟也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1152666_comment'></div>往年随我，肄业上都。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1152666_comment'></div>刻苦读书，三馀之习无废；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1152666_comment'></div>孝谨成性，万石之德不衰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1152666_comment'></div>君亦既见止，弥加教督。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1152666_comment'></div>会稽栝羽，何用不臧？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1152666_comment'></div>于公里门，于兹必大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1152666_comment'></div>君戾止未久，归欤兴叹，且以鄙夫昔留池阁二咏及群公佳章，俾之示朝右之贤，庶乎知隐居之志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1152666_comment'></div>安定大谏，赵郡阁老，及上邽、富春晁、陈诸紫微，暨秘阁潘公，咸乐善无厌，慕义不足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1152666_comment'></div>竞抉秘思，发为雅篇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1152666_comment'></div>千里寄题，岂人遐而室迩；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1152666_comment'></div>七闽传诵，盖玉振以金相。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1152666_comment'></div>诚足为吾党之美谈，宁独光幽人之肥遁也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1152666_comment'></div>予与君，先畴接畛，鸡犬相闻，奕世联姻，丝萝有素。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1152666_comment'></div>早亲长者之论，备知高世之行，因叙始末，用冠篇首云耳。</div><div id='poem_sentence_39_1152666_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1002&endYear=1002')">1002年</a>　《历代铨政要略》或作于本年。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1003&endYear=1003')">1003年2月18日</a>　扈从帝游戏马场，观习武，有诗纪事。作品：咸平六年二月十八日扈从宸游因成纪事二十二韵。<div id='poem_129415' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_129415' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/129415?labeling=true' target='_blank'>咸平六年二月十八日扈从宸游因成纪事二十二韵</a><span class='authorDate'>（1003年2月18日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_129415")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_129415_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_129415'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_129415'>步辇下明光，鸣鞘出未央。<div id='poem_sentence_0_129415_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_129415'>属车多载酒，夹道竞焚香。<div id='poem_sentence_1_129415_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_129415'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_129415", 129415, "Clauses/4/Comments/0")'>云管</span>飘<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_129415", 129415, "Clauses/4/Comments/1")'>梅吹</span>，蜺旌错鸟章。<div id='poem_sentence_2_129415_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_129415'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_129415", 129415, "Clauses/6/Comments/0")'>从臣</span>沙苑马，卫士羽林枪。<div id='poem_sentence_3_129415_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_129415'>玉辂天行健，金壶<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_129415", 129415, "Clauses/9/Comments/0")'>昼漏</span>长。<div id='poem_sentence_4_129415_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_129415'>光风汎兰蕙，仙雾拂旂常。<div id='poem_sentence_5_129415_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_129415'>宿雨收林薄，晨曦艳屋梁。<div id='poem_sentence_6_129415_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_129415'>闾阎空里巷，旄罕<span class='inlineComment2'>（明刻本作钺）</span>隘康庄。<div id='poem_sentence_7_129415_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_129415'>托乘奉珍使，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_129415", 129415, "Clauses/17/Comments/0")'>先驱</span>执戟郎。<div id='poem_sentence_8_129415_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_129415'>从桥初转毂，凭轼见垂裳。<div id='poem_sentence_9_129415_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_129415'>暂驻时龙驭，前临戏马场。<div id='poem_sentence_10_129415_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_129415'>由来讲武事，所以服遐荒。<div id='poem_sentence_11_129415_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_129415'>电影流<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_12_129415", 129415, "Clauses/24/Comments/0")'>机石</span>，鸦群发大黄<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_12_129415_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_129415'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_13_129415", 129415, "Clauses/26/Comments/0")'>千钧</span>宁觉重，七札岂曾妨。<div id='poem_sentence_13_129415_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_129415'>卒勇如虓虎，人观若堵墙。<div id='poem_sentence_14_129415_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_129415'>腰鞬晋元帅，扈跸汉诸王。<div id='poem_sentence_15_129415_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_129415'>聊用誇<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_16_129415", 129415, "Clauses/32/Comments/0")'>胡客</span>，还闻詟鬼方。<div id='poem_sentence_16_129415_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_129415'>回舆百里囿，锡宴九霞觞。<div id='poem_sentence_17_129415_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_129415'>射以驺虞节，歌为白雪倡。<div id='poem_sentence_18_129415_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_129415'>仙山鲸海上，御苑斗城旁。<div id='poem_sentence_19_129415_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_129415'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_20_129415", 129415, "Clauses/40/Comments/0")'>周镐</span>欢麀鹿，虞韶集凤凰。<div id='poem_sentence_20_129415_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_129415'>瑶池春水渌，犹误濯沧浪。<div id='poem_sentence_21_129415_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_129415'></div><div id='poem_sentence_22_129415_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_129415'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_12_129415_0'>⑴ 自注：是日御讲武台，观放抛石及发连弩。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_129415_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1003&endYear=1003')">1003年3月16日</a>　侍帝后苑赏花钓鱼，应制赋诗。作品：后苑赏花钓鱼应制。<div id='poem_129070' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_129070' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/129070?labeling=true' target='_blank'>后苑赏花钓鱼应制<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup></a><span class='authorDate'>（1003年3月16日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_129070")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_129070_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_129070_0'>① 咸平六年三月十六日奉圣旨以芳字为韵</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_129070'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_129070'>宜春小苑斗城旁，锡宴群仙奉紫皇。<div id='poem_sentence_0_129070_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_129070'>汉沼乳鱼偏傍钓，青陵舞蝶自寻芳。<div id='poem_sentence_1_129070_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_129070'>波平鳌背浮昆阆，日转金茎艳赭黄。<div id='poem_sentence_2_129070_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_129070'>满酌流霞侍臣醉，暖风宫蕊杂炉香。<div id='poem_sentence_3_129070_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_129070'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_129070_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1003&endYear=1003')">1003年</a>　春，贺李沆纳婿，观花烛，有诗。沆婿即王曾。作品：仆射李相公宅观花烛。<div id='poem_129022' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_129022' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/129022?labeling=true' target='_blank'>仆射李相公宅观花烛<span class='inlineComment2'>（时纳状元王曾为婿）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1003年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_129022")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_129022_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_129022'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_129022'>孙阁相君和鼎贵，秦楼爱婿坦床贤。<div id='poem_sentence_0_129022_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_129022'>东方千骑还居上，南极三星正在天。<div id='poem_sentence_1_129022_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_129022'>路入桃源花烂漫，桥横银汉水漪涟。<div id='poem_sentence_2_129022_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_129022'>乘龙择对真无比，月桂宫中第一仙。<div id='poem_sentence_3_129022_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_129022'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_129022_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1003&endYear=1003')">1003年</a>　内弟李生求更名，亿为之名曰休复，字德邻，作序说之。作品：与内弟李休复序。<div id='poem_1152650' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152650' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152650?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与内弟李休复序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1003年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152650")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152650_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152650'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152650'>陇西李生，予之内弟也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152650_comment'></div>才十数岁，能属文，善楷隶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152650_comment'></div>性端谨介特，外直而内温，不读非圣之书，不入非类之室，孜孜为学匪懈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152650_comment'></div>州里之内，名称蔼然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152650_comment'></div>咸平二年，奉乡老荐书，就试春官氏，实在高第，扬于王庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152650_comment'></div>天子以其新进少年，欲抑之，俾进其业，遂用旅退，曾不屑怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152650_comment'></div>去年本郡凡贡士三十八人，实冠其首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152650_comment'></div>西望而笑，与计吏偕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1152650_comment'></div>方摩厉以须，虚憍恃气，将乘长风而破巨浪，运南溟而徙天池。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1152650_comment'></div>适有功缌之丧，不克其志，怀宝待价，岂虑迷邦，杜门燕居，亦云知命，斯可尚也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1152650_comment'></div>一日，再拜而言曰：「夫名以定体，有自来矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1152650_comment'></div>始肄业乡校，名宗元，及举进士，更之曰琼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1152650_comment'></div>繇琼以来，一不利见，再不克。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1152650_comment'></div>就试礼部，求所以易之者」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1152650_comment'></div>予应之曰：「《复》之六二：『休复，吉』。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1152650_comment'></div>《象》曰：『休复之吉，以下仁也』。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1152650_comment'></div>盖得位处中，协比初九。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1152650_comment'></div>初九有仁德，而能附顺之，所以为亲仁善邻之象，复之休也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1152650_comment'></div>《左氏传》曰：『亲仁善邻，国之宝也』。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1152650_comment'></div>《语》曰：『德不孤，必有邻』。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1152650_comment'></div>夫七日来复，天地之心也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1152650_comment'></div>照邻殆庶，颜子之德也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1152650_comment'></div>处复而休，择邻以德，非君子儒者，其孰能从事于斯矣？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1152650_comment'></div>宜更名曰休复，字德邻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1152650_comment'></div>若乃率性循道，自诚而明，《复》之体也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1152650_comment'></div>迈种务滋，聿修无忝，德之度也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1152650_comment'></div>所宜探中庸性命之理，无或怵迫；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1152650_comment'></div>亲大雅明哲之士，与之切劘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1152650_comment'></div>使德妙玄同，虚室生白，鸣谦受益，心逸日休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1152650_comment'></div>勤而行之，进吾往也，固宜立功立事，为世伟人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1152650_comment'></div>岂徒发策决科，智效一官而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1152650_comment'></div>古人耻名浮于实，幸吾弟勉之哉」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1152650_comment'></div>外兄某序。</div><div id='poem_sentence_32_1152650_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1003&endYear=1003')">1003年5月</a>　宰相吕蒙正以疾求罢，帝命李沆抚问，赐药，亿代撰谢状。作品：代司空相公谢抚问状。<div id='poem_1152536' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152536' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152536?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代司空相公谢抚问状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1003年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152536")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152536_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152536'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152536'>右：臣昨日晚李沆等到臣私第，奉传圣旨，以臣所患，令安心将治，中书无事者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152536_comment'></div>处弼谐之任，曾乏于谋猷；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152536_comment'></div>乖摄养之方，自生于疾疢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152536_comment'></div>蓬荜适居于假告，冕旒仍示于记怜，特令当国之臣，曲谕如纶之旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152536_comment'></div>慰安弥极，跼蹐靡遑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152536_comment'></div>盖念臣本出诸生，素无远略，幸以遭逢景运，际会先朝，但持孤直之心，获玷具瞻之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152536_comment'></div>跛鳖安能于致远，短绠非可以汲深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152536_comment'></div>衮章莫效于弥缝，鼎实每虞于倾覆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1152536_comment'></div>爰从策免，复预畴咨，虽竭肺腑，曷裨尘露？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1152536_comment'></div>终荷保全之惠，缪升师长之崇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1152536_comment'></div>皇帝陛下恭己奉先，虚怀求旧，式污揆路，再冠台司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1152536_comment'></div>比三入于承明，殊非光宠；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1152536_comment'></div>享万全于黄阁，尤负腼惭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1152536_comment'></div>宵衣岂减于忧勤，尸禄唯甘于嘲诮，果贻瞰室，遂致卧漳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1152536_comment'></div>瞻八彩之眉，暂违尧陛；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1152536_comment'></div>赐十全之药，便降秦医。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1152536_comment'></div>命星使以宣传，若天颜之咫尺；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1152536_comment'></div>荷照临之所及，诚陨越以难胜！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1152536_comment'></div>敢谓特遣辅臣，同过陋巷，备形问讯，益示温存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1152536_comment'></div>教以安心，俾达农皇之养命；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1152536_comment'></div>谕之无事，盖虑孔明之伤神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1152536_comment'></div>窃佩训词，仰衔睿眷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1152536_comment'></div>顿袪沈痼，丹九转以何功；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1152536_comment'></div>誓报生成，身一毛而为喻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1152536_comment'></div>感恩之至，雪涕无从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1152536_comment'></div>臣无任。</div><div id='poem_sentence_25_1152536_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1003&endYear=1003')">1003年8月</a>　奉敕撰《洞霄宫碑铭》，黄夷简见而称许之，亿以诗酬。作品：进洞霄宫碑。重修亳州洞霄宫碑铭并序。酬秘阁黄少卿因见所作洞霄宫碑且有题记。<div id='poem_1152543' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152543' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152543?labeling=true' target='_blank'>进洞霄宫碑状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1003年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152543")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152543_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152543'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152543'>右，臣昨奉敕，令臣撰《亳州洞霄宫碑文》进呈者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152543_comment'></div>闻命魂惊，抽毫思辍，率罄驽拙，绵历旬时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152543_comment'></div>窃以玄元诞育之区，光灵未泯；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152543_comment'></div>睿哲钦崇之旨，修奉惟寅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152543_comment'></div>爰毕塈涂，将刊琬琰，合资大手，用志新宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152543_comment'></div>而臣猥奉佥谐，获当撰述。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152543_comment'></div>乏色丝之妙，曷示方来？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152543_comment'></div>参衡石之馀，空尘圣览。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1152543_comment'></div>内循鄙陋，尤负腼惭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1152543_comment'></div>其碑铭今已撰成，谨随状上进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1152543_comment'></div>干冒宸严。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1152543_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1152693' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152693' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152693?labeling=true' target='_blank'>重修亳州洞霄宫碑铭<span class='inlineComment2'>（并序　奉敕撰）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1003年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152693")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152693_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152693'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152693'>臣闻：昔者大道之行，异人间出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152693_comment'></div>洪惟柱史，寔畅真宗，叙《道德》之二篇，述慈俭之三宝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152693_comment'></div>玩志众妙，理洞于帝先；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152693_comment'></div>垂训方来，尊居于教父。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152693_comment'></div>故尹喜望气，爰识真人；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152693_comment'></div>史迁编年，首推黄老。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152693_comment'></div>或谓之隐君子，著书五千文；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152693_comment'></div>或以为太史儋，享寿二百岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1152693_comment'></div>立言垂于不朽，乘化入于无间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1152693_comment'></div>惟苦县厉乡，即降神之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1152693_comment'></div>土风杂乎南楚，郡境介于陈留。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1152693_comment'></div>盖尸而祝之，㟪𡾊作庚桑之社；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1152693_comment'></div>思且爱矣，陕郊存召伯之棠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1152693_comment'></div>后人缅慕玄风，周爰旧壤，聿因灵迹，肇建严祠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1152693_comment'></div>历代封崇，樵苏之禁弥肃；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1152693_comment'></div>昔贤赞述，金石之刻具存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1152693_comment'></div>又往者圣质诞祥，元符冥合，乘白鹿而下，爰自九天，感流星之精，生于左腋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1152693_comment'></div>指李树以为姓，由聃耳而立名，禀粹斗魁，发祥井脉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1152693_comment'></div>佥以为涂山祀夏，式脩启母之祠；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1152693_comment'></div>后稷配天，乃建姜嫄之庙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1152693_comment'></div>恭惟圣母，实育至人，陵谷未移，光灵如在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1152693_comment'></div>又因遗址，别启殊庭，目之为李母祠，盖有年矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1152693_comment'></div>虽洁粢致享，不领天子之祠官；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1152693_comment'></div>而閒馆栖神，具载职方之地志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1152693_comment'></div>岁月寖远，遗构仅存，期运环周，祥符显发，施及唐室，系自仙源。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1152693_comment'></div>乾封中以锡羡流光，肇开鸿绪，似续蕃衍，袭庆本支。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1152693_comment'></div>且念太极之先，冠二仪而首出；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1152693_comment'></div>盛德之后，垂百世以弥昌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1152693_comment'></div>追崇长乐之名，用显始基之迹，由是追封圣母为先天太后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1152693_comment'></div>又以列真之宇，神光烛于宫坛；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1152693_comment'></div>集灵之虚，紫气干乎霄极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1152693_comment'></div>琳房绛阙，窈窱重光，孔盖翠旌，裴回戾止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1152693_comment'></div>盖方舆之福地，乃虚皇之密都。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1152693_comment'></div>由是改命祠宇为「洞霄宫」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1152693_comment'></div>香火无废于熏修，栋宇益增于轮奂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1152693_comment'></div>南望吾子，飞观凌云；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1152693_comment'></div>左带临溪，清流漱石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1152693_comment'></div>行人胥畏，颇类轩台；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1152693_comment'></div>游者忘归，更疑秦洞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1152693_comment'></div>至乃玄贶昭格，冥感彰闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1152693_comment'></div>或旭景朝跻，非烟绚䌽；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1152693_comment'></div>或柔条夕劲，甘露垂滋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1152693_comment'></div>或千仞凤翔，览德晖而下集；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1152693_comment'></div>或九井龙见，乘云气以上腾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1152693_comment'></div>往昔海县尘飞，萑蒲蚁聚，流矢集屋，束蕴乘墉，即必黑气塞川，愁霖贯序。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1152693_comment'></div>凶党不能肆毒，阖境率以宁居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1152693_comment'></div>当时降玺书以旌扬，垂方策而标记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1152693_comment'></div>求诸故府，盖图牒之未刊；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1152693_comment'></div>岿然灵光，实神明之所庇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1152693_comment'></div>皇朝接千岁之统，按九州之图，包举海隅，并走群望，讲求祀典，咸秩无文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1152693_comment'></div>诞扬清净之风，式契玄元之旨，深诏谯郡，崇奉灵场，缮究匪亏，焚修弥洁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1152693_comment'></div>崇文广武圣明仁孝皇帝之在宥天下也，恭默思道，斋慄事神，绍祖宗之耿光，集乾坤之景命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1152693_comment'></div>端拱南面，唯轸念于苍生；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1152693_comment'></div>閒宴西清，乃娱情于玄牝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1152693_comment'></div>顺风之拜，几慕于崆峒；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1152693_comment'></div>赤水之珍，靡徵于𧩶诟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1152693_comment'></div>驱民寿域，日用而不知；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1152693_comment'></div>决事斋居，天行而弥健。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1152693_comment'></div>乃至探求三五之载籍，致恭上下之神祇，黍稷牺牲，悉用先王之礼；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1152693_comment'></div>坛场圭币，无取方士之言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1152693_comment'></div>正违治烦，脩弊起废。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1152693_comment'></div>陈信策告，蔑闻秘祝之官；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1152693_comment'></div>备物荐尝，奚馁若敖之鬼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1152693_comment'></div>乃至山川作镇于地，出云雨以嘉生；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1152693_comment'></div>卿士有益于人，垂竹帛而悠久。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1152693_comment'></div>莫不咨询典故，弥缝阙漏，丰洁苾芬而致用，聪明正直之是依。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1152693_comment'></div>用能陟降泰畤，与三灵交欢；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1152693_comment'></div>端委明堂，俾诸神受祀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1152693_comment'></div>帝锡纯嘏，百禄是膺，洛出图书，九畴式叙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1152693_comment'></div>盛德大业，光表格天，固非名言之所能及也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1152693_comment'></div>乃眷亳社，时惟谷阳，仁里未迁，清都斯在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1152693_comment'></div>曩以神虬跃于沮泽，阴魄离于罕车，雩禜偶愆，水潦荐降。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1152693_comment'></div>云不待族，雨及我私，甫田或害于粢盛，樊圃几勤于浸灌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1152693_comment'></div>是宫也虽面势爽垲，取规《大壮》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1152693_comment'></div>在山楶藻棁，于焉胜人；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1152693_comment'></div>非麦曲鞠穷，何以御湿？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1152693_comment'></div>屋瓦斯漏，梁木其摧，本郡以闻，当阳太息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1152693_comment'></div>即日降明诏，遣近臣，案行故墟，周视层搆，度费制用，庀徒僝工。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1152693_comment'></div>之子于垣，百堵皆作，灵台经始，不日而成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1152693_comment'></div>云锸募农隙之民，风斤得艺成之匠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1152693_comment'></div>朱扉洞呀于广陌，绀殿崛起于中天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1152693_comment'></div>榱桷交持，见阴虬之腾倚；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1152693_comment'></div>觚棱四注，状名翚之翰飞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1152693_comment'></div>绘素彰施，模晬容而克肖；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1152693_comment'></div>吉蠲享献，表明德之惟馨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1152693_comment'></div>空歌洞章，萧寥乎旦暮；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1152693_comment'></div>飙轮欻驾，出入于虚无。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1152693_comment'></div>固以昭戬谷于圣神，誇壮丽于方国，契宸心于妙有，跻氓俗于无何。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1152693_comment'></div>行将追七十二君，告成功于日观；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1152693_comment'></div>享万八千岁，比圣历于天皇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1152693_comment'></div>玄同至真，永锡难老，如斯而已矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1152693_comment'></div>秋八月，新宫成，主者上言，愿志能事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1152693_comment'></div>大君有命，允属下臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1152693_comment'></div>臣学古非优，闻道素浅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1152693_comment'></div>草宽大之诏，无东里润色之才；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1152693_comment'></div>谈恍愡之宗，增吾党狂简之愧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1152693_comment'></div>踯躅燥吻，谨为之铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1152693_comment'></div>其铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_97_1152693'>至哉玄元，权舆太极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1152693_comment'></div>象帝之先，昧者奚觌？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1152693_comment'></div>矫矫伯阳，自天生德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1152693_comment'></div>其道犹龙，人靡能测。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1152693_comment'></div>厥初诞祥，时惟厉乡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1152693_comment'></div>领垂缟发，室照神光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1152693_comment'></div>蹈十把五，舌舑而长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1152693_comment'></div>井泉涌脉，星精耀芒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1152693_comment'></div>集灵之址，玄祠崛起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1152693_comment'></div>桧亦手植，树曾亲指。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1152693_comment'></div>圣母遗阡，右环涡水。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1152693_comment'></div>福地旁连，清都对峙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1152693_comment'></div>瓜瓞其昌，锡羡于唐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1152693_comment'></div>宝册追谥，云篆龙章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1152693_comment'></div>金阙易号，丹台绛房。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1152693_comment'></div>明灵如存，祀典不忘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1152693_comment'></div>帝临赤县，乘正御辩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1152693_comment'></div>致恭神祈，大庇黎献。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1152693_comment'></div>德馨流闻，沼毛登荐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1152693_comment'></div>鬼有所归，民亦不倦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1152693_comment'></div>帝居紫宸，味道全真。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1152693_comment'></div>格天在宥，易俗还淳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1152693_comment'></div>阴阳大顺，关石和钧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1152693_comment'></div>亮采时叙，辉光日新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1152693_comment'></div>乃眷东顾，钦崇教父。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1152693_comment'></div>定之方中，增修祠宇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1152693_comment'></div>閒馆相望，飞軿攸驻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1152693_comment'></div>日薄星回，池平树古。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1152693_comment'></div>申命中人，王言如纶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1152693_comment'></div>鸠工底法，即旧谋新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1152693_comment'></div>三时之隙，百日之勤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1152693_comment'></div>恍若神化，以栖灵真。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1152693_comment'></div>瞰鲜原兮靡迤，面皇州兮密迩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1152693_comment'></div>气蓊蔚兮上腾，波奫沦兮东委。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1152693_comment'></div>唯列仙之殊庭，干青霄兮特起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1152693_comment'></div>竦金阁兮崔嵬，荐兰蒸兮裴回。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1152693_comment'></div>缄紫箓兮难见，秘灵符兮不开。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1152693_comment'></div>伊九天之神母，御琼轮兮下来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1152693_comment'></div>祝圣人兮富寿，延宝历兮京垓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1152693_comment'></div>又何必迎年之馆兮，通天之台！</div><div id='poem_sentence_136_1152693_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_129432' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_129432' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/129432?labeling=true' target='_blank'>酬秘阁黄少卿因见所作洞霄宫碑且有题记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1003年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_129432")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_129432_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_129432'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_129432'>谯郡增严李母祠，神龟矫首负金碑。<div id='poem_sentence_0_129432_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_129432'>豆萁已乏不休思，齑臼兼无绝妙辞。<div id='poem_sentence_1_129432_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_129432'>翠琰雄文惭内史<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>，黄庭美翰枉羲之<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：翰林裴待诏奉敕书。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_2_129432_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_129432'>蓬丘丽句偏相许，胜得山龙衮服披。<div id='poem_sentence_3_129432_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_129432'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_129432_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_129432'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_2_129432_0'>⑴ 自注：隋内史薛道衡有《老君祠庭碑》。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_129432_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1003&endYear=1003')">1003年12？</a>　十二月或稍前，为钱若水撰墓志铭。作品：宋故推诚保德翊戴功臣邓州管内观察使金紫光禄大夫检校司空兼御史大夫上柱国长城郡开国公食邑二千四百户食实封四百户赠户部尚书钱公墓志铭。<div id='poem_1152702' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152702' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152702?labeling=true' target='_blank'>宋故推诚保德翊戴功臣邓州管内观察使金紫光禄大夫检校司空兼御史大夫上柱国长城郡开国公食邑二千四百户食实封四百户赠户部尚书钱公墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1003年12？）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152702")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152702_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152702'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152702'>咸平六年秋七月，诏邓州观察使、并代等州经略使长城公归京师，疾故也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152702_comment'></div>上开宣室，御武帐，延登前席，劳问数四。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152702_comment'></div>以公美疹初复，未任朝谒，赐告就第，俾之颐养。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152702_comment'></div>汔九月，勿药有喜，入谒未央宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152702_comment'></div>自是五鼓登车，晨趋无废；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152702_comment'></div>三杯退食，常膳载加。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152702_comment'></div>朝野之人，室家相庆，喜良臣之获祐，而斯文之未丧也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152702_comment'></div>十月戊寅，宿戒知友，会竺乾之宇，为桑门之馔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1152702_comment'></div>与开士辈，谈苦空，赞真谛，俄起更衣，偃然就枕，若假寐焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1152702_comment'></div>少顷视之，乃风眩暴作，如大醉状。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1152702_comment'></div>肩舁归第，是夕以不起闻，享年四十有四。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1152702_comment'></div>上临轩震悼，遣使吊问。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1152702_comment'></div>法赙之数，有加常等；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1152702_comment'></div>窀穸之事，悉从官给。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1152702_comment'></div>翌日，诏赠户部尚书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1152702_comment'></div>天子以公母夫人在喜惧之年，有羸老之疾，不克终堂之养，实深挤壑之痛，特命中贵人面赐白金三十觔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1152702_comment'></div>礼极哀荣，恩沾存殁，君臣之际，斯为至矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1152702_comment'></div>公讳若水，字淡成，河南新安人，盖凌烟功臣、巢国公九陇之后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1152702_comment'></div>世胄阀阅，谱牒存焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1152702_comment'></div>赠太子太保萼，追封琅琊郡太夫人王氏，曾祖、妣也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1152702_comment'></div>赠太子太傅柔，追封清河郡太夫人丁氏，祖、妣也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1152702_comment'></div>尚书司门员外郎、赠太子太师文敏，烈考也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1152702_comment'></div>往者，公参掌万机，追荣三代，始赠孤卿，再跻极品，至于延赏之命，乃尉令伯之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1152702_comment'></div>盖由夫锡羡贻谋，重世始大，臧孙于焉有后，太丘以之无惭者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1152702_comment'></div>公始在孩稚，颖悟不群，爰自青衿，即齿乡校，开卷成诵，发言有章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1152702_comment'></div>才十岁，能属文；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1152702_comment'></div>逮志学之年，已博涉六艺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1152702_comment'></div>方领矩步，比肩诸生，而符采超迈，襟怀散朗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1152702_comment'></div>山庭月角，盖有公侯之相；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1152702_comment'></div>琼树瑶林，自是风尘外物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1152702_comment'></div>华山陈抟一见公，以为有仙风道骨，名在丹台紫府中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1152702_comment'></div>柏阁僧宗裔者，有人伦之鉴，独识公于侪辈，且云：「斯人者，异日登金门，上玉堂，升赤霄，捧白日矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1152702_comment'></div>太平兴国七年，诏郡国贡士，河南太守以公首荐于贤能之书，时才弱冠，会有期功之丧，不克随计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1152702_comment'></div>再上，登甲科，解褐同州观察推官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1152702_comment'></div>专以经术，缘饰吏事，至有邻郡之民，滞讼未决，不远千里，来求片言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1152702_comment'></div>时先太师掌内帑于西都，仓卒捐馆，公见星而往，指景悼生，泣血倚庐，柴毁骨立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1152702_comment'></div>左冯之人，相与列状太守，且云：「失贤从事，民将畴依」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1152702_comment'></div>升闻于天，特俾权夺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1152702_comment'></div>公墨缞而赞幕画，心丧以毕礼经，郡政倚成，氓颂尤塞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1152702_comment'></div>今三司使、夏官侍郎上谷公，时任枢密学士、领选部，方与天子论思帷幄之中，进退天下之士，而品藻人物，讲求茂异，孜孜慰笃，唯恐不及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1152702_comment'></div>当是时，公及太原王扶，颍川陈充、同郡钱熙，皆为外诸侯宾属，即抗章以闻，咸传召归阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1152702_comment'></div>天子命丞相府召试，以公文最高，超拜秘书丞、直史馆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1152702_comment'></div>中谢日，面赐绯衣银鱼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1152702_comment'></div>自扶而下，只除殿中丞，不得与公比。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1152702_comment'></div>明年，拜右正言、知制诰，与今给事中柴公成务、吕公祐之、谏议冯公起、参知政事王公旦，同制并命焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1152702_comment'></div>淳化三年，郡国贡士几二万人，贡举以来，莫斯为盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1152702_comment'></div>天子诏公同掌文柄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1152702_comment'></div>数月，又命案行平凉、五原等郡，公乘驿至塞下，尽得其利病。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1152702_comment'></div>归奏于青琐中，画地聚米，如指斯掌，天子嘉叹，且谕以登用之意，公辞以身被逢掖，业在黄卷，得司诰命，为词臣足矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1152702_comment'></div>天子乃召公入翰林为学士，自屯田员外郎迁职方，仍赐三品服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1152702_comment'></div>审官辩论人材，周太宰之任，银台出纳王命，汉尚书之职，又诏公兼总二司焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1152702_comment'></div>至道元年春正月，命公为右谏议大夫、同知枢密院事，进阶朝散，赐勋柱国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1152702_comment'></div>枢衡之任，机务在焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1152702_comment'></div>自唐朝以来，皆二府兼领；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1152702_comment'></div>逮朱梁之后，与三事抗衡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1152702_comment'></div>至若赤白之囊，晓传边奏，輶轩之使，夕发兵符，承密旨于禁中，授神算于阃外，丞相有所不闻也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1152702_comment'></div>天子以公忠肃明允，温恭笃类，付以是任，一二咨之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1152702_comment'></div>未几，太宗上仙，圣皇绍统，擢拜金紫光禄大夫、尚书工部侍郎，进封长城郡侯，策勋上柱国，馀如故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1152702_comment'></div>上以公顾命大臣，股肱良弼，虚怀延纳，垂拱仰成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1152702_comment'></div>公亦夙夜在公，憔悴事国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1152702_comment'></div>小大之务，思竭其才而致其身；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1152702_comment'></div>谟猷之言，必沃乎心而逆乎耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1152702_comment'></div>穆清体貌，曾靡达颜；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1152702_comment'></div>私庭休沐，不遑调膳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1152702_comment'></div>一日，乘清閒之宴，面陈至诚，直以圣朝之日长，高堂之齿暮，愿得䌽衣膝下，以奉其欢心，上敦谕再三，不俞其请；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1152702_comment'></div>公两奉奏牍，确乎不拔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1152702_comment'></div>上将欲崇进其秩，公顿首固辞，即以本官罢机务，充集贤院学士、判院事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1152702_comment'></div>俄受诏修永熙国书，公即引给事中柴公成务、侍御史南阳宗度、秘阁校理濮阳吴淑，及亿亦在选中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1152702_comment'></div>曾未期年，书成奏御，既终乙夜之览，爰备名山之藏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1152702_comment'></div>上又以太祖皇帝十七年中，经营四方，削平海内，规模宏远，功德茂盛，当时史臣，殊为简略，又命公举尔所知，再加论次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1152702_comment'></div>公辞不获免，乃奏故刑部郎中、知制诰王公禹偁，今翰林学士梁公颢，知制诰李公宗谔，赵公安仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1152702_comment'></div>才及周星，俄已绝笔，弥缝阙漏，号为详备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1152702_comment'></div>两朝大典，出于公手，百代而下，垂于信书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1152702_comment'></div>俄掌吏部三铨兼秋曹案谳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1152702_comment'></div>会鸣镝入寇，大辂亲征，公扈从钩陈，驻跸全魏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1152702_comment'></div>或爟火传警，羽檄交驰，天骄举南牧之师，云台有未决之议，上必遣亲近，咨其计策，给以笔札，受其条对。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1152702_comment'></div>六骡宵遁，万乘天旋，命公权开封府事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1152702_comment'></div>邺都缺帅，北顾是忧，命公知天雄军府兼兵马部署。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1152702_comment'></div>言事者以上郡之地，控扼党项，宜修复城隍，大聚兵谷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1152702_comment'></div>朝廷惑之，发卒万人，赢粮深入，因举夫版筑之役，而谋夫盈廷，利害蜂起，上未能决。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1152702_comment'></div>适公自魏乘驿会师于离石，以幄幕九张，兵车百乘，意决野宿，凡五日造废垒焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1152702_comment'></div>公据鞍少选，当机立断，辄罢其役。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1152702_comment'></div>飞章以闻，宸襟洞开，疑谋冰释。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1152702_comment'></div>因诣阙而白其状，上嘉纳慰劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1152702_comment'></div>适属亲试贡士，命近臣考甲乙科第，俾公预焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1152702_comment'></div>东堂校文，时推精识；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1152702_comment'></div>西清赐对，帝善其言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1152702_comment'></div>数日，又命公抚巡陕西缘边诸郡，且以便宜从事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1152702_comment'></div>凡七旬复命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1152702_comment'></div>上谓公曰：「《天官书》：上将、次将，位在文昌宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1152702_comment'></div>汉宣亦云：『边境有事，左右之臣皆将帅也』。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1152702_comment'></div>文武是宪，内外迭处，亦何常之有」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1152702_comment'></div>公不能谕上旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1152702_comment'></div>翌日，有获下之拜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1152702_comment'></div>上以太原西北劲兵处，控带雁门、云中，匈奴之所走集，思得贤帅，付以师律，即命公兼并代等州经略等使、判并州事，尽付诸将，倚为长城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1152702_comment'></div>又下诏案行边塞，周视亭障。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1152702_comment'></div>并土严凝，穷冬尤剧，擐甲胄者或至堕指，袭狐貉者仅如怀冰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1152702_comment'></div>公夙驾载驰，蒙犯霜霰，且多饮醇酒，以御寒气，因伤肺得疾，颇施针砭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1152702_comment'></div>忽伤溃于胫，流血石馀，四体薾然，仅存微喘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1152702_comment'></div>上遣中使、太医，冠盖相望，又别赐手札，丁宁欸密。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1152702_comment'></div>初蒙药石之效，未任军旅之事，适会府州有所经度，公将力疾而往，上亟令止之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1152702_comment'></div>虽漳滨有瘳，而卫幕多故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1152702_comment'></div>伐谋制胜，固可以坐筹；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1152702_comment'></div>破虏鏖兵，亦难于卧护。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1152702_comment'></div>乃降优诏，俾之来朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1152702_comment'></div>方将验上池之十全，延明庭之三接，出驱六纛，授鈇钺以专征；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1152702_comment'></div>入序九功，登岩廊而论道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1152702_comment'></div>为国方、召，播美于声诗；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1152702_comment'></div>致君尧、舜，跻俗于仁寿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1152702_comment'></div>如何奄忽，乃至云亡！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1152702_comment'></div>里巷辍舂，搢绅挥涕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1152702_comment'></div>管公明不及嫁娶，遗恨终天；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1152702_comment'></div>张元伯顿隔死生，绪言在耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1152702_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1152702_comment'></div>即以其年十二月壬申，归葬于河南府新安县暖泉乡，祔于先茔，礼也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1152702_comment'></div>公历阶至金紫，策勋上柱国，视秩水土，兼职风宪，三进爵为郡公，真食至四百户，功臣之号，凡三加焉，禄位官封，亦云盛矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1152702_comment'></div>一子延年，秘书省正字，始七岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1152702_comment'></div>虽在稚齿，了无童心，擗踊哀摧，啜泣孺慕，出于天性，殆过成人，藐是遗孤，庶乎有后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1152702_comment'></div>公母范阳卢氏，累封濮阳郡太夫人；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1152702_comment'></div>夫人荥阳郑氏，故殿中丞处升之女，封北海郡夫人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1152702_comment'></div>皆以公贵也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1152702_comment'></div>兄若讷、若虚，早亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1152702_comment'></div>若愚今任大理评事，通判台州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1152702_comment'></div>公于昆弟中为最幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1152702_comment'></div>虢州虢略簿若冲，从父弟也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1152702_comment'></div>大理评事维周，前河南永城簿智周，兄之子也，皆由公而成立焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1152702_comment'></div>公眉宇秀拔，宝箓标映。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1152702_comment'></div>体二邻几，识探《系》《象》；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1152702_comment'></div>下学上达，文成雅诰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1152702_comment'></div>克己恕物，殆过放麑之仁；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1152702_comment'></div>虚受兼容，乃有涵牛之量。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1152702_comment'></div>善谈名理，听之者更仆忘疲，多识典故，扣之者撞钟辄应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1152702_comment'></div>品题人物，汝南之子将；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1152702_comment'></div>坐镇雅俗，东晋之安石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1152702_comment'></div>挹其仪表者，若披云雾；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1152702_comment'></div>与之游从者，如薰椒兰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1152702_comment'></div>盖所谓钻之弥坚，仰之弥高，澄之不清，挠之不浊者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1152702_comment'></div>公在先朝时，为北门学士，与故刑部侍郎张公洎同日侍上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1152702_comment'></div>天子喜金鳌之得贤，咏《嘉鱼》而申美，特诏宣奏国乐，鱼龙杂戏，近臣咸预，式宴尽欢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1152702_comment'></div>时方隅未宁，斥候屡警，在于内署，实司密令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1152702_comment'></div>每天子临便坐，决启奏，军书手诏，急于星火。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1152702_comment'></div>斧扆之侧，授简立成，曲尽事机，不加点窜，秉笔者推之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1152702_comment'></div>掌审官之柄也，如良工斲材，轮辕咸适其用，虽小人怀土，胡越不违其情，罢斥蒙于安全，淑慝以之区别。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1152702_comment'></div>居中枢之地也，罄竭谟谋，参决机务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1152702_comment'></div>守正持重，曾不将迎；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1152702_comment'></div>忧边思职，屡蒙惠问。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1152702_comment'></div>属衅起益部，盗据坤维，絓汤网者居多，皆《吕刑》之不宥，赖公全活，实繁有徒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1152702_comment'></div>且以慎密自持，弥纶无迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_147_1152702_comment'></div>诡词而出，虽温树以不言；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_148_1152702_comment'></div>阴德岂诬，在里门而终大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_149_1152702_comment'></div>尝以为百年之计，莫如树人，三代之昌，皆由得士，姑务引翼，以答恩遇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_150_1152702_comment'></div>祁司马之举善，外不避雠；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_151_1152702_comment'></div>郑当时之荐贤，言之有味。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_152_1152702_comment'></div>又以难进易退，儒者之行，既得患失，鄙夫所为，乃辞禄枢府，退就书殿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_153_1152702_comment'></div>士林歌颂，堆案盈几；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_154_1152702_comment'></div>驰竞顿息，风俗归厚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_155_1152702_comment'></div>既而述唐、虞之二典，极班、马之三长，西狩终篇，南箕起谤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_156_1152702_comment'></div>或以不署宰衡，是为专美；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_157_1152702_comment'></div>或以倒置昭穆，于焉渎宗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_158_1152702_comment'></div>公讨寻故实，援引诏令，廷诤数四，策书乃定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_159_1152702_comment'></div>郡邪侧目，正人增气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_160_1152702_comment'></div>领选部也，山公启事，多所荐陈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_161_1152702_comment'></div>掌秋曹也，不疑平反，号为宽大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_162_1152702_comment'></div>权莅京毂也，狱囚数百，一旦决之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_163_1152702_comment'></div>桴鼓稀鸣，钩距靡设，虽曰浩穰，殆臻清静。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_164_1152702_comment'></div>出抚魏郡，其政亦同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_165_1152702_comment'></div>乃有元戎贵侯，高牙大旆，提七校之师；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_166_1152702_comment'></div>中人内侍，银珰左貂，从九天而降。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_167_1152702_comment'></div>公卮酒大胾，率以交欢；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_168_1152702_comment'></div>郊劳饮饯，曾无违礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_169_1152702_comment'></div>奉缗靡给，私帑屡空，坦然放怀，不以屑虑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_170_1152702_comment'></div>及罢上郡之役，而晋民息肩；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_171_1152702_comment'></div>握大卤之兵，而胡驺屏迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_172_1152702_comment'></div>乃至易箦而没，家无馀财，行路之间，人皆流涕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_173_1152702_comment'></div>非诚信素著，譬李广之不言，仁惠见思，同子产之遗爱者，安能及是哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_174_1152702_comment'></div>公有德有言，多材多艺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_175_1152702_comment'></div>精覈数术，善评书画。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_176_1152702_comment'></div>雅好班固《汉书》，常日读一卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_177_1152702_comment'></div>周急好施，劳谦善下，多所折券，未常治产。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_178_1152702_comment'></div>收养孤幼，侔郈成分宅之仁；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_179_1152702_comment'></div>协比亲戚，掩游吉亢宗之说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_180_1152702_comment'></div>勤接士类，皆虚往而实归；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_181_1152702_comment'></div>善与人交，必相先而莫逆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_182_1152702_comment'></div>荐引后进，有知人之明；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_183_1152702_comment'></div>购求坠简，侔秘书之副。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_184_1152702_comment'></div>每燕居私第，角巾东道，叩虚课寂，味兹玄关。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_185_1152702_comment'></div>近年深信佛乘，雅习禅观，隐几终日，陶然自得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_186_1152702_comment'></div>归全之明日，上遣近侍求两朝策书遗草，若冲等搜于巾箱，尽以进御，且述素志，愿得薄葬，免于劳民，上亦允其请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_187_1152702_comment'></div>茂陵遗札，幸天子之见求；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_188_1152702_comment'></div>京兆新阡，固乡人之不犯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_189_1152702_comment'></div>族子光禄寺丞易，卓荦稽古，时之闻人，集公生平文章为二十卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_190_1152702_comment'></div>某辱公之顾，为日斯久，道同气合，心照神交。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_191_1152702_comment'></div>亲奉斋终，幸无怛化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_192_1152702_comment'></div>知音逝矣，空绝伯牙之弦；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_193_1152702_comment'></div>冢树怆然，谁表延陵之墓？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_194_1152702_comment'></div>含酸陨涕，且为之铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_195_1152702_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_196_1152702'>明堂肇基，众材具施。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_196_1152702_comment'></div>如何栋梁，中道而隳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_197_1152702_comment'></div>元首眷怀，同体是宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_198_1152702_comment'></div>吁嗟股肱，一旦而亏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_199_1152702_comment'></div>腹背何益，铩兹六翮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_200_1152702_comment'></div>珷玞奚为，丧我垂棘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_201_1152702_comment'></div>人失司南，国亡遗直。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_202_1152702_comment'></div>空馀话言，布在方策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_203_1152702_comment'></div>嗟太山兮其颓，悲玉树兮将埋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_204_1152702_comment'></div>怅浮生兮朝露，閟英魂兮夜台。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_205_1152702_comment'></div>伊南州之高土兮临紫陌，启新阡兮从旧域。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_206_1152702_comment'></div>严封树兮禁樵苏，志泉扃兮刻金石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_207_1152702_comment'></div>谅西土之耆老兮，盍树碑以表德<span class='inlineComment2'>（《武夷新集》卷九。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_208_1152702_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_209_1152702'>宝：原阙，据明本补。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_209_1152702_comment'></div>又，「□箓」，库本作「丰神」。</div><div id='poem_sentence_210_1152702_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1003&endYear=1003')">1003年</a>　去岁十二月，与陈恕试常举人，得刘筠等七人校龙图阁藏书，逾年而毕；至是，授筠秘阁校理。亿以启贺之。作品：贺刘校理启。<div id='poem_1152626' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152626' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152626?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺刘校理启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1003年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152626")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152626_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152626'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152626'>册府藏书，是居清禁；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152626_comment'></div>公车待诏，必择名流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152626_comment'></div>某官擢秀丘园，策名场屋，自牵丝而筮仕，颇栖棘以兴嗟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152626_comment'></div>属天官会课之初，乃仙馆抡材之际，聿从明识，克副精求。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152626_comment'></div>既彰汗简之勤，果拜丝纶之宠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152626_comment'></div>佐九卿于棘寺，聊示陟明；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152626_comment'></div>校四部于蓬山，更资稽古。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152626_comment'></div>方隆乃眷，岂测怒飞！</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1152626_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1003&endYear=1003')">1003年</a>　岁暮，王承衍出知凤翔府，有诗送之。作品：王尚食知凤翔。<div id='poem_129042' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_129042' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/129042?labeling=true' target='_blank'>王尚食知凤翔<span class='inlineComment2'>（曾领延安）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1003年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_129042")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_129042_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_129042'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_129042'>露冕分忧辍近班，朝阳鸣凤古岐山。<div id='poem_sentence_0_129042_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_129042'>三刀吉梦频为郡，驷马高车又出关。<div id='poem_sentence_1_129042_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_129042'>宴客羽觞那有算，题诗䌽笔莫教閒。<div id='poem_sentence_2_129042_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_129042'>将坛义府平生事，早立边功振凯还。<div id='poem_sentence_3_129042_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_129042'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_129042_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1003&endYear=1003')">1003年</a>　岁暮，僓、伸二弟归乡，有诗送之。作品：弟僓归乡。弟伸归乡。<div id='poem_129137' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_129137' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/129137?labeling=true' target='_blank'>弟僓归乡</a><span class='authorDate'>（1003年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_129137")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_129137_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_129137'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_129137'>客儿诗思掩春塘，杖策来观上国光。<div id='poem_sentence_0_129137_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_129137'>举白万钱酤酒饮，杀青千卷买书藏。<div id='poem_sentence_1_129137_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_129137'>梁园绿筱将攲<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>雪，楚岸苍葭已变霜。<div id='poem_sentence_2_129137_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_129137'>跃马还家那隔岁，预应乾鹊报高堂。<div id='poem_sentence_3_129137_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_129137'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_129137_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_129137'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_2_129137_0'>⑴ 原作歌，据祝刻本改</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_129137_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_129135' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_129135' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/129135?labeling=true' target='_blank'>弟伸归乡</a><span class='authorDate'>（1003年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_129135")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_129135_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_129135'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_129135'>泽国思归咏采兰，束书携剑出长安。<div id='poem_sentence_0_129135_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_129135'>天涯朝暮倚门望，岁晏风霜行路难。<div id='poem_sentence_1_129135_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_129135'>闽岭夕岚乡树老，楚江寒浪客衣单。<div id='poem_sentence_2_129135_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_129135'>岩前旧勒移文处，到日重须拂藓看。<div id='poem_sentence_3_129135_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_129135'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_129135_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1003&endYear=1003')">1003年</a>　有诗送王嗣宗出知并州。作品：并州王谏议。<div id='poem_129074' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_129074' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/129074?labeling=true' target='_blank'>并州王谏议</a><span class='authorDate'>（1003年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_129074")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_129074_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_129074'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_129074'>锁闱聊辍皂囊封，昼锦还乡意气雄。<div id='poem_sentence_0_129074_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_129074'>别墅挥金延父老，近郊骑竹见儿童。<div id='poem_sentence_1_129074_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_129074'>蒲卢善化终成政，蟋蟀深思未变风。<div id='poem_sentence_2_129074_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_129074'>更待出师平黠虏，戎衣献捷大明宫。<div id='poem_sentence_3_129074_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_129074'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_129074_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1003&endYear=1003')">1003年</a>　在知制诰任，自云岁久受谤，见之于文辞。作品：送倚序。<div id='poem_1152653' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152653' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152653?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送倚序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1003年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript:
