ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152653")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152653_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152653'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152653'>我之先，繇永嘉之难，避地江外，占数于上饶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152653_comment'></div>及刘展之寇，又迁于闽粤，治产殖货，以财雄于建安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152653_comment'></div>世为彊宗，高上武力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152653_comment'></div>唐室之季，乱离云瘼，礼乐征伐，不出本朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152653_comment'></div>无种而起为王侯，称兵而分据州郡，故王氏奄有无诸六郡之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152653_comment'></div>盘牙相错，莫非勍敌；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152653_comment'></div>候望走集，悉严兵备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152653_comment'></div>故我内外家世，皆服缦胡而冠武弁，总舆师而提尺籍，辎軿鼓吹，盛于一方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1152653_comment'></div>而群从叔季，凭藉世资，习尚豪举，竞养声利，争为节侠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1152653_comment'></div>唯玉山府君劳谦降志，刻苦读书，好学之名，闻于州里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1152653_comment'></div>以孝廉射策，委质江吴；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1152653_comment'></div>以儒雅从政，仕至宰邑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1152653_comment'></div>无何，黄旗运尽，琴堂秩满，考槃故里，启手归全。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1152653_comment'></div>太常府君博涉艺文，尤深《左氏》，终鲜兄弟，不遑充赋，未及中寿，遘兹大祸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1152653_comment'></div>家无担石之蓄，门无强近之亲，藐视诸孤，朝不谋夕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1152653_comment'></div>我是时以一命为兰台正字，尚未及志学之岁，遽罹悯凶，将就死灭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1152653_comment'></div>尔曹皆丱角稚齿，俱未成人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1152653_comment'></div>田园污莱，裘葛不具。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1152653_comment'></div>堂构颓替，弓冶渐微。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1152653_comment'></div>既泣血终丧，即割慈游宦，艰难险阻，备尝之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1152653_comment'></div>既而索米都下，薄游外郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1152653_comment'></div>又三岁，以文三十篇献于公车，始得为太常奉礼，且有中旨，阅书于秘府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1152653_comment'></div>日享公膳，月受俸缗，未能亢宗，财足糊口。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1152653_comment'></div>而太夫人与汝曹，仰给薄产，终岁食贫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1152653_comment'></div>我又智效一官，相去万里，晨夕引领，不觉涕之无从也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1152653_comment'></div>我亦进德励行，脩词聚学，又得册府秘书，夙夜研习，曾未期月，颇有文章出于人间，为前辈所许。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1152653_comment'></div>又频诣金马门献赋颂，天子益知名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1152653_comment'></div>凡再岁间，一召试内署，一应制行在，得光禄丞，赐进士第，复受诏直集贤院。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1152653_comment'></div>星律载周，宠光举集，稽古之力，岂诬也哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1152653_comment'></div>得禄既丰，思养弥切。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1152653_comment'></div>削牍为奏，赐告言归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1152653_comment'></div>自建安扶迎太夫人，并挈汝曹，尽室西上，侨寓辇毂，迨兹岁星一周于天矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1152653_comment'></div>而我以不肖之质，中人之才，黄屋过听，擢司雅诰，敢不摩揣铅钝，励精夙夜，期有以润色帝载，与三代同气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1152653_comment'></div>奈何力不逮心，位过其量，岁祀逾久，官谤嚣然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1152653_comment'></div>不能上封自劾，幞被引退，乃犹束带就列，俛首取容，碌碌于荐绅间，亦颜之厚矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1152653_comment'></div>今年，汝举进士，有司荐名，我时侍从穆清，亲逢旦暮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1152653_comment'></div>天子又赐汝高第，自丙科而升乙科。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1152653_comment'></div>俄顷之间，恩奖蕃缛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1152653_comment'></div>汝之仲兄及季弟，比年来圣人诞生之辰，延赏近侍，并得解褐，试秩蓬丘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1152653_comment'></div>每朔旦列拜膝下，私门嘉庆，岁时伏腊，捧觞上寿，怀黄佩玉，趋走左右，固足以慰太夫人之心；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1152653_comment'></div>而伯仲森列，门无白丁，亦足以为乡曲之美谈，交游之光宠也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1152653_comment'></div>今汝由天官调补，掌簿四明，期以来年，往代其任，且将归省松槚，盘桓里闾，俟春夏之交，乃莅厥职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1152653_comment'></div>汝当念为士之道，以仁义是务，而閒宴不可忘；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1152653_comment'></div>为吏之方，以法令是师，而资材不可彊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1152653_comment'></div>事上贵乎恭，而慎于谄；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1152653_comment'></div>临下尚乎简，而惩其违。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1152653_comment'></div>至于淳素之风，清白之训，盖我之家法耳，岂复郑重而言之哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1152653_comment'></div>若乃博约文史，切磋道术，此又朋友之事也，吾何与焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1152653_comment'></div>汝之归，吾党之人有问我者，为言受恩寖深，莅官无状，如卫鹤之有禄位，若社鼷之载车马，悲愁忧畏，不遑宁处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1152653_comment'></div>幸天子一旦澄汰流品，考覈名实，不能者止，奉身而退，固愿返初服，奉版舆，从诸乡先生优游以卒岁也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_49_1152653_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1003&endYear=1003')">1003年</a>　李宗讷卒，作挽歌四首。作品：故比部李郎中挽歌四首。<div id='poem_129202' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_129202' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/129202?labeling=true' target='_blank'>故比部李郎中挽歌四首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1003年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_129202")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_129202_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_129202'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_129202'>陇右华宗贵，朝端懿范存。<div id='poem_sentence_0_129202_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_129202'>哀乌光列宿，驷马庆高门。<div id='poem_sentence_1_129202_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_129202'>谒帝承明署，娱宾金谷园。<div id='poem_sentence_2_129202_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_129202'>人生忽至此，天道亦难论。<div id='poem_sentence_3_129202_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_129202'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_129202_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_129201' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_129201' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/129201?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1003年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_129201_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_129201'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_129201'>睦族衣无主，传家鼎有铭。<div id='poem_sentence_0_129201_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_129201'>沙堤连里巷，玉树接阶庭。<div id='poem_sentence_1_129201_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_129201'>北海樽常满，西山药不灵。<div id='poem_sentence_2_129201_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_129201'>肯堂归棣萼，含笑入泉扃。<div id='poem_sentence_3_129201_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_129201'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_129201_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_129200' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_129200' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/129200?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1003年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_129200_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_129200'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_129200'>雁序分台阁，春卿有职司。<div id='poem_sentence_0_129200_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_129200'>云屏三殿宴，绵蕝一王仪。<div id='poem_sentence_1_129200_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_129200'>风韵灵和柳，襟怀叔度陂。<div id='poem_sentence_2_129200_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_129200'>善人无复见，执绋泪空垂。<div id='poem_sentence_3_129200_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_129200'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_129200_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_129199' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_129199' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/129199?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其四 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1003年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_129199_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_129199'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_129199'>美疢漳滨卧，营魂东岱归。<div id='poem_sentence_0_129199_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_129199'>故人空渍酒，侍史罢薰衣。<div id='poem_sentence_1_129199_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_129199'>画像留家庙，铭旌出帝畿。<div id='poem_sentence_2_129199_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_129199'>浮生除寿考，享福似君稀。<div id='poem_sentence_3_129199_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_129199'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_129199_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1003&endYear=1003')">1003年</a>　郑国公主出降王贻永，亿代贻庆撰《进财表》，代贻永撰《谢赐宅表》作品：代王氏为公主出降进财表。代驸马王都尉谢赐宅表。<div id='poem_1152468' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152468' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152468?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代王氏为公主出降进财表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1003年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152468")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152468_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152468'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152468'>臣贻庆言：臣弟贻贞，幸以孱微，获叨选尚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152468_comment'></div>单平之族，骤集庆于高门：柔近之辰，冀承荣于筑馆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152468_comment'></div>欲恭陈于厥篚，须仰黩于凝旒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152468_comment'></div>臣某<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>窃以《诗》美王姬，聿称于下嫁，《易》载帝妹，亦重于有归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152468_comment'></div>盖风化之所由，谅古今之共贯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152468_comment'></div>自非阀阅，宁得拟抡？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152468_comment'></div>伏念臣世本文儒，家惟寒素。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152468_comment'></div>寝丘遗业，几至荒芜，扶阳旧封，已嗟废绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1152468_comment'></div>固弓裘之莫续，亦堂构之将隳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1152468_comment'></div>臣与弟贻贞，每励自强，期于克荷，誓不衰于孝谨，庶有奉于蒸尝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1152468_comment'></div>敢谓尊号皇帝陛下察以颛愚，悯其陵替，俾联姻于帝胄，永庇族于天光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1152468_comment'></div>顾孺子之何知，实先臣之不朽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1152468_comment'></div>预长安之戚里，幸会居多；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1152468_comment'></div>开堂邑之山林，荣华斯在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1152468_comment'></div>今者礼当纳币，事等献芹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1152468_comment'></div>载循菲薄之愆，益负凌兢之恳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1152468_comment'></div>黩尊弥甚，获戾是宜<span class='inlineComment2'>（云云）</span>。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1152468_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1152473' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152473' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152473?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代驸马王都尉谢赐宅表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1003年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152473")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152473_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152473'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152473'>臣某言：今月某日，中使某至，奉宣圣旨，赐臣安远门外永宁坊宅一区者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152473_comment'></div>恩宠便蕃，心魂战慄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152473_comment'></div>臣某<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>窃以功宣带砺，方闻赐第之荣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152473_comment'></div>业绍箕裘，乃孚高门之庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152473_comment'></div>如臣者，家承阀阅，性颇颛蒙，早违怙恃之慈，靡及义方之训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152473_comment'></div>每进修而自励，期孝谨之不衰，俄被天光，获参戚里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152473_comment'></div>顾惟荣忝，寔越常伦，敢谓俯降纶言，特颁甲第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152473_comment'></div>栋宇式彰于轮奂，堂皇更极于高明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1152473_comment'></div>渥泽所加，方增华于鲁馆；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1152473_comment'></div>孱微何幸，谬席宠于沁园。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1152473_comment'></div>愈怀冰谷之忧，曷报乾坤之施？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1152473_comment'></div>臣无任感天荷圣激切屏营之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1152473_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1003&endYear=1003')">1003年</a>　李虚己荐晏殊于亿，亿延之，使闻于世。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1003&endYear=1003')">1003年</a>　约于本年，有诗送舒雅出知舒州。作品：秘阁舒职方知舒州。<div id='poem_129252' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_129252' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/129252?labeling=true' target='_blank'>秘阁舒职方知舒州</a><span class='authorDate'>（1003年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_129252")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_129252_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_129252'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_129252'>西昆册府控千庐，铅笔多年校鲁鱼。<div id='poem_sentence_0_129252_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_129252'>厌享双鸡太官膳，贪乘五马使君车。<div id='poem_sentence_1_129252_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_129252'>明光画省辞青琐，天柱仙坛访紫书。<div id='poem_sentence_2_129252_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_129252'>只恐政成抛印绶，携家深入白云居。<div id='poem_sentence_3_129252_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_129252'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_129252_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1004&endYear=1004')">1004年1月</a>　百丈大智禅师创立禅宗清规为《古清规》，正月，亿为之序。作品：古清规序。<div id='poem_1152668' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152668' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152668?labeling=true' target='_blank'>古清规序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1004年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152668")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152668_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152668'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152668'>百丈大智禅师以禅宗肇自少室，至曹溪以来，多居律寺，虽列别院，然于说法住持，未合规度，故常尔介怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152668_comment'></div>乃曰：「佛祖之道，欲诞布化元，冀来际不泯者，岂当与诸部阿笈摩教为随行耶」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152668_comment'></div>或曰：「《瑜珈论》、《璎珞经》是大乘戒律，胡不依随哉」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152668_comment'></div>师曰：「吾所宗，非局大小乘，非局大小乘，当博约折中，设于制范，务其宜也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152668_comment'></div>于是创意，别立禅居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152668_comment'></div>凡具道眼者，有可尊之德，号曰「长老」，如西域道高腊长呼「须菩提」等之谓也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152668_comment'></div>即为化主，即处于方丈，同净名之室，非私寝之室也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152668_comment'></div>不立佛殿，唯树法堂者，表佛祖亲嘱受当代为尊也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1152668_comment'></div>所裒学众无多少，无高下，尽入僧堂，依夏次安排。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1152668_comment'></div>设长连床，施椸架挂搭道具。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1152668_comment'></div>卧必斜枕床唇、右胁吉祥睡者，以其坐禅既久，略偃息而已，具四威仪也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1152668_comment'></div>除入室请益，任学者勤怠，或上或下，不拘常准。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1152668_comment'></div>其阖院大众朝参夕聚，长老上堂升座，主事、徒众雁立侧聆，宾主问酬激扬宗要者，示依法而住也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1152668_comment'></div>斋粥随宜，一时均遍者，务于节俭，表法食双运也，行普请法，上下均力也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1152668_comment'></div>置十务，谓之寮舍，每用首领一人管多人，营事令各司其局也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1152668_comment'></div>或有假号窃形，混于清众，别致喧挠之事，即当维那检举，抽下本位挂搭，摈令出院者，贵安清众也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1152668_comment'></div>或彼有所犯，即以拄杖杖之，集众烧衣钵道具，遣逐从偏门而出者，示耻辱也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1152668_comment'></div>详此一条，制有四益：一不污清众，生恭信故；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1152668_comment'></div>二不毁僧形，循佛制故；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1152668_comment'></div>三不扰公门，省狱讼故；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1152668_comment'></div>四不泄于外，护宗纲故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1152668_comment'></div>四来同居，圣凡孰办？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1152668_comment'></div>且如来应世，尚有六群之党；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1152668_comment'></div>况今像末，岂得全无？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1152668_comment'></div>但见一僧有过，便雷例讥诮，殊不知轻众坏法，其损甚大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1152668_comment'></div>今禅门若稍无妨害者，宜依百丈丛林规式，量事区分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1152668_comment'></div>且立法防奸，不为贤士，然宁可有格而无犯，不可有犯而无教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1152668_comment'></div>惟大智禅师护法之益，其大矣哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1152668_comment'></div>禅门独行，自此老始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1152668_comment'></div>清规大要，遍示后学，令不忘本也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1152668_comment'></div>其诸轨度，集详备矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1152668_comment'></div>亿幸叨睿旨，删定《传灯》，成书图进，因为序引。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1152668_comment'></div>时景德改元，岁次甲辰，良月吉日书。</div><div id='poem_sentence_32_1152668_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1152668'><span class='label'>按：</span>《百丈清规》卷八，𠐺加藏腾一○。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1152668_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1004&endYear=1004')">1004年2月1日</a>　以家贫，上表乞领郡江左。作品：求解职领郡表。<div id='poem_1152479' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152479' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152479?labeling=true' target='_blank'>求解职领郡表<span class='inlineComment2'>（景德元年二月一日上）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1004年2月1日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152479")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152479_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152479'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152479'>臣某言：臣幸尘近列，获掌命书，既无补于休明，岂合披于诚慊？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152479_comment'></div>盖内怀于危迫，须不避于诛锄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152479_comment'></div>臣某<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢）</span>伏念臣本出寒微，且非茂异，由先朝而筮仕，预秘殿之雠书，叨结绶于士林，久滥巾于册府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152479_comment'></div>幸值崇文广武圣明仁孝皇帝陛下绍隆丕祚，首霈鸿恩，擢践谏垣，骤登闺籍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152479_comment'></div>属刊修于国典，亦陪厕于史官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152479_comment'></div>既终麟笔之功，复遂隼旟之便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152479_comment'></div>洎言归于京阙，方接武于班行，遽蒙慎柬之私，得齿代言之末。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152479_comment'></div>地居禁掖，日奉内朝，官曹所谓于清华，职业唯专于润色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1152479_comment'></div>内顾草茅之贱，已怀负乘之惭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1152479_comment'></div>既积日以弥多，愈循涯而自失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1152479_comment'></div>然念有犯无隐，臣诚由是上通；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1152479_comment'></div>居高听卑，天道于焉下济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1152479_comment'></div>臣所以扣帝阍而自述，冒萧斧以无疑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1152479_comment'></div>盖念臣扶侍慈亲，提挈贱累，族寓辇毂三十口有馀，离去乡关四千里而远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1152479_comment'></div>只请本官之俸给，别无负郭之生涯，衣食所资，尽出于是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1152479_comment'></div>乃至庭闱之旨甘或阙，晨夕之饘粥屡空。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1152479_comment'></div>臣母见臣窘急栖迟，动静嗟悯，欲将诸弟南归故乡，丐索亲姻，庶图存活。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1152479_comment'></div>臣亲弟化，有妻孥数口寄止润州，一房伶俜，都无所托。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1152479_comment'></div>家贫固难于团聚，俸薄不可以分沾，穷饿流离，诚堪轸念。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1152479_comment'></div>臣又有亲弟倚等，见臣资储乏绝，藜藿靡充，且欲客游，违离膝下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1152479_comment'></div>臣母钟爱尤甚，不忍令漂泊道涂，进退徬徨，莫知为计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1152479_comment'></div>臣未尝不拊心太息，危坐端忧，涕泣涟如，方寸乱矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1152479_comment'></div>盖由臣窃代耕之禄，莫能为工为商；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1152479_comment'></div>乏适时之才，以至不堪不可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1152479_comment'></div>侏儒之耕田力作，且不及人；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1152479_comment'></div>子云之篆刻雕虫，终非晓事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1152479_comment'></div>萃兹短拙，以至困穷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1152479_comment'></div>然臣学古入官，出身事主，含毫弄翰，岂甘为腐烂之儒？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1152479_comment'></div>露冕褰帷，所愿作循良之吏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1152479_comment'></div>伏望皇帝陛下矜臣危蹙之恳，察臣激切之心，罢去纶掖之资，假以藩条之任，于苏、湖、常、润等处，令典一州，庶获养亲，兼谐聚族。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1152479_comment'></div>鱼盐稍贱，聊救于食贫；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1152479_comment'></div>水薤是规，终期于报政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1152479_comment'></div>幸免翳桑之困，永衔魏阙之恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1152479_comment'></div>沥血吁天，必期得请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1152479_comment'></div>干冒宸严，臣无任<span class='inlineComment2'>（云云）</span>。</div><div id='poem_sentence_34_1152479_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1004&endYear=1004')">1004年2月</a>　十余日后，再上表陈情，乞解职领郡，适诏知通进银台司，兼门下封驳事，未进。又有状乞兼职加给，亦未上。作品：再乞解职表。陈乞奏状。<div id='poem_1152480' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152480' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152480?labeling=true' target='_blank'>再乞解职表<span class='inlineComment2'>（写毕，有银台之命，因不敢复上。）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1004年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152480")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152480_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152480'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152480'>臣某言：臣近写危诚，备形尺奏，辄冒万死，仰叩九重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152480_comment'></div>沥恳虽达于云天，俟命已逾于旬浃，徒浼盖高之听，未蒙恻隐之仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152480_comment'></div>臣某<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢）</span>窃以国家澄汰品流，登进茂异，至于典掌诰命，步武掖垣，乃推择之所先，盖宦游之最美，礼秩殊厚，班著颇崇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152480_comment'></div>三殿内朝，日趋翔于文陛；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152480_comment'></div>六飞法从，时陪扈于属车。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152480_comment'></div>常瞻咫尺之颜，专裁宽大之诏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152480_comment'></div>此固山东逢掖夙夜祷祠之所求也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152480_comment'></div>如臣出于遐陬，本无长技，得厕从臣之末，获司王者之言，此乃羊服虎皮，鴳披隼翼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1152480_comment'></div>固陋之质，荣幸踰涯，又岂敢厌承明之深严，愿辞侍从之职；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1152480_comment'></div>去长安之全盛，求领卑湿之邦！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1152480_comment'></div>盖桂玉之所煎，恐沟隍之行及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1152480_comment'></div>涸鳞在辙，将悬肆而有期；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1152480_comment'></div>穷猿奔林，谅择木之何暇？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1152480_comment'></div>既堪忧于四壁，亦难事于三缄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1152480_comment'></div>盖念臣职虽词臣，身乃羁客，扶老携幼，去里离邦，良贱相从，三十馀口，衣食所给，并出于臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1152480_comment'></div>且无负郭之田园，固乏满堂之金玉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1152480_comment'></div>凡百经费，只仰俸缗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1152480_comment'></div>至若管库之微，亦有走卒以执御；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1152480_comment'></div>幸从大夫之后，不可徒步而趋朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1152480_comment'></div>又须分钱刀以僦奴，市刍粟而饲马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1152480_comment'></div>用度非一，悉数难周，并出于本官俸钱二十五贯中，更无他给。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1152480_comment'></div>供甘之养多阙，量入之费屡殚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1152480_comment'></div>饘粥糊口之不充，进退触籓之无计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1152480_comment'></div>原宪诚知其非病，介推岂可以不言？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1152480_comment'></div>窃念臣获掌命书，四更年籥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1152480_comment'></div>同列之内，或蒙添给俸钱，乃至四补皇华，将命藩邸，并沾濡润，迭被恩私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1152480_comment'></div>唯臣贫悴绝伦，照临靡及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1152480_comment'></div>臣未尝不内自循省，惕然战兢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1152480_comment'></div>盖由臣蟠木之姿，偶厕皇王之器；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1152480_comment'></div>滥竽之吹，谬参《韶》、《濩》之音。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1152480_comment'></div>才不逮于等侪，宠难希于均及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1152480_comment'></div>然而皇帝陛下已从误听，置在司言，过咎未彰，不欲令其襆被；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1152480_comment'></div>含容至大，又岂忍于置渊？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1152480_comment'></div>所以令臣窃位妨贤，贪荣就列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1152480_comment'></div>汉臣之饿且欲死，难免侏儒之嗤；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1152480_comment'></div>孔徒之病不能兴，敢怀子路之愠？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1152480_comment'></div>行作若敖之馁鬼，徒辱甘泉之从官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1152480_comment'></div>实由臣无寸长之可称，有五短而为累。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1152480_comment'></div>不能辟土殖谷，竭力以事亲；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1152480_comment'></div>反乃束带立朝，素餐而辱国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1152480_comment'></div>致滫瀡之养，莫奉于庭闱；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1152480_comment'></div>期功之亲，将罹于冻馁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1152480_comment'></div>困穷至此，职臣之由。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1152480_comment'></div>臣母将挈婢媪而归故乡，庶图存活；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1152480_comment'></div>臣弟先有妻孥而寄外郡，并绝供须。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1152480_comment'></div>更有亲弟倚等，皆欲游索江淮，舍亲而去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1152480_comment'></div>臣之危迫，何以自安？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1152480_comment'></div>虽前表之罄情，恐至仁之未察，再兹剖露，不避缕烦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1152480_comment'></div>伏望陛下霈曲成之私，矜倒悬之急，尚恕触鳞之罪，未加御魅之刑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1152480_comment'></div>察以江湖之间，鱼米甚贱，晨夕之养，甘滑可期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1152480_comment'></div>恢孝治之风，推恩逮下；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1152480_comment'></div>体高明之德，以欲从人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1152480_comment'></div>特于苏、湖、常、润等州，假一郡之寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1152480_comment'></div>至于宣布皇泽，抚养黎氓，圣人有言，尚东周之可冀，循吏何远，岂西汉之难偕？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1152480_comment'></div>三牲傥获于承颜，五月誓期于报政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1152480_comment'></div>然臣素知廉耻，无所侥求。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1152480_comment'></div>固于官常，不敢贪冒，只希罢免，非望改迁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1152480_comment'></div>以七人补衮之资，荷千里颁条之寄，于臣之分，所得已多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1152480_comment'></div>况今多士盈庭，君子在位，如臣之比，实繁有徒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1152480_comment'></div>至于润色鸿猷，羽仪琐闼，傥加慎柬，何患乏材？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1152480_comment'></div>若臣者茍蒙锡类之仁，得遵量力之训，乌鸟反哺，但期踯躅于一枝；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1152480_comment'></div>䲡鳝并逃，岂足盈虚于九罭！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1152480_comment'></div>披肝沥血，仰俟允俞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1152480_comment'></div>干犯宸严，臣无任<span class='inlineComment2'>（云云）</span>。</div><div id='poem_sentence_63_1152480_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1152544' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152544' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152544?labeling=true' target='_blank'>陈乞奏状<span class='inlineComment2'>（不曾上）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1004年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152544")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152544_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152544'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152544'>右，臣窃以穹旻覆物，所贵于听卑；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152544_comment'></div>臣子事君，固许其无隐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152544_comment'></div>敢倾肺腑，上黩冕旒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152544_comment'></div>伏念臣本出单平，素非茂异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152544_comment'></div>先皇怜其好学，寘在清华；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152544_comment'></div>陛下采以虚名，骤加甄擢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152544_comment'></div>预谏诤七人之列，掌丝纶五色之言，身纡三品之服章，日奉九重之朝谒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152544_comment'></div>实为儒之健羡，诚受恩之寖深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1152544_comment'></div>敢不策励疲驽，服勤官次？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1152544_comment'></div>终亏称职之誉，空累知臣之明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1152544_comment'></div>每循省以若惊，在报效而无所，岂合更倾私恳，上浼公朝！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1152544_comment'></div>盖以臣世异膏粱，迹本羁旅，负郭素无于别业，北堂方侍于慈颜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1152544_comment'></div>自委质效官，代耕得禄，期功相聚，莫匪至亲，衣食所资，悉皆仰给。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1152544_comment'></div>虽职司之甚重，在俸入以极微。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1152544_comment'></div>至于吉凶庆吊之资，仆马薪刍之费，凡百用度，皆出其中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1152544_comment'></div>谅饘粥糊口之不充，岂甘旨养亲之能及？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1152544_comment'></div>早者以迫于旅火，曾扣帝阍，述屡空之可忧，冀倒悬之或解。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1152544_comment'></div>而曦轮晃朗，未照于覆盆；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1152544_comment'></div>河鲋焦熬，愈悲于涸辙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1152544_comment'></div>盖念处掖垣清切之地，受帝王特达之知，出入于金门玉堂，陟降于赤墀文陛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1152544_comment'></div>茍尺帛寸粟，稍有资储，夕膳晨羞，不亏奉养，且无求于丰泰，况粗守于廉隅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1152544_comment'></div>又岂愿以区区之诚，上烦君父；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1152544_comment'></div>籍籍之口，腾诮搢绅？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1152544_comment'></div>既挤壑之是虞，亦触鳞而无避。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1152544_comment'></div>伏望皇帝陛下道存恻隐，仁极表微，悯其聚族于京师，只请本官之俸料，或馆阁之内，俾兼著撰之职司，或甸服之间，特授藩方之忧寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1152544_comment'></div>庶稍沾于加给，聊有救于固穷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1152544_comment'></div>其于燕谷回春，西江激水，顿苏暖律，骤跃洪澜，并出殊私，非敢有望云云。</div><div id='poem_sentence_26_1152544_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1004&endYear=1004')">1004年2月</a>　陈世卿自太常博士出知建州，亿赠诗，因抒羡领郡之意。作品：陈太博知建州。<div id='poem_129406' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_129406' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/129406?labeling=true' target='_blank'>陈太博知建州</a><span class='authorDate'>（1004年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_129406")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_129406_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_129406'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_129406'>梦笔山连化剑津，两乡人看锦衣新。<div id='poem_sentence_0_129406_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_129406'>北堂滫瀡三牲膳，南陌骖驔五马尘。<div id='poem_sentence_1_129406_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_129406'>画角声残铃阁暮，露牙香细茗园春。<div id='poem_sentence_2_129406_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_129406'>瓯闽自昔多居士，谁是贤侯席上珍。<div id='poem_sentence_3_129406_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_129406'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_129406_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1004&endYear=1004')">1004年</a>　三月十五日，皇太后崩，十七日亿为百官撰表请听政。不允，二十一日，又代宰相李沆等奏请听政。作品：百官请听政第三表。代中书请听政状。<div id='poem_1152482' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152482' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152482?labeling=true' target='_blank'>百官请听政第三表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1004年3月17日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152482")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152482_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152482'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152482'>臣某等言：臣等今者两陈章奏，备沥恳诚，因遗诰之明文，请临轩而听政，猥奉答诏，未赐允俞，群情悚惶，不敢宁处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152482_comment'></div>臣某等<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>窃以寰海至广，事有万机；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152482_comment'></div>家国异宜，理非一致。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152482_comment'></div>恭惟皇帝陛下至孝之德，上通神明，宅忧已来，哀动左右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152482_comment'></div>永怀罔极，痛深创钜，乃于听断，未忍躬亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152482_comment'></div>而况长乐上仙，顾命斯在；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152482_comment'></div>奉常掌礼，典训具存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152482_comment'></div>盖以宵旰务烦，君人位重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1152482_comment'></div>万方仰戴，不可以谅阴；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1152482_comment'></div>百度财成，岂宜于旷废？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1152482_comment'></div>故前代酌中而立制，治命郑重而为言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1152482_comment'></div>伏望稍抑至怀，仰遵遗旨，念宗社之大计，稽载籍之旧章，俯徇舆情，临决庶政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1152482_comment'></div>所冀百执各扬于乃职，群臣获睹于清光，慰中外之翘诚，副华夷之徯望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1152482_comment'></div>臣等无任祈天俟命、兢惶激切之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1152482_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1152548' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152548' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152548?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代中书请听政状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1004年3月21日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152548")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152548_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152548'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152548'>右，臣等伏以先后升遐，宸衷哀慕，痛深创钜，擗摽伤摧，殆兹弥旬，茕然在疚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152548_comment'></div>虽三日听政，备遗诰之丁宁；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152548_comment'></div>四表叫阍，罄群情之恳倒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152548_comment'></div>而诏旨敦谕，形于未忍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152548_comment'></div>朝野惶骇，罔知所图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152548_comment'></div>窃以机务至繁，不可以暂旷；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152548_comment'></div>治命至重，不可以辄违。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152548_comment'></div>自先皇后圣体弗康，载离寒暑，皇帝陛下衣不解带，药必先尝，躬祷神祇，遍走群望，亲候安否，日至寝门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1152548_comment'></div>或当膳之载加，然乃御食；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1152548_comment'></div>虽中夕而屡起，靡敢宁居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1152548_comment'></div>动静承颜，勤劳不匮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1152548_comment'></div>天子之孝，载籍所无。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1152548_comment'></div>及兹上仙，追怀罔极，充穷永感，谅闇不言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1152548_comment'></div>臣等获造倚卢，面陈至恳，愿以宗社为念，少抑哀怀；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1152548_comment'></div>望遵顾命之文，俯临庶政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1152548_comment'></div>而易月之制，圣情誓守于几筵；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1152548_comment'></div>宅忧已来，天颜殆至于栾棘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1152548_comment'></div>臣等兢惶屏息，不敢仰视。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1152548_comment'></div>伏望陛下循祖宗之旧典，克保彝章；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1152548_comment'></div>禀母后之遗言，勿违慈旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1152548_comment'></div>节哀顺变，式协前经；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1152548_comment'></div>垂拱向明，躬决庶务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1152548_comment'></div>以天下而为大计，俾群臣而睹清光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1152548_comment'></div>如此即长乐如在之灵，实歆孝德；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1152548_comment'></div>有司各扬之职，不紊官常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1152548_comment'></div>所系非轻，期于得请。</div><div id='poem_sentence_25_1152548_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1004&endYear=1004')">1004年</a>　六月前，制命陈尧咨知制诰，亿代其父省华作谢表。作品：代鸿胪陈少卿谢男知制诰表。<div id='poem_1152481' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152481' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152481?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代鸿胪陈少卿谢男知制诰表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1004年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152481")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152481_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152481'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152481'>臣某言：臣第三男秘书省著作郎、直史馆尧咨，伏奉制命，特授右正言、知制诰者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152481_comment'></div>恩覃贝阙，庆集蓬门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152481_comment'></div>荷奖擢以非常，但兢营而失据。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152481_comment'></div>臣某<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>窃以典掌诏令，步武掖垣，参班缀于赤墀，陪豫游于清跸，自非髦彦，岂副选抡？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152481_comment'></div>臣男尧咨，学谢淹通，才非茂异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152481_comment'></div>趋庭禀训，惭无诗礼之规；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152481_comment'></div>束带效官，已玷图书之任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152481_comment'></div>岂谓尊号皇帝陛下俯垂柬拔，特超群伦，俾升鸡省之近司，对演龙纶之雅诰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1152481_comment'></div>况尧咨冠甲科之选，早愧非宜；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1152481_comment'></div>通闺籍已来，殊为未久。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1152481_comment'></div>便掌大君之书命，辄与先生而并行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1152481_comment'></div>俯偻虽训以益恭，负乘且虞于致寇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1152481_comment'></div>实光生于举族，但感极于寸心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1152481_comment'></div>涕泗不觉以沾濡，魂爽更惊于飞越。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1152481_comment'></div>盖念臣孱微绪息，丛集宠光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1152481_comment'></div>长男尧叟，忝尘宥密之司，翊赞枢机之务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1152481_comment'></div>虽夙夜之诚益励，而乾坤之造弥深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1152481_comment'></div>次男尧佐，冒宠周行，兼荣史阁，出分忧寄，式涖藩垣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1152481_comment'></div>而臣亚秩象河，方惭厚禄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1152481_comment'></div>趋朝辩色，尚玷清班。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1152481_comment'></div>渥泽荐臻，鸿私累洽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1152481_comment'></div>虽藉时来之幸，常忧鬼瞰之灾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1152481_comment'></div>今尧咨又拜命于九重，复冒荣于四禁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1152481_comment'></div>蚊蚋贱质，谅何力以负山？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1152481_comment'></div>葵藿微生，但倾心而向日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1152481_comment'></div>聚首唯怀于感咽，捐躯誓报于高明。</div><div id='poem_sentence_25_1152481_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1004&endYear=1004')">1004年</a>　夏，钱惟演夜直秘阁寄诗，亿和酬之。作品：和酬秘阁钱少卿夜直见寄次韵。<div id='poem_129153' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_129153' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/129153?labeling=true' target='_blank'>和酬秘阁钱少卿夜直见寄次韵</a><span class='authorDate'>（1004年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_129153")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_129153_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_129153'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_129153'>甘瓜朱李郢醪浓，素绠银床荫碧桐。<div id='poem_sentence_0_129153_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_129153'>赐第旧连丹凤阙，直庐今在未央宫。<div id='poem_sentence_1_129153_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_129153'>承云仙掌延年露，转蕙薰弦解愠风。<div id='poem_sentence_2_129153_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_129153'>此夕蓬山好逃暑，月轩清话恨难同。<div id='poem_sentence_3_129153_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_129153'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_129153_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1004&endYear=1004')">1004年</a>　夏，黄震出知南郑县，有诗送之。作品：黄小著震知兴元府南郑县。<div id='poem_129272' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_129272' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/129272?labeling=true' target='_blank'>黄小著震知兴元府南郑县</a><span class='authorDate'>（1004年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_129272")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_129272_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_129272'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_129272'>藏室仙郎罢属辞，暑天驱传出京畿。<div id='poem_sentence_0_129272_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_129272'>流年两鬓生华发，宰邑全家住翠微。<div id='poem_sentence_1_129272_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_129272'>九折坂长须叱驭，三声猿苦莫沾衣<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_2_129272_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_129272'>金门荐鹗知音在<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑵</sup>，不到瓜时捧诏归。<div id='poem_sentence_3_129272_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_129272'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_129272_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_129272'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_2_129272_0'>⑴ 自注：右歌词云巴东三峡猿鸣悲，猿鸣三声泪沾衣。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_3_129272_0'>⑵ 自注：政事夕郎太原公常抗章称荐。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_129272_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1004&endYear=1004')">1004年</a>　以知处州时雄道人所惠石枕赠王旦，有诗叙之。作品：送石枕与参政王给事。<div id='poem_129225' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_129225' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/129225?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送石枕与参政王给事<span class='inlineComment2'>（雄道人所惠者）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1004年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_129225")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_129225_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_129225'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_129225'>千古碧潭秋水骨，琢成孤枕冷于冰。<div id='poem_sentence_0_129225_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_129225'>因为江外朱轮守，得自林閒白足僧。<div id='poem_sentence_1_129225_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_129225'>月幌光寒吞桂魄，暑轩气爽压梅蒸。<div id='poem_sentence_2_129225_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_129225'>奇章好尚非流俗，愿向萧斋代曲肱。<div id='poem_sentence_3_129225_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_129225'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_129225_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1004&endYear=1004')">1004年</a>　六月，给事中柴成务卒，稍后，为撰行状及墓志铭。作品：宋故太中大夫行给事中上柱国临汾郡开国侯食邑一千二百户赐紫金鱼袋平阳柴公墓志铭。故大中大夫行给事中上柱国临汾郡开国侯食邑一千二百户赐紫金鱼袋柴公行状。<div id='poem_1152705' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152705' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152705?labeling=true' target='_blank'>宋故太中大夫行给事中上柱国临汾郡开国侯食邑一千二百户赐紫金鱼袋平阳柴公墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1004年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152705")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152705_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152705'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152705'>公讳成务，字宝臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152705_comment'></div>其先平阳人，汉棘蒲侯之后也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152705_comment'></div>世乱流寓，不常厥居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152705_comment'></div>公之远祖，占籍河朔，积德有后，宗派盛焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152705_comment'></div>五代祖赓，因官曹南，遂家于济阴郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152705_comment'></div>大王父纲，庐州别驾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152705_comment'></div>王父允，隐居求志，藏器不耀，累赠太子右赞善大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152705_comment'></div>祖妣刘氏，追封彭城县太君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1152705_comment'></div>烈考自牧举进士乙科，应聘戎阃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1152705_comment'></div>晋末之乱，奉武行德于河桥，蹈危机，画奇策，尊立汉室，底定中原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1152705_comment'></div>天步既清，赏典不及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1152705_comment'></div>逮周邦之启，始通闺籍，践历台省，淹徊郎署，终兵部员外郎；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1152705_comment'></div>而王父、祖妣追荣锡命，皆由兵部之故也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1152705_comment'></div>自公之贵，兵部累赠礼部侍郎；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1152705_comment'></div>妣丁氏，追封谯县太君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1152705_comment'></div>锡羡流光，斯不诬矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1152705_comment'></div>公风度夷雅，襟灵冲粹，始在孩稚，迥如老成，靡事尘游，不杂儿戏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1152705_comment'></div>横经就学，昂昂有千里之姿；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1152705_comment'></div>从赋干名，籍籍致同人之誉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1152705_comment'></div>每投诚执贽，前达为之致恭；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1152705_comment'></div>秉笔属文，倾都以之传写。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1152705_comment'></div>春官宗伯，常虚甲科以待之，而公思值名公，伸于知己。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1152705_comment'></div>乾德中，礼部员外郎、知制诰王公祜，适典贡部，公始就乡举，即以公冠于诸生，当时朝野，耸得贤之议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1152705_comment'></div>解褐宿州军事推官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1152705_comment'></div>秩满，为曹单观察从事，被所知之举，迁大理寺丞，监潭州茶场。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1152705_comment'></div>筦榷之利，实佐于用度；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1152705_comment'></div>羡馀之绩，具载于简书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1152705_comment'></div>畴其干蛊之才，委以外计之任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1152705_comment'></div>改太常丞、峡路转运副使，赐五品服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1152705_comment'></div>拜监察御史、知果州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1152705_comment'></div>转殿中、知苏州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1152705_comment'></div>满岁，移充两浙转运使，改户部员外郎、直史馆，赐服金紫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1152705_comment'></div>除本曹郎中、充三司户部判官，选为光禄少卿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1152705_comment'></div>未几，充高丽国信使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1152705_comment'></div>复命，领京东转运。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1152705_comment'></div>入为司封郎中、知制诰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1152705_comment'></div>迁左谏议大夫、知河中府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1152705_comment'></div>今上践阼，拜给事中、知梓州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1152705_comment'></div>归朝，受诏同修永熙《实录》，俄知扬州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1152705_comment'></div>入判尚书刑部。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1152705_comment'></div>小吏犯法，怒而笞之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1152705_comment'></div>黠胥无赖，伏阙自诉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1152705_comment'></div>适有中旨，薄责其状。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1152705_comment'></div>公以为天子从官，领秋曹六卿之任，抶吏被劾，禁止朝谒，亦何面目复据堂决事耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1152705_comment'></div>即上言解职，以本官奉朝请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1152705_comment'></div>未几，腠理生疾，勿药靡徵，哲人其萎，颓山兴叹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1152705_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1152705_comment'></div>公以景德元年六月某日，考终于正寝，享年七十有一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1152705_comment'></div>公寝疾弥留，方寸不乱，口占遗奏，以六岁孤儿为言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1152705_comment'></div>上悯之，特授太常寺奉礼郎，赋以廪禄，俾终丧纪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1152705_comment'></div>即以某年某月某日，奉公之灵柩，归葬于开封县新里乡汴南里小边村汴南原，举前二夫人祔焉，礼也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1152705_comment'></div>公始娶赵氏，故宗正少卿齐之女；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1152705_comment'></div>后娶张氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1152705_comment'></div>今夫人李氏，封赞皇县君，故水部员外郎岧之女也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1152705_comment'></div>宜家之美，内助居多；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1152705_comment'></div>德茂亢宗，义敦偕老。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1152705_comment'></div>三娶令族，晚有儿息，年六十有六，始得今奉礼焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1152705_comment'></div>二女：长许适太常寺太祝张太初，今户部侍郎雍之爱子也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1152705_comment'></div>次尚幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1152705_comment'></div>二弟：曰成象，举进士，终秘书省著作佐郎；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1152705_comment'></div>曰成文，任三班奉职，实公之保任也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1152705_comment'></div>弟之子曰贞范，将作监丞；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1152705_comment'></div>曰贞简，秘书省校书郎：皆自公而成立焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1152705_comment'></div>公文行首出，时名籍甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1152705_comment'></div>自濯缨筮仕，束带登朝，佐幕从军，颇闻婉婉之画；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1152705_comment'></div>剸烦治剧，盖有飘飘之刃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1152705_comment'></div>先朝以卿士惟月，时惟古官，位实象河，行有鸣玉，典掌尤重，表著并崇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1152705_comment'></div>自唐以来，目为散地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1152705_comment'></div>思矫前失，以振旧规，乃选诸曹正郎有才望者十人，并补少列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1152705_comment'></div>而公首膺兹任，群议允归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1152705_comment'></div>至若辰韩之区，是为君子之国，世修职贡，乃心本朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1152705_comment'></div>而尺诏颁恩，輶轩遣使，抚柔殊俗，震叠皇灵，自非专对之才，或致君命之辱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1152705_comment'></div>而公奉辞于役，裔壤咸怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1152705_comment'></div>矧内史西台，专掌训诰，代言之选，居第一流；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1152705_comment'></div>而公允是佥谐，润色鸿业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1152705_comment'></div>前朝国书，藏在册府，论次大典，厥惟难才；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1152705_comment'></div>而公肃奉拟伦，裁成信史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1152705_comment'></div>逮于出典剧郡，必树于风声；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1152705_comment'></div>入奉内朝，式瞻于仪表。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1152705_comment'></div>经笥学海，河东之三箧尽通；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1152705_comment'></div>辨囿谈丛，稷下之千人皆伏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1152705_comment'></div>多识前训，钻之弥坚；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1152705_comment'></div>善与人交，久而无改。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1152705_comment'></div>雅奉玄元之教，妙达养生之旨；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1152705_comment'></div>深通医砭之术，屦获蠲痾之效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1152705_comment'></div>其风规酝藉，学术该博，亦足为儒林之丈人，公朝之旧德矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1152705_comment'></div>某昔刊青简，尝接绪言，今志佳城，无惭直笔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1152705_comment'></div>庶几传信，以永方来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1152705_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_88_1152705'>浊河奔流，羽虫日化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1152705_comment'></div>逝者如斯，不舍昼夜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1152705_comment'></div>新阡郁起，原隰龙鳞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1152705_comment'></div>死而可赎，人百其身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1152705_comment'></div>呜呼柴公，名高乡品。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1152705_comment'></div>给事左曹，行将十稔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1152705_comment'></div>享年从心，考终正寝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1152705_comment'></div>日月之吉，龟筮叶从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1152705_comment'></div>牛眠卜宅，马鬣增封。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1152705_comment'></div>九原宿草，千古长松。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1152705_comment'></div>唯令名兮不灭，与编简兮无穷<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1152705_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_99_1152705'>编：原脱，据明本补。</div><div id='poem_sentence_99_1152705_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1152705'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_98_1152705_0'>⑴ 《武夷新集》卷一○。又见雍正《山西通志》卷六四。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1152705_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_1152691' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152691' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152691?labeling=true' target='_blank'>故大中大夫行给事中上柱国临汾郡开国侯食邑一千二百户赐紫金鱼袋柴公行状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1004年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152691")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152691_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152691'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152691'>曾祖丕皇，任庐州别驾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152691_comment'></div>祖允，赠太子右赞善大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152691_comment'></div>考自牧皇，任尚书兵部员外郎，累赠礼部侍郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152691_comment'></div>曹州济阴县沛郡乡崇儒里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152691_comment'></div>柴成务，字宝臣，年七十一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152691_comment'></div>公之先，平阳人，由高、曾已来，占籍济阴，因而土著，遂为著姓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152691_comment'></div>先大夫以文行首出，一上登进士科，历佐使府，终于郎署。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152691_comment'></div>公爰在童幼，发言成章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1152691_comment'></div>总角之年，出就外傅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1152691_comment'></div>横经学问，迥如宿习，秉笔属文，动偕作者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1152691_comment'></div>甫及冠岁，志业大成，尚复藏器待伸，养勇俟斗，誓得当世儒学宗匠为门下生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1152691_comment'></div>乾德中，礼部员外郎、知制诰王公祜，受诏典礼部，公即踊跃从赋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1152691_comment'></div>王公览其文而奇之，擢冠多士，朝论翕然，有得人之美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1152691_comment'></div>解褐峡州军事推官，秩满，为曹单观察府中从事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1152691_comment'></div>所知论荐，改大理寺丞，监潭州茶场。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1152691_comment'></div>筦榷之利，颇致增羡；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1152691_comment'></div>干蛊之誉，扬于王庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1152691_comment'></div>擢受太常丞、峡路转运副使，赐五品服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1152691_comment'></div>迁监察御史、知果州，转殿中、知苏州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1152691_comment'></div>满岁，移充两浙转运使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1152691_comment'></div>改户部员外郎、直史馆，赐服金紫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1152691_comment'></div>除本曹郎中，充三司户部判官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1152691_comment'></div>太宗皇帝讲求化源，畴咨典故，且以列卿之职，实惟古官，各有攸司，所掌甚重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1152691_comment'></div>爰自唐室，以台阁相高，汔至于今，目为散地，由郎署而授者，例同左迁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1152691_comment'></div>浚发德音，丕变颓俗，乃选尚书诸曹正郎有才望者，凡十人，次补诸寺少卿监。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1152691_comment'></div>仍著令，自今非曾历少列，不得拟给、舍、谏议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1152691_comment'></div>公首预兹选，拜光禄少卿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1152691_comment'></div>辰韩之墟，称藩海外，属有恩诏，慎求使材，命公为高丽国信使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1152691_comment'></div>公雍容儒雅，博闻强记，衣冠之国，文物盛焉，举措话言，是法是效，《皇华》之美，至今称之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1152691_comment'></div>复命为京东水陆转运使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1152691_comment'></div>召入，拜司封郎中、知制诰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1152691_comment'></div>迁左谏议大夫，出知河中府，得脱户八百家，附于版籍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1152691_comment'></div>今上践祚，拜给事中、知梓州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1152691_comment'></div>归朝，受诏同修《太宗实录》，十月而毕，劳赐策勋，宠数优渥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1152691_comment'></div>未几，以本官知扬州，入判尚书刑部。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1152691_comment'></div>小吏干犯，怒而笞之，诣阙诉冤，朝官问状。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1152691_comment'></div>公以为抶一胥而被劾，何面目复据堂决事耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1152691_comment'></div>即上书解职，以本官奉朝请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1152691_comment'></div>至是考终于正寝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1152691_comment'></div>遗奏以六岁孤儿为言，上悯之，特授太常寺奉礼郎，命赋以禄，俾终丧纪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1152691_comment'></div>公始娶赵氏，故宗正少卿齐之女也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1152691_comment'></div>后娶张氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1152691_comment'></div>今夫人李氏，封赞皇县君，故水部员外郎岧之女也，实有令德，洽于宗姻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1152691_comment'></div>公三娶良家，晚有儿息，行年六十有六，始得今奉礼焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1152691_comment'></div>公好学多能，博物稽古。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1152691_comment'></div>始在贡部，为时闻人，奋藻属词，流辈推服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1152691_comment'></div>或有所述作，必传写都下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1152691_comment'></div>终以才望，入司训诰，发挥帝命，颇为称职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1152691_comment'></div>而襟怀夷坦，无有城府，音容和粹，煦如阳春。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1152691_comment'></div>善与人交，久弥笃也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1152691_comment'></div>好治家事，勤不匮也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1152691_comment'></div>善谈名理，口无择言；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1152691_comment'></div>广聚坟史，手不释卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1152691_comment'></div>雅性奉道，遍阅金简玉笈之文；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1152691_comment'></div>平生多病，深穷恶石青囊之术。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1152691_comment'></div>恬淡以养性，蔓衍以穷年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1152691_comment'></div>其风规酝藉，阀阅深厚，亦足以为儒林丈夫矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1152691_comment'></div>记事之职，良史在焉，谨书世家，以告册府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1152691_comment'></div>谨状。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_58_1152691'></div><div id='poem_sentence_58_1152691_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1004&endYear=1004')">1004年</a>　寇准受赐《晋书》，亿为代撰谢状。作品：代集贤寇相公谢赐晋书状。<div id='poem_1152561' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152561' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152561?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代集贤寇相公谢赐晋书状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1004年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152561")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152561_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152561'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152561'>右，臣今日中使至，奉宣圣旨，赐臣印本《晋书》一部，计六十九册者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152561_comment'></div>两晋遗编，具列秘书之目；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152561_comment'></div>九重稽古，新成镂板之功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152561_comment'></div>夫何寡闻，仰膺蕃锡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152561_comment'></div>伏惟皇帝陛下缵戎御极，执契临人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152561_comment'></div>负将圣之多能，尚观文而阐化；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152561_comment'></div>以史笔之所记，有龟鉴以具存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152561_comment'></div>鲁鱼特命于校雠，方牍更加于摹印，俾前言之不坠，亦副本之广传。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1152561_comment'></div>臣谬预持衡，实惭昧道，辄上干于宸扆，果垂锡于策书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1152561_comment'></div>学古无功，固已嗟于捍格；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1152561_comment'></div>传家知幸，但永誓于缄藏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1152561_comment'></div>恭承临照之私，益励倾输之节。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1152561_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1004&endYear=1004')">1004年8月7日</a>　寇准拜相，亿草制。及制下，又代寇准撰让官表三道。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1004&endYear=1004')">1004年</a>　秋，查道自许州以书荐张士逊于亿，亿促士逊献文阙下，介于执政；又书答查道，以禅理非士逊“簪组非累身”之说。作品：答史馆查正言书。<div id='poem_1152581' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152581' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152581?labeling=true' target='_blank'>答史馆查正言书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1004年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152581")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152581_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152581'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152581'>某再拜正言学士足下：顷者前襄阳张令至，辱示手笔，备形慰诲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152581_comment'></div>耽玩无斁，鄙吝都遣，客尘洞分，神明来舍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152581_comment'></div>凉若醍醐之灌顶，快如灵曜之炙背。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152581_comment'></div>荷知识之启迪，为昏愚之归依。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152581_comment'></div>幸甚幸甚！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152581_comment'></div>然障覆重复，义趣深远，或所犹豫，固容咨决。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152581_comment'></div>窃味雅旨，有「簪组非累身」之说，蒙有滞焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152581_comment'></div>盖念无始轮回，积劫孤露，偶薰习于种子，获遭值于仁贤，幸于此生，得悟本性。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1152581_comment'></div>而前尘外境，如棼丝乱绳，本觉妙心，殆秋毫野马，举为牵制，动即沦胥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1152581_comment'></div>先德亦云道力尪微，必处静而能照；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1152581_comment'></div>宗门所谓悟解超顿，须渐修而乃成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1152581_comment'></div>傥或以初殖之德芽，沦无边之爱网，浮沉阴入之界，趋走声利之场，自以了达苦空，脱去事理，谓生死而无怖，谓富贵而傥来，此适足以长无明支，成增上慢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1152581_comment'></div>若夫现三十二应，化千百亿身，居士王臣，随方设教；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1152581_comment'></div>猿猴鹿马，与物利生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1152581_comment'></div>此须功行圆成，福智满足，登地證果，乃及于斯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1152581_comment'></div>自馀涉川救人，未免俱溺；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1152581_comment'></div>哺糟处世，何能独醒？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1152581_comment'></div>载寻善诱之言，盖有造微之旨，岂非虑鄙夫尚迷真谛，犹恋荣名，便令舍去，恐致迷闷？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1152581_comment'></div>然固陋之志，亦小异焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1152581_comment'></div>傥寿量颇延，缘累自薄，当俟夫四五十，须背俗息见，反本循元。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1152581_comment'></div>脩天台之止观，专曹溪之无念，庶于此报，必證菩提。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1152581_comment'></div>俟兜率下生，龙华后会，为之主伴，请转法轮，对越人天，亲受佛记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1152581_comment'></div>虽二乘而弗学，岂三界以能安？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1152581_comment'></div>慺慺之心，实在于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1152581_comment'></div>足下众德普会，八部归依，暂显宰官之身，常脩菩萨之行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1152581_comment'></div>济度群品，引翼有情，作十园林，具四誓愿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1152581_comment'></div>传受心印，直指不疑；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1152581_comment'></div>演说色空，辩才无碍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1152581_comment'></div>傥矜其可教，望惠之好音。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1152581_comment'></div>所期奉以周旋，不敢失坠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1152581_comment'></div>或理参邪见，旨失真宗，未至膏肓，可施针石，亦希提奖，无便弃捐，幸甚幸甚！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1152581_comment'></div>秋气变衰，王事鞅掌，强食慎疾，副兹仰瞻。</div><div id='poem_sentence_31_1152581_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1004&endYear=1004')">1004年10月27日</a>　自三月皇太后崩，罢乐。十月二十七日，中书、枢密院三上表请举乐，亿代撰三表。作品：代中书密院请举乐第一表。代中书密院请举乐第二表。代中书密院请举乐第三表。<div id='poem_1152490' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152490' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152490?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代中书密院请举乐第一表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1004年10月27日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152490")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152490_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152490'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152490'>臣某等言：臣等窃以天子之广孝也，刑四海而加百姓；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152490_comment'></div>先王之作乐也，荐上帝而谐神人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152490_comment'></div>是以顺变从宜之规，著于经礼；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152490_comment'></div>不为将坏之叹，播于前闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152490_comment'></div>斯乃邦国之大猷，方策之丕训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152490_comment'></div>抑而未举，阙孰甚焉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152490_comment'></div>臣某等<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>伏以尊号皇帝陛下浚哲丕承，淳熙累洽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152490_comment'></div>达聪明而求治，体慈俭以爱人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1152490_comment'></div>敦奉先思孝之心，得事亲尽礼之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1152490_comment'></div>恭自灾缠长乐，痛结紫宸，勉遵易月之文，益厚因心之戚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1152490_comment'></div>乃至克终园寝，升祔宗祧，蒸尝之荐享聿修，公私之情礼俱毕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1152490_comment'></div>有位之士，伏閤上言，深引唐、汉之旧规，厚举咸英之备乐，而陛下屡颁明诏，誓守通丧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1152490_comment'></div>属六飞展义之有期，且群臣叫阍而弥切。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1152490_comment'></div>聊鼓吹之振作，以壮戎容；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1152490_comment'></div>逮旅恺之班旋，复停雅奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1152490_comment'></div>俄属就阳报本，备物告虔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1152490_comment'></div>必六变之同和，乃三灵而昭格。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1152490_comment'></div>允兹抗疏，盖示从权。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1152490_comment'></div>但致恭于神祇，固不施于享宴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1152490_comment'></div>彝章垂世，虽载籍之具存，至性格天，非公议之能夺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1152490_comment'></div>聿尊服纪，以及裨馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1152490_comment'></div>今者燧火屡迁，祥琴在御，三年之制不可以踰，九奏之音无容久废。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1152490_comment'></div>伏望陛下光昭前训，申饬有司，诏后夔以守官，俾师乙之肄业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1152490_comment'></div>使周《雅》各得其所，虞《韶》无相夺伦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1152490_comment'></div>诞扬尽善之称，聿致来仪之瑞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1152490_comment'></div>岂惟臣等幸甚，实亦天下幸甚！</div><div id='poem_sentence_25_1152490_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1152491' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152491' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152491?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代中书密院请举乐第二表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1004年10月27日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152491")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152491_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152491'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152491'>臣某等言：臣等近者共援典故，同拜封章，愿遵方策之文，式举咸韶之奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152491_comment'></div>猥蒙答诏，未允下诚，搢绅之间，启处无措。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152491_comment'></div>臣某等<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>窃以礼经制作之意，家国异宜；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152491_comment'></div>载籍沿袭之规，古今共守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152491_comment'></div>盖前代立训，允叶于酌中；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152491_comment'></div>故圣人抑情，不忘于俯就。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152491_comment'></div>简编所纪，轨范攸存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152491_comment'></div>恭惟尊号皇帝陛下浚哲在躬，钦明抚运，孝思光格，德教诞敷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1152491_comment'></div>然而祗率典常，畴咨故实，是彝是宪，不愆不忘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1152491_comment'></div>伏况丙殿上仙，云陵复土，公除已久，吉祭屡行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1152491_comment'></div>新谷既升，爰载周于天吏；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1152491_comment'></div>閟宫有侐，早昭配于神宗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1152491_comment'></div>中外之间，情礼俱毕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1152491_comment'></div>而乃享宴之际，金石未陈，莫循旧章，深郁群望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1152491_comment'></div>矧惟大乐之作，同和于二仪；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1152491_comment'></div>饫赐之恩，示慈于百辟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1152491_comment'></div>六代并举，乃盛德之是观；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1152491_comment'></div>三年不为，亦雅音之将坏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1152491_comment'></div>茍自图于缄默，靡再黩于高明，废稽古之大猷，诚有位之深责。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1152491_comment'></div>伏望陛下俯遵舆诵，启迪前规，特诏有司，奉行故事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1152491_comment'></div>聿举在悬之乐，诞扬治世之音。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1152491_comment'></div>崇德象功，光昭于鸿业；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1152491_comment'></div>来仪率舞，延集于嘉祥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1152491_comment'></div>俾人神之克谐，致天地之交泰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1152491_comment'></div>岂惟臣等幸甚，实亦天下幸甚！</div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1152491_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1152492' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152492' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152492?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代中书密院请举乐第三表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1004年10月27日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152492")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152492_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152492'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152492'>臣某等言：臣等近以园寝即安，已毕公除之制；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152492_comment'></div>宗祧升祔，克修吉祭之仪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152492_comment'></div>殆兹踰月之间，尚阙在悬之奏，遂共徵于典故，辄再上于封章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152492_comment'></div>猥奉诏书，未垂俞允。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152492_comment'></div>天听弥高而是惧，舆情若厉以不遑，臣某等<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>窃以备乐之作，与天地以同和；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152492_comment'></div>变礼之文，实古今之共守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152492_comment'></div>在汉即易月之后，更无遏密之仪；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152492_comment'></div>暨唐乃配庙已还，便申宴享之乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1152492_comment'></div>沿袭于兹而为盛，典训繇是以具存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1152492_comment'></div>伏况丙殿升遐，已终于远日；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1152492_comment'></div>閟宫合食，便祔于神宗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1152492_comment'></div>公私之间，情礼俱毕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1152492_comment'></div>而尊号皇帝陛下犹切永怀之痛，靡遵顺变之规。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1152492_comment'></div>至于九成治世之音，八佾象功之舞，皆所以导群情于和乐，昭盛德之形容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1152492_comment'></div>既以谐于人神，且用调于律吕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1152492_comment'></div>而乃寝停雅奏，度越礼文，虽明诏形未忍之言，而历代有酌中之制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1152492_comment'></div>矧今《云门》、《大吕》，将荐于圜丘；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1152492_comment'></div>《湛露》、《钧天》，合施于广宴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1152492_comment'></div>省方巡狩，亦陈诗而观风；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1152492_comment'></div>临轩会朝，当作乐以侑食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1152492_comment'></div>横汾展豫，既伸箫鼓之娱；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1152492_comment'></div>破虏勤归，固有凯歌之盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1152492_comment'></div>国之大事，实在于兹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1152492_comment'></div>伏望陛下采群臣之瞽言，稽前朝之成式，特诏执事，申明旧章，命协律而考雅音，俾广庭而陈法曲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1152492_comment'></div>尽善尽美，用还正始之风；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1152492_comment'></div>不愆不忘，率由方策之训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1152492_comment'></div>岂独臣等幸甚，实亦天下幸甚！</div><div id='poem_sentence_26_1152492_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1004&endYear=1004')">1004年</a>　随真宗北巡，至澶州。尝与寇准饮歌于行营。先是，契丹侵澶，朝议不决，独亿与寇准主北伐。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1004&endYear=1004')">1004年</a>　以契丹出境，议将回师，帝作《回銮诗》，亿有和作；及车驾还京，又代两制撰谢赐御诗状。作品：奉和御制《契丹出境将议回銮》五首六韵诗。两制谢赐御诗状。<div id='poem_129342' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_129342' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/129342?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奉和御制契丹出境将议回銮五言六韵诗</a><span class='authorDate'>（1004年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_129342")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_129342_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_129342'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_129342'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_129342", 129342, "Clauses/0/Comments/0")'>戎辂</span>巡河右，天威詟鬼方。<div id='poem_sentence_0_129342_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_129342'>五营开细柳，三令凛飞霜。<div id='poem_sentence_1_129342_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_129342'>氛祲消千里，声名耀八荒。<div id='poem_sentence_2_129342_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_129342'>灵旗风助顺，黄道日<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_129342", 129342, "Clauses/7/Comments/0")'>呈祥</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_129342_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_129342'>偃革边关静，回銮海县康。<div id='poem_sentence_4_129342_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_129342'>欣陪从臣末，归跸奉高骧。<div id='poem_sentence_5_129342_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_129342'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_129342_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1152552' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152552' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152552?labeling=true' target='_blank'>两制谢赐御诗状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1004年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152552")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152552_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152552'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152552'>右，臣今日入内内侍高班赵诚信至，奉传圣旨，赐臣等《契丹出境将议回銮》五言六韵诗一首，令依韵和来者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152552_comment'></div>天骄犯塞，銮辂时巡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152552_comment'></div>继好息民，式启和戎之利；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152552_comment'></div>回辕返旆，将闻振旅之期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152552_comment'></div>慰生民傒后之心，叶载籍止戈之义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152552_comment'></div>皇帝陛下躬亲栉沭，蒙犯风霜，巡细柳之营，貔貅贾勇；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152552_comment'></div>赋《大风》之什，云汉垂文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152552_comment'></div>克宣治世之音，实显圣人之作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1152552_comment'></div>臣等谬忝司言之任，惭无护跸之劳，辱示宸章，俾窥睿藻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1152552_comment'></div>璧月珠星之彩，既获于仰瞻；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1152552_comment'></div>《阳春》《白雪》之篇，仍容于属和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1152552_comment'></div>拭目之荣虽积，燥吻之虑弥深，徒共抉于荒芜，诚预惭于鄙浅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1152552_comment'></div>感惧之至，殒越无从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1152552_comment'></div>臣等云云。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1152552_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1004&endYear=1004')">1004年12月24日</a>　受诏与李宗谔等详定《正辞录》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1004&endYear=1004')">1004年12月29日</a>　帝以契丹南侵贻祸河北，下罪己诏；宰臣毕士安等上表待罪，亿代撰表。及帝答以优诏，又代中书密院撰谢表。作品：代中书密院待罪表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（原书作“中书秘院”据《全宋文》改。）</span>代中书密院谢降诏表。<div id='poem_1152486' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152486' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152486?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代中书密院待罪表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1004年12月29日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152486")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152486_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152486'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152486'>臣某等言：臣等闻无用之臣，明君靡畜；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152486_comment'></div>不材之木，良匠所捐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152486_comment'></div>虽天地之心，专务于匿瑕含垢；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152486_comment'></div>而邦国之典，所重于黜幽陟明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152486_comment'></div>既内省以不遑，须上言而自劾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152486_comment'></div>臣某等<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>窃以鼎铉之司，是处弼谐之任；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152486_comment'></div>枢机之地，盖参宥密之谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152486_comment'></div>率土具瞻，一人注意，庶政并从于关决，当阳每示于咨询。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1152486_comment'></div>自非蕴经邦成务之才，负尊主庇民之术，运奇兵于掌上，外镇抚于四夷，画成算于幄中，远决胜于千里，致穆清垂裳而无事，蒸黎击壤以不知，乃可备元首之股肱，始免玷公朝之名器。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1152486_comment'></div>如臣等，性皆庸昧，识本空疏，曾乏寸长，蔑闻片善，荐阶通显，并出遭逢，宠荣盖值于时来，崇高非由于德举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1152486_comment'></div>乘轩窃位，深怀卫鹤之惭；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1152486_comment'></div>食肉无谋，甘被鲁人之诮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1152486_comment'></div>一昨控弦入寇，插羽徵师，万旅戒严，四鄙入保。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1152486_comment'></div>负扆临轩而旰食，列城摩垒以交锋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1152486_comment'></div>爟火延袤于两河，武帐便蕃于三接。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1152486_comment'></div>而臣等当前席之际，既不能启沃而矢谟；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1152486_comment'></div>逮群居之时，又不能佥同而建议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1152486_comment'></div>徙薪取譬，无智者先见之明；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1152486_comment'></div>借箸前筹，乏愚夫一得之虑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1152486_comment'></div>乃至鸣镝渐侵于甸服，翠华将议于时巡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1152486_comment'></div>栉沐之劳，犹切爱君之志；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1152486_comment'></div>金革之事，请严责帅之科。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1152486_comment'></div>尊号皇帝陛下运上圣之沉机，排群言之妄作，独建非常之断，用宣大定之功，亲御六师，尽护诸将。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1152486_comment'></div>连薨徯后，家若解于倒悬；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1152486_comment'></div>案节劳军，人尽同于挟纩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1152486_comment'></div>果上玄之助顺，致骄子之乞盟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1152486_comment'></div>遂继好于交兵，永输诚而保塞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1152486_comment'></div>玉帛通欢于绝域，干戈载戢于中原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1152486_comment'></div>实九庙之降灵，开万世之美利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1152486_comment'></div>集兹巨伐，并出宸襟，若信诸臣，几误大事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1152486_comment'></div>乃至二城陷没，比户惊骚，多转死于沟隍，或不免于锋镝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1152486_comment'></div>黄屋深在予之责，丹诏形罪己之言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1152486_comment'></div>搆厉阶之若斯，亦庙谟而安在？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1152486_comment'></div>臣等诚惭短拙，共愧迂疏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1152486_comment'></div>自知甚明，岂敢昧于方寸？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1152486_comment'></div>不能者止，况昭著于格言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1152486_comment'></div>若冒宠于清朝，且偷安于显位，其如萤爝之耀，既无助于三光；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1152486_comment'></div>腹背之毛，亦何资于六翮？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1152486_comment'></div>徒积素餐之谤，更贻瞰室之殃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1152486_comment'></div>伏望陛下推赏罚于至公，示劝惩于来者，责以弥缝之无状，暴其辅佐之非才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1152486_comment'></div>诞告万方，申儆百执，拘于司败，用正常刑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1152486_comment'></div>然后玄德升闻，可召和平之气；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1152486_comment'></div>彝伦攸序，更无侥倖之人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1152486_comment'></div>克臻治定之期，永固延鸿之祚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1152486_comment'></div>岂但臣等幸甚，实亦天下幸甚！</div><div id='poem_sentence_44_1152486_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1152488' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152488' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152488?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代中书密院谢降诏表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1004年12月29日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋",
