"杨亿", "poem_title_1152488")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152488_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152488'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152488'>臣某等言：臣等昨以戎骑侵骚，边城震骇，兵锋日警，烦车驾之省方；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152488_comment'></div>羽卫天旋，纡诏书而罪己。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152488_comment'></div>盖帷幄前筹之无状，固冰渊内省之不遑，共拜封章，甘俟刑典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152488_comment'></div>忽承芝检，深谕丝言，载推善下之仁，曲恕已然之咎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152488_comment'></div>丁宁备至，启处无从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152488_comment'></div>臣某等<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>伏念臣等皆是琐才，滥尘贵士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152488_comment'></div>参鼎司之调燮，靡副民瞻；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152488_comment'></div>预机务之弥纶，莫熙帝载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1152488_comment'></div>一昨控弦犯塞，造膝论兵，侍宸扆于穆清，奉忧勤于旰昃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1152488_comment'></div>备尧岳畴咨之列，曾乏谟猷；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1152488_comment'></div>厕周臣同德之伦，空坚诚节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1152488_comment'></div>乃至引弓深入，插羽交驰，俯逼洪河，颇惊近甸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1152488_comment'></div>樽俎之画，愧千里之折冲；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1152488_comment'></div>霜露之行，劳六龙而展义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1152488_comment'></div>方式遏于乱略，乃大庇于生民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1152488_comment'></div>致欸塞之乞盟，将止戈而不用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1152488_comment'></div>此盖尊号皇帝陛下契上玄之眷命，考前代之令猷，姑务远图，昭示大信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1152488_comment'></div>排盈庭之众议，克彰独断之明；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1152488_comment'></div>许绝域之通欢，式启太平之业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1152488_comment'></div>并繄睿算，集此殊庸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1152488_comment'></div>臣等徒愧备员，莫能补职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1152488_comment'></div>当前席忧边之际，既无决胜之谋；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1152488_comment'></div>及登坛择帅之初，又阙指踪之效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1152488_comment'></div>固乏庙堂之远略，曷逃乡校之深讥？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1152488_comment'></div>亦窃位以胡颜，辄上言而请罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1152488_comment'></div>合议三章之法，以慰诸夏之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1152488_comment'></div>而陛下体成汤之至仁，尚兹引咎；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1152488_comment'></div>恢汉高之大度，曲示包荒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1152488_comment'></div>颁紫诏以封泥，霈鸿恩于疏网。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1152488_comment'></div>靡斥归于散地，特矜免于常刑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1152488_comment'></div>戴玄造以难胜，揣丹衷而失据。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1152488_comment'></div>溟渤之量，虽表于纳污；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1152488_comment'></div>驽蹇之姿，何能于致远？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1152488_comment'></div>敢不共加策励，同切倾输！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1152488_comment'></div>寸有所长，庶伸于后效；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1152488_comment'></div>退思补过，恭佩于前言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1152488_comment'></div>用毕微生，少酬洪覆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1152488_comment'></div>臣等无任<span class='inlineComment2'>（云云）</span>。</div><div id='poem_sentence_37_1152488_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1004&endYear=1004')">1004年</a>　有诗送梁鼎出知凤翔府。作品：梁四谏议知凤翔府。<div id='poem_129263' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_129263' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/129263?labeling=true' target='_blank'>梁四谏议知凤翔府</a><span class='authorDate'>（1004年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_129263")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_129263_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_129263'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_129263_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_129263'>云幕杯盘三省近，星邮章奏九门通。<div id='poem_sentence_2_129263_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_129263_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1004&endYear=1004')">1004年</a>　陈尧拱致仕归蜀，亿有诗送之。作品：陈尧拱廷评致仕归蜀。<div id='poem_129150' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_129150' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/129150?labeling=true' target='_blank'>陈尧拱廷评致仕归蜀<span class='inlineComment2'>（西枢给事之兄也）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1004年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_129150")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_129150_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_129150'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_129150'>一家今有十朱轮，独忆云山欲退身。<div id='poem_sentence_0_129150_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_129150'>天邑繁华行乐厌，月曹清要命书新。<div id='poem_sentence_1_129150_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_129150'>西风跃马经秦甸，东道椎牛宴孟邻。<div id='poem_sentence_2_129150_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_129150'>秋稼万箱僮百指，羲皇之上更何人。<div id='poem_sentence_3_129150_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_129150'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_129150_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1004&endYear=1004')">1004年</a>　有诗送表玄禅师归处州，追怀昔日与雄道人游。作品：表玄师归缙云有怀故雄阇黎成转韵六十四句。<div id='poem_129411' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_129411' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/129411?labeling=true' target='_blank'>表玄师归缙云有怀故雄阇黎成转韵六十四句</a><span class='authorDate'>（1004年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_129411")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_129411_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_129411'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_129411'>栝苍古名郡，生齿三万家。<div id='poem_sentence_0_129411_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_129411'>我昔自仙殿，捧诏临军牙。<div id='poem_sentence_1_129411_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_129411'>清心治期月，讼息民无哗。<div id='poem_sentence_2_129411_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_129411'>雄公真大士，宴坐绵岁华。<div id='poem_sentence_3_129411_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_129411'>驾言造梵宇，室迩惊人遐。<div id='poem_sentence_4_129411_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_129411'>迎门虎溪屐，布地牛头花。<div id='poem_sentence_5_129411_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_129411'>庭松偃翠盖，涧泉漱金沙。<div id='poem_sentence_6_129411_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_129411'>坐闻狮子吼，归恨踆乌斜。<div id='poem_sentence_7_129411_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_129411'>驿召还上都，腾装即修路。<div id='poem_sentence_8_129411_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_129411'>别师黄金园，赠我碧云句。<div id='poem_sentence_9_129411_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_129411'>我归步赤墀，代言红药署。<div id='poem_sentence_10_129411_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_129411'>弹指知苦空，观心得降住。<div id='poem_sentence_11_129411_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_129411'>藏识惭宿薰，轮回悲晚悟。<div id='poem_sentence_12_129411_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_129411'>折简问南宗，寄言满缃素。<div id='poem_sentence_13_129411_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_129411'>绝念契真如，忘筌离文字。<div id='poem_sentence_14_129411_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_129411'>劫烧虽洞然，龙华决同遇。<div id='poem_sentence_15_129411_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_129411'>师名达宸扆，恩诏颁方袍。<div id='poem_sentence_16_129411_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_129411'>欢喜黑白众，萧衰霜雪毛。<div id='poem_sentence_17_129411_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_129411'>毗邪见有疾，示身如幻泡。<div id='poem_sentence_18_129411_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_129411'>双林忽归寂，人天但哀号。<div id='poem_sentence_19_129411_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_129411'>堆案遗札在，满钵香饭销。<div id='poem_sentence_20_129411_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_129411'>只应伸臂顷，未觉他方遥。<div id='poem_sentence_21_129411_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_129411'>犀柄挂空壁，雁塔干层霄。<div id='poem_sentence_22_129411_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_129411'>七返暂来去，四大非坚牢。<div id='poem_sentence_23_129411_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_129411'>口占成尺题，手泽著纸尾。<div id='poem_sentence_24_129411_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_129411'>亲遣上足师，浮杯渡江水。<div id='poem_sentence_25_129411_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_26_129411'>云朵摇笔精，玉音锵里耳。<div id='poem_sentence_26_129411_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_27_129411'>遗我方石枕，斑文剪霞绮。<div id='poem_sentence_27_129411_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_28_129411'>谕我求菩提，心坚正如此。<div id='poem_sentence_28_129411_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_29_129411'>怆然悲梦形，汍澜泪盈眦。<div id='poem_sentence_29_129411_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_30_129411'>上足今去归，焚修益勤止。<div id='poem_sentence_30_129411_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_31_129411'>当续祖灯明，无令社莲死。<div id='poem_sentence_31_129411_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_32_129411'></div><div id='poem_sentence_32_129411_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1004&endYear=1004')">1004年</a>　上书知青州张齐贤。作品：上青州张相公书。<div id='poem_1152632' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152632' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152632?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上青州张相公书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1004年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152632")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152632_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152632'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152632'>窃以表海名邦，全齐旧地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152632_comment'></div>成周赐履，实重营丘；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152632_comment'></div>炎汉苴茅，肇分青社。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152632_comment'></div>统两蕃之职贡，拥十乘之麾幢，允属圣朝，是为雄屏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152632_comment'></div>长人之寄，注意尤深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152632_comment'></div>恭惟兵部相公业茂经论，望高廊庙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152632_comment'></div>爰自弼谐二圣，陟降三阶，奉尧舜之吁俞，有邴魏之风彩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152632_comment'></div>天垂北斗，回步武于中台；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1152632_comment'></div>地险东秦，委藩宣于右地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1152632_comment'></div>卧理暂烦于旧德，行春伫洽于欢谣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1152632_comment'></div>使竹临戎，岂久容于偃息；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1152632_comment'></div>公槐论道，将再预于燮调。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1152632_comment'></div>幅员之心，寤寐增切。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1152632_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1004&endYear=1004')">1004年</a>　受僧道原请托，为其编纂的《佛祖同参集》作序。道原进其书于帝，其后帝命杨亿等刊正，题曰《景德传灯录》，复有序。作品：佛祖同参集序。<div id='poem_1152665' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152665' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152665?labeling=true' target='_blank'>佛祖同参集序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1004年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152665")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152665_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152665'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152665'>昔如来于然灯佛所，亲蒙记莂，实无少法可得，是号大觉能仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152665_comment'></div>既而后智滋兴，悲心显发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152665_comment'></div>念四生之沉溺，轮回六趣之中；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152665_comment'></div>为一事之因缘，出现五浊之世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152665_comment'></div>奈何根器各异，机感有殊，由是开三乘权实之门，设一时顿渐之教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152665_comment'></div>具偏圆半满之义，分悟證伏断之差，演之为十二部经，广之为百千万颂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152665_comment'></div>随类各解，始虽自于一音；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152665_comment'></div>达本忘言，终乃同于二月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1152665_comment'></div>故纯陀末供之后，鹤林示灭之辰，以正法眼，付大迦叶，内传真印，外授信衣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1152665_comment'></div>作世导师，为佛嫡子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1152665_comment'></div>凡二十七世，至达摩大师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1152665_comment'></div>哀此土之人，昧即心之理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1152665_comment'></div>分别名相而不已，类入海以算沙；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1152665_comment'></div>攀缘生灭而为因，但认贼而作子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1152665_comment'></div>聿来震旦，宴坐少林，不事语言，不立文字。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1152665_comment'></div>既得人而传付，乃趣寂以返真，是为东方之初祖也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1152665_comment'></div>自尔本系相承，旁支别出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1152665_comment'></div>敷华结果，五叶之谶可徵；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1152665_comment'></div>续燄分辉，千灯之照弥广。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1152665_comment'></div>至于出离生死一门，證于涅槃；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1152665_comment'></div>诱导愚迷万行，以之差别。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1152665_comment'></div>由二祖而下，迄至于今。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1152665_comment'></div>以诸夏之利根，叶西土之悬记，得道之者，实繁有徒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1152665_comment'></div>其或抵掌盱衡，乃了知于风力；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1152665_comment'></div>摇唇鼓舌，即悟入于言枢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1152665_comment'></div>或针芥相投，金鍮力辩；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1152665_comment'></div>或经尘将破，啐啄同时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1152665_comment'></div>示现方便以既殊，但遭因缘而亦异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1152665_comment'></div>咸有轨迹，著为筌蹄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1152665_comment'></div>譬诸三藏之文，结集于钵罗之窟；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1152665_comment'></div>七佛所说，秘藏于娑蝎之宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1152665_comment'></div>茍撰述之无闻，使后来而安仰？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1152665_comment'></div>先是，诸方大士各立宗徒，互显师承，迭存语录。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1152665_comment'></div>圭山患其如是也，会合众说，著为《禅诠》，融通诸家，圆成一味，盖祖门之能事毕矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1152665_comment'></div>历岁弥久，《都序》仅存，百卷之文，不传于世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1152665_comment'></div>东吴道原禅师者，乃觉场之龙象，实人天之眼目，慨然以为祖师法裔，颇论次之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1152665_comment'></div>未详草堂遗编，亦嗣续之孔《易》，乃驻锡辇毂，依止王臣，购求亡逸，载离寒暑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1152665_comment'></div>自饮光尊者讫法眼之嗣，因枝振叶，寻波讨源。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1152665_comment'></div>乃至语句之对酬，机缘之契合，靡不包举，无所漏脱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1152665_comment'></div>孜孜纂集，成二十卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1152665_comment'></div>理有未显，加东里润色之言；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1152665_comment'></div>词或不安，用《春秋》笔削之体。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1152665_comment'></div>或但存名号，而蔑有事迹者，亦犹乎《史记》之阙文；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1152665_comment'></div>或兼采歌颂，附出编联者，颇类夫载籍之广记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1152665_comment'></div>大矣哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1152665_comment'></div>禅师之用心，盖述而不作者矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1152665_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1152665_comment'></div>法界无际，众生无边。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1152665_comment'></div>凡厥有情，莫非同体。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1152665_comment'></div>终日圆觉，触目真如，而迷失妙明，增长虚妄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1152665_comment'></div>分别影事，牵制于六尘；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1152665_comment'></div>积集苦因，流浪于三有。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1152665_comment'></div>善知识悯其如是也，不历事相，直指本源。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1152665_comment'></div>但一念不生，即三际俱断；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1152665_comment'></div>十方消殒，诸圣现前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1152665_comment'></div>识珠在衣，匪从他得；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1152665_comment'></div>如金出矿，岂复重为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1152665_comment'></div>圆顿之门，妙如此矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1152665_comment'></div>稽所證之道，然后知原师也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1152665_comment'></div>生如来家，真法王子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1152665_comment'></div>究所诠之理，然后明斯集也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1152665_comment'></div>了第一义，真最上乘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1152665_comment'></div>当使末法之年，初心之类，去圣逾远，开卷得解。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1152665_comment'></div>一弹指顷，齐肩古佛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1152665_comment'></div>不起于座，入般涅槃，虽利益之若斯，于灭度而无取。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1152665_comment'></div>即知施七宝而满刹土，徒为漏业之资；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1152665_comment'></div>化二乘而等河沙，适重败根之罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1152665_comment'></div>师之法施，岂思议之所及哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1152665_comment'></div>新集既成，咨予为序。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1152665_comment'></div>辄摭梗概，冠于篇首云耳。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_69_1152665'></div><div id='poem_sentence_69_1152665_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1004&endYear=1004')">1004年</a>　约于本年，有诗送钱易赴蕲州通判，并称其诗有太白骨。作品：钱易赴蕲春。<div id='poem_129368' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_129368' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/129368?labeling=true' target='_blank'>钱易赴蕲春</a><span class='authorDate'>（1004年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_129368")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_129368_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_129368'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_129368'>名重星垣试，官閒月寺中。<div id='poem_sentence_0_129368_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_129368'>竹符千里郡，花浪一帆风。<div id='poem_sentence_1_129368_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_129368'>尘隙驹从度，霞觞酒莫空。<div id='poem_sentence_2_129368_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_129368'>公堂封笔冢，邮舍递诗筒。<div id='poem_sentence_3_129368_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_129368'>骚客休怀楚，词臣合荐雄。<div id='poem_sentence_4_129368_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_129368'>长庚谪仙骨，须入抃鳌宫。<div id='poem_sentence_5_129368_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_129368'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_129368_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1004&endYear=1004')">1004年</a>　约本年前后，遍览前代名公诗集，独爱李商隐，以为有无穷味；由是孜孜求访，得五百八十二首，后人夸传于书林文苑。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1004&endYear=1004')">1004年</a>　又手录李商隐诗数十首，真迹为后世所宝。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1005&endYear=1005')">1005年1月</a>　右谏议大夫潘慎修卒，亿为撰墓志铭。作品：宋故翰林侍读学士朝奉大夫右谏议大夫骑都尉赐紫金鱼袋荥阳潘公墓志铭。<div id='poem_1152703' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152703' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152703?labeling=true' target='_blank'>宋故翰林侍读学士朝奉大夫右谏议大夫骑都尉赐紫金鱼袋荥阳潘公墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1005年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152703")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152703_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152703'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152703'>咸平初，天子端委穆清，顺考故道，思近耆德，乐闻话言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152703_comment'></div>于是徵汉代金华之旧闻，考唐室翰林之故事，特置侍讲学士之职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152703_comment'></div>时予从祖七兵尚书、故户部夏侯贰卿、今侍郎河间邢公、中丞吕公，并预兹选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152703_comment'></div>后三岁，今丞相毕公自上党驿召，既至，即以命之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152703_comment'></div>又再岁，自郎署擢河南潘公为谏议大夫，授以兹任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152703_comment'></div>八年之间，六人而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152703_comment'></div>公亦既拜命，人无间言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152703_comment'></div>时属天骄犯边，军烽日警。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1152703_comment'></div>天子将躬秉武节，展义两河，而公以肃乂之姿，处切近之地，旰朝备问，言多沃心，中涓谕旨，退必削槁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1152703_comment'></div>及舆驾薄伐，勤劳扈从，昼骖乘于襄野，夕宿卫于勾陈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1152703_comment'></div>从羽猎于储胥，陪玉食于云󷕚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1152703_comment'></div>蒙犯霜霰，因而遘疾，犹亲奉宸旨，致祭洪河，沈璧浮牲，精意恳恻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1152703_comment'></div>及复命行在，移幸澶渊，晨趋暮召，夙夜匪懈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1152703_comment'></div>中乾愈甚，束带不任，中人国医，存省相继。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1152703_comment'></div>嘉言入奏，启沃未忘；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1152703_comment'></div>美疹渐滋，皇慈弥渥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1152703_comment'></div>特奉明旨，先还上都。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1152703_comment'></div>肩舁启行，邮亭先置。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1152703_comment'></div>星言夙驾，有加无瘳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1152703_comment'></div>及旅凯班旋，膏肓沉痼，精爽将竭，方寸不乱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1152703_comment'></div>月正元日，殆于弥留，犹召故人，执手为别。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1152703_comment'></div>且占遗奏，不令托孤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1152703_comment'></div>叹逝者之如斯，痛主恩之未报，言讫瞑目，至夕奄然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1152703_comment'></div>皇上轸悼良臣，赗襚加等，以其子太庙斋郎汝士为大理评事，正字汝砺为太常奉礼，咸赋以禄，俾之终丧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1152703_comment'></div>又诏有司，给方舟载甚柩，归葬豫章，从遗志也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1152703_comment'></div>恩礼之厚，无以为比。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1152703_comment'></div>公讳慎修，字成德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1152703_comment'></div>其先荥阳中牟人，唐末避乱，迁于闽粤，治产作业，遂为著姓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1152703_comment'></div>当王氏之偏霸也，曾祖武源，以丘园之秀预弓旌之招，受署福州古田令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1152703_comment'></div>祖宗裔，种德务滋，怀才不试，世难方棘，肥遁终身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1152703_comment'></div>烈考承佑，属云雷之遘屯，负公台之伟量，尝仕吴为蕲州法曹掾，郡守以非法致死罪，抗议不夺，投手版而归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1152703_comment'></div>王延政据建安，且欲倚以为相。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1152703_comment'></div>时阋墙结衅，寻戈继日，引经义而廷诤，因禁锢而家居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1152703_comment'></div>江南平建州，若得剧孟之一敌国也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1152703_comment'></div>累服大僚，专掌剧务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1152703_comment'></div>辞荣致政，得刑部尚书，归隐洪州之西山，优游没齿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1152703_comment'></div>妣清河张氏，以从夫之贵，封本郡君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1152703_comment'></div>而公之显祖，赠太常少卿；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1152703_comment'></div>祖妣，河间邢氏，封本县太君，皆由尚书之故也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1152703_comment'></div>公少负俊才，习闻义训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1152703_comment'></div>观书学剑，包文武以兼资；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1152703_comment'></div>点漆凝脂，越风尘而特秀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1152703_comment'></div>才十馀岁，随先尚书归金陵，得秘书省正字。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1152703_comment'></div>岁满，迁校书郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1152703_comment'></div>未几，入省为水部员外郎，赐五品服，才冠岁矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1152703_comment'></div>俄迁膳部。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1152703_comment'></div>先府君悬车告老，公求便官就养，得知洪州丰城县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1152703_comment'></div>岁馀，以忧解职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1152703_comment'></div>卒哭，起复旧官，改上元令，以刑部员外郎知杂，赐服金紫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1152703_comment'></div>执法甚平，持宪尤肃，江右耆旧，至今称之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1152703_comment'></div>除水部郎中兼起居舍人，判待制院，领郡国之上书，评诸曹之奏议，盖一时之剧任也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1152703_comment'></div>开宝末，蚩尤之旗亘天，龙骧之师渡水。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1152703_comment'></div>公将危邦之命，以市宴为名，使交兵之间，履不测之险。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1152703_comment'></div>既陈土贡于宰旅，且留别馆于都亭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1152703_comment'></div>时后主先命同气之亲，来谢不朝之罪，羁縻未遣，休戚攸同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1152703_comment'></div>王师所加，捷音继至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1152703_comment'></div>金汤失守，固宗国之将亡；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1152703_comment'></div>玉帛旅庭，齿外臣而致贺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1152703_comment'></div>邸吏惧其后至，所司督其不供，公慨然抗义，以为不可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1152703_comment'></div>每内朝称庆，但拜章待罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1152703_comment'></div>太祖重其知礼，嘉其有辞，特遣贵臣，亲谕上旨，改命供帐，增给饩牵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1152703_comment'></div>及青盖来朝，朱扉赐第，太祖以公质性忠厚，特授太子右赞善大夫，俾事故君，是为上介。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1152703_comment'></div>思乔木于故国，尚见世臣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1152703_comment'></div>曳长裾于王门，兼掌记室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1152703_comment'></div>太宗嗣位，以恩例累进阶勋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1152703_comment'></div>后主考终，由府罢，复预朝请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1152703_comment'></div>历太常博士，虞部、仓部、考功三员外郎、郎中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1152703_comment'></div>出通判寿州，知湖州、梓州，凡十年在外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1152703_comment'></div>故邓帅太傅李公典领中秘书，方求硕儒，以充近署，遂引公入直秘阁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1152703_comment'></div>出入交戟，偃息周庐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1152703_comment'></div>刊正遗编，盖手不释卷；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1152703_comment'></div>祗膺清问，必膝之前席。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1152703_comment'></div>善谈名理，言为阳秋；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1152703_comment'></div>勤接士类，心无城府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1152703_comment'></div>江东人物，率执贽以宗予；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1152703_comment'></div>汉庭公卿，多致恭而尚齿，允所谓南州之高士，儒林之丈人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1152703_comment'></div>然自博极群书，优游一纪，素发垂领，仅类郎潜，凝尘满席，不婴世务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1152703_comment'></div>婚嫁未毕，屡求典于方州；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1152703_comment'></div>年德俱高，果入参于近侍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1152703_comment'></div>将记言于惇史，遽归全于厚夜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1152703_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1152703_comment'></div>享年六十九。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1152703_comment'></div>公前娶汝南周氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1152703_comment'></div>今夫人东海徐氏，封本县君，即故中书侍郎、上饶郡君景逊之女也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1152703_comment'></div>建康大姓，连姻戚里，柔怀惠问，宜家睦族。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1152703_comment'></div>俄遘未亡之戚，实深偕老之痛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1152703_comment'></div>率其二子，奉公之丧，归于洪州，祔先尚书之茔，从治命也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1152703_comment'></div>公四子：长玄亮，端拱中举进士，补大名朝城尉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1152703_comment'></div>次玄成，皆早亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1152703_comment'></div>五女：长适福州宁德令邵良弼，次适苏州常熟令岑頔，先公而逝；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1152703_comment'></div>次适兴元府观察推官龚纪；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1152703_comment'></div>次适大理寺丞张安期，故参政刑部侍郎洎之子也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1152703_comment'></div>一尚幼，而许嫁待年而未行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1152703_comment'></div>公风度详闲，襟怀夷旷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1152703_comment'></div>旁通多可，虚受兼容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1152703_comment'></div>雅善棋弈，技臻绝品。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1152703_comment'></div>先皇帝万机之暇，常以方罫自娱，公屡蒙三接之召，亲奉一枰之戏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1152703_comment'></div>退而作《棋说》以献，天子异之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1152703_comment'></div>盖多艺多材，姬公自许；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1152703_comment'></div>执御执射，仲尼之言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1152703_comment'></div>虽馀力之使然，亦天机之独妙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1152703_comment'></div>参掌记注，犹及金匮之阙文；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1152703_comment'></div>屡奉宴游，尝续《柏梁》之高韵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1152703_comment'></div>生平著撰，叠委筐箱，诸郎等方在哀迷，未遑论次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1152703_comment'></div>长卿遗札，冀武皇之见求；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1152703_comment'></div>叔夜孤儿，幸山公之尚在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1152703_comment'></div>永怀旧德，髣髴绪言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1152703_comment'></div>挥涕濡毫，以志陵谷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1152703_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_108_1152703'>全吴之地，缵唐之祀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1152703_comment'></div>公臣旧邦，罔有贰事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1152703_comment'></div>开宝之季，王师摩垒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1152703_comment'></div>公使交兵，兹亦尽瘁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1152703_comment'></div>一心事君，典训攸闻，公之奉上，茂贞纯兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1152703_comment'></div>十年不调，先民是悼，公之为郎，殆华皓兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1152703_comment'></div>西清北门，宴见咨询，簪笔持橐，奉至尊兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1152703_comment'></div>灵旗大辂，徂征赫怒，巾车脂辖，陪天步兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1152703_comment'></div>公已白首，始遘元后，富贵之来，逼蒲柳兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1152703_comment'></div>公践玉堂，入侍圣皇，寒暑之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1152703_comment'></div>在膏肓兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1152703_comment'></div>时不与兮道攸远，志将亨兮命弥蹇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1152703_comment'></div>旅榇归兮春草长，铭旌飘兮白日晚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1152703_comment'></div>瞻冢树兮成行，悲逝川兮不返。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1152703_comment'></div>永赍志兮首丘，长垂名兮汗简。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_122_1152703'></div><div id='poem_sentence_122_1152703_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1005&endYear=1005')">1005年3月</a>　奉敕撰策试草泽刘牧。作品：景德二年三月试草泽刘牧策一。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1005&endYear=1005')">1005年3月</a>　弟倚特赐进士二等及第，有谢表。作品：谢弟倚特赐进士第二等及第表。<div id='poem_1152494' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152494' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152494?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢弟倚特赐进士第二等及第表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1005年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152494")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152494_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152494'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152494'>臣某言：臣亲弟进士倚，伏蒙圣慈，特赐本科第二等及第者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152494_comment'></div>恩出公朝，庆深寒族，感激之至，忭蹈无从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152494_comment'></div>臣某<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>伏念臣爰从幼岁，即丧所天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152494_comment'></div>无负郭之田园，以供糊口；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152494_comment'></div>有既孤之弟妹，俱未成人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152494_comment'></div>世家渐坠于衣缨，旦慕将沦于沟壑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152494_comment'></div>臣是以激昂志节，博涉艺文，割爱游方，出身事主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152494_comment'></div>自神宗之御极，忝仙殿之雠书；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1152494_comment'></div>迹游君子之林，月赋上农之禄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1152494_comment'></div>爰归故里，亲奉安舆，尽挈孤遗，寓居辇毂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1152494_comment'></div>臣弟适当幼稚，早失义方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1152494_comment'></div>春诵夏弦，再亲加于教导；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1152494_comment'></div>羹藜含糗，固均给于有无。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1152494_comment'></div>殆踰既冠之年，辄齿命乡之荐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1152494_comment'></div>春官较艺，幸预奏名；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1152494_comment'></div>日昃临轩，躬承明试。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1152494_comment'></div>方惧吹竽之滥，敢希中鹄之荣？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1152494_comment'></div>尊号皇帝陛下简在宸襟，形于清问，俯念司言之近列，特推延赏之深仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1152494_comment'></div>擢自群伦，置于科级，仍载颁于睿旨，更超践于等夷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1152494_comment'></div>侧听德音，感深骨髓；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1152494_comment'></div>传闻私室，喜动庭闱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1152494_comment'></div>顾同气之至亲，荷自天之殊泽，荣过始望，事出非常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1152494_comment'></div>内省微躯，上衔厚施，非土木之无识，岂不知恩？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1152494_comment'></div>顾龟蛇之甚微，犹能报德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1152494_comment'></div>誓匪躬而自效，庶毕命以为期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1152494_comment'></div>臣无任云云。</div><div id='poem_sentence_25_1152494_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1005&endYear=1005')">1005年</a>　知郑州王矩求科名，特赐进士及第，亿喜作诗贺之。作品：喜王虞部赐进士及第。<div id='poem_129278' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_129278' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/129278?labeling=true' target='_blank'>喜王虞部赐进士及第<span class='inlineComment2'>（时知郑州，奉诏乘驿赴闻喜宴）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1005年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_129278")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1005&endYear=1005')">1005年</a>　三月后，有诗送舅翁章实下第东归。此前后屡有诗送人下第。作品：送章四十舅翁东归。张泌东归。外弟张湜西游。范仪下第东归。章群下第东归。<div id='poem_129232' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_129232' id='poem_sentence_4_129268_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1005&endYear=1005')">1005年4月8日</a>　奖州刺史李继昌上表请以上党旧庐为祠，赐名“承天禅院”，四月八日杨亿为撰记。作品：潞州新敕赐承天禅院记。<div id='poem_1152679' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152679' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152679?labeling=true' target='_blank'>潞州新敕赐承天禅院记</a><span class='authorDate'>（景德二年四月八日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152679")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152679_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152679'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152679'>景德元年冬，天子巡狩澶渊，驻跸河上，始议和戎之利，慎柬使乎之才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152679_comment'></div>乃诏西京左藏库使、蒋州刺史、陇西李公继昌，奉将信币，克成盟好。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152679_comment'></div>复命行在，不逾浃旬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152679_comment'></div>奏事宸居，沃心称旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152679_comment'></div>时黄屋值流虹之庆，帷宫举称觞之典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152679_comment'></div>执玉万国，涂山无后至之刑；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152679_comment'></div>舞羽两阶，灵台有偃兵之议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152679_comment'></div>纯嘏之锡，上帝是赉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1152679_comment'></div>富寿之祝，率土攸同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1152679_comment'></div>公因顿首上言，以上党旧邦，卜居累世，有环堵之室，乃先人之庐，而自参表著于朝内，占名数于京邑，乔木犹在，高台未倾，愿为仁祠，以施开士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1152679_comment'></div>增饰轮奂，肃奉焚修，庶以众善之因，仰助无疆之算。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1152679_comment'></div>上览奏嘉叹，即命俞之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1152679_comment'></div>申锡玺书，旌以懿号，曰「承天禅院」，从其志也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1152679_comment'></div>夫箕裘善继，前典攸称；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1152679_comment'></div>桑梓敬恭，先民所重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1152679_comment'></div>虽知乐之至，不忘所生；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1152679_comment'></div>而似续之贤，由于肯构。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1152679_comment'></div>矧壶关之壤，上应昴毕；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1152679_comment'></div>羊头之阨，北当燕赵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1152679_comment'></div>国俗尚武，人气多豪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1152679_comment'></div>控山东列郡之冲，乃天下劲兵之处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1152679_comment'></div>悲歌慷慨，寖以成风，土厚水深，居之不疾，而公之先正，兹焉挺生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1152679_comment'></div>蕴翁归文武之才，茂荀息忠贞之力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1152679_comment'></div>始事周室，迨于皇朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1152679_comment'></div>功济生民，道合明主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1152679_comment'></div>历计相之剧任，处宣猷之上列，乃至正位机密，允辅大政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1152679_comment'></div>当太祖皇帝夙兴夜寐，经营四方，料敌伐谋，指纵千里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1152679_comment'></div>前席借箸，允集大勋；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1152679_comment'></div>持节建牙，出临巨屏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1152679_comment'></div>功成身退，高朗令终。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1152679_comment'></div>惟公经德体仁，象贤济美，职在清禁，爵为通侯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1152679_comment'></div>门戟鼎铭，昭阀阅之盛；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1152679_comment'></div>朱轓佩玉，显车服之贵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1152679_comment'></div>誓师边徼，威肃巴賨；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1152679_comment'></div>作牧藩垣，政成海岱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1152679_comment'></div>单介使虏，通玉帛之驩；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1152679_comment'></div>三接承恩，居心膂之任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1152679_comment'></div>万乘亲倚，群公倾慕，盖所谓人伦之佳士，帝右之信臣者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1152679_comment'></div>先是，公之载诞，亦在旧居，指树尚存，藏环可验。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1152679_comment'></div>烝尝奉祀，履霜露而长怀；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1152679_comment'></div>井臼思归，顾枌榆而永感。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1152679_comment'></div>然而高扉纳驷，奕叶珥貂，爽垲不迁，亲邻素择。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1152679_comment'></div>褒成徙籍，盖出主恩；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1152679_comment'></div>杨仆移关，敢罹特议？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1152679_comment'></div>且深信内典，勤修白业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1152679_comment'></div>念昊天之罔极，报德无阶；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1152679_comment'></div>繄觉海之大雄，归心有素。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1152679_comment'></div>恭承明诏，肇开净土。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1152679_comment'></div>栋宇之制，侔七宝之庄严；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1152679_comment'></div>苾刍之徒，极四事之供养。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1152679_comment'></div>匠石殚巧，天龙荐祥，金碧炫彩于晨曦，钟梵交音于空界。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1152679_comment'></div>问安之寝，聿为道场；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1152679_comment'></div>学礼之庭，更张法席。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1152679_comment'></div>足以滋殖德本，发挥善利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1152679_comment'></div>香象负重，广集弥天之流；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1152679_comment'></div>水鸟谈空，更同极乐之国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1152679_comment'></div>福祉之盛，岂可量哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1152679_comment'></div>昔者南朝诸公，多割宅而为寺；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1152679_comment'></div>西域长者，竞舍财以供僧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1152679_comment'></div>简策相传，风流未远，贝多所记，报应非虚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1152679_comment'></div>订公之为，斯一致耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1152679_comment'></div>曩者，太尉先生居显位，受厚禄，宠锡蕃庶，私帑充牣，奉身甚约，事佛尤谨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1152679_comment'></div>生平饭僧七十万，造千佛像。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1152679_comment'></div>修绀殿以严宝刹，饰琅函以秘金文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1152679_comment'></div>又以方牍，摹印《金刚》、《上生》等经，施于四众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1152679_comment'></div>山门禅苑，多所缮完；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1152679_comment'></div>什器道具，率用营置。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1152679_comment'></div>深达实相，不滞根尘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1152679_comment'></div>尽此报身，当得解脱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1152679_comment'></div>君子谓李公诒谋锡羡，源深流长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1152679_comment'></div>福履所绥，凡情叵测。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1152679_comment'></div>何只积善馀庆，启八世之莫京；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1152679_comment'></div>定须当来下生，首三会而授记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1152679_comment'></div>父作子述，不其韪欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1152679_comment'></div>予职在右曹，心师西竺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1152679_comment'></div>辱公之请，至于再三。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1152679_comment'></div>僶俛挥毫，以谨岁月而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1152679_comment'></div>时景德二年，岁次乙巳，四月八日记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_77_1152679_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1005&endYear=1005')">1005年4月21日</a>　召赴龙图阁观太宗御书及四库图书，有谢状及应制诗，帝手批答，又有谢状。作品：谢宣召赴龙图阁宴会及观御书状。龙图阁会宴应制。谢批答状。<div id='poem_1152563' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152563' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152563?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢宣召赴龙图阁宴会及观御制御书状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1005年4月21日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152563")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152563_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152563'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152563'>右，臣今月某日，伏蒙圣慈召赴龙图阁，观太宗之御制御书，及圣制碑赞，并四库图书，仍赐御诗，兼预宴会者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152563_comment'></div>上帝藏书，肇开册府；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152563_comment'></div>圣人有作，爰勒金碑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152563_comment'></div>许拭目以荣观，寔扪心而知幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152563_comment'></div>伏惟皇帝陛下顺考古道，启迪人文，执左契以御庶邦，运大钧而播群品。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152563_comment'></div>车书无外，咸归舆地之图；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152563_comment'></div>弓矢载櫜，式开仁寿之域。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152563_comment'></div>而乃讲求前训，润色大猷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1152563_comment'></div>拟石渠、天禄之旧规，聿新层构；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1152563_comment'></div>搜汲冢、羽陵之坠简，并集群言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1152563_comment'></div>敦奉先思孝之心，显继志守文之盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1152563_comment'></div>盖以先朝之述作，为后世之楷模，萃手泽于缣缃，穷笔精于翰墨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1152563_comment'></div>秘宸编于延阁，用垂示于方来；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1152563_comment'></div>奋睿藻于贞珉，式揄扬于盛美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1152563_comment'></div>金石颂德，实旷古之无阶；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1152563_comment'></div>云汉成章，亦群生之共睹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1152563_comment'></div>眷惟近列，首获仰瞻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1152563_comment'></div>侧管窥天，宁测盖高之量；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1152563_comment'></div>闻《韶》忘味，徒萌窃抃之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1152563_comment'></div>矧又赐玉斝之醇醪，示柏梁之绝唱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1152563_comment'></div>饮河之腹，既叹于属厌；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1152563_comment'></div>下俚之音，靡容于缄默。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1152563_comment'></div>并陈巴拙，上黩皇明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1152563_comment'></div>虽蒙善下之仁，终抱黩尊之愧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1152563_comment'></div>内循孱薄，曲荷恩私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1152563_comment'></div>阅东序之图书，奉文思而知幸；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1152563_comment'></div>陪西清之宴豫，沐慈惠以难胜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1152563_comment'></div>唯共誓于糜捐，庶少酬于临照云云<span class='inlineComment2'>（《武夷新集》卷一八。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1152563_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_28_1152563'>云云：原无，据明本补。</div><div id='poem_sentence_28_1152563_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_129061' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_129061' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/129061?labeling=true' target='_blank'>龙图阁会宴应制<span class='inlineComment2'>（景德二年四月二十一日）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1005年4月21日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_129061")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_129061_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_129061'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_129061'>册府藏书在紫微，退朝稽古助论思。<div id='poem_sentence_0_129061_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_129061'>中天召宴衢樽满，乙夜观文列象垂。<div id='poem_sentence_1_129061_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_129061'>䌽凤翩翻巢绮阁，灵龟夭矫冠金碑。<div id='poem_sentence_2_129061_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_129061'>大风发唱群臣和，元首康哉庶绩熙。<div id='poem_sentence_3_129061_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_129061'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_129061_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1152564' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152564' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152564?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢批答状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1005年4月21日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152564")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152564_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152564'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152564'>右，臣近者恭陪镐饮，仰黩乾文，实揣己以知荣，辄拜章而叙感。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152564_comment'></div>猥蒙批答，备极恩私，捧读周旋，庆抃交集。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152564_comment'></div>伏惟皇帝陛下道高列辟，功济中区，体神武以怀柔，法天明而覆帱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152564_comment'></div>抚群生之重畜，朽索居怀；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152564_comment'></div>考历代之元龟，青编在御。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152564_comment'></div>肇新宏搆，总萃前言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152564_comment'></div>先朝之奋藻摛华，并藏麟阁；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152564_comment'></div>圣主之披文相质，高揭龟趺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1152564_comment'></div>因万务之馀间，召诸臣而宴喜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1152564_comment'></div>金简玉字，既容下士之窃窥；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1152564_comment'></div>《白雪》、《阳春》，更许巴人而属和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1152564_comment'></div>仰奉观文之德，荐承饫赐之仁，共庆遭逢，徒深踊跃，爰陈奏牍，虔述寸诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1152564_comment'></div>敢谓陛下浚发睿谟，俯颁优诏，曲形敦谕，倍极恩慈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1152564_comment'></div>演丝为纶，闻圣言而知感；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1152564_comment'></div>摩顶至踵，励臣节以弥坚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1152564_comment'></div>誓毕微生，少酬玄造。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1152564_comment'></div>臣无任云云。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1152564_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1005&endYear=1005')">1005年4月25日</a>　有诗贺王钦若为新置资政殿学士、刑部侍郎。作品：贺资政学士王侍郎。<div id='poem_129223' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_129223' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/129223?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺资政学士王侍郎</a><span class='authorDate'>（1005年4月25日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_129223")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_129223_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_129223'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_129223'>沥恳青规动帝心，秋曹月殿宠光深。<div id='poem_sentence_0_129223_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_129223'>论思东序清閒宴，偃息西昆翰墨林。<div id='poem_sentence_1_129223_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_129223'>私第藏书皆有副，公庭种竹待成阴。<div id='poem_sentence_2_129223_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_129223'>卧龙禁闼应非久，救旱还须起作霖。<div id='poem_sentence_3_129223_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_129223'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_129223_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1005&endYear=1005')">1005年5月</a>　五月，宰相李沆丧将葬，亿为撰墓志铭。作品：宋故推忠协谋佐理功臣光禄大夫尚书左仆射兼门下侍郎同中书门下平章事监修国史上柱国陇西郡开国公食邑三千八百户食实封一千二百户赠太尉中书令谥曰文靖李公墓志铭。<div id='poem_1152704' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152704' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152704?labeling=true' target='_blank'>宋故推忠协谋佐理功臣光禄大夫尚书左仆射兼门下侍郎同中书门下平章事监修国史上柱国陇西郡开国公食邑三千八百户食实封一千二百户赠太尉中书令谥曰文靖李公墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1005年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152704")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152704_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152704'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152704'>景德元年秋七月乙酉，大丞相、仆射陇西公早朝至待漏舍，不俟钥出而归，疾故也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152704_comment'></div>粤翌日，车驾幸其第，亲至卧内，存抚甚厚，赐白金三百斤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152704_comment'></div>既还宫，以不起闻，上又临哭出涕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152704_comment'></div>初，公之疾也，中人、太医，络绎旁午于道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152704_comment'></div>迨公之薨也，千乘万骑，一日再幸其居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152704_comment'></div>国殒宗臣，帝失元辅，都城为之罢市，功女以之寝机。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152704_comment'></div>同体既亏，实太上之深戚；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152704_comment'></div>斯文将丧，顾天下而谁宗？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1152704_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1152704_comment'></div>真古之遗爱也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1152704_comment'></div>公讳沆，字太初，其先赵郡人，广武君之后也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1152704_comment'></div>策书所载，世德茂焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1152704_comment'></div>泰陵令、累赠侍中丰，追封虢国太夫人滕氏，曾祖父母也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1152704_comment'></div>洺州团练判官、累赠中书令滔，追封鲁国太夫人苗氏，王父母也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1152704_comment'></div>侍御史、累赠尚书令炳，追封陈国太夫人周氏，考妣也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1152704_comment'></div>公韵宇宏廓，襟灵冲粹，特资异禀，卓然不群。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1152704_comment'></div>甫及成童，性靡好弄；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1152704_comment'></div>逮于就傅，言必有章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1152704_comment'></div>七岁能属文，十岁通五经大义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1152704_comment'></div>服膺素业，既冠而大成；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1152704_comment'></div>比肩诸生，命乡而高荐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1152704_comment'></div>时春官氏方虚甲科以待，属丁先府君之忧，自大梁而抵群舒，几二千里，见星泣血，哀感道涂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1152704_comment'></div>食鬻倚庐，毁深栾棘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1152704_comment'></div>先府君历佐使府、及剖郡符，徇公灭私，轻财好施，以经遗子，市义于人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1152704_comment'></div>暨启手之辰，无兼金之蓄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1152704_comment'></div>公承清白之训，持穷绝之家，有原宪贫病之忧，茂张仲孝友之德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1152704_comment'></div>太平兴国五年，举进士得高弟，解褐将作监丞、通判潭州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1152704_comment'></div>郊祀，迁太子右赞善大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1152704_comment'></div>八年，归朝为著作郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1152704_comment'></div>当是时也，天子方端委穆清，详求茂异，崇建册府，养育人材。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1152704_comment'></div>公之莅长沙也，椒兰之德在人，金玉之音盈耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1152704_comment'></div>輶轩密启，外台陟状，稔熟于上听，喧塞于公议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1152704_comment'></div>中谢日，太宗命中贵人送丞相府试文一通，以本官直史馆，赐五品服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1152704_comment'></div>雍熙中，今工部尚书王公化基任左拾遗，上封公车，大言自荐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1152704_comment'></div>太宗谓执政曰：「李沆、宋湜，皆佳士也，可并试之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1152704_comment'></div>明日，并命为右补阙、知制诰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1152704_comment'></div>公之位在二公之次，上特令公首冠焉，又赐钱百万。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1152704_comment'></div>天子知公贫，多权钱富家，出倍称之息，又别赐三十万，俾偿之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1152704_comment'></div>端拱初，迁职方员外郎，掌诰如故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1152704_comment'></div>来年，受诏与今学士承旨、礼部尚书宋公白同知贡举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1152704_comment'></div>是时，天子始命复旧制，委有司，贡部翕然，有得人之誉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1152704_comment'></div>未几，召入翰林充学士，赐金紫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1152704_comment'></div>又奉诏与今丞相上谷公同掌选部，澄汰流品，旌别淑慝，清通简要，时誉归之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1152704_comment'></div>公之在内署也，或乙夜观书之馀，备前席受釐之问，风规酝藉，占对娴雅，弼违献可，上多沃心，称善举能，言皆有味。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1152704_comment'></div>天子知其才可以缉熙帝载，察其德可以镇厚风俗，乃有意于大用也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1152704_comment'></div>淳化二年，拜给事中、参知政事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1152704_comment'></div>是时，天子方循名实以考百揆，谨吏事而责三公，公励翼一心，将明庶政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1152704_comment'></div>水潦近止，闾阎息愁叹之声；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1152704_comment'></div>名器有伦，搢绅绝侥倖之路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1152704_comment'></div>弥缝阙职，汔至小康。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1152704_comment'></div>俄罢政事，以本官奉朝请，虽坐策免，时望弥重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1152704_comment'></div>未几，丁太夫人忧，柴毁过礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1152704_comment'></div>先是，公疏戚同居，功缌百口。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1152704_comment'></div>昆弟致美，家人忘贫；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1152704_comment'></div>赋禄虽优，量入都尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1152704_comment'></div>及罢枢务，复罹哀疢，居丧尽礼，送终竭力，殆于食贫，曾不屑虑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1152704_comment'></div>优诏起复，辞不复请，俄以本官知升州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1152704_comment'></div>因奉玺书，请对便坐，天子留而不遣，改命知河南府、兼留守司事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1152704_comment'></div>二周变风，期月报政，才及满岁，召归阙庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1152704_comment'></div>属光启承华，克固邦本，畴咨羽翼，辅导元良，即以公为礼部侍郎兼太子宾客。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1152704_comment'></div>特诏宾护之职，一用师傅之礼，仍屈储君之重，先施下拜之仪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1152704_comment'></div>公请见顿首，辞不获免。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1152704_comment'></div>皇上践极，拜户部侍郎、参知政事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1152704_comment'></div>未几，以本官平章事、监修国史，进位中书侍郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1152704_comment'></div>属鸣镝犯边，翠华薄伐，居守之任，根本斯系。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1152704_comment'></div>关中图籍，委酂侯以无疑；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1152704_comment'></div>东郊保釐，非毕公之为比。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1152704_comment'></div>上亲握武节，躬御六师，北涉大河，驻跸全魏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1152704_comment'></div>劳军而连营贾勇，展义而编氓案堵，胡马引去，边尘载清，无有南顾之忧，克定一戎之业者，繄公之力也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1152704_comment'></div>公亦坐镇京邑，兼容狱市，令行禁止，不戮一人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1152704_comment'></div>千门万户，曾无吠犬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1152704_comment'></div>及銮辂恺旋，谒见行在，置酒幄殿，奉觞上寿，劳问优缛，体貌尤异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1152704_comment'></div>清中除道，奉迎至尊，同德一心，光辅大政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1152704_comment'></div>来年，进位门下侍郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1152704_comment'></div>属有事南郊，加尚书右仆射，馀如故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1152704_comment'></div>公践师长之秩，处丞弼之地，属西北二鄙，金革未息，伐谋制胜，实赖前筹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1152704_comment'></div>调发军输，曾不暇给，当宁靡宁于旰食，宰府专职于忧边。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1152704_comment'></div>公夙夜自公，憔悴事国，任重责大，智困神疲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1152704_comment'></div>休浣在辰，稀得出沐；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1152704_comment'></div>腠理徵疹，不敢宁居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1152704_comment'></div>筋力渐衰，精爽坐竭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1152704_comment'></div>岑江陵之尽瘁，天子先忧；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1152704_comment'></div>张司空之云亡，星文告变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1152704_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1152704_comment'></div>享年五十有八。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1152704_comment'></div>诏辍视朝五日，赠太尉、中书令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1152704_comment'></div>上又别次发哀，群臣奉慰，追录嗣子，逮于周亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1152704_comment'></div>乃至外姻诸甥，常从给使，咸被延赏之泽，悉膺非次之命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1152704_comment'></div>又特命昭宣使、恩州团练使李公神福，监视葬事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1152704_comment'></div>太常考行，谥曰「文靖」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1152704_comment'></div>发引之日，有司具卤簿，大鸿胪持节护丧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1152704_comment'></div>即以今年五月庚申，归葬于河南府洛阳县贤相乡积润里，从尚书令府君之茔，礼也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1152704_comment'></div>公积阶至光禄大夫，策勋上柱国，三进爵为公，真食至千二百户。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1152704_comment'></div>功臣之号，凡再加焉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1152704_comment'></div>禄位宠名，皆人臣之极也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1152704_comment'></div>前娶清河张氏，永兴军司马忠辅之女。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1152704_comment'></div>生一子，曰翁朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1152704_comment'></div>三女：长适右谏议大夫薛映；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1152704_comment'></div>次适奉礼向传正，相国河内公之子也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1152704_comment'></div>次数岁而夭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1152704_comment'></div>及公之薨，张夫人之所生无复存者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1152704_comment'></div>今夫人沛国朱氏，累封越国夫人，故太常少卿致仕、累赠工部侍郎洞之女。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1152704_comment'></div>嫔于台宰，宜其室家，作范中闱，启封大国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1152704_comment'></div>齐眉举案，礼极如宾，昼哭帷堂，痛深偕老。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1152704_comment'></div>生四子：三皆早夭；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1152704_comment'></div>幼曰宗简，大理评事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1152704_comment'></div>五女：长适著作郎、直史馆王曾，执丧过哀，遇疾而逝；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1152704_comment'></div>次皆幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1152704_comment'></div>公三弟，曰贽，虞部员外郎、知洛阳县，陈力就列，负适时之才；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1152704_comment'></div>曰源，太子中舍，裕蛊亢宗，真保家之主；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1152704_comment'></div>曰维，户部员外郎、直集贤院，文行第一，见推朝论，克荷世家，允为国器。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1152704_comment'></div>公风鉴融朗，天性谨厚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1152704_comment'></div>自结发为学，靡杂尘游；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1152704_comment'></div>虽燕居慎独，如临宾祭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1152704_comment'></div>视童无诳，处闇罔欺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1152704_comment'></div>韦编屡绝，不阅非圣之典；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1152704_comment'></div>束带未既，不答严君之召。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1152704_comment'></div>先府君常语人曰：「此儿异日必至公辅」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1152704_comment'></div>知子之明，盖无愧矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1152704_comment'></div>及计偕续食，发策决科，引籍周行，通直延阁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1152704_comment'></div>水怀珠而川媚，林养栋以材成，繇是升右掖以司言，入内庭而待诏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1152704_comment'></div>五代已还，文体一变，至于雅诰，殊未复古。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1152704_comment'></div>公之书命也，启迪前训，润色鸿业，善为辞令，长于著书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1152704_comment'></div>考三代之质文，取两汉之标格，使国朝谟训，与元和、长庆同风者，繄公之故也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1152704_comment'></div>及参贰政柄，弥纶事典，守正持重，不务将迎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1152704_comment'></div>出莅锁闱，恪居官次，靖恭夙夜，曾无澄挠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1152704_comment'></div>尹正西洛，茂宣恺悌之风；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1152704_comment'></div>调护东朝，助成明两之德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1152704_comment'></div>暨再掌钧轴，正位岩廊，斟酌治体，辨论官材，人斯具瞻，帝用亲倚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1152704_comment'></div>谋事补阙，夜思昼行，纳诲尽规，有犯无隐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1152704_comment'></div>深识大体，务行故事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1152704_comment'></div>终年公府，未尝案吏；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1152704_comment'></div>退食私第，靡有谢宾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1152704_comment'></div>加以慎默寡言，执直无矫，百执延见，多虚往而实归，两府论议，必守经而据古。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1152704_comment'></div>将顺归美，而不喜诡随；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1152704_comment'></div>夕惕补过，而深惩满假。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1152704_comment'></div>兹所谓皇家之柱石，神化之丹青也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1152704_comment'></div>至如喜怒不形，进退可度，陟降尽室，尺寸靡差。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1152704_comment'></div>吐呕车茵，醉饱必恕，赋禄虽厚，奉身甚薄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1152704_comment'></div>万钱之入，周急屡空；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1152704_comment'></div>数亩之居，偪下已甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1152704_comment'></div>不问家事，不恤人言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1152704_comment'></div>畴昔交游，淡水之情无改；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1152704_comment'></div>平生恩德，一饭之报不忘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1152704_comment'></div>性绝玩好，专聚图籍，孜孜缮写，躬自雠对。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1152704_comment'></div>崇奉内典，洞晓真谛，每燕居静虑，深念无生，旁行四句，堆案盈几。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1152704_comment'></div>雅善笔札，特臻其妙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1152704_comment'></div>尝所著述，遗橐颇多，季弟维，论次编联成二十卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_147_1152704_comment'></div>立言不朽，其在兹乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_148_1152704_comment'></div>诸弟等以某为相府舍人，多历年所，钦奉全德，饱闻绪言，见徵铭篆之词，以防陵谷之变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_149_1152704_comment'></div>某早在荐绅之末，特蒙国士之知，虽年辈相辽，位貌非等，更仆之论，固尝莫逆于心，沉石之文，庶几传信乎后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_150_1152704_comment'></div>是为实录，谅无愧焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_151_1152704_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_152_1152704'>圣作物睹，帝赉元辅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_152_1152704_comment'></div>如鼎三足，犹天八柱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_153_1152704_comment'></div>翊宣大猷，康济庶务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_154_1152704_comment'></div>衮职有阙，仲山是补。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_155_1152704_comment'></div>显允相国，光弼大君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_156_1152704_comment'></div>谟明亮采，师古经文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_157_1152704_comment'></div>道类矢直，政无丝棼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_158_1152704_comment'></div>百工时乂，九流洞分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_159_1152704_comment'></div>公德如风，孰不霍靡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_160_1152704_comment'></div>公言如兰，人斯服媚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_161_1152704_comment'></div>文成典谟，学探《象》《系》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_162_1152704_comment'></div>呜呼彼苍，胡不慭遗？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_163_1152704_comment'></div>公心如秤，重轻诚悬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_164_1152704_comment'></div>公道犹龙，钻仰弥坚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_165_1152704_comment'></div>功熙帝载，识穷化源。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_166_1152704_comment'></div>哀哉哲人，胡不永年，它人蹄涔，可以揭厉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_167_1152704_comment'></div>公陂万顷，涵泳无际。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_168_1152704_comment'></div>它人垝垣，殆见室家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_169_1152704_comment'></div>公墙数仞，德音孔遐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_170_1152704_comment'></div>公掌大钧，平章百揆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_171_1152704_comment'></div>思职忧边，匪躬尽瘁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_172_1152704_comment'></div>哲人其萎，二竖生沴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_173_1152704_comment'></div>桃茢临丧，礼优赗襚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_174_1152704_comment'></div>公辅大政，高朗令终。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_175_1152704_comment'></div>易名赠秩，褒德显庸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_176_1152704_comment'></div>十世犹宥，九原启封。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_177_1152704_comment'></div>卤簿赐葬，都城辍舂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_178_1152704_comment'></div>马悲鸣兮车结辙，弩矢驱兮班剑列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_179_1152704_comment'></div>灵輀驾兮祖奠彻，铭旌飘兮楚挽咽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_180_1152704_comment'></div>伊人生之共尽兮，唯大名兮不灭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_181_1152704_comment'></div>邙之麓兮洛之涯，泉台阒兮陇树微。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_182_1152704_comment'></div>宿草短兮朝露晞，苍烟暝兮夕鸟飞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_183_1152704_comment'></div>茍逝者之可作兮，非我公兮曷归？</div><div id='poem_sentence_184_1152704_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1005&endYear=1005')">1005年5月10日</a>　帝作《乾坤宝典序》，赐群臣，亿代中书撰谢状。作品：代中书谢赐乾坤宝典序状。<div id='poem_1152565' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152565' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152565?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代中书谢赐圣制乾坤宝典序状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1005年5月10日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152565")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152565_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152565'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152565'>右，臣今日中使至，伏蒙圣慈赐臣等御制《乾坤宝典序》各一本者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152565_comment'></div>星使俯临，宸章下赐，莫窥玄远，徒极欢呼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152565_comment'></div>窃以颁历授时，前王之令典；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152565_comment'></div>观文察变，大《易》之格言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152565_comment'></div>故璇玑齐政于有虞，铜浑设象于东汉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152565_comment'></div>珠连璧合，定疏密于诸家；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152565_comment'></div>夏造商因，分指归于三统。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152565_comment'></div>是以阴阳之学，著于九流；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1152565_comment'></div>羲和之官，列于百执。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1152565_comment'></div>历代而下，何莫由兹？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1152565_comment'></div>然而象纬之文，颇多脱简，星历之史，罕或研精。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1152565_comment'></div>金匮、石室之中，既纷纶而无纪；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1152565_comment'></div>宣夜、浑天之术，亦涉猎以非工。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1152565_comment'></div>允属钦明，畴咨古训，聿脩茂典，光集大猷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1152565_comment'></div>伏惟皇帝陛下道迈帝先，智周物表，自天攸纵，将圣多能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1152565_comment'></div>执古御今，视八方于指掌；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1152565_comment'></div>穷神知变，韬万化于襟灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1152565_comment'></div>而乃惧司历之失官，虑畴人之废业，尽搜亡逸，大补阙遗，分别部居，刊正讹谬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1152565_comment'></div>与乾坤而𦜩合，肇建嘉名；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1152565_comment'></div>法云汉以成章，更抒睿藻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1152565_comment'></div>诞扬能事，式冠首篇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1152565_comment'></div>臣等数日前被召穆清，获亲册府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1152565_comment'></div>幸睹圣人之述作，寔为后世之楷模，辄祈副本以颁宣，庶遂洗心而披绎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1152565_comment'></div>敢谓俯从人欲，曲允下情！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1152565_comment'></div>卿云发祥，已窃窥于凡目；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1152565_comment'></div>玉牒不秘，更传宝于私门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1152565_comment'></div>内惟懵昧之姿，得味渊冲之旨，瞻天莫测，游圣无阶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1152565_comment'></div>仰法穹旻，见勋、华之稽古；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1152565_comment'></div>奉传简策，有南、董之当官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1152565_comment'></div>伏望宣付史臣，播于直笔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1152565_comment'></div>岂独臣等幸甚，实亦天下幸甚！</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_30_1152565'></div><div id='poem_sentence_30_1152565_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1005&endYear=1005')">1005年9月22日</a>　受诏与王钦若修《历代君臣事迹》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1005&endYear=1005')">1005年9月22日</a>　受诏修《历代君臣事迹》，有诗述怀感事。刘筠和之。作品：受诏修书述怀感事三十韵。<div id='poem_129363' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_129363' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/129363?labeling=true' target='_blank'>受诏修书述怀感事三十韵</a><span class='authorDate'>（1005年9月22日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_129363")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_129363_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_129363'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_129363'>太极垂裳日，中原偃革初。<div id='poem_sentence_0_129363_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_129363'>楼船秋发咏，衡石夜程书。<div id='poem_sentence_1_129363_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_129363'>好问虚前席，徵贤走传车。<div id='poem_sentence_2_129363_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_129363'>蓬莱侔汉制，煨烬访秦馀。<div id='poem_sentence_3_129363_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_129363'>䌷绎资金匮，规模出<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_129363", 129363, "Clauses/9/Comments/0")'>玉除</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_4_129363_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_129363'>纷纶开四部，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_129363", 129363, "Clauses/11/Comments/0")'>秘邃</span>接千庐。<div id='poem_sentence_5_129363_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_129363'>饫赐双鸡膳，亲回六尺舆。<div id='poem_sentence_6_129363_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_129363'>华芝下阊阖，白羽拥储胥。<div id='poem_sentence_7_129363_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_129363'>望气成龙虎，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_129363", 129363, "Clauses/17/Comments/0")'>披文</span>辩<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_129363", 129363, "Clauses/17/Comments/1")'>鲁鱼</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_8_129363_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_129363'>清光无咫尺，玄览亦踌躇。<div id='poem_sentence_9_129363_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_129363'>群彦挥铅笔，微生滥石渠。<div id='poem_sentence_10_129363_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_129363'>嵇康真懒慢，谢客本<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_11_129363", 129363, "Clauses/23/Comments/0")'>空疏</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_11_129363_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_129363'>讲学情田埆，谈经<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_12_129363", 129363, "Clauses/25/Comments/0")'>腹笥</span>虚。<div id='poem_sentence_12_129363_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_129363'>月评依许劭，文体慕相如。<div id='poem_sentence_13_129363_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_129363'>雅饮欢娱洽，清言鄙吝祛。<div id='poem_sentence_14_129363_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_129363'>弥旬容<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_15_129363", 129363, "Clauses/30/Comments/0")'>出沐</span>，终日喜群居。<div id='poem_sentence_15_129363_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_129363'>抚已惭<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_16_129363", 129363, "Clauses/32/Comments/0")'>鸣玉</span>，归田忆荷锄。<div id='poem_sentence_16_129363_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_129363'>池笼养鱼鸟，章服裹猿狙。<div id='poem_sentence_17_129363_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_129363'>圜府愁尸禄，天阍愧弊裾。<div id='poem_sentence_18_129363_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_129363'>虚名同<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_19_129363", 129363, "Clauses/38/Comments/0")'>郑璞</span>，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_19_129363", 129363, "Clauses/39/Comments/0")'>散质</span>类<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_19_129363", 129363, "Clauses/39/Comments/1")'>庄樗</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_19_129363_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_129363'>国士谁知我，邻家或侮予。<div id='poem_sentence_20_129363_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_129363'>放怀齐指马，屏息度<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_21_129363", 129363, "Clauses/43/Comments/0")'>羲舒</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_21_129363_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_129363'>寡妇宜忧纬，三公亦灌蔬。<div id='poem_sentence_22_129363_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_129363'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_23_129363", 129363, "Clauses/46/Comments/0")'>危心</span>惟觳觫，直道忍蘧蒢。<div id='poem_sentence_23_129363_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_129363'>往圣容巢许，先儒美宁蘧。<div id='poem_sentence_24_129363_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_129363'>晨趋叹<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_25_129363", 129363, "Clauses/50/Comments/0")'>劳止</span>，夕惕念归与。<div id='poem_sentence_25_129363_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_26_129363'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_26_129363", 129363, "Clauses/52/Comments/0")'>秦痔</span>疏杯酒，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_26_129363", 129363, "Clauses/53/Comments/0")'>颜瓢</span>赖斗储。<div id='poem_sentence_26_129363_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_27_129363'>如谐曲肱卧，犹可直钩渔。<div id='poem_sentence_27_129363_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_28_129363'>矫矫龟衔印，翩翩隼画旟。<div id='poem_sentence_28_129363_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_29_129363'>一麾终<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_29_129363", 129363, "Clauses/58/Comments/0")'>遂志</span>，阮籍去骑驴。<div id='poem_sentence_29_129363_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_30_129363'></div><div id='poem_sentence_30_129363_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1005&endYear=1005')">1005年</a>　秋，有诗送章頔宰巴陵。作品：送章頔寺丞之巴陵。<div id='poem_129234' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_129234' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/129234?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送章頔寺丞之巴陵</a><span class='authorDate'>（1005年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_129234")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_129234_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_129234'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_129234'>涔阳从事有嘉声，外计封章荐姓名。<div id='poem_sentence_0_129234_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_129234'>再命便为千室宰，于飞又出九重城。<div id='poem_sentence_1_129234_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_129234'>腰悬铜墨才犹屈，吟对江山思转清。<div id='poem_sentence_2_129234_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_129234'>楚客十年偏遂意，秋风满箸紫莼羹。<div id='poem_sentence_3_129234_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_129234'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_129234_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1005&endYear=1005')">1005年</a>　秋，有诗送章频宰南昌。<div id='poem_129269' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_129269' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/129269?labeling=true' target='_blank'>章频宰<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup>南昌</a><span class='authorDate'>（1005年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_129269")'>杨亿</a></span><br class='poemContent' id='poem_content_129269'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_129269'>孺亭洪井古南昌，曾是梅仙试吏乡。<div id='poem_sentence_0_129269_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_129269'>一邑弦歌荣制锦，几程鸡犬接维桑。<div id='poem_sentence_1_129269_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_129269'>年深为客貂裘敝，秋晚还家菊径荒。<div id='poem_sentence_2_129269_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_129269'>平昔题桥今遂志，且斟寿酒献高堂。<div id='poem_sentence_3_129269_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_129269'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_129269_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1005&endYear=1005')">1005年</a>　表弟章得象知玉山县，有诗送之。县为亿出生地，因言及之。作品：表弟廷评章得象知信州玉山县。<div id='poem_129192' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_129192' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/129192?labeling=true' target='_blank'>表弟廷评章得象知信州玉山县</a><span class='authorDate'>（1005年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a class='poemContent' id='poem_content_129192'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_129192'>怀玉烟霞接武夷，我思祖德涕沾衣。<div id='poem_sentence_0_129192_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1005&endYear=1005')">1005年</a>　梁鼎自洛阳寄诗言志，酬之。作品：梁大谏自凤翔乞留台寄诗言志次韵酬之。<div id='poem_129427' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_129427' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_content_129427'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_129427'>联飞仙掖旧心朋<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：子云云朋而不心，面朋也。）</span>，笑我池笼出未能。<div id='poem_sentence_0_129427_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_129427'>文陛彯缨空自愧，香山蜡屐与谁登。<div id='poem_sentence_1_129427_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1005&endYear=1005')">1005年</a>　元奉宗进士甲科及第，授绩溪县令，亿有诗送之。作品：元奉宗宰绩溪。<div id='poem_129024' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_129024' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a
