id='poem_sentence_4_129024'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_129024_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1005&endYear=1005')">1005年</a>　故人吴待问赴蒙城主簿任，有诗送之。作品：吴待问之蒙城簿。<div id='poem_129130' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_129130' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/129130?labeling=true' target='_blank'>吴待问之蒙城簿</a><span class='authorDate'>（1005年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_129130")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_129130_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_129130'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_129130'>西来赴调合关繻，黄绶风尘厌九衢。<div id='poem_sentence_0_129130_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_129130'>祖席且同开口笑，公庭未免折腰趋。<div id='poem_sentence_1_129130_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_129130'>长安车马偏欺客，鲁国衣冠肯戏儒。<div id='poem_sentence_2_129130_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_129130'>共忆故园归计晚，旧游烟树隔重湖。<div id='poem_sentence_3_129130_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_129130'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_129130_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1005&endYear=1005')">1005年</a>　有诗送杨覃出知潭州。作品：从叔郎中知潭州。<div id='poem_129310' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_129310' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/129310?labeling=true' target='_blank'>从叔郎中知潭州</a><span class='authorDate'>（1005年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_129310")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_129310_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_129310'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_129310'>藩阃分忧重，关山去路赊。<div id='poem_sentence_0_129310_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_129310'>含香滞郎署，乘驲倦天涯。<div id='poem_sentence_1_129310_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_129310'>土贡千头橘，神祠万里沙。<div id='poem_sentence_2_129310_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_129310'>金碑纪风物，宝瑟怨年华。<div id='poem_sentence_3_129310_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_129310'>粉箨斑文簟，云腴紫笋芽。<div id='poem_sentence_4_129310_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_129310'>民田两岐麦，郡圃四时花。<div id='poem_sentence_5_129310_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_129310'>别恨休攀柳，归期待及瓜。<div id='poem_sentence_6_129310_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_129310'>鳣庭有遗训，清白自传家。<div id='poem_sentence_7_129310_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_129310'></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_129310_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1005&endYear=1005')">1005年11月</a>　十一月郊祀前，代邢炳撰陈状，乞为亡兄沾赠典，亡妻蒙追封。作品：代侍讲邢侍郎陈乞状。<div id='poem_1152537' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152537' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152537?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代侍讲邢侍郎陈乞状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1005年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152537")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152537_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152537'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152537'>右，臣伏有恳诚，贮于肝膈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152537_comment'></div>盖属禋燔之庆，方覃涣汗之恩，冒昧上陈，怔忪自失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152537_comment'></div>窃念臣有亡兄某，早承义训，少习文儒，肄业胶庠，服勤简素，颇有词藻，见推辈流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152537_comment'></div>俯邻壮室之年，未及命乡之荐，忽婴疾疹，遽至沦亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152537_comment'></div>臣亡妻某氏，是臣二亲在堂为臣聘娶，亲执箕帚，逮事舅姑，躬调滑甘，奉养晨夕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152537_comment'></div>而臣未升朝籍，臣妻已掩泉途，靡及汤沐之封，徒切糟糠之感。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152537_comment'></div>今者郊丘布泽，幽显怀仁，臣不胜同气之亲，痛深终鲜；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152537_comment'></div>勉思齐体之义，情极悼亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1152537_comment'></div>罔避鈇钺之诛，辄干旒冕之听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1152537_comment'></div>伏望皇帝陛下俯矜恳悃，特霈宠章，俾臣兄沾赠典之徽，光生吉第；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1152537_comment'></div>而臣妻蒙追封之命，恩洽漏泉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1152537_comment'></div>傥玄造之曲成，乃微愿之永毕，誓倾勤瘁，以补遭逢。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1152537_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1005&endYear=1005')">1005年</a>　南郊前，上奏状，为舅氏张仅请官，未准；南郊后复奏状，请纳南郊所加恩命回赐舅一官。作品：南郊奏舅状。纳南郊所加恩命乞回授亲舅状。<div id='poem_1152556' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152556' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152556?labeling=true' target='_blank'>南郊奏舅状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1005年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152556")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152556_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152556'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152556'>右，臣辄有恳私，上烦君父。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152556_comment'></div>盖属严禋之庆，仰祈锡类之仁，既内迫于肺肝，固难逃于鼎镬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152556_comment'></div>臣有亲舅张仅，年四十岁，是臣母亲弟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152556_comment'></div>素通书计，兼习刑名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152556_comment'></div>缘艺业不至于专门，且齿发既登于强仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152556_comment'></div>进难干于场屋，归仍乏于田园。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152556_comment'></div>臣外祖顷仕伪邦，累宰剧邑，所得俸入，尽买图书，须彰清白之名，蔑有膏腴之产，下世才离于寒暑，尺椽莫庇于子孙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152556_comment'></div>故臣舅自来只在臣处均衣共食，历岁踰年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1152556_comment'></div>臣去冬幸因载诞之辰，曾沥由衷之恳，属以釐革外姓，莫遂私心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1152556_comment'></div>今者玉帛配天，雷雨作解；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1152556_comment'></div>兑泽咸均于动植，皇明俯烛于幽微，臣是敢重写危诚，再祈玄造。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1152556_comment'></div>伏望皇帝陛下矜其悃愊，恕以僭踰，悯臣爰自孩提，臣母已嗟孀独。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1152556_comment'></div>自幼龄而鞠育，微臣曷报于劬劳；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1152556_comment'></div>顾外族之替凌，臣母每多于伤感。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1152556_comment'></div>敢冀陛下念臣之遭逢有素，察臣舅之蹭蹬无图，特霈异恩，获沾卑秩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1152556_comment'></div>俾臣于晨昏就养，有慰于慈亲；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1152556_comment'></div>即臣非土木无知，终报于明主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1152556_comment'></div>跼蹐俟命，启处不遑。</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1152556_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1152557' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152557' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152557?labeling=true' target='_blank'>纳南郊所加恩命乞回授亲舅状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1005年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152557")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152557_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152557'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152557'>右，臣辄披肺腑，上干君亲，盖缘危迫之诚，难逃诛夷之典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152557_comment'></div>臣有亲舅张仅，年四十岁，是臣母亲弟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152557_comment'></div>外祖顷在江左，尝事伪邦，宰邑字人，周旋数任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152557_comment'></div>颇著循良之政，见誉当时；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152557_comment'></div>誓敦清白之规，以遗后嗣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152557_comment'></div>凡得俸入，尽买图书，并无田园，可庇亲族。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152557_comment'></div>下世才踰于期岁，臣舅已叹于流离。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152557_comment'></div>微臣自忝官荣，臣舅遂相依倚，均衣共食，历岁踰年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1152557_comment'></div>虽逢下武之期，且乏专门之艺，昭代无从而进取，流光渐叹于蹉跎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1152557_comment'></div>前年因祝寿之休辰，适推恩于近列，臣曾陈章奏，仰扣高明，虽迫切于私心，方釐革于外姓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1152557_comment'></div>去岁严禋云毕，庆泽遂行，臣亦首露血诚，上尘天听，庶于臣舅，获被鸿私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1152557_comment'></div>二年并竭于丹衷，一命未谐于始愿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1152557_comment'></div>窃以人伦情义，惟外族而最优；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1152557_comment'></div>母党姻亲，于舅氏而为重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1152557_comment'></div>况臣爰当稚齿，臣母已是寡居，抚养之仁，劬劳备至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1152557_comment'></div>顾外门之衰谢，且臣舅之羁孤，痛伤之怀，晨昏在念。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1152557_comment'></div>臣是敢更冒万死，再渎九重，欲乞纳臣昨者南郊所加朝散大夫及爵邑、户封，与臣舅换一卑秩，冀沾宠渥，用慰慈颜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1152557_comment'></div>伏望皇帝陛下念臣幸以蠢愚，特蒙甄奖，获预代言之任，别无出位之思，盖迫庭闱之情，须犯冕旒之听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1152557_comment'></div>兼臣有三人亲弟，并已长成，凡再遇于覃恩，未敢干于当宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1152557_comment'></div>实缘臣舅单孑无依，敢冀俯察由衷，特回殊造，许令臣陈纳所加恩命，回赐臣舅一卑品末流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1152557_comment'></div>自叶流根，傥荷涵濡之泽，摩顶至踵，誓坚报效之诚。</div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1152557_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1005&endYear=1005')">1005年11月13日</a>　和御制南郊诗，又代中书乞免和诗。作品：奉和御制南郊七言六韵诗。代中书乞免和御制南郊诗状。<div id='poem_129408' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_129408' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/129408?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奉和御制南郊七言六韵诗</a><span class='authorDate'>（1005年11月13日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_129408")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_129408_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_129408'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_129408'>洁斋恭己奉苍旻，报本圜坛备物陈。<div id='poem_sentence_0_129408_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_129408'>酒缩楚茅三献毕，灰飞嶰管一阳新。<div id='poem_sentence_1_129408_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_129408'>高空瑞气长随辇，永夕清霜暗湿巾。<div id='poem_sentence_2_129408_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_129408'>泰畤迎年严汉祀，六宗祈福盛虞禋。<div id='poem_sentence_3_129408_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_129408'>鸿恩涣汗沾穷发，睿藻昭回动紫宸。<div id='poem_sentence_4_129408_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_129408'>庶汇熙熙蒙帝力，徒知击壤效尧民。<div id='poem_sentence_5_129408_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_129408'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_129408_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1152568' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152568' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152568?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代中书乞免和御制南郊诗状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1005年11月13日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152568")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152568_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152568'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152568'>右，臣今日中使至，伏蒙圣慈，赐臣等御制《南郊》七言六韵诗一首，令依韵和来者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152568_comment'></div>因长日以陈仪，方修毖祀；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152568_comment'></div>体《大风》而发唱，爰著雅草。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152568_comment'></div>俄赐及于近司，实光生于凡目。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152568_comment'></div>伏惟皇帝陛下先天合德，下武膺期，以明察而事二仪，用慈俭而抚诸夏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152568_comment'></div>外薄四海，罔不怀柔；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152568_comment'></div>日揽万机，未尝暇逸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152568_comment'></div>致群生之茂遂，果玄德之升闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1152568_comment'></div>乾符坤珍，荐臻于纯嘏；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1152568_comment'></div>雁山鸡塞，永息于妖氛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1152568_comment'></div>遗黎得睹于承平，率土方跻于仁寿，百姓莫知于帝力，一人思报于天功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1152568_comment'></div>乃因周正之辰，恭修汉畤之祭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1152568_comment'></div>弁冕端委，率礼弥恭；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1152568_comment'></div>圭币牲牢，无文咸秩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1152568_comment'></div>故得三日先甲，密雪清尘；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1152568_comment'></div>六师纂严，光风拂衽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1152568_comment'></div>盻蚃昭答，福禄来同，克符永锡之祥，用合无疆之祉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1152568_comment'></div>而陛下恭膺景贶，浚发睿文，穷六义之渊微，导三神之眷祐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1152568_comment'></div>圣人有作，幸获于仰瞻；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1152568_comment'></div>下里何知，更令于属和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1152568_comment'></div>共循荒陋，但极忧兢，虽效冥搜，终成累句。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1152568_comment'></div>阳乌委照，爝火岂敢以呈辉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1152568_comment'></div>轩鉴高悬，嫫母或期于掩恶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1152568_comment'></div>必希矜免，庶息怔忪。</div><div id='poem_sentence_23_1152568_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1005&endYear=1005')">1005年11月19日</a>　宰相寇准加中书尚书，兼工部侍郎，亿代撰让恩命表及谢表。作品：代中书相公让恩命第一表。代中书相公让恩命第二表。代中书相公谢表。<div id='poem_1152498' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152498' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152498?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代中书相公让恩命第一表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1005年11月19日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152498")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152498_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152498'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152498'>臣某言：伏奉今月九日麻制，伏蒙圣恩，授臣行中书侍郎、兼工部尚书、依前同中书门下平章事、加食邑一千户、食实封四百户，馀如故者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152498_comment'></div>紫坛备物，方毕于严禋；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152498_comment'></div>黄閤何功，首膺于茂宠？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152498_comment'></div>仰荷便蕃之泽，弥增跼蹐之怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152498_comment'></div>臣某<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>窃以太微西掖，中书乃列于右曹；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152498_comment'></div>文昌六卿，冬官是称于起部。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152498_comment'></div>典章所纪，名器甚崇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152498_comment'></div>自匪当仁，即为虚授。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1152498_comment'></div>如臣者，材惟琐陋，誉愧英髦，幸偶休辰，谬阶贵仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1152498_comment'></div>由先朝之振拔，参近列之论思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1152498_comment'></div>俄陪贰于宰司，实预闻于国政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1152498_comment'></div>莫著沃心之效，深怀濡翼之羞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1152498_comment'></div>伏自尊号皇帝陛下纂绍丕图，诞敷骏命，而臣外守藩翰，虔奉诏条。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1152498_comment'></div>方入觐于天庭，即权临于京邑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1152498_comment'></div>荐委计司之剧务，亟迁省闼之崇资。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1152498_comment'></div>徒受宠之若惊，固涖官之无状。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1152498_comment'></div>俄膺明命，骤正中枢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1152498_comment'></div>当求治之辰，但有素餐之诮；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1152498_comment'></div>属事边之际，曾无前箸之筹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1152498_comment'></div>乃至扈清跸以时巡，奉翠华而饮至，莫裨睿算，允谓具臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1152498_comment'></div>既避位之不容，益妨贤而为惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1152498_comment'></div>今者三垂彻警，克臻下武之期；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1152498_comment'></div>万国骏奔，爰毕肇禋之礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1152498_comment'></div>大赍载周于县县，鸿私首及于台衡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1152498_comment'></div>进秩紫垣，兼荣于题剑；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1152498_comment'></div>益封菜地，增数于爰田。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1152498_comment'></div>仰睿哲之眷怀，盖宠私之繁缛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1152498_comment'></div>徵周器之训，既深戒于满盈；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1152498_comment'></div>考宋鼎之铭，固不遑于俯偻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1152498_comment'></div>须倾丹欸，上扣宸慈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1152498_comment'></div>伏望陛下察以至诚，矜其非据，追寝前诏，式示至公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1152498_comment'></div>如此即赏典无私，允洽大中之道；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1152498_comment'></div>人言可畏，免腾不称之讥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1152498_comment'></div>干犯宸严，期于得请。</div><div id='poem_sentence_33_1152498_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1152499' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152499' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152499?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代中书相公让恩命第二表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1005年11月19日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152499")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152499_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152499'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152499'>臣某言：臣伏蒙恩制，寻拜让章，罄述丹诚，愿回玄鉴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152499_comment'></div>猥降封泥之诏，备形出綍之言，曾未赐于允俞，实不遑于启处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152499_comment'></div>臣某<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>窃以受爵不让，前典之深讥；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152499_comment'></div>为官择人，哲王之丕训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152499_comment'></div>矧西台禁掖，文昌法宫，侍从穆清，赞丝纶之密命；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152499_comment'></div>详评政典，居喉舌之要司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152499_comment'></div>自非时髦，曷允公议？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152499_comment'></div>如臣者谬尘鼎席，莫代天工，乏仲山补职之劳，昧商说绥民之略。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1152499_comment'></div>固弼谐之无取，已爵位之踰涯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1152499_comment'></div>恭惟尊号皇帝陛下祗率旧章，躬修严祀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1152499_comment'></div>合祭天地，荷纯锡之无疆；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1152499_comment'></div>大赍寰区，敷至仁于有截。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1152499_comment'></div>乃与策勋之典，聿先执政之臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1152499_comment'></div>名数崇高，既踰于列辟；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1152499_comment'></div>宠光渥缛，并集于微躯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1152499_comment'></div>扪心但极于怔忪，闻命岂胜于陨越！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1152499_comment'></div>扣帝阍而沥恳，期寝鸿恩；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1152499_comment'></div>捧尺诏之飞文，未俞素志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1152499_comment'></div>终莫安于方寸，须再黩于九重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1152499_comment'></div>伏望陛下浚发宸慈，曲回殊造，特轸盖高之听，俯矜难夺之诚，申饬有司，追还成命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1152499_comment'></div>如此即乡校之议，稍息于群言；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1152499_comment'></div>公朝之恩，更无于虚授。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1152499_comment'></div>臣之愚慊，实在于斯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1152499_comment'></div>干冒冕旒，期于得请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1152499_comment'></div>臣无任云云。</div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1152499_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1152500' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152500' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152500?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代中书相公谢表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1005年11月19日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152500")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152500_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152500'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152500'>臣某言：复奉制命，蒙恩特授臣行中书侍郎、兼工部尚书、依前同中书门下平章事、加食邑一千户、食实封四百户，馀如故者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152500_comment'></div>吉土荐诚，式修于大祭；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152500_comment'></div>公朝锡命，首及于中枢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152500_comment'></div>自蒙加等之恩，再沥由衷之恳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152500_comment'></div>猥奉明诏，莫允虔祈，仍俾断于来章，岂敢烦于睿听？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152500_comment'></div>祗荷光宠，伏切忧兢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152500_comment'></div>臣某<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>伏念臣学术空疏，器能鄙陋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152500_comment'></div>爰自策名委质，获逢下武之期；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1152500_comment'></div>陈力效官，并集非常之遇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1152500_comment'></div>自先朝之奖擢，奉清宴之吁俞，参万机宥密之谋，佐三事弼谐之任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1152500_comment'></div>运筹帷幄，莫著于嘉猷；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1152500_comment'></div>充位岩廊，颇惭于舆诵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1152500_comment'></div>爰偶继明之运，外分求瘼之权，肃奉教条，恪守官次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1152500_comment'></div>暨入趋于文陛，方就列于周行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1152500_comment'></div>乏赵、张之政能，遽釐京邑；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1152500_comment'></div>无研、桑之心虑，仍总计司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1152500_comment'></div>方怀旷职之忧，忽荷登庸之拜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1152500_comment'></div>当黄屋焦劳之际，乃林胡俶扰之辰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1152500_comment'></div>杼轴其空，曾昧富人之略；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1152500_comment'></div>金革未息，莫知决胜之方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1152500_comment'></div>尘鼎鼐之司，但愧挈瓶之智；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1152500_comment'></div>参栋梁之任，诚非构厦之材。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1152500_comment'></div>逮兹承平，并系睿算。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1152500_comment'></div>顾备员于衡轴，实负愧于朝晡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1152500_comment'></div>今者礼行于郊，爰备物以报本；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1152500_comment'></div>饮至于寝，方舍爵以策勋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1152500_comment'></div>乃眷辅臣，首覃茂渥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1152500_comment'></div>正内史西台之秩，兼冬卿常伯之崇，乃进户封，特优宠数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1152500_comment'></div>人言可畏，荐陈固让之诚；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1152500_comment'></div>天听弥高，莫寝已成之命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1152500_comment'></div>此盖尊号皇帝陛下荷纯嘏之锡，茂集于神休；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1152500_comment'></div>覃涣汗之恩，过优于宰执。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1152500_comment'></div>靡责将明之效，用伸毗倚之私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1152500_comment'></div>敢不励翼丹衷，服膺前训，罄一心而率职，副万乘之虚怀？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1152500_comment'></div>誓竭颛愚，少裨恩奖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1152500_comment'></div>臣无任云云。</div><div id='poem_sentence_35_1152500_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1005&endYear=1005')">1005年12月1日</a>　婺州开元寺新建藏经楼，求亿撰文以记。十二月一日，撰成《大藏经楼记》作品：婺州开元寺新建大藏经楼记。<div id='poem_1152678' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152678' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152678?labeling=true' target='_blank'>婺州开元寺新建大藏经楼记</a><span class='authorDate'>（景德二年十二月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152678")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152678_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152678'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152678'>昔如来登菩提坐，为天人师，万德庄严，十号其足，大千世界，以愿力而摄受；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152678_comment'></div>十二部经，自悲心而流出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152678_comment'></div>所以宣畅了义，提拯群迷，开方便门，示真实相。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152678_comment'></div>有条不紊，譬以线而贯花；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152678_comment'></div>得象忘言，如标指之见月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152678_comment'></div>自鹤林示灭，大教方行，并龙宫秘藏，所传无几。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152678_comment'></div>爰暨像法之运，乃流震旦之区。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152678_comment'></div>大士继生，广绎五天之语；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1152678_comment'></div>精庐错峙，并缄三藏之文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1152678_comment'></div>于是大雄之法音，雷震于兹土矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1152678_comment'></div>勾吴之域，介于海隅；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1152678_comment'></div>东阳之墟，上直婺女。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1152678_comment'></div>蒙太伯至德之化，俗敦廉让之风；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1152678_comment'></div>渐初平好道之馀，人禀清真之气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1152678_comment'></div>有耻且格，见善乃迁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1152678_comment'></div>邑居相望，悉奉竺乾之教；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1152678_comment'></div>弦诵之隙，必阅贝多之言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1152678_comment'></div>繇是弃尘劳而为苾刍者，实繁有徒；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1152678_comment'></div>辟净土而崇塔庙者，比比而是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1152678_comment'></div>开元寺者，兹郡之大招提也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1152678_comment'></div>前临九逵，旁接万井。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1152678_comment'></div>金碧绚彩，上拟天宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1152678_comment'></div>钟梵交音，居然福地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1152678_comment'></div>土木壮且丽矣，岁祀寖以远矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1152678_comment'></div>龙象六和之众，禅律交修；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1152678_comment'></div>香灯四事之供，檀施总萃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1152678_comment'></div>而琅函宝揭，有所缺然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1152678_comment'></div>乃有本寺僧文靖，与本州都知兵马使曹维旭，同发志诚，共营胜利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1152678_comment'></div>爰以淳化中，相率诣阙，击登闻鼓，求借方版，摹印真文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1152678_comment'></div>奏牍上闻，帝俞其请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1152678_comment'></div>逮至道初，维旭等始共辇置楮墨之直，聿来京都。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1152678_comment'></div>诏免关市之征，授以要券。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1152678_comment'></div>缮造既毕，护持而归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1152678_comment'></div>特给上计之回舟，俾达金华之本郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1152678_comment'></div>维旭等又相与刻轴以文木，织绦以色丝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1152678_comment'></div>香芸染签，丹漆涂匣，崇饰既以备矣，誓愿既已圆矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1152678_comment'></div>而经台旧基，圮毁滋久，轩庑摧挠，墁绘舛駮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1152678_comment'></div>维旭等遂请于郡阁，躬诣属城，遍募有情，共成众善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1152678_comment'></div>鸠工度费，即旧谋新，建重楼，开法藏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1152678_comment'></div>其上级置卢舍那、文殊、普贤及十六大阿罗汉之像；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1152678_comment'></div>中级设虎座，作八神王箕踞捧持；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1152678_comment'></div>其下象七金山，法四大海。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1152678_comment'></div>宝地平布，祥云周绕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1152678_comment'></div>缔构雕镂，殚匠石之精能；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1152678_comment'></div>像设焚修，见天龙之护卫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1152678_comment'></div>固使黑白之众有所归依，利钝之根因而起发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1152678_comment'></div>皮纸骨笔，学道者靡涉于艰辛；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1152678_comment'></div>宝藏金言，开卷者并谐于悟入。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1152678_comment'></div>广大利益，岂胜言哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1152678_comment'></div>维旭又尝于雍熙中，募众缘累甓为浮屠，凡七级，直经楼之南十数步。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1152678_comment'></div>讫役之日，白光烛天，晴空泬寥，久之始灭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1152678_comment'></div>行路瞻睹，道俗嗟叹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1152678_comment'></div>斯亦树善之冥感，殖福之昭报也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1152678_comment'></div>予咸平中罢守缙云，道出兹郡，维旭者捧持事状，拜于道周，求得片文，以刻贞石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1152678_comment'></div>会予入掌书命，不遑官次，而勤请弥笃，践言是冀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1152678_comment'></div>予固从事于空宗者也，随喜称赞，岂有吝焉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1152678_comment'></div>削简含毫，兹用无愧云耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1152678_comment'></div>时景德二年，岁次乙巳，十二月朔日记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_57_1152678_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1005&endYear=1005')">1005年12月7日</a>　授王钦若兵书侍郎、充资政殿大学士，亿代撰让官表。作品：代资政侍郎让表。<div id='poem_1152501' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152501' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152501?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代资政侍郎让表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1005年12月7日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152501")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152501_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152501'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152501'>臣某言：伏奉制命，蒙恩特授臣尚书兵部侍郎、充资政殿大学士，馀如故者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152501_comment'></div>殊常之命，忽降于重霄；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152501_comment'></div>非据之忧，若临于冰谷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152501_comment'></div>既不遑于肺腑，须上黩于高明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152501_comment'></div>臣某<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>窃以秘殿宏开，皇坟允集，是资旰昃，式奉论思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152501_comment'></div>矧著位禁庭，特异深严之选；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152501_comment'></div>列名儒学，盖延鸿硕之流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152501_comment'></div>至于司会分曹，文昌取象。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1152501_comment'></div>职级斯辨，实重于夏官；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1152501_comment'></div>等威肇分，最隆于天秩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1152501_comment'></div>自非望高朝右，识洞化源，荐荷宠私，必骇群听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1152501_comment'></div>如臣者，时名素薄，人地非优。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1152501_comment'></div>本以诸生，仅取太常之第；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1152501_comment'></div>俄由下位，特承明主之知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1152501_comment'></div>乃至度越等夷，典司训诰，未踰期岁，入践禁林。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1152501_comment'></div>方尘鳌岛之资，深冒鹈梁之刺，遽参裨于大政，获陪贰于中枢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1152501_comment'></div>智类挈瓶，惟虞于覆餗；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1152501_comment'></div>任当补衮，莫效于弥纶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1152501_comment'></div>已屡革于炎凉，但内惭于尸素。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1152501_comment'></div>遂沥由衷之恳，罔辞再黩之愆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1152501_comment'></div>本期退就班行，寅奉朝请，陛下特隆宸眷，弥厚鸿私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1152501_comment'></div>增秩秋曹，兼荣月殿，恩私渥缛，礼遇便蕃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1152501_comment'></div>而臣日践赤墀之涂，斋庄假寐，时奉清间之宴，肃穆承颜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1152501_comment'></div>遂拱极之私心，荷自天之殊顾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1152501_comment'></div>岂于表著之际，辄以名级为心？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1152501_comment'></div>比欲虔露至诚，愿从外任，冀奉惟良之寄，少分求瘼之忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1152501_comment'></div>寻属祇事于禋燔，谬获典司于法从，又总修书之任，方专汗简之功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1152501_comment'></div>肃奉圣谟，未申愚慊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1152501_comment'></div>岂谓伏蒙尊号皇帝陛下过优命数，特霈恩光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1152501_comment'></div>建书殿之大名，表儒林之殊事；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1152501_comment'></div>进五兵之崇秩，茂三锡之徽章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1152501_comment'></div>汉诏俯临，备形于褒饰；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1152501_comment'></div>尧心下烛，曲示于眷怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1152501_comment'></div>而臣自揣庸虚，素守涯分，岂于非次，更敢贪荣？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1152501_comment'></div>窃考简编，遐询典故，唐朝宰相，尝辞去于崇名；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1152501_comment'></div>晋国贤卿，亦见褒于能让。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1152501_comment'></div>名器无假，盖史笔之攸称；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1152501_comment'></div>俯偻益恭，固鼎铭之斯在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1152501_comment'></div>敢因前训，罄叙丹诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1152501_comment'></div>伏望陛下垂天地覆载之仁，察冰壑战兢之恳，特颁睿旨，追寝命书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1152501_comment'></div>所冀人之多言，免罹于公议；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1152501_comment'></div>物禁太甚，靡速于身灾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1152501_comment'></div>臣之寸心，实在于此。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_42_1152501'></div><div id='poem_sentence_42_1152501_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1005&endYear=1005')">1005年</a>　弟倚进士及第，调补四明主簿，莅任前，归省浦城里闾，亿作序送之，。其《少年游》词，或为送倚作。作品：送倚序。少年游（江南节物）<div id='poem_1152653' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152653' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152653?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送倚序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1003年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152653")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152653_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152653'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152653'>我之先，繇永嘉之难，避地江外，占数于上饶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152653_comment'></div>及刘展之寇，又迁于闽粤，治产殖货，以财雄于建安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152653_comment'></div>世为彊宗，高上武力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152653_comment'></div>唐室之季，乱离云瘼，礼乐征伐，不出本朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152653_comment'></div>无种而起为王侯，称兵而分据州郡，故王氏奄有无诸六郡之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152653_comment'></div>盘牙相错，莫非勍敌；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152653_comment'></div>候望走集，悉严兵备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152653_comment'></div>故我内外家世，皆服缦胡而冠武弁，总舆师而提尺籍，辎軿鼓吹，盛于一方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1152653_comment'></div>而群从叔季，凭藉世资，习尚豪举，竞养声利，争为节侠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1152653_comment'></div>唯玉山府君劳谦降志，刻苦读书，好学之名，闻于州里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1152653_comment'></div>以孝廉射策，委质江吴；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1152653_comment'></div>以儒雅从政，仕至宰邑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1152653_comment'></div>无何，黄旗运尽，琴堂秩满，考槃故里，启手归全。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1152653_comment'></div>太常府君博涉艺文，尤深《左氏》，终鲜兄弟，不遑充赋，未及中寿，遘兹大祸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1152653_comment'></div>家无担石之蓄，门无强近之亲，藐视诸孤，朝不谋夕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1152653_comment'></div>我是时以一命为兰台正字，尚未及志学之岁，遽罹悯凶，将就死灭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1152653_comment'></div>尔曹皆丱角稚齿，俱未成人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1152653_comment'></div>田园污莱，裘葛不具。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1152653_comment'></div>堂构颓替，弓冶渐微。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1152653_comment'></div>既泣血终丧，即割慈游宦，艰难险阻，备尝之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1152653_comment'></div>既而索米都下，薄游外郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1152653_comment'></div>又三岁，以文三十篇献于公车，始得为太常奉礼，且有中旨，阅书于秘府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1152653_comment'></div>日享公膳，月受俸缗，未能亢宗，财足糊口。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1152653_comment'></div>而太夫人与汝曹，仰给薄产，终岁食贫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1152653_comment'></div>我又智效一官，相去万里，晨夕引领，不觉涕之无从也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1152653_comment'></div>我亦进德励行，脩词聚学，又得册府秘书，夙夜研习，曾未期月，颇有文章出于人间，为前辈所许。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1152653_comment'></div>又频诣金马门献赋颂，天子益知名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1152653_comment'></div>凡再岁间，一召试内署，一应制行在，得光禄丞，赐进士第，复受诏直集贤院。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1152653_comment'></div>星律载周，宠光举集，稽古之力，岂诬也哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1152653_comment'></div>得禄既丰，思养弥切。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1152653_comment'></div>削牍为奏，赐告言归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1152653_comment'></div>自建安扶迎太夫人，并挈汝曹，尽室西上，侨寓辇毂，迨兹岁星一周于天矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1152653_comment'></div>而我以不肖之质，中人之才，黄屋过听，擢司雅诰，敢不摩揣铅钝，励精夙夜，期有以润色帝载，与三代同气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1152653_comment'></div>奈何力不逮心，位过其量，岁祀逾久，官谤嚣然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1152653_comment'></div>不能上封自劾，幞被引退，乃犹束带就列，俛首取容，碌碌于荐绅间，亦颜之厚矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1152653_comment'></div>今年，汝举进士，有司荐名，我时侍从穆清，亲逢旦暮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1152653_comment'></div>天子又赐汝高第，自丙科而升乙科。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1152653_comment'></div>俄顷之间，恩奖蕃缛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1152653_comment'></div>汝之仲兄及季弟，比年来圣人诞生之辰，延赏近侍，并得解褐，试秩蓬丘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1152653_comment'></div>每朔旦列拜膝下，私门嘉庆，岁时伏腊，捧觞上寿，怀黄佩玉，趋走左右，固足以慰太夫人之心；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1152653_comment'></div>而伯仲森列，门无白丁，亦足以为乡曲之美谈，交游之光宠也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1152653_comment'></div>今汝由天官调补，掌簿四明，期以来年，往代其任，且将归省松槚，盘桓里闾，俟春夏之交，乃莅厥职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1152653_comment'></div>汝当念为士之道，以仁义是务，而閒宴不可忘；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1152653_comment'></div>为吏之方，以法令是师，而资材不可彊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1152653_comment'></div>事上贵乎恭，而慎于谄；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1152653_comment'></div>临下尚乎简，而惩其违。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1152653_comment'></div>至于淳素之风，清白之训，盖我之家法耳，岂复郑重而言之哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1152653_comment'></div>若乃博约文史，切磋道术，此又朋友之事也，吾何与焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1152653_comment'></div>汝之归，吾党之人有问我者，为言受恩寖深，莅官无状，如卫鹤之有禄位，若社鼷之载车马，悲愁忧畏，不遑宁处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1152653_comment'></div>幸天子一旦澄汰流品，考覈名实，不能者止，奉身而退，固愿返初服，奉版舆，从诸乡先生优游以卒岁也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_49_1152653_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_129477' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_129477' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/129477?labeling=true' target='_blank'>少年游</a><span class='authorDate'>（1005年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_129477")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_129477_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_129477'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_129477'>江南节物，水昏云淡，飞雪满前村。<div id='poem_sentence_0_129477_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_129477'>千寻翠岭，一枝芳艳，迢递寄归人。<div id='poem_sentence_1_129477_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_129477'>寿阳妆罢，冰姿玉态，的的写天真。<div id='poem_sentence_2_129477_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_129477'>等闲风雨又纷纷，更忍向、笛中闻。</div><div id='poem_sentence_3_129477_comment'></div></div><div class='poemComment' id='poem_comment_129477'><a href='javascript: ShowPoemComment(129477)'>评注</a><span class='inlineComment4'>（点击查看或隐藏评注）</span></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1005&endYear=1005')">1005年</a>　岁暮，有诗抒怀寄刘五。作品：书怀寄刘五。<span class='inlineComment2'>（刘五，疑指刘师道。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1005&endYear=1005')">1005年</a>　修《册府元龟》，王钦若居功，诿过于杨亿以下。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1005&endYear=1005')">1005年</a>　仍知通进银台司。诏流内铨主事王太冲擢授大理评事，亿以为不宜，封还诏书。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1006&endYear=1006')">1006年</a>　仍知通进银台司，延召日本僧寂照。尝于寂照来华东游之初，以诗赠之；后寂照归国，有书寄亿。作品：身随客槎远，心学海鸥亲。<span class='inlineComment2'>（该句《全宋诗》未收。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1006&endYear=1006')">1006年</a>　宰臣毕士安卒葬，正月，为撰墓志铭。作品：宋故推忠协谋佐理功臣金紫光禄大夫行尚书吏部侍郎同中书门下平章事监修国史上柱国太原郡开国公食邑二千户食实封四百户赠太傅中书令谥曰文简毕公墓志铭。<div id='poem_1152707' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152707' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152707?labeling=true' target='_blank'>宋故推忠协谋佐理功臣金紫光禄大夫行尚书吏部侍郎同中书门下平章事监修国史上柱国太原郡开国公食邑二千户食实封四百户赠太傅中书令谥曰文简毕公墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1006年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152707")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152707_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152707'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152707'>景德二年十月乙酉，上御崇政殿，丞相、太原公早朝，方候对于殿庐中，与同列议所以条奏之事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152707_comment'></div>侃侃自若，俄顷风眩暴作，不能入谒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152707_comment'></div>上亟令太医切脉，饵以良药，遣中贵人络绎致问。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152707_comment'></div>良久疾甚，殆不知人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152707_comment'></div>上不俟驾，躬自临视。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152707_comment'></div>肩舁归第，即日以不起闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152707_comment'></div>上又亲至其居，临哭之恸，赐白金三百斤，诏废朝五日，册赠太傅、中书令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152707_comment'></div>君臣之际，斯为至矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1152707_comment'></div>哀荣之数，亡以加矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1152707_comment'></div>公讳士安，字舜举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1152707_comment'></div>其先文王之昭，功参于并建；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1152707_comment'></div>魏万之后，兆启于大名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1152707_comment'></div>锡羡流光，世德弥劭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1152707_comment'></div>衣冠阀阅，史策相沿，盖为海内之名宗，无愧山东之著姓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1152707_comment'></div>公之远祖，占籍于代郡之雁门，以财力雄边，敦尚气节；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1152707_comment'></div>以义方训子，蕴积庆灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1152707_comment'></div>至公之曾王父宗昱，以州里推贤，孝廉中选，仕至云州云中令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1152707_comment'></div>王父球，位罔克量，仕不越乡，终本州别驾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1152707_comment'></div>烈考乂林，以廊庙之姿，屈于州县，以清白之训，遗于子孙，终澶州观城令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1152707_comment'></div>逮公之光辅大政，若时登庸，缉熙庶工，平章百揆，天子嘉同德之美，尊奖于宰司，举追命之典，褒崇于先正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1152707_comment'></div>乃诏有司，赠公太王父为太子太保，曾祖母吴氏，追封邓国太夫人；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1152707_comment'></div>王父太子太傅，祖母史氏韩国太夫人；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1152707_comment'></div>烈考太子太师，妣乐氏代国太夫人，继母祝氏邓国太夫人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1152707_comment'></div>盛德之后，垂裕乎百世；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1152707_comment'></div>自天之泽，光被于九原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1152707_comment'></div>蕃衍之祥，斯不诬矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1152707_comment'></div>公器宇宏廓，风规爽迈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1152707_comment'></div>爰自稚齿，逮于成人，介然不群，卓尔有立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1152707_comment'></div>横经乡校，拳拳服膺；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1152707_comment'></div>视膳庭闱，烝烝就养。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1152707_comment'></div>公始在襁褓，即失所生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1152707_comment'></div>既罹悯凶，鞠于祖母。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1152707_comment'></div>先太师继室以刘氏、祝氏历事之，率礼无违，因心不匮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1152707_comment'></div>纯孝之德，士类攸称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1152707_comment'></div>胜冠之年，缠忧曷怙，几筵号慕，栾棘尽哀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1152707_comment'></div>既而阅先君手泽之遗文，披奕世家藏之群籍，念立身扬名之训，思切磋博习之规。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1152707_comment'></div>而澶渊近畿，逢掖盖寡，交游所及，孤陋是虞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1152707_comment'></div>且闻郑之圃田，雅多君子，因奉祝夫人徙居焉，乃得今杨徵君璞、工部韩侍郎丕、及故光禄刘少卿锡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1152707_comment'></div>博约浸润，遂通百家之言；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1152707_comment'></div>直谅多闻，是为三益之友。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1152707_comment'></div>岁祀未久，至业大成，从赋春官，时名籍甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1152707_comment'></div>乾德中，礼部员外郎、知制诰王公祐，以名德掌贡部，乃擢公上第焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1152707_comment'></div>邠帅杨廷璋备璧马之聘，延置幕府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1152707_comment'></div>赞樽俎之画，允为嘉宾，伸于己知，尽心所事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1152707_comment'></div>俯及二毛之岁，始沾一命之荣，除济州军事推官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1152707_comment'></div>时所亲李公谦浦适牧是郡，筦榷之利，俾公专掌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1152707_comment'></div>岁致馀羡，民用胥悦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1152707_comment'></div>太祖闻其名，徵赴阙，面授兖州观察推官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1152707_comment'></div>太平兴国初，迁大理寺丞，兼掌河运。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1152707_comment'></div>方船之粟，转漕攸资；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1152707_comment'></div>九年之储，廪庾斯实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1152707_comment'></div>属吴越王修来朝之礼，献益地之图，海隅苍生，初被皇化，慎柬良吏，抚绥远民，即以公知临海郡事，就迁太子左赞善大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1152707_comment'></div>江东诸州，鄱阳为大，地征甚厚，户籍尤富，非有济时周物之用，拨烦治剧之才，临于是邦，鲜不败事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1152707_comment'></div>公自台徙饶，踰年报政，职务修举，吏民便之，改殿中丞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1152707_comment'></div>归朝，为监察御史，受诏知乾州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1152707_comment'></div>公以母夫人在喜惧之年，有羸老之疾，咸秦之地，驿置尤赊，扶侍之官，登顿良苦，因上言求督汝坟公田，以奉甘旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1152707_comment'></div>官闲务简，遂其所好；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1152707_comment'></div>家贫俸薄，不以婴怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1152707_comment'></div>属太宗皇帝崇建戚藩，夹辅王室，精择僚佐，翊赞亲贤，即以公为左拾遗、冀王府记室参军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1152707_comment'></div>侍从平台，从容朱邸，成碣馆好贤之美，赞东平乐善之风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1152707_comment'></div>至于曳裾王门，仙姿冠玉，抽毫客右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1152707_comment'></div>藻思凌云，独步一时，夐出群萃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1152707_comment'></div>藉田毕，就转考功员外郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1152707_comment'></div>未几，以本官知制诰，藩王以借留为请，天子不之许也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1152707_comment'></div>再岁，召入翰林为学士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1152707_comment'></div>公上言「祢庙二名，有所嫌避」，明诏敦谕，不容辞职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1152707_comment'></div>天子嘉得贤之美，议者蔚知礼之称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1152707_comment'></div>又受诏与苏易简同知贡举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1152707_comment'></div>是岁，郡国贡士以二万数，奏名亦数千人，至公无私，群议归美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1152707_comment'></div>会郊祀，拜主客郎中，学士如故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1152707_comment'></div>俄授右谏议大夫、知颍州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1152707_comment'></div>属淫雨降灾，嘉谷不稔，公乞开公廪以振乏绝，望赐田租以惠疲瘵，帝俞其请，民实受赐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1152707_comment'></div>会今上尹正京府，宠绥神州，驿召公为开封府判官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1152707_comment'></div>未几，肇启储闱，并设官属，申命公兼太子右庶子，迁给事中，领职如故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1152707_comment'></div>属大明继照，苍震丕承，拜工部侍郎、充枢密直学士、兼知开封府事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1152707_comment'></div>邦畿之间，实方国之都会；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1152707_comment'></div>辇毂之下，盖市狱之兼容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1152707_comment'></div>簿书期会之烦，豪右侵并之弊，公击断无滞，浩穰以清。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1152707_comment'></div>俄抗封章，求解剧任，即拜礼部侍郎，再入翰林为学士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1152707_comment'></div>前席虚伫，清宴延登，动静咨询，周旋献纳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1152707_comment'></div>且以禁林书诏之填委，周庐宿直之勤劳，屡面至尊，辞以目疾，除兵部侍郎、知上党郡事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1152707_comment'></div>水深土厚，足以养疴；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1152707_comment'></div>尚德兴廉，于焉静理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1152707_comment'></div>神明之化，期月有闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1152707_comment'></div>秩满徵还，以本官充翰林侍读学士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1152707_comment'></div>数月，兼秘书监。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1152707_comment'></div>金华侍讲，允谓深严；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1152707_comment'></div>秘府刊书，是资鸿博。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1152707_comment'></div>论思慎密，体温室之不言；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1152707_comment'></div>学问淹通，蕴河东之默识。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1152707_comment'></div>为儒林之领袖，实朝右之羽仪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1152707_comment'></div>然而民望攸归，公议斯逼，果跻鼎席，同秉国钧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1152707_comment'></div>景德元年七月，以公为吏部侍郎、参知政事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1152707_comment'></div>踰月，以本官平章事、监修国史，与今中书上谷公并命焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1152707_comment'></div>是月冬，天骄寇边，銮舆薄伐，公以美疹之故，不果扈从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1152707_comment'></div>旦夕治疗，幸其有瘳，追及澶渊，见于行在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1152707_comment'></div>是时皇上讲和戎之利，继好以息民；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1152707_comment'></div>修弭兵之盟，天旋而饮至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1152707_comment'></div>公运筹汉幄，早启兴邦之言；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1152707_comment'></div>偃节灵台，亲逢《下武》之运。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1152707_comment'></div>同心一德，叶赞于钦明；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1152707_comment'></div>夙兴夜寐，弥纶于职业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1152707_comment'></div>无何腠理生疾，赐告家居，中人国医，冠盖相望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1152707_comment'></div>公以为三事之任，四海具瞻，镇抚外夷，将明万务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1152707_comment'></div>陟降帝右，非可以贪荣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1152707_comment'></div>寅亮天工，非可以旷职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1152707_comment'></div>遂陈手疏，愿解枢轴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1152707_comment'></div>上特降优诏，不允其请，申命近臣，俾之谕旨，丁宁备至，靡容逊让。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1152707_comment'></div>公感极以泣，疾亦稍平，入觐穆清，面陈至恳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1152707_comment'></div>上敦奖尤异，毗倚弥深，而公常膳载加，自公匪懈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1152707_comment'></div>有犯无隐，方宣补衮之勤；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1152707_comment'></div>外强中乾，忽起逝川之叹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1152707_comment'></div>梁木斯坏，何哲人之云亡；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1152707_comment'></div>同体忽亏，实元后之深痛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1152707_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1152707_comment'></div>享年六十有八。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1152707_comment'></div>上特为制服发哀，群臣奉慰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1152707_comment'></div>追录嗣子，及于诸孙，乃至给使之微，咸蒙甄奖之泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1152707_comment'></div>又特命皇城使、爱州刺史卫公绍钦监护葬事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1152707_comment'></div>太常考行，谥曰「文简」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1152707_comment'></div>发引之日，有司具卤簿、鼓吹，大鸿胪持节护丧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1152707_comment'></div>即以今年正月辛酉，归葬于郑州管城县马亭乡庐村之南原，从先太师之茔，礼也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1152707_comment'></div>公积阶至金紫，策勋上柱国，三进爵为公，加真食之封，益功臣之号，人爵之盛，曷以加焉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1152707_comment'></div>娶东阳骆氏，累封陈国夫人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1152707_comment'></div>出于华宗，作合君子，享是偕老，宜其永年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1152707_comment'></div>二子：长曰世长，太子中舍，裕蛊驰称，道光于济美；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1152707_comment'></div>次曰庆长，大理寺丞，闻《诗》禀训，志耸于象贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1152707_comment'></div>三女：长适故刑部员外郎李象，次适进士张扶，先公而逝；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1152707_comment'></div>次适江州德化簿刘宗诲，职方郎中蒙叟之子也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1152707_comment'></div>二孙：从善、从古，俱任将作监主簿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1152707_comment'></div>虽在羁丱之年，并敦孝谨之行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1152707_comment'></div>有后之庆，岂诬也哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1152707_comment'></div>公通介有常，谦卑不伐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1152707_comment'></div>接下和易，未尝轻于匹夫；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1152707_comment'></div>与人久要，以是称为长者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1152707_comment'></div>居然俭约，不爽于素风；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1152707_comment'></div>中外践更，克守于清节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1152707_comment'></div>善谈名理，听者忘疲；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1152707_comment'></div>多识典故，酌之不竭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1152707_comment'></div>屡掌书命，润色之美居多；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1152707_comment'></div>亟预畴咨，献替之勤斯至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1152707_comment'></div>洎入参大政，荐陟中枢，年耆益明，人望唯允。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1152707_comment'></div>展四体以率职，曾无越思；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1152707_comment'></div>奉三接以矢暮，于焉尽瘁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1152707_comment'></div>居位之日尚浅，致君之略未伸，遽兹归全，盖有遗恨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1152707_comment'></div>性嗜坟史，手不释卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1152707_comment'></div>晚年写书百卷，字皆方寸，躬自雠对，以备观览。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1152707_comment'></div>常所著述，遗札颇多，诸孤等孜孜编缀，为三十卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_147_1152707_comment'></div>垂世不朽，其在兹乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_148_1152707_comment'></div>某早奉音徽，屡陪谈宴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_149_1152707_comment'></div>矧又紫垣掌诰，联颜、范之官曹；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_150_1152707_comment'></div>黄閤拜尘，熟丙、魏之风采。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_151_1152707_comment'></div>且令嗣之勤请，迫玄寝之有期，愿志幽扃，岂敢牢让。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_152_1152707_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_153_1152707'>毕氏之先，肇基洪源。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_153_1152707_comment'></div>大名启胄，后裔实蕃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_154_1152707_comment'></div>公之乃祖，始居雁门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_155_1152707_comment'></div>吏于州县，不违丘樊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_156_1152707_comment'></div>显允太师，贻谋济美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_157_1152707_comment'></div>有志四方，考终百里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_158_1152707_comment'></div>公之既孤，不学斯耻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_159_1152707_comment'></div>徙居圃田，郑多君子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_160_1152707_comment'></div>杖策从赋，登名太常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_161_1152707_comment'></div>随牒应聘，嘉言孔彰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_162_1152707_comment'></div>乃督河漕，乃佩郡章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_163_1152707_comment'></div>岁满增秩，寘彼周行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_164_1152707_comment'></div>乃佐戚藩，乃司雅诰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_165_1152707_comment'></div>蕴藉风规，周旋辅导。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_166_1152707_comment'></div>雍容内庭，涣汗大号。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_167_1152707_comment'></div>谏官长人，善政云报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_168_1152707_comment'></div>翼翼京邑，巍巍东朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_169_1152707_comment'></div>珥笔垂绅，是为元僚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_170_1152707_comment'></div>宥密枢衡，深严禁署。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_171_1152707_comment'></div>侍从论思，再至迭处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_172_1152707_comment'></div>上党之治，民惟去思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_173_1152707_comment'></div>宣室之对，帝乃畴咨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_174_1152707_comment'></div>入践岩廊，冠于宰司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_175_1152707_comment'></div>民具尔瞻，百工允釐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_176_1152707_comment'></div>永年未登，二竖兴沴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_177_1152707_comment'></div>人之云亡，天不憖遗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_178_1152707_comment'></div>恩极临丧，礼优赠襚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_179_1152707_comment'></div>帝念良臣，永怀遗懿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_180_1152707_comment'></div>野苍茫兮风飕飕，马萧萧兮旐悠悠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_181_1152707_comment'></div>背都城兮遵广陌，溯新阡兮归故丘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_182_1152707_comment'></div>俯咸、洛之大道兮，介溱洧之通流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_183_1152707_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_184_1152707_comment'></div>贤相之墓兮在此，陇树拱兮春复秋。</div><div id='poem_sentence_185_1152707_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1006&endYear=1006')">1006年2月25日</a>　宰相寇准罢为刑部尚书，亿代撰谢表。作品：代刑部尚书寇相公谢表。<div id='poem_1152504' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152504' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152504?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代刑部寇相公谢表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1006年2月25日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152504")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152504_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152504'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152504'>臣某言：伏奉制命，蒙恩特授行刑部尚书、仍改赐推诚保德翊戴功臣、散官勋封如故者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152504_comment'></div>久玷中枢，无裨大政，合拘司败，以正常刑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152504_comment'></div>猥颁芝检之文，止罢鼎司之任，仍进周官之秩，尚尘汉陛之班。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152504_comment'></div>荷玄造之曲成，乃具臣之深幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152504_comment'></div>臣某<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>伏念臣识非经远，才不逮人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152504_comment'></div>徒以禀训日严，克传于素业；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152504_comment'></div>荐名秋赋，偶中于悬科。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152504_comment'></div>旋忝朝伦，遽升谏署。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1152504_comment'></div>励诤臣之节，尝慕于前修；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1152504_comment'></div>结明主之知，誓由于直道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1152504_comment'></div>乏先容之为助，唯孤立以自持。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1152504_comment'></div>先皇帝察其无隐之诚，矜以敢言之节，擢居上位，俾直禁庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1152504_comment'></div>未逾再岁之间，参掌万机之务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1152504_comment'></div>洎出临于表海，复入赞于持衡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1152504_comment'></div>虽无开物之才，粗有报君之绩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1152504_comment'></div>进言敢怠于罄竭，当官耻效于依违。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1152504_comment'></div>庶坚尽瘁之心，少答非常之遇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1152504_comment'></div>讵能致远？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1152504_comment'></div>但荷包荒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1152504_comment'></div>寻罢秩于台司，更分忧于侯阃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1152504_comment'></div>式处长人之任，荐逢嗣统之初。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1152504_comment'></div>假守盟津，改辕冯翊，乃至岐阳重镇，秦甸奥区。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1152504_comment'></div>亟换圭符，莫布《周南》之化；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1152504_comment'></div>屡更星琯，敢忘魏阙之心！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1152504_comment'></div>数年前，入觐圣颜，虔遵宝位，俄宠迁于省闼，且权涖于神州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1152504_comment'></div>曲荷保全，获逃旷败。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1152504_comment'></div>旋以主计之任，适有更张，慎柬之难，俾之总领。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1152504_comment'></div>属边烽之尚警，惟军实之甚繁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1152504_comment'></div>当旰食之畴咨，固治财之无状。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1152504_comment'></div>方惭忝冒，莫副倚毗，敢谓尊号皇帝陛下独出宸衷，力排舆议，擢升公辅，同掌大钧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1152504_comment'></div>俯偻叨荣，凌兢奉职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1152504_comment'></div>荷两朝之殊遇，但思报于国恩；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1152504_comment'></div>处列辟之具瞻，颇不遑于官次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1152504_comment'></div>矧乃远夷怀德，殊俗归仁，圣政日跻，睿谋天纵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1152504_comment'></div>万务尚烦于听断，三时或轸于忧劳，所宜引咎以退身，岂合包羞而窃禄！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1152504_comment'></div>竭驽骀之力，亦奚补于大猷；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1152504_comment'></div>罄夙夜之诚，谅莫资于至化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1152504_comment'></div>但满盈而是惧，实颠覆以为忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1152504_comment'></div>敢谓陛下矜坠屦之微，深怜于旧物；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1152504_comment'></div>念挈瓶之鄙，终乏于远图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1152504_comment'></div>垂覆载之深仁，霈生成之大惠，俯全薄质，特解重权。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1152504_comment'></div>矧又进常伯之显官，易功臣之懿号。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1152504_comment'></div>赞书锡命，表一人终始之私；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1152504_comment'></div>束带趋朝，处三品崇高之秩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1152504_comment'></div>省循知幸，陨越无从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1152504_comment'></div>顾惟草木之馀生，曷酬乾坤之再造！</div><div id='poem_sentence_45_1152504_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1006&endYear=1006')">1006年2月26日</a>　授冯拯兵部侍郎，依前参知政事。亿代撰让官表，谢表。作品：代参政冯侍郎让表。代参政冯侍郎谢表。<div id='poem_1152502' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152502' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152502?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代参政冯侍郎让表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1006年2月26日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152502")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152502_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152502'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152502'>臣某言：伏奉制命，蒙恩特授臣尚书兵部侍郎、依前参知政事，仍进封开国公，加食邑五百户、食实封二百户，馀如故者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152502_comment'></div>如纶之命，忽降于云霄；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152502_comment'></div>若厉之诚，乍临于渊谷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152502_comment'></div>省循斯极，启处无从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152502_comment'></div>臣某<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>窃以万机所总，实在于中枢；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152502_comment'></div>六职肇分，并隆于司会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152502_comment'></div>名器斯重，表著甚崇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152502_comment'></div>茍翊亮之无闻，何以膺加等之命？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1152502_comment'></div>或望实之非允，即必腾虚授之讥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1152502_comment'></div>如臣者，早肩褒博之流，滥登茂异之选，学非足用，才不逮人，徒以遭值休期，阶缘宠遇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1152502_comment'></div>掌乌台之错杂，莫振颓纲；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1152502_comment'></div>奉丹地之论思，无裨清问。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1152502_comment'></div>俄参司于枢务，旋贰秩于台衡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1152502_comment'></div>属边候之未宁，当旰朝之求理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1152502_comment'></div>挈瓶之智，奚补于大猷；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1152502_comment'></div>蟠木之姿，空尸于重位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1152502_comment'></div>荷天地含容之造，励夙宵勤瘁之诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1152502_comment'></div>窃禄妨贤，顾炎凉之屡改；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1152502_comment'></div>悉心举职，谅尘露以何施？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1152502_comment'></div>盖内省之不遑，岂贪荣之是冀！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1152502_comment'></div>今者命书荐降，兑泽光临。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1152502_comment'></div>曲示褒扬，更加崇进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1152502_comment'></div>文昌七秩之兵，式峻官联；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1152502_comment'></div>井田五等之封，弥优爵品。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1152502_comment'></div>是谓便蕃之泽，并臻固陋之躯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1152502_comment'></div>得不自揣丹衷，侧聆舆议？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1152502_comment'></div>盈满之惧，既佩服于前言，俯偻之诚，宜景行于先哲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1152502_comment'></div>须干睿听，希寝明恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1152502_comment'></div>伏望尊号皇帝陛下深念愚诚，曲回玄造，宽其罪戾，惠以始终，特诏有司，俾停茂渥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1152502_comment'></div>如此即陟明之典，允洽于至公；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1152502_comment'></div>非据之危，少安于方寸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1152502_comment'></div>恳倒之至，陨越于兹。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_31_1152502'></div><div id='poem_sentence_31_1152502_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1152503' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152503' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152503?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代参政冯侍郎谢表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1006年2月26日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152503")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152503_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152503'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152503'>臣某言：近奉明恩，荐加茂渥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152503_comment'></div>寻奉章而固让，辱优诏之下临。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152503_comment'></div>备谕宸慈，靡收成命，仰高穹而跼蹐，俯深谷以凌兢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152503_comment'></div>祗荷宠灵，岂任荣感！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152503_comment'></div>臣某<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>伏念臣学惭稽古，才谢适时，无丘园耿介之姿，滥乡里贤能之选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152503_comment'></div>自策名于仕籍，谬接武于朝伦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152503_comment'></div>就列七人，曾乏诤臣之誉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152503_comment'></div>颁条万里，蔑闻循吏之称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1152503_comment'></div>庆属重熙，恩隆慎柬，由郎曹而振迹，预宪著之提纲，未踰期岁之间，更践中枢之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1152503_comment'></div>掌铨衡之品藻，莫叙九流；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1152503_comment'></div>奉清宴之论思，无裨三接。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1152503_comment'></div>便参机务，莫济于忧勤；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1152503_comment'></div>俄贰台司，愈惭于尸旷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1152503_comment'></div>虽复罄寸长而自敩，展四体以从公，在砥砺以空勤，实弥纶之无状。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1152503_comment'></div>顾星霜之屡改，盖尘露之未申。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1152503_comment'></div>荐膺加等之文，深黩大中之训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1152503_comment'></div>今者夏官掌武，骤进于崇资；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1152503_comment'></div>井赋真封，更隆于异数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1152503_comment'></div>以无功而受赏，谅有识以腾嗤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1152503_comment'></div>徒坚难夺之诚，莫寝已行之诏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1152503_comment'></div>当汉宣贡实之际，颇玷于至公；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1152503_comment'></div>念周任陈力之言，益惊于非据。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1152503_comment'></div>虽僶俛而受命，固陨越以交怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1152503_comment'></div>此盖伏蒙尊号皇帝陛下道极包荒，仁非求备，特恕妨贤之咎，弥敦注意之私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1152503_comment'></div>敢不警策疲驽，揣摩铅钝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1152503_comment'></div>尽瘁事国，励夙夜匪懈之诚；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1152503_comment'></div>竭节当官，佐天地财成之化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1152503_comment'></div>庶倾勤拙，少答高明云云。</div><div id='poem_sentence_27_1152503_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1006&endYear=1006')">1006年</a>　春，有诗寄刘师道，时刘知秀州。作品：寄刘秀州。<div id='poem_129261' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_129261' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/129261?labeling=true' target='_blank'>寄刘秀州<span class='inlineComment2'>（连典吴中诸郡）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1006年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_129261")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_129261_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_129261'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_129261'>骑置迢迢阻<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_129261", 129261, "Clauses/0/Comments/0")'>玉音</span>，左鱼江海遂初心。<div id='poem_sentence_0_129261_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_129261'>朱弦道直消浮谤，春草才多动苦吟。<div id='poem_sentence_1_129261_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_129261'>震泽析酲干树橘，华亭惊梦九皋禽。<div id='poem_sentence_2_129261_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_129261'>郡楼晴日东西望，几处甘棠接翠阴。<div id='poem_sentence_3_129261_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_129261'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_129261_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1006&endYear=1006')">1006年</a>　春，刘综拜枢密直学士，亿代撰谢表。作品：代三司刘密学谢表。<div id='poem_1152489' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152489' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152489?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代三司刘密学谢表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1006年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152489")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152489_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152489'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152489'>臣某言：臣一昨以典掌邦计，经度军储，奉銮辂以省巡，忧职司之废阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152489_comment'></div>属王师之振凯，幸玄造以包荒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152489_comment'></div>虽未正于典刑，亦不遑于官次，辄陈封奏，愿解事权。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152489_comment'></div>猥辱诏书，靡俞诚请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152489_comment'></div>臣某<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>伏念臣早尘官牒，莫振时名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152489_comment'></div>爰自先朝，谬升通籍，尝出司于漕挽，亦共治于方州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152489_comment'></div>无心计以可称，唯诏条之是守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152489_comment'></div>幸遇飞龙之庆，复参流马之权。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1152489_comment'></div>红粟转输，曷致九年之蓄；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1152489_comment'></div>青蒲伏奏，时亲三接之颜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1152489_comment'></div>尊号皇帝陛下过听庸虚，特加委任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1152489_comment'></div>锦帐正名于郎署，牙筹贰秩于省闱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1152489_comment'></div>岁律未周，天慈弥渥，特改中枢之近职，旋兼会计之剧司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1152489_comment'></div>刃非可以投虚，力岂任于负重！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1152489_comment'></div>夙夜匪懈，虽不敢以告劳；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1152489_comment'></div>名器假人，但深虞于致寇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1152489_comment'></div>俄属羽书狎至，黄屋亲征。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1152489_comment'></div>当万乘之时巡，有千金之日费，急如星火，繁若米盐，虽内罄于丹心，终仰系于洪覆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1152489_comment'></div>免拘司败，保全之德已深；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1152489_comment'></div>复涖厥官，腼冒之颜斯厚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1152489_comment'></div>遂沥由衷之恳，乞从解职之求。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1152489_comment'></div>而陛下靡惩尸禄之愆，尚恕叫阍之僭，特颁优诏，俯及下臣，示丝纶存恤之言，慰芒刺兢忧之抱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1152489_comment'></div>敢不恭膺圣训，益励愚诚！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1152489_comment'></div>罄一心以事君，更坚报效；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1152489_comment'></div>展四体以率职，用补旷遗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1152489_comment'></div>庶竭颛蒙，少酬万一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1152489_comment'></div>臣无任云云。</div><div id='poem_sentence_26_1152489_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1006&endYear=1006')">1006年</a>　春，有诗送许洞归吴中，钱惟演、刘筠和之。<div id='poem_129400' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_129400' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/129400?labeling=true' target='_blank'>许洞归吴中</a><span class='authorDate'>（1006年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_129400")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_129400_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_129400'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_129400'>春渚归艎不暂留，青丝如葆恐逢秋。<div id='poem_sentence_0_129400_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_129400'>骚人已得江山助，赋客终陪霰雪游。<div id='poem_sentence_1_129400_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_129400'>三径未荒休叹鵩，十浆先馈定惊鸥。<div id='poem_sentence_2_129400_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_129400'>洞庭霜橘疁田粟，岁计犹堪比彻侯。<div id='poem_sentence_3_129400_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_129400'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_129400_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1006&endYear=1006')">1006年4月5日</a>　帝幸编修所观编修《历代君臣事迹》，有所询问，亿悉以条对，又有《谢状》作品：谢驾幸编修所状。<div id='poem_1152570' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152570' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152570?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢驾幸编修所状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1006年4月5日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152570")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152570_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152570'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152570'>右，臣昨日伏蒙圣驾临幸编修所者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152570_comment'></div>竹简汗青，方勤于官次；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152570_comment'></div>金舆旋轸，俄烛于天光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152570_comment'></div>表宸极之眷怀，耸士林之观听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152570_comment'></div>臣等窃寻往谍，载考旧闻，称制石渠，甘露遂成于故事；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152570_comment'></div>修书仙殿，开元肇锡于嘉名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152570_comment'></div>为儒墨之殊荣，乃皇帝之巨美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152570_comment'></div>恭惟皇帝陛下端居清宴，博考前言，日昃劳谦，畴咨好问。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1152570_comment'></div>贲帛旁求于髦彦，荣河上荐于图书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1152570_comment'></div>乙夜观文，每自程于衡石；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1152570_comment'></div>秋风发咏，实光被于筦弦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1152570_comment'></div>而乃允迪睿谋，聿脩秘典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1152570_comment'></div>发凡变例，同宣圣之授经；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1152570_comment'></div>钦明文思，见陶唐之稽古。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1152570_comment'></div>臣等并惭梼昧，虔禀指踪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1152570_comment'></div>抱椠怀铅，服勤于夙夜；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1152570_comment'></div>持蠡侧管，窥测于高深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1152570_comment'></div>抉小智于胸襟，冀成书于旦暮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1152570_comment'></div>敢谓陛下特迂羽葆，垂顾鸿都，亲阅缣缃，深形问讯，数刻尚回于玄览，群臣徒仰于清光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1152570_comment'></div>惭无善对之才，莫奉好文之德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1152570_comment'></div>矧又临轩前席，并示于延登；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1152570_comment'></div>厥篚兼金，更均于宠锡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1152570_comment'></div>荷纶恩之渥缛，增艺圃之光辉，敢不内省庸虚，共思罄竭！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1152570_comment'></div>拜君之锡，弥怀虚授之惭；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1152570_comment'></div>为儒之荣，曷报非常之遇？</div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1152570_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1006&endYear=1006')">1006年4月24日</a>　帝宴送隐士种放归终南山，亿应制赋诗。作品：秘阁赐宴送右谏议大夫种放得假归终南山应制。<div id='poem_129253' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_129253' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/129253?labeling=true' target='_blank'>秘阁赐宴送右谏议大夫种放得假归终南山应制</a><span class='authorDate'>（1006年4月24日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_129253")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_129253_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_129253'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_129253'>琐闱聊辍皂囊封，赐告归寻一亩宫。<div id='poem_sentence_0_129253_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_129253'>关路蒲轮千里远，岩扉蕙帐几年空。<div id='poem_sentence_1_129253_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_129253'>百壶天酒凝甘露，二雅宸章掩大风。<div id='poem_sentence_2_129253_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_129253'>旧隐暂还非久住，心期献可沃尧聪。<div id='poem_sentence_3_129253_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_129253'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_129253_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1006&endYear=1006')">1006年5月1日</a>　太阳不亏，代宰相撰贺表。作品：代宰相贺太阳不亏表。<div id='poem_1152506' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152506' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152506?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代宰相贺太阳不亏表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1006年5月1日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152506")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152506_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152506'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152506'>臣某等言：伏睹司天监、翰林天文院「今月一日，太阳当亏」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152506_comment'></div>自五更五点后，西南方起苍黑云，良久，遍天阴暗，至辰时不见亏蚀，与不蚀同者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152506_comment'></div>玄德升闻，灵符显发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152506_comment'></div>三辰式叙，万国仰瞻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152506_comment'></div>凡在照临，咸增庆抃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152506_comment'></div>臣某等<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>窃以薄蚀之数，盖天象之常文；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152506_comment'></div>推步而知，由日官之谨职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152506_comment'></div>茍云物蔽亏而表异，乃乾坤眷祐以储祥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1152506_comment'></div>伏惟尊号皇帝陛下奉若元符，诞膺骏命，用忧勤而致治，体慈俭以化人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1152506_comment'></div>先而不违，实道侔于洪覆；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1152506_comment'></div>宽以御众，遂泽浸于群生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1152506_comment'></div>聿臻下武之期，光启同文之运。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1152506_comment'></div>而万方有过，必形罪己之言；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1152506_comment'></div>九叙惟歌，犹切无灾之惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1152506_comment'></div>近者历官以告，辰象或亏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1152506_comment'></div>逮阴生慝作之辰，无伐鼓用币之事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1152506_comment'></div>而陛下斋庄寅畏，端委劳谦，对越穹旻，畴咨旰昃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1152506_comment'></div>朱丝营社，博访于旧章；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1152506_comment'></div>紫宸罢朝，特申于明诏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1152506_comment'></div>果至诚之昭格，致玄感以冥符。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1152506_comment'></div>油然作云，才肤寸而自合；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1152506_comment'></div>吐者外壤，谅侧管以难窥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1152506_comment'></div>允谓休徵，式昭景贶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1152506_comment'></div>臣等幸尘近列，获睹殊祥，欢抃之诚，倍越常品。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1152506_comment'></div>伏望宣付史氏，书之简编，传示方来，用光册府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1152506_comment'></div>臣等云云<span class='inlineComment2'>（《武夷新集》卷一五。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1152506_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_26_1152506'>臣等云云：原无，据明本、库本补。</div><div id='poem_sentence_26_1152506_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1006&endYear=1006')">1006年</a>　初秋，刘筠属疾请告，有诗，亿与钱惟演和之。作品：初秋属疾。<div id='poem_129124' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_129124' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/129124?labeling=true' target='_blank'>初秋属疾</a><span class='authorDate'>（1006年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_129124")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_129124_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_129124'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_129124'>潘郎已是入秋悲，属疾犹贪桂补<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>羸。<div id='poem_sentence_0_129124_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_129124'>密雪才高閒赋笔，流波意远托<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_129124", 129124, "Clauses/3/Comments/0")'>琴丝</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_129124_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_129124'>离愁尽日吟青案，蠲渴何人寄紫梨。<div id='poem_sentence_2_129124_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_129124'>昨夜西楼<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作风）</span>凉月满，清谈偏忆庾元规<span class='inlineComment2'>（以上《西昆酬唱集》卷上）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_129124_comment'></div></div><div
