ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1006&endYear=1006')">1006年7月2日</a>　任中正出知益州，有诗送之。作品：密直任学士知益州。<div id='poem_129369' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_129369' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_129369")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_129369_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_129369'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_129369'>玉垒求贤牧，金门辍近臣。<div id='poem_sentence_0_129369_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_129369'>龙荒使传远，鸡省命书新。<div id='poem_sentence_1_129369_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_129369'>殿柱题名久，刀州入梦频。<div id='poem_sentence_2_129369_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_129369'>悬鱼喧旧政<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：前牧东川。）</span>，叱驭继芳尘。<div id='poem_sentence_3_129369_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_129369'>珠履平原客，壶浆左蜀人。<div id='poem_sentence_4_129369_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_129369'>北堂牵远念，南诏抚殊邻。<div id='poem_sentence_5_129369_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_129369'>宴榭峨眉雪，歌筵濯锦春。<div id='poem_sentence_6_129369_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_129369'>乐章传辩士，卜肆访逋民。<div id='poem_sentence_7_129369_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_129369'>幕府觞无算，池塘思有神。<div id='poem_sentence_8_129369_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_129369'>知谁预交辟，空羡吐车茵。<div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1006&endYear=1006')">1006年7月7日</a>　杨亿作《七夕》诗，刘筠、钱惟演和之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1006&endYear=1006')">1006年</a>　杨亿作《秋夜对月》诗，刘筠、钱惟演和之。<div id='poem_129350' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_129350' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/129350?labeling=true' target='_blank'>秋夜对月</a><span class='authorDate'>（1006年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_129350")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_129350_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_129350'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_129350'>孤云飞陇首，颢气满商中。<div id='poem_sentence_0_129350_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_129350'>警鹤仙盘外，圆蟾浴殿东。<div id='poem_sentence_1_129350_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_129350'>浦寒珠有泪，岩迥树生风。<div id='poem_sentence_2_129350_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_129350'>星彩沈榆荚，霜华袭桂丛。<div id='poem_sentence_3_129350_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_129350'>光摇银烛乱，影射玉壶空。<div id='poem_sentence_4_129350_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_129350'>露馆迷秦甸，冰台接魏宫。<div id='poem_sentence_5_129350_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_129350'>绕枝惊暗鹊，促杼思阴虫。<div id='poem_sentence_6_129350_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_129350'>更想离居恨，回肠几处同。<div id='poem_sentence_7_129350_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_129350'></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_129350_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1006&endYear=1006')">1006年</a>　钱惟演作《小园秋夕》诗，刘筠、杨亿和之。<div id='poem_129019' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_129019' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/129019?labeling=true' target='_blank'>小园秋夕</a><span class='authorDate'>（1006年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_129019")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_129019_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_129019'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_129019'>鸿都归晚直城赊，墙外连营咽暮笳。<div id='poem_sentence_0_129019_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_129019'>玉井梧倾犹待凤，金塘柳密更藏鸦。<div id='poem_sentence_1_129019_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_129019'>心摇云阙传疏漏，目断星津过迥槎。<div id='poem_sentence_2_129019_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_129019'>已是秋来移带眼，可堪玄鬓有霜华。<div id='poem_sentence_3_129019_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_129019'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_129019_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1006&endYear=1006')">1006年</a>　知建州高惠连寄所赋郡中景物诗十首，亿因亦继作。高君治郡斋三亭成，八月一日，亿为撰文以记。作品：建溪十韵并序。<span class='inlineComment2'>（十咏分别为《武夷山》、《北苑焙》、《朗山寺》、《陆羽井》、《梨山庙》、《勤公亭》、《大中塔》、《仙人洲》、《延平津》、《毛竹洞》）</span>建安郡斋三亭记。<div id='poem_1152680' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152680' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152680?labeling=true' target='_blank'>建安郡斋三亭记</a><span class='authorDate'>（景德三年八月一日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152680")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152680_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152680'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152680'>夫好尚非一，仁智有山水之殊；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152680_comment'></div>居处异宜，高广致阴阳之沴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152680_comment'></div>故《书》称「肯构」，《诗》咏「斯干」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152680_comment'></div>列国之礼贤，渠渠夏屋；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152680_comment'></div>先圣之谈道，申申燕居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152680_comment'></div>矧乃专城按郡之崇，观风布政之隙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152680_comment'></div>经始不日，无土木胜人之讥；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152680_comment'></div>退食自公，有宴饮合欢之所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1152680_comment'></div>斯固君子之作事，良牧之用心者已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1152680_comment'></div>建安大邦，保界闽、粤，绵地八百里，生齿十万室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1152680_comment'></div>赋兴杂错，民俗豪举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1152680_comment'></div>国朝肇建戎阃，必作镇以壮王；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1152680_comment'></div>乃眷县道，亦精择于健令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1152680_comment'></div>即良二千石之寄，从可知矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1152680_comment'></div>渤海高君，由曲台绵蕝之任，领兹郡山泽之征，就降玺书，委之符竹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1152680_comment'></div>而君正身以律下，清心而治烦，释其磐互，陈之艺极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1152680_comment'></div>讼既息矣，徽纆弃置于圜扉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1152680_comment'></div>化之行焉，弦诵流闻于乡校。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1152680_comment'></div>豪猾屏气，逋亡悉归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1152680_comment'></div>颐指而诸曹承风，坐啸而一郡无事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1152680_comment'></div>君且念居室先后之训，著于《礼》经；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1152680_comment'></div>台榭高明之说，存诸时令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1152680_comment'></div>蓬壶溟渤，形诗人之歌咏；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1152680_comment'></div>观阁池沼，播名卿之序引。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1152680_comment'></div>于是周爰公舍，眷求遗址。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1152680_comment'></div>方塘白水，皎鉴澄明；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1152680_comment'></div>虚榭危檐，摧颓圮毁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1152680_comment'></div>即命匠石，授以楷模，曾未旬时，汔终力役。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1152680_comment'></div>审曲面势，疏为三亭；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1152680_comment'></div>反宇飞甍，瞰兹一水。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1152680_comment'></div>俯北岸曰「勤公」，仍其旧也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1152680_comment'></div>其西曰「旭景」，其南曰「澄鲜」，皆缭以修廊，状翚飞之制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1152680_comment'></div>巍然层构，侔鳌负之雄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1152680_comment'></div>池之东，累土积石，为千岩万壑之态；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1152680_comment'></div>亭之南，筑堋设次，习六钧七札之事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1152680_comment'></div>每棠郊听讼，有憩茇之勤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1152680_comment'></div>铃閤思政，乘鞅掌之暇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1152680_comment'></div>狱既决矣，隐悼伏念以无冤；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1152680_comment'></div>吏且休矣，栖迟偃仰而多适。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1152680_comment'></div>君必巾褠自便，屣履而登。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1152680_comment'></div>送目泬寥，养浩然之气；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1152680_comment'></div>披襟轩槛，当快哉之风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1152680_comment'></div>固已遣仲举之鄙吝，生蒙庄之虚白。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1152680_comment'></div>至若輶轩一介，有于役之劳；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1152680_comment'></div>盛府初筵，有从事之乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1152680_comment'></div>郊劳饯饮之外，爰洽于宴私；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1152680_comment'></div>羽书幕画之馀，率多于暇豫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1152680_comment'></div>君必殽核维旅，履舄交错。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1152680_comment'></div>裁雕章于寸烛，豆泣釜中；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1152680_comment'></div>奏妙曲于繁弦，鱼跃波际。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1152680_comment'></div>固已展《春秋》地主之礼，尽宾客杯酒之欢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1152680_comment'></div>其馀即咏叹发于如仁，尸祝宗乎全德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1152680_comment'></div>去如始至，嘉叔孙之能贤；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1152680_comment'></div>岿然独存，期灵光而为比。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1152680_comment'></div>经搆之旨，岂徒然哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1152680_comment'></div>某占数乐郊，名参户版，滥官近署，迹系君门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1152680_comment'></div>少游下泽之车，空深怀土；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1152680_comment'></div>正平爵里之刺，不获望尘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1152680_comment'></div>恭佩高风，钦闻新政，而况图绘胜槩，覼缕尺题。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1152680_comment'></div>金玉其音，日月以冀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1152680_comment'></div>幸叨史氏之职，愿纪舆人之诵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1152680_comment'></div>才少思轧，亦不敢辞，进牍含毫，用谨岁月而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1152680_comment'></div>时景德三年，岁次丙午，八月一日记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_62_1152680_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1006&endYear=1006')">1006年</a>　八月前，奉诏撰太常乐章七首。作品：太常乐章又七首。<div id='poem_129435' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_129435' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/129435?labeling=true' target='_blank'>太常乐<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup>章又七首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span>白帝迎神高安曲</a><span class='authorDate'>（1006年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_129435")'>杨亿</a></span><br class='poemContent' id='poem_content_129435'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_129435'>西颢腾精，天地始肃。<div id='poem_sentence_0_129435_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_129435'>盛德在金，百嘉阜育。<div id='poem_sentence_1_129435_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_129435'>彍弩射牲，筑场<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_129435", 129435, "Clauses/5/Comments/0")'>登谷</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_2_129435_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_129435'>明灵格思，旄罕纷属。<div id='poem_sentence_3_129435_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_129435'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_129435_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_129437' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_129437' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/129437?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span>奉币嘉安曲</a><span class='authorDate'>（1006年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>四言诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_129437_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_129437'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_129437'>博硕肥腯，以炰以烹。<div id='poem_sentence_0_129437_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_129437'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_129437", 129437, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>嘉栗</span>旨酒，有㳽斯盈。<div id='poem_sentence_1_129437_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_129437'>殽蓛维旅，肃肃蒸蒸。<div id='poem_sentence_2_129437_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_129437'>吉蠲备物，享于克诚。<div id='poem_sentence_3_129437_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_129437'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_129437_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_129438' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_129438' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/129438?labeling=true' class='poemContent' id='poem_content_129438'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_129438'>飙轮戾止，光烛灵坛。<div id='poem_sentence_0_129438_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_129438'>金奏绎如，白露漙漙。<div id='poem_sentence_1_129438_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_129438'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_129438_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_129441' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_129441' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/129441?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其四 </span>朝日迎神</a><span class='authorDate'>（1006年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>四言诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_129441_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_129441'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_129441'>阳德之母，羲御寅宾。<div id='poem_sentence_0_129441_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_129441'>得天久照，首兹三辰。<div id='poem_sentence_1_129441_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_129441'>正辞备物，肃肃振振。<div id='poem_sentence_2_129441_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_129441'>沦精降鉴，克享明禋。<div id='poem_sentence_3_129441_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_129441'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_129441_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_494165' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_494165' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/494165?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其五 </span>奉币</a><span class='authorDate'>（1006年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>四言诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_494165_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_494165'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_494165'>醴齐良洁，有牲斯纯。<div id='poem_sentence_0_494165_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_494165'>大采玄冕，乃昭其文。<div id='poem_sentence_1_494165_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_494165'>王宫定位，粢盛苾芬。<div id='poem_sentence_2_494165_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_494165'>民事以叙，玄德升闻。<div id='poem_sentence_3_494165_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_494165'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_494165_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_129440' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_129440' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/129440?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其六 </span>送神</a><span class='authorDate'>（1006年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>四言诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_129440_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_129440'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_129440'>悬象著明，照临下土。<div id='poem_sentence_0_129440_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_129440'>降福穰穰，德施周普。<div id='poem_sentence_1_129440_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_129440'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_129440_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_129436' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_129436' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/129436?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其七 </span>饮福酒广安曲</a><span class='authorDate'>（1006年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>四言诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_129436_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_129436'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_129436'>簠簋既陈，吉蠲登荐。<div id='poem_sentence_0_129436_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_129436'>洗心防邪，肃祗祭典。<div id='poem_sentence_1_129436_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_129436'>陟降惟寅，笾豆有践。<div id='poem_sentence_2_129436_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_129436'>百禄咸宜，淳耀丕显。<div id='poem_sentence_3_129436_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_129436'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_129436_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1006&endYear=1006')">1006年9月11日</a>　代宰相撰谢许士庶游宴休假表。作品：代宰相谢赐御札许士庶游宴及休假放朝表。<div id='poem_1152507' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152507' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152507?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代宰相谢赐御札许士庶游宴及休假放朝表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1006年9月11日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152507")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152507_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152507'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152507'>臣某等言：伏奉今月十一日御札，许士庶任便宴乐，及赐内外百官休假，并文武职官、军员将校，遇祁寒盛暑及大雨雪，当议放朝者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152507_comment'></div>宽大之诏，浚发于穆清；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152507_comment'></div>涣汗之恩，旁流于溥率。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152507_comment'></div>实太平之盛事，振史册之休光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152507_comment'></div>臣某等<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>窃以饮食之会，所以合欢；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152507_comment'></div>休沐之文，存乎著令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152507_comment'></div>在昔禁网疏阔，称炎汉之爱民；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152507_comment'></div>仪制申明，自开元之垂法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1152507_comment'></div>而犹聚宴有罚，乃至于赐酺；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1152507_comment'></div>沾服必朝，止延于传点。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1152507_comment'></div>恭惟尊号皇帝陛下凝神玄扈，观象璇枢，契千载之昌期，立一王之宪度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1152507_comment'></div>导德齐礼，临下以宽简之风；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1152507_comment'></div>利用厚生，驱民于仁寿之域。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1152507_comment'></div>至仁不伤于行苇，大信爰及于渊鱼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1152507_comment'></div>九序惟歌，尚侧身而思道；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1152507_comment'></div>一言之善，必虚己以畴咨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1152507_comment'></div>夤畏天明，勤劳夕惕，故得昊穹眷命，蕃锡嘉生，异俗怀柔，输诚景附。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1152507_comment'></div>边尘息警，一尉候以无虞；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1152507_comment'></div>农亩有秋，万仓箱而流咏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1152507_comment'></div>玄化神行而独运，蒸民日用而不知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1152507_comment'></div>而陛下嘉朝野之欢娱，因闾阎之富庶，恺乐之惠，思及于群黎，鞅掌之繁，俯矜于百执。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1152507_comment'></div>一笑相乐，念坐曹之或非；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1152507_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_1152507'>雨其滂，亦假盖之不易。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1152507_comment'></div>特颁明诏，式霈鸿慈，俾宴衎及于公私，而假告遵乎令式。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1152507_comment'></div>辨色谒帝，免衣裳颠倒之讥；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1152507_comment'></div>洗沐在家，绝簿领沉迷之叹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1152507_comment'></div>固将恩德沦于骨髓，歌颂播在管弦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1152507_comment'></div>事国无憔悴之人，卒岁有优游之适。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1152507_comment'></div>一日之泽，更陋于前编；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1152507_comment'></div>中衢之谣，岂迷于玄造！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1152507_comment'></div>臣等幸居著位，获奉德音，抃蹈之诚，实异伦品。</div><div id='poem_sentence_30_1152507_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1006&endYear=1006')">1006年9月</a>　奉敕撰制科试策；考毕，赐宴，有《谢状》作品：景德三年九月试贤良方正能直言进谏科策。考制策毕学士院赐宴谢状。<div id='poem_1152439' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152439' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152439?labeling=true' target='_blank'>景德三年九月试贤良方正能直言极谏科策<span class='inlineComment2'>（奉敕撰）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1006年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152439")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152439_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152439'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152439'>皇帝若曰：我国家奄宅中土，勤恤庶邦，念前代求贤之劳，思昔王好问之裕，浚发明诏，详延俊民，乐闻谠言，用裨至化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152439_comment'></div>兹子大夫韫椟待价，藏器俟时，射隼有功，逆鳞无忌之际也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152439_comment'></div>方今边候彻警，戎索载清。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152439_comment'></div>与民息肩，爰戢不祥之器；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152439_comment'></div>为国生事，深戒守方之臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152439_comment'></div>盖巳卧鼓灭烽，卖剑买犊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152439_comment'></div>下劝农之诏，勖游惰以反耕；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152439_comment'></div>置常平之仓，谨丰凶而平籴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1152439_comment'></div>劝课之道斯至，备豫之术具颁，而流庸未尽归，污莱未尽辟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1152439_comment'></div>陈陈之粟，尚郁京坻之谣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1152439_comment'></div>蚩蚩之氓，竞逐锥刀之末。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1152439_comment'></div>倚市门者，鄙于刺绣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1152439_comment'></div>为马衣者，至于击钟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1152439_comment'></div>使寒耕热耘之民，有粗衣菲食之叹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1152439_comment'></div>厚生敦本，何以尽驱于力田？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1152439_comment'></div>既富而教，何以一变而至道？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1152439_comment'></div>若夫慎重名器，先儒之格训；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1152439_comment'></div>辩论官材，为邦之令典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1152439_comment'></div>著位峻于堂陛，效用适于轮辕，固亦周爰咨诹，宴见敷纳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1152439_comment'></div>徵保任于公举，观试可于吏能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1152439_comment'></div>黜陟幽明，稽有虞之彝制；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1152439_comment'></div>综核名实，遵汉宣之故事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1152439_comment'></div>其有尤异之课，即申以增秩之文；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1152439_comment'></div>若乃非常之才，必待以不次之位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1152439_comment'></div>我有好爵，兹用縻贤；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1152439_comment'></div>国无败官，于焉致治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1152439_comment'></div>而庶尹卿士，郡邑牧宰，暨于黄绶一命，青纶半通，虽有司殿最之申严，外台刺举之详察，尚或贪墨以获戾，罢软而废职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1152439_comment'></div>徇公者伤于苛刻，贾誉者病于脂韦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1152439_comment'></div>致有嚚讼升闻，烦轺车之案劾；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1152439_comment'></div>具狱来奏，上丹笔之科条。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1152439_comment'></div>但采于风谣，或察廉之失实；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1152439_comment'></div>专取于课第，亦茂异之见遗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1152439_comment'></div>将何以致《棫朴》之咏，兴蒲卢之政，洽授方任能之道，著亮采惠畴之业？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1152439_comment'></div>昭巍巍大朝，有官人之盛；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1152439_comment'></div>济济多士，无彼己之讥？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1152439_comment'></div>子大夫强学多闻，稽古博识，究历代之损益，明当今之利病，所宜穷斯民雅俗之弊，极谈耻格之方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1152439_comment'></div>考庶官治乱之由，深陈用乂之术。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1152439_comment'></div>迟闻嘉话，以阐大猷，当悉乃心，勿有所隐。</div><div id='poem_sentence_37_1152439_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1152519' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152519' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152519?labeling=true' target='_blank'>考制策毕学士院赐宴谢状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1006年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152519")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152519_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152519'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152519'>右，伏蒙圣慈，以臣等考制策毕，特降中使，就学士院赐酒食管领者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152519_comment'></div>临轩策试，方举于旧章；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152519_comment'></div>前席咨询，屡承于睿顾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152519_comment'></div>信宿才终于考校，云天忽被于沾濡，特就禁林，俾开盛宴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152519_comment'></div>辍大庖而供拟，为近署之光华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152519_comment'></div>挹中衢之樽，徒知充量；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152519_comment'></div>享大官之膳，弥愧素餐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152519_comment'></div>仰荷天慈，臣等无任云云。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1152519_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1006&endYear=1006')">1006年9月</a>　休沐日，与刘筠、钱惟演、李维等同咏王钦若宅新菊。作品：枢密王左丞宅新菊。<div id='poem_129344' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_129344' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/129344?labeling=true' target='_blank'>枢密王左丞宅新菊</a><span class='authorDate'>（1006年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_129344")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_129344_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_129344'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_129344'>中枢多暇日，小圃占秋光。<div id='poem_sentence_0_129344_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_129344_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1006&endYear=1006')">1006年</a>　秋，有诗寄舒雅，钱惟演、刘筠和之。时舒雅知舒州秩满掌灵仙观，有诗答。作品：寄灵仙观舒职方学士。<div id='poem_sentence_0_129262_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_129262'>华阴<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_129262", 129262, ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1006&endYear=1006')">1006年</a>　秋，作《直夜》诗，钱惟演、刘筠和之。<div id='poem_129187' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_129187' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_sentence_1_129187_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_129187'>阶前槁叶惊寒雨，天际孤鸿答迥砧。<div id='poem_sentence_2_129187_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_129247' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_129247' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/129247?labeling=true' target='_blank'>晏殊奉礼归宁</a><span class='authorDate'>（1006年）</span><span id='poem_sentence_4_129247_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1006&endYear=1006')">1006年</a>　休沐日，有诗怀钱惟演；钱惟演、刘筠、陈越、李维和之。作品：休沐端居有怀希圣少卿学士。<div /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_129063_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_129063'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_129063'>凝尘满榻素琴横，岸帻孤吟意未平。<div id='poem_sentence_0_129063_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_129063'>茗粥露芽消昼夜，柘浆云液浣朝酲。<div id='poem_sentence_1_129063_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_129063'>水沈朱李金瓶涩，风猎幽兰羽扇轻。<div id='poem_sentence_2_129063_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_129063_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1006&endYear=1006')">1006年10？</a>　十月或稍后，奉敕撰夔王、周王二墓志铭。铭成，状进上。夔王光赞，太祖、太宗之弟；周王元佑，真宗之子。作品：进夔王周王铭文状。大宋赠侍中追封夔王墓志铭。大宋故光禄大夫检校太保左卫上将军兼御史大夫上柱国信国公食邑一千户食实封二百户追封周王谥悼献墓志铭。<div id='poem_1152575' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152575' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152575?labeling=true' target='_blank'>进夔王周王志文状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1006年10？）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152575")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152575_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152575'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152575'>右，臣先奉敕撰故夔王、周王志文者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152575_comment'></div>窃以奉大君之明诏，纪贤王之令猷，爰刻贞珉，以志幽壤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152575_comment'></div>自非鸿笔，曷振清芬？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152575_comment'></div>如臣者谬典王言，久尘官次，发挥寡誉，尸旷怀惭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152575_comment'></div>岂谓宸慈，更令撰述，祗膺严命，伏用兢惶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152575_comment'></div>辄已罄竭謏闻，奉扬遗懿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152575_comment'></div>属词之妙，既异于色丝；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152575_comment'></div>褒德之称，敢同于华衮！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1152575_comment'></div>徒踯躅以燥吻，寔忸怩而厚颜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1152575_comment'></div>芜秽颇多，悚惕兹甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1152575_comment'></div>其志文二首，谨缮写随状上进云云。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1152575_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1152708' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152708' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152708?labeling=true' target='_blank'>大宋赠侍中追封夔王墓志铭<span class='inlineComment2'>（奉敕撰）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1006年10？）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152708")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152708_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152708'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152708'>昔者周建戚藩，重之以执膰之数；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152708_comment'></div>汉封宗室，申之以歃血之盟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152708_comment'></div>所以隆敦叙之恩，崇纠合之义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152708_comment'></div>其有炳灵帝胄，擢秀天枝，属宝历之肇兴，顾徽音之早谢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152708_comment'></div>友于致美，极太上之孔怀；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152708_comment'></div>典章锡命，播策书于悠久。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152708_comment'></div>亲亲之德，厚莫重焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152708_comment'></div>王讳光赞，顺祖惠元皇帝、惠明皇后桑氏，曾王父母也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1152708_comment'></div>翼祖简恭皇帝、简穆皇后刘氏，王父母也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1152708_comment'></div>宣祖昭武皇帝、昭宪皇后杜氏，考妣也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1152708_comment'></div>太祖英武圣文神德皇帝、太宗神功圣德文武皇帝，王之兄也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1152708_comment'></div>曩者木德下衰，三灵改卜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1152708_comment'></div>赤符启运，百姓与能，历数有归，讴歌允属。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1152708_comment'></div>太祖皇帝握荣河之秘纪，应耀魄之玄符，受诸夏之乐推，为生民之司牧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1152708_comment'></div>帝出于《震》，龙飞在天，奄宅中区，允升大宝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1152708_comment'></div>卜世三十，与成周而比隆；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1152708_comment'></div>执玉万国，无防风之后至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1152708_comment'></div>于是右贤左戚，崇德报功，咨询稽古之言，讲求固本之术。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1152708_comment'></div>裂茅土以利建，著丹书铁券之文；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1152708_comment'></div>分宝玉以展亲，增维城磐石之固。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1152708_comment'></div>若乃嗟棣华之早陨，慨桐叶之前闻，轸同气之深情，学漏泉之茂典，于是建隆三年诏皇第五弟赠侍中，追封夔王，仍赐今名，厚饰终而峻追命也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1152708_comment'></div>黄门监之品秩，貂冠蝉緌；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1152708_comment'></div>诸侯王之名数，金玺盭绶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1152708_comment'></div>泥书出于右掖，密印贲于九原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1152708_comment'></div>盖白水中兴演也，胙全齐之壤；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1152708_comment'></div>黄武建国策也，启长沙之封。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1152708_comment'></div>所以光照大猷，发挥遗懿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1152708_comment'></div>宪章前代，肇天命于维新；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1152708_comment'></div>光宠公族，致民德以归厚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1152708_comment'></div>丕显淳耀，莫之与京。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1152708_comment'></div>今上绍休继明，奉先追远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1152708_comment'></div>念本枝之盛，永惟叔父之亲；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1152708_comment'></div>顾佳城之制，当用真王之礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1152708_comment'></div>启新阡于毕陌，祔玄寝于桥山，相善地于牛眠，得吉卜于龟食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1152708_comment'></div>窀穸之事，所以即安；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1152708_comment'></div>卤簿之仪，悉从备物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1152708_comment'></div>中人庀徒而蒇役，鸿胪持节以护丧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1152708_comment'></div>先远戒期，哀荣举集，即以景德三年十月二十八日，归葬于河南府巩县南訾乡邓封村，顺也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1152708_comment'></div>夫志陵谷之变者，必传信之辞；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1152708_comment'></div>形金石之刻者，乃不朽之事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1152708_comment'></div>下臣奉诏，猥当纪述，伏纸流汗，愧不能文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1152708_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_41_1152708'>皇矣帝胄，发源灵长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1152708_comment'></div>锡羡蕃衍，德厚流光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1152708_comment'></div>呜呼不淑，丧我贤王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1152708_comment'></div>炎灵勃兴，高穹睿命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1152708_comment'></div>玄壤封崇，绿绨褒赠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1152708_comment'></div>修睦兴仁，简编辉映。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1152708_comment'></div>帝曰叔父，永怀茂亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1152708_comment'></div>岁月增逝，辉光日新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1152708_comment'></div>改卜真宅，于洛之滨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1152708_comment'></div>风萧条兮木叶脱，野苍茫兮班剑列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1152708_comment'></div>燕𡑞启兮静而安，薤歌发兮凄以咽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1152708_comment'></div>国有史兮扬德音，圹有铭兮志徽烈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1152708_comment'></div>垂万祀兮千龄，飞英声兮昭晰。</div><div id='poem_sentence_53_1152708_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1152709' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152709' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152709?labeling=true' target='_blank'>大宋故光禄大夫检校太保左卫上将军兼御史大夫上柱国信国公食邑一千户食实封二百户追封周王谥悼献墓志铭<span class='inlineComment2'>（奉敕撰）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1006年10？）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152709")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152709_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152709'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152709'>昔者骍旄之誓，示天下以怀柔；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152709_comment'></div>《麟趾》之诗，明公族之信厚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152709_comment'></div>陶唐之圣，华封陈三者之祝；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152709_comment'></div>太姒之贤，《大雅》垂百斯之颂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152709_comment'></div>其有分辉帝胄，毓德皇闱，至性出于自然，积庆由乎锡羡，而乃参驾鹤之侣，同子晋之上宾，标秤象之能，叹苍舒之早世，恻宸襟于丹极，蔼休裕于青编。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152709_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉，见之于周王矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152709_comment'></div>王讳元祐，字庆长，今上之第二子也，以至道元年十一月二十四日生于东宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152709_comment'></div>昊穹眷怀，承华多庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1152709_comment'></div>石墙银榜，表天地长男之祥；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1152709_comment'></div>甲观画堂，处世嫡皇孙之贵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1152709_comment'></div>而王禀温恭之德，挺岐嶷之姿，亦既免怀，未尝好弄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1152709_comment'></div>虽在稚齿，宛如成人，雅尚文史，尤嗜笔札。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1152709_comment'></div>辨寿街之牍，精识造微；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1152709_comment'></div>对长安之日，神机绝俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1152709_comment'></div>八岁，制授光禄大夫、检校太保、左卫上将军兼御史大夫、上柱国、信国公、食邑一千户、食实封二百户。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1152709_comment'></div>元子比士，虽《礼》经之旧章；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1152709_comment'></div>半楚以封，实太上之谦德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1152709_comment'></div>维城之美，克茂于本枝；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1152709_comment'></div>齿胄之仪，未遑于外傅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1152709_comment'></div>俄遘阴阳之沴，遽成膏肓之疹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1152709_comment'></div>日跻厥德，冀三善之弥彰；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1152709_comment'></div>天夺之年，何九龄之弗祐？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1152709_comment'></div>以咸平六年四月二十三日薨于宫中，年始九岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1152709_comment'></div>衅生鹤禁，悲缠椒掖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1152709_comment'></div>震宫虚位，感极天慈；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1152709_comment'></div>都人罢市，痛深行路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1152709_comment'></div>特诏废朝五日，追封周王，有司奏谥曰「悼献」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1152709_comment'></div>盖夏王钟爱，元宗繇是以赐名；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1152709_comment'></div>临淮早亡，世祖不遑于进爵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1152709_comment'></div>方策所纪，布于前闻，哀荣之数，斯为极致。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1152709_comment'></div>先以其年五月十有三日，权窆于开封府开封县汴阳乡之禅惠僧舍，即以景德三年十月二十八日，备卤簿鼓吹，陪葬于永熙陵，遵吉卜而安壤树也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1152709_comment'></div>自初窆及归葬，并诏供备库副使、入内内侍副都知张景宗监护焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1152709_comment'></div>惟王玉振金相，竹苞松茂，荷兹百禄，体自九重，而明允笃诚，英敏聪悟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1152709_comment'></div>起居祖习，了无童心；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1152709_comment'></div>被服造次，必于儒者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1152709_comment'></div>奉两宫之欢爱，左右咸宜；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1152709_comment'></div>躬三朝之候问，夙夜匪懈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1152709_comment'></div>及胜衣趋拜，胙土启封。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1152709_comment'></div>并建戚藩，立爱以固邦本；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1152709_comment'></div>外总宿卫，经武以重亲贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1152709_comment'></div>德望弥宣，徽猷益盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1152709_comment'></div>仁孝爱士，将从四人之游；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1152709_comment'></div>博习亲师，式伫三雍之对。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1152709_comment'></div>无何庭兰方茂，奄至惊秋；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1152709_comment'></div>隙驷靡停，莫闻留景。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1152709_comment'></div>吴客致问，知玉体之不康；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1152709_comment'></div>太史观文，骇前星之失色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1152709_comment'></div>斯盖天人之合应，灵真之降祥，暂表瑞于皇家，复收神于太素。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1152709_comment'></div>望思不已，轸汉后之深慈；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1152709_comment'></div>封树克终，从桥山之真宅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1152709_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1152709_comment'></div>佳城一闭，夜台千古。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1152709_comment'></div>拱木合抱，怅岁月之推移；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1152709_comment'></div>深谷为陵，庶文字之传信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1152709_comment'></div>臣恭膺明诏，获当撰述。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1152709_comment'></div>在昔苴茅锡社，常奉行于命书；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1152709_comment'></div>今兹卜兆开阡，又勒铭于玄寝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1152709_comment'></div>濡毫感怆，诚无愧辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1152709_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_58_1152709'>皇图三叶兮，邦家会昌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1152709_comment'></div>锡祚蕃衍兮，源发灵长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1152709_comment'></div>猗兰积庆兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1152709_comment'></div>黄离降祥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1152709_comment'></div>帝锡纯嘏兮，挺生贤王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1152709_comment'></div>在傅不勤兮，英姿聿彰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1152709_comment'></div>为善最乐兮，嘉言载扬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1152709_comment'></div>天既难忱兮，命亦靡常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1152709_comment'></div>秀而不实兮，今也即亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1152709_comment'></div>愁云繁兮岁将暮，清霜凝兮天向曙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1152709_comment'></div>森骑吹兮前引，俨刍灵兮先路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1152709_comment'></div>祔宅兆兮文园，怆风烟兮巩树。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1152709_comment'></div>唯青简兮翠珉，垂令名兮终古。</div><div id='poem_sentence_70_1152709_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1006&endYear=1006')">1006年10月28日</a>　葬太宗明德皇后，前此，亿奉敕撰挽歌词五首，又五首。作品：明德皇太后挽歌词五首。<div id='poem_129175' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_129175' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/129175?labeling=true' target='_blank'>明德皇太后挽歌词五首<span class='inlineComment2'>（奉敕撰）</span><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1006年10月28日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_129175")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_129175_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_129175'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_129175'>母仪垂二纪，坤顺翊玄功。<div id='poem_sentence_0_129175_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_129175'>望断苍梧野，尊归长乐宫。<div id='poem_sentence_1_129175_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_129175'>金涂烘晓日，椒壁起香风。<div id='poem_sentence_2_129175_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_129175'>奄忽违尘世，攀号泣舜瞳。<div id='poem_sentence_3_129175_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_129175'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_129175_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_129177' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_129177' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/129177?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1006年10月28日）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_129177_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_129177'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_129177'>轩星光太极，阴教正中闱。<div id='poem_sentence_0_129177_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_129177'>外戚黄金穴，深宫大练衣。<div id='poem_sentence_1_129177_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_129177'>雀台愁雾隔，驹隙暗尘飞。<div id='poem_sentence_2_129177_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_129177'>贝阙三山路，飘飖仙驭归。<div id='poem_sentence_3_129177_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_129177'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_129177_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_129181' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_129181' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/129181?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1006年10月28日）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_129181_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_129181'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_129181'>德契河洲什，心依黄老书。<div id='poem_sentence_0_129181_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_129181'>濯龙规诫在，飞羽豫游疏。<div id='poem_sentence_1_129181_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_129181'>复土文园接，凝尘丙殿虚。<div id='poem_sentence_2_129181_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_129181'>蒸蒸天子孝，泣血望涂车。<div id='poem_sentence_3_129181_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_129181'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_129181_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_129173' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_129173' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/129173?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其四 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1006年10月28日）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_129173_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_129173'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_129173'>世载河山誓，门无恩泽侯。<div id='poem_sentence_0_129173_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_129173'>公桑空茧馆，仙药阻蓬丘。<div id='poem_sentence_1_129173_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_129173'>悯册藏幽壤，哀笳咽素秋。<div id='poem_sentence_2_129173_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_129173'>后宫彤管在，千古纪徽猷。<div id='poem_sentence_3_129173_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_129173'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_129173_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_129180' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_129180' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/129180?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其五 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1006年10月28日）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_129180_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_129180'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_129180'>阃范留椒闼，神游返玉清。<div id='poem_sentence_0_129180_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_129180'>鱼灯照玄寝，骑吹咽重城。<div id='poem_sentence_1_129180_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_129180'>运迫升仙日，人伤丧妣情。<div id='poem_sentence_2_129180_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_129180'>宫中旧长御，行哭尽吞声。<div id='poem_sentence_3_129180_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_129180'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_129180_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1006&endYear=1006')">1006年11月7日</a>　召为翰林学士。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1006&endYear=1006')">1006年</a>　奉旨撰《邠州灵应公庙记》，成，状进之。<div id='poem_1152681' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152681' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152681?labeling=true' target='_blank'>邠州灵应公庙记<span class='inlineComment2'>（奉敕撰）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1006年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152681")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152681_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152681'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152681'>夫有天下者，遍祭于百神，载祀典者，非止于一族。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152681_comment'></div>故成周之盛，咸秩无文，《春秋》所记，并走群望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152681_comment'></div>秦并六国，祠官之领实繁；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152681_comment'></div>汉继三代，有司之传弥广。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152681_comment'></div>是知出云见怪，不必主于山川；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152681_comment'></div>捍患御灾，固悉存于尸祝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152681_comment'></div>牲玉有等，庙貌斯严。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152681_comment'></div>斋肃吉蠲，荐之以馨德；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1152681_comment'></div>聪明正直，降之以嘉生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1152681_comment'></div>然后百工允釐，纳民于轨物；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1152681_comment'></div>三时不害，跻俗于仁寿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1152681_comment'></div>兹盛德之事也，非圣人孰能隆之哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1152681_comment'></div>咸秦之区，上直鹑首，山河四塞，幅员千里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1152681_comment'></div>雍州爽垲，秦畤神明之隩；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1152681_comment'></div>豳土深厚，公刘王业所基。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1152681_comment'></div>列地百城，提封万井。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1152681_comment'></div>崇墉浚洫，制拟通都；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1152681_comment'></div>比户连甍，俗成乐国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1152681_comment'></div>有神保顺公者，斯土之灵祇也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1152681_comment'></div>幽赞无方，休徵叵测。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1152681_comment'></div>血食制位，巧历不记其年；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1152681_comment'></div>公衮锡封，良史颇逸其事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1152681_comment'></div>岁月增逝，修奉弥勤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1152681_comment'></div>神光烛坛，野雉皆雊；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1152681_comment'></div>回风翼驾，青虬载翔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1152681_comment'></div>诚既感而必通，灵虽久而靡歇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1152681_comment'></div>郡或致祷，爰昭报而格思；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1152681_comment'></div>民苟不虔，乃凭怒而伸儆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1152681_comment'></div>繇是爱之若邵伯之树，畏之如共工之台。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1152681_comment'></div>天或降灾，克销愆伏之咎；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1152681_comment'></div>人斯搆厉，能弭札瘥之殃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1152681_comment'></div>百祥荐臻，一境是赖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1152681_comment'></div>盖社稷均享，同㟪𡾊之宗亢仓；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1152681_comment'></div>歌舞致诚，比沅湘之祠太乙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1152681_comment'></div>神道设教，是之谓乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1152681_comment'></div>而必葺以来，为日斯久，缭垣有复隍之惧，崇构几桡栋之凶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1152681_comment'></div>守臣上言，俞旨遄降。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1152681_comment'></div>经始以度费，因时而僝工。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1152681_comment'></div>取《大壮》之新规，贲集灵之旧址。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1152681_comment'></div>成之不日，升闻于天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1152681_comment'></div>特赐号曰「灵应公」，昭神贶也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1152681_comment'></div>且有明命，属于下臣，聿徵鄙词，以志休烈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1152681_comment'></div>恭惟驭神以祀者，大国之大事；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1152681_comment'></div>为民祈福者，天子之深意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1152681_comment'></div>有虞望秩，璿衡齐政而靡愆；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1152681_comment'></div>姬文怀柔，宝龟卜载而弥永。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1152681_comment'></div>祚德储祉，岂诬也哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1152681_comment'></div>谨述謏闻，惭于漏略。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1152681_comment'></div>时景德三年月日记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_48_1152681_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1006&endYear=1006')">1006年</a>　河中府开元寺僧令操迁其师重宣灵骨安置于塔，如京请亿为撰记，亿因记之。作品：河中府开元寺坛长赐紫僧重宣塔记。<div id='poem_1152677' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152677' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152677?labeling=true' target='_blank'>故河中府开元寺坛长赐紫僧重宣塔记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1006年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152677")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152677_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152677'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152677'>师姓赵氏，中条虞乡人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152677_comment'></div>由河沙劫来，殖众德本，未断后有，复生人中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152677_comment'></div>积习闻薰，童幼颖异，宿机冥契，割爱舍家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152677_comment'></div>十五礼文彻师为沙弥，二十一依澄晖师受具戒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152677_comment'></div>亦既持乞士钵，披水田衣，深念善财，遍参知识。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152677_comment'></div>尤慕庆喜，具足多闻，振锡游方，刳心求法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152677_comment'></div>其始以比邱持律，才许五年，诸佛度生，是为初教，且从本师，受四分律。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152677_comment'></div>又以如来出世，盖一事之因缘；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1152677_comment'></div>众生无边，有万殊之根器。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1152677_comment'></div>爰自降神兜率，视灭鹤林，宣说十二部经，震动大千世界。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1152677_comment'></div>其间具偏圆半满之义，开权实顿渐之门，虽文字性空，语言相离，然而标指见月，乃理事之兼通；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1152677_comment'></div>得鱼忘筌，始觉照之都泯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1152677_comment'></div>师是以从归一和尚传《无量寿经》，依行满法师阐《因明论》，尽达宗旨，咸有师承。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1152677_comment'></div>终身受持，为人演说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1152677_comment'></div>盖四句之偈，福利居多；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1152677_comment'></div>一音所宣，悟解斯众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1152677_comment'></div>又复专持《首楞》秘密之咒，遍阅毗卢方广之文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1152677_comment'></div>八郡归依，天宫办香积之供；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1152677_comment'></div>四众围绕，空界雨曼殊之花。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1152677_comment'></div>凡读《大藏经》一万馀通，诵《佛顶真言》三十万过。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1152677_comment'></div>镐京蒲坂，实有缘化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1152677_comment'></div>前后登甘露法坛，宣尸罗净戒，得度者仅千馀人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1152677_comment'></div>破尘出经，多蒙利益；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1152677_comment'></div>传灯分照，岂有穷尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1152677_comment'></div>马祖门下，皆一时之利根；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1152677_comment'></div>龙华会中，实当来之眷属。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1152677_comment'></div>人天主伴，夫岂偶然？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1152677_comment'></div>秋官贰卿、上谷寇公，早在先朝，参预大政，重师之行，荐于帝庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1152677_comment'></div>诏赐紫方袍，以旌其德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1152677_comment'></div>处六和之众而天子知名，介三法之微而王臣外护，非蕴空漏尽，神足知圆，为彼岸之舟航，作释天之日月者，畴能致是哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1152677_comment'></div>师以咸平四年四月庚戌，示身有疾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1152677_comment'></div>迨至弥留，尽召其徒，授之治命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1152677_comment'></div>薪尽火灭，神往形留，相好俨然，道俗倾慕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1152677_comment'></div>报龄七十有九，僧腊五十有八。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1152677_comment'></div>甲子，奉金身阇维于南郭之外，得舍利三十馀粒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1152677_comment'></div>以某年某月某日迁灵骨，于其原建浮屠焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1152677_comment'></div>上足弟子、赐紫令操，入室推贤，传衣善继，思欲奉扬遗懿，昭示将来，戾止上都，以塔记为请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1152677_comment'></div>予素服能仁之教，尤钦开士之风，且与上谷公道契无生，心专趣大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1152677_comment'></div>乐天绮语，固愿赞于佛乘；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1152677_comment'></div>执戟虫文，岂能宣于真谛？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1152677_comment'></div>聊摭梗槩，幸免枝游云耳。</div><div id='poem_sentence_40_1152677_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1006&endYear=1006')">1006年</a>　约于本年，孙仅惠笺，亿有启答之。作品：与孙舍人启。<div id='poem_1152620' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152620' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152620?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与孙舍人启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1006年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152620")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152620_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152620'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152620'>窃以三代誓命，著于《尚书》；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152620_comment'></div>两汉训词，号为《尔雅》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152620_comment'></div>然而经祖龙绝学之后，颇多阙文；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152620_comment'></div>处金马切问之司，止令视草。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152620_comment'></div>故方策之言未备，亦润色之业非专。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152620_comment'></div>尔后慎选台郎，入居禁闼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152620_comment'></div>殿壁涂粉，始更主于文书；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152620_comment'></div>省树栖鸡，亦通掌于制诰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1152620_comment'></div>施及唐室，实司尧言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1152620_comment'></div>职业涖于掖垣，备存《六典》；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1152620_comment'></div>判署联于台鼎，是号五花。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1152620_comment'></div>乃至奉武帐之论思，平文昌之奏议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1152620_comment'></div>泛楼船于汾水，举觞中流；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1152620_comment'></div>校羽猎于长杨，献赋行在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1152620_comment'></div>陡降上帝之右，亲日月之光华；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1152620_comment'></div>践履赤墀之涂，接夔龙之步武。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1152620_comment'></div>盖从臣之佳选，固明主之简心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1152620_comment'></div>舍人素履时中，英词鼓动，敏行具圣人之体，博闻推君子之儒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1152620_comment'></div>爰自委质休辰，飞鸣华贯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1152620_comment'></div>鸿都汗简，复《春秋》之旧章；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1152620_comment'></div>螭陛含毫，成起居之新注。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1152620_comment'></div>适属畴咨俊乂，启迪徽猷，俄召试于宰司，遂荣登于禁掖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1152620_comment'></div>言成纶綍，用裁诞告之文；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1152620_comment'></div>腰佩龟緺，更旌稽古之力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1152620_comment'></div>钦闻成命，允叶至公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1152620_comment'></div>某夙以孱庸，滥尘清切，妨贤有素，补职无闻，愧弥切于滥竽，荣遽谐于倚玉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1152620_comment'></div>盈川自省，谬居卢、骆之前；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1152620_comment'></div>文园后来，合处邹、枚之右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1152620_comment'></div>尚兹始隗，安敢望回？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1152620_comment'></div>踧踖唯觉于负芒，澄汰诚甘于幞被。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1152620_comment'></div>忽承笺简，过示谦冲，仰荷眷私，伏增铭悚。</div><div id='poem_sentence_30_1152620_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='15c000cf595548d2b2cbcc04aaf7f950_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("15c000cf595548d2b2cbcc04aaf7f950");'><span id='15c000cf595548d2b2cbcc04aaf7f950_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1007&endYear=1013')">1007-1013年</a>，34-40岁</div><div id='15c000cf595548d2b2cbcc04aaf7f950' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1007&endYear=1007')">1007年</a>　真宗疑杨亿议谤，谒陵回，借故敲击之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1007&endYear=1007')">1007年</a>　春，作《洞户》诗，刘筠和之。<div id='poem_129214' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_129214' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/129214?labeling=true' target='_blank'>洞户</a><span class='authorDate'>（1007年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_129214")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_129214_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_129214'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_129214'>洞户飞甍接绮寮，一春幽恨寄兰苕。<div id='poem_sentence_0_129214_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_129214'>书题枉是藏三岁，壶矢谁同赛百娇。<div id='poem_sentence_1_129214_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_129214'>水国风霜凋社橘，仙山云雾隔江潮。<div id='poem_sentence_2_129214_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_129214'>东城剑骑何曾出，祇为离愁髀肉销。<div id='poem_sentence_3_129214_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_129214'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_129214_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1007&endYear=1007')">1007年4月15日</a>　郭皇后卒，亿奉敕撰哀册文。作品：庄穆皇后哀册。<div id='poem_1152440' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152440' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152440?labeling=true' target='_blank'>庄穆皇后哀册文</a><span class='authorDate'>（景德四年四月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152440")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152440_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152440'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152440'>维景德四年，岁次丁未，四月丁卯朔，十五日辛巳，大行皇后郭氏崩于万岁殿之后殿，有司奏谥曰「庄穆」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152440_comment'></div>以其年六月乙未朔，二十一日乙卯，将迁座于灵台，礼也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152440_comment'></div>朱火昏中，灵輴夙驾，惨画月于素旗，咽悲风于广厦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152440_comment'></div>皇帝轸深怀于丙殿，痛淑德于长秋，感璧台之不遇，嗟黼帐之将收，降辙宾阶，亲临祖馈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152440_comment'></div>爰诏词臣，奉扬遗懿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152440_comment'></div>其词曰：厚德载物，至哉坤元。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152440_comment'></div>著明垂象，倬彼星轩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152440_comment'></div>《关雎》教始，倪天礼尊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1152440_comment'></div>章明内治，启迪化源。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1152440_comment'></div>庆属休辰，运钟元圣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1152440_comment'></div>诸夏宅心，三灵眷命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1152440_comment'></div>稽若前经，述宣内令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1152440_comment'></div>玉玺疏荣，兰闺布政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1152440_comment'></div>文昭贵胄，号仲遐枝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1152440_comment'></div>家承金穴，祥开翠衣，菖华瑞命，荇菜声诗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1152440_comment'></div>女图是宪，象服攸宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1152440_comment'></div>列邸承化，东朝作俪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1152440_comment'></div>言无出阃，义敦主馈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1152440_comment'></div>涂山翼替，周姜思媚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1152440_comment'></div>誉蔼掖庭，礼均娣姒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1152440_comment'></div>允升中壸，寅奉皇姑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1152440_comment'></div>承颜左右，上食朝晡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1152440_comment'></div>礼待阴、郭，辅佐唐、虞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1152440_comment'></div>嫔风载穆，阴教诞敷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1152440_comment'></div>厌翟斯皇，濯龙希从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1152440_comment'></div>江汉化行，祎褕礼重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1152440_comment'></div>薄氏仁善，靡徼恩宠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1152440_comment'></div>大家经书，习闻《雅》《颂》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1152440_comment'></div>外戚禀训，谦冲静退。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1152440_comment'></div>嫔御怀仁，祝延饮酹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1152440_comment'></div>半楚启邦，罔循私爱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1152440_comment'></div>裒纪旧章，尚辞封拜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1152440_comment'></div>陪游温洛，致孝南陵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1152440_comment'></div>亲易脂泽，躬荐粢盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1152440_comment'></div>帝车来复，朏魂载盈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1152440_comment'></div>衅生椒掖，灾缠玉京。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1152440_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1152440_comment'></div>顾兔沦辉，腾龙变彩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1152440_comment'></div>地震芳舆，人谣素奈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1152440_comment'></div>西山药兮杳无期，聚窟香兮不可待。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1152440_comment'></div>欻驾逝兮靡留，玉音琤兮如在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1152440_comment'></div>金釭凝兮夜何长，白驹度兮时易改。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1152440_comment'></div>中庭悽兮缘草生，洞户寂兮流尘晦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1152440_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1152440_comment'></div>宸居怆悼，戚里悲伤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1152440_comment'></div>痛深臣妾，哀极嫔嫱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1152440_comment'></div>蔼兰宫兮女史，阒茧馆兮公桑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1152440_comment'></div>掩遗书兮无复视，念故剑兮何时忘！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1152440_comment'></div>閟珠襦兮画梓，湛银海兮玄堂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1152440_comment'></div>望懿藩兮毕陌，从先后兮云阳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1152440_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1152440_comment'></div>统五鼓兮严城晓，俨六衣兮清吹度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1152440_comment'></div>陈忞册兮祖庭，咽边箫兮上路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1152440_comment'></div>洒涕兮重瞳，吞声兮长御。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1152440_comment'></div>背直城而右转，历重冈而遐骛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1152440_comment'></div>溯迤逦之周京，指萧条之巩固。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1152440_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1152440_comment'></div>陵园黯兮将闭，景象凄兮若秋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1152440_comment'></div>瞻乐宫兮永叹，览云屋兮增愁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1152440_comment'></div>毕九虞兮祔营魄，即一惠兮阐大猷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1152440_comment'></div>挹遗芳兮彤营，诸贤德兮河洲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1152440_comment'></div>京音徽之不泯，旷载祀以弥休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1152440_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉！</div><div id='poem_sentence_62_1152440_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1007&endYear=1007')">1007年6月</a>　刘综出镇并州，亿有诗送之。作品：关榆渐落边鸿过，谁劝刘郎酒十分。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1007&endYear=1007')">1007年8月9日</a>　真宗至崇文院观新编《历代君臣事迹》，亿等以草本进上，又答真宗关于修《太宗实录》问，谓“凡是有依据可载简册者，方得记录”。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1007&endYear=1007')">1007年8月24日</a>　与王旦同奉诏修国史。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1007&endYear=1007')">1007年</a>　秋，刘筠以疾在告，亿作诗赠之。刘筠有和作。作品：刘校理属疾。<div id='poem_129066' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_129066' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/129066?labeling=true' target='_blank'>刘校理属疾</a><span class='authorDate'>（1007年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_129066")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_129066_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_129066'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_129066'>北窗风劲雪云繁，移疾端居避世喧。<div id='poem_sentence_0_129066_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_129066'>载酒谁过杨子宅，张罗休署翟公门。<div id='poem_sentence_1_129066_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_129066'>多才最许飘飘气，少别还销黯黯魂。<div id='poem_sentence_2_129066_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_129066'>促尔徘徊忆真赏，远天新月照黄昏。<div id='poem_sentence_3_129066_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_129066'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_129066_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1007&endYear=1007')">1007年10月30日</a>　次咸平元年出知处州以来十年诗文，为二十卷，命之曰《武夷新集》，十月三十日序之。作品：武夷新集自序。<div id='poem_1152654' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152654' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152654?labeling=true' target='_blank'>武夷新集自序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1007年10月30日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152654")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152654_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152654'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152654'>予咸平戊戌岁九月，受诏知括苍郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152654_comment'></div>逮十有二月戊子朏，始达治所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152654_comment'></div>凡再更年籥，复朝于京师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152654_comment'></div>未半载，入西台掌诰命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152654_comment'></div>迄景德三祀，龙集丙午，仲冬之七日，被召入翰林。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152654_comment'></div>会庚戌诏书，许百执事以旬休出沐，颇燕居多暇，因取十年来诗笔，条次为二十编，目之曰《武夷新集》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152654_comment'></div>盖山林之士，不忘维桑之情；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152654_comment'></div>雕篆之文，窃怀敝帚之爱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1152654_comment'></div>命题之意，良在是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1152654_comment'></div>予亦励精为学，抗心希古，期漱先民之芳润，思觌作者之壸奥，而志力浅局，襟灵底滞，大惧夫绝膑于龙文之鼎，伤吻于蚁封之埒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1152654_comment'></div>非不勉也，恐致败焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1152654_comment'></div>亦由凫鹤之质自然，胡能损益；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1152654_comment'></div>姜桂之性素定，岂可变迁？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1152654_comment'></div>鸿丽之客，当见恕矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1152654_comment'></div>辄将假词大手，序以冠篇，又虑其相先与进，掩瑕溢美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1152654_comment'></div>刻画无盐，祗足益其陋；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1152654_comment'></div>穿凿混沌，弥以丧其真。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1152654_comment'></div>故不避乎厚颜，聊爰笔以自述云耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1152654_comment'></div>时丁未岁十月晦日，翰林学士、朝散大夫、行左司谏、知制诰、同修国史、判史馆事、柱国、虢略县开国子、食邑六百户、赐紫金鱼袋杨亿序。</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1152654_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1007&endYear=1007')">1007年12月3日</a>　任修《历代君臣事迹》，以王钦若诿过，十二月三日，帝对杨亿以下有所督责。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1007&endYear=1007')">1007年</a>　周启明举贤良方正，召试京师。亿与钱惟演、刘筠并有诗赠。作品：与客启明。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗为钱惟演首唱。）</span><div id='poem_129014' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_129014' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/129014?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与客启明</a><span class='authorDate'>（1007年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_129014")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_129014_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_129014'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_129014'>越客逃名误凿坯，汉庭初聘碧鸡才。<div id='poem_sentence_0_129014_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_129014'>操心四十知无惑，削牍三千耻自媒。<div id='poem_sentence_1_129014_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_129014'>苦吟多年依洛社，赋成他日上兰台。<div id='poem_sentence_2_129014_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_129014'>郡斋悬榻流尘满，七见东风落楚梅。<div id='poem_sentence_3_129014_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_129014'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_129014_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1007&endYear=1007')">1007年</a>　约于本年，作《宣曲》诗，刘筠、钱惟演和之。作品：宣曲二十二韵。<div id='poem_129416' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_129416' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/129416?labeling=true' target='_blank'>宣曲二十二韵</a><span class='authorDate'>（1007年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_129416")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_129416_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_129416'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_129416'>宣曲更衣宠，高堂荐枕荣。<div id='poem_sentence_0_129416_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_129416'>十洲银阙峻，三阁玉梯横。<div id='poem_sentence_1_129416_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_129416'>鸾扇裁纨制，羊车插竹迎。<div id='poem_sentence_2_129416_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_129416'>南楼看马舞，北埭听鸡鸣。<div id='poem_sentence_3_129416_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_129416'>䌽缕知延寿，灵符为避兵。<div id='poem_sentence_4_129416_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_129416'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_129416", 129416, "Clauses/10/Comments/0")'>粟眉</span>长占额，虿发俯侵缨。<div id='poem_sentence_5_129416_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_129416'>莲菂沈寒水，芝房照<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_129416", 129416, "Clauses/13/Comments/0")'>画楹</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_6_129416_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_129416'>麝脐熏翠被，鹿爪试银筝。<div id='poem_sentence_7_129416_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_129416'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_129416", 129416, "Clauses/16/Comments/1")'>秦凤</span>来何晓<span class='inlineComment2'>（周王合注本、四库本作晚）</span>，燕兰梦未成。<div id='poem_sentence_8_129416_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_129416'>丝囊晨露湿，椒壁夜寒轻。<div id='poem_sentence_9_129416_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_129416'>绮段馀霞散，瑶林密雪晴。<div id='poem_sentence_10_129416_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_129416'>流风秘舞罢，初日靓妆明。<div id='poem_sentence_11_129416_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_129416_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_129416'>洛媛迷芝馆，星妃滞斗城。<div id='poem_sentence_14_129416_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_129416'>七丝縆绿绮，六箸斗明琼。<div id='poem_sentence_15_129416_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_129416'>惯听端门<span ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1008&endYear=1008')">1008年3月3日</a>　预玉津园赐宴，有诗。刘筠先作，杨亿、钱惟演继和。作品：上巳玉津园赐宴。<div id='poem_129304' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_129304' class='poemTitle id='poem_title_129142' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/129142?labeling=true' target='_blank'>李舍人独直</a><span class='authorDate'>（1008年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span id='poem_sentence_0_129142_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_129142'>十行汉札如丝出，六幕尧天倚杵低。<div id='poem_sentence_1_129142_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1008&endYear=1008')">1008年</a>　春，累有诗怀旧居，念故园，挂冠之意日增。钱惟演、刘筠有诗和之。作品：怀旧居。偶怀。<div id='poem_129139' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_129139' class='poemTitle class='poemContent' id='poem_content_129139'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_129139'>武夷仙穴近吾庐，斗鸭阑摧菌阁虚。<div id='poem_sentence_0_129139_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' href='/Writing/129259?labeling=true' target='_blank'>偶怀</a><span class='authorDate'>（1008年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_129259")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_129259_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_129259'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_129259'>银砾飞晴霰，兰英湛冻醪。<div id='poem_sentence_0_129259_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_129259'>年光侵葆发，春恨寄云袍。<div id='poem_sentence_1_129259_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_129259'>燕重衔泥远，鸿惊避弋高。<div id='poem_sentence_2_129259_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_129259'>平生林壑志，误佩吕虔刀。<div id='poem_sentence_3_129259_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_129259'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_129259_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1008&endYear=1008')">1008年4月4日</a>　三月以来，宰相等四上表请封禅，皆诏不许；及五请，乃于四月四日诏，以今年十月有事于泰山。亿草诏，有“不求神仙，不为奢侈”等语，不可帝意，乃以帝意作修改。作品：答宰相等请封禅第五表诏。<div id='poem_1152441' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152441' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152441?labeling=true' target='_blank'>答宰相等请封禅第五表诏</a><span class='authorDate'>（大中祥符元年四月甲午）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152441")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152441_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152441'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152441'>朕博考简编，遐观往昔，若乃诞膺帝箓，抚有中区，华夏底宁，珍符沓至，曷尝不陟降东岱，对越上穹？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152441_comment'></div>益厚增高，让德而崇化；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152441_comment'></div>昭姓考瑞，建号以飞声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152441_comment'></div>由无怀已来，略可概举；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152441_comment'></div>逮开元之后，因而旷废。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152441_comment'></div>我国家诞膺骏命，肇启丕图，太祖以神武济三才，太宗以至仁绥六合。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152441_comment'></div>丰功美利，累洽重熙，盖五十年于兹矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152441_comment'></div>肆朕凉薄，获承基构，惧德弗类，因时而惕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1152441_comment'></div>励精以求治，虚己以纳善，案节以展义，洁粢以事神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1152441_comment'></div>仰畏高明，不遑中昃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1152441_comment'></div>赖宗祊之储祉，荷灵祗之愿怀，鉴兹小心，介以景福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1152441_comment'></div>五兵载戢，百谷屡丰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1152441_comment'></div>县县谧清，王猷允穆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1152441_comment'></div>而又真官预告，秘检下临，示卜世之休期，表自天之眷命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1152441_comment'></div>恭承景祐，靡敢遑宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1152441_comment'></div>期以大享明堂，聿脩郊礼，备伸昭事，以达至诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1152441_comment'></div>不谓鲁国诸生，东山黎老，来自千里，同竭一心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1152441_comment'></div>连袂荐臻，扣阍有请，罄陈徯望之恳，愿举升中之仪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1152441_comment'></div>而宰衡官师，岳牧庶尹，缁黄将校，酋长耆年，不谋而同，奉疏来上，叙天人之交感，述方册之前闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1152441_comment'></div>以为登岱勒封，古之盛典；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1152441_comment'></div>奉符行事，今也其时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1152441_comment'></div>五表继陈，众愿弥确，荐加敦谕，难夺倾输。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1152441_comment'></div>若以荷无疆之休，当盛德之事，发挥茂实，丕显成功，益用愧怀，非所宜请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1152441_comment'></div>止于报谢天地，备物而告虔；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1152441_comment'></div>升配祖宗，尊亲而致孝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1152441_comment'></div>式扬先烈，以耀大猷，是为素心，何敢崇让！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1152441_comment'></div>朕以今年十月内，式遵典礼，有事于太山，咨尔百执之臣，掌礼之士，各扬乃职，勿旷攸司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1152441_comment'></div>朕之是行，昭答神贶，匪求仙而邀福，在报本以洁诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1152441_comment'></div>至乃圭币所须，牲牷攸给，并资丰备，以格神明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1152441_comment'></div>其有司供帐之规，乘舆服御之物，悉从节减，勿致烦劳，式尽严恭，务遵简俭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1152441_comment'></div>凡百费用，并支官物，一路止增修馆舍，就建行宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1152441_comment'></div>经由州县，所用什物，亦以官物置办，不得差扰辄借及有科率。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1152441_comment'></div>诸司须索，非敕命，州县不得供给。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1152441_comment'></div>所在驰道，勿差丁夫广有修葺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1152441_comment'></div>其香台画瓮，青绳阑干，亦不须设。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1152441_comment'></div>诸路长吏，无得擅离本任，来赴行在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1152441_comment'></div>仍勿以修贡助祭为名，辄有率敛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1152441_comment'></div>起居章表，附驿以闻。</div><div id='poem_sentence_37_1152441_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1008&endYear=1008')">1008年4月5日</a>　亿等受命为东封泰山详定仪注。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1008&endYear=1008')">1008年</a>　暑热，有诗寄梅询，刘筠和之。时梅询直集贤院。作品：暑咏寄梅集贤。<div id='poem_129281' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_129281' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a
