id='poem_sentence_6_129429'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_129429_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1008&endYear=1008')">1008年</a>　集当世人述作，为《笔苑时文录》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1008&endYear=1008')">1008年</a>　本年秋或其后，编次景德以来与修《历代君臣事迹》诸公十五人唱和诗二百五十首，题曰《西昆酬唱集》，序之。作品：西昆酬唱集序。<div id='poem_1152667' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152667' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152667?labeling=true' target='_blank'>西昆酬唱集序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1008年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152667")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152667_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152667'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152667'>余景德中，忝佐修书之任，得接群公之游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152667_comment'></div>时今紫微钱君希圣、秘阁刘君子仪，并负懿文，尤精雅道，雕章丽句，脍炙人口，予得以游其墙藩而咨其模楷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152667_comment'></div>二君成人之美，不我遐弃，博约诱掖，寘之同声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152667_comment'></div>因以历览遗编，研味前作，挹其芳润，发于希慕，更迭唱和，互相切劘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152667_comment'></div>而予以固陋之姿，参酬继之末。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152667_comment'></div>入兰游雾，虽获益以居多；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152667_comment'></div>观海学山，叹知量而中止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152667_comment'></div>既恨其不至，又犯乎不韪，虽荣于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_1152667", 1152667, "Clauses/27/Comments/0")'>托骥</span>，亦愧乎续貂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1152667_comment'></div>间然于兹，颜厚何已！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1152667_comment'></div>凡五、七言律诗二百四十七章，其属而和者又十有五人，析为二卷，取玉山策府之名，命之曰《西昆酬唱集》云尔。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1152667_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1152667'><span class='label'>按：</span>《西昆酬唱集》卷首，四部丛刊本。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1152667_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1008&endYear=1008')">1008年</a>　晤西域僧觉称。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1008&endYear=1008')">1008年</a>　益都金绳院，唐末禅月大师贯休曾住之龙华院遗址也。今住持惠聪师即旧图新，作为佛殿，诏赐今名。师请记于亿，乃记之。作品：金绳院记。<div id='poem_1152683' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152683' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152683?labeling=true' target='_blank'>金绳院记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1008年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152683")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152683_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152683'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152683'>夫西竺之教，被于震旦，而像运千岁，塔庙之制勃兴；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152683_comment'></div>东井之络，主于益部，而沃壤千里，礼俗之化归厚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152683_comment'></div>蚕丛古之建国，铜梁天之设险。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152683_comment'></div>带二江之流，为一都之会，四民州处，万商成渊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152683_comment'></div>稽河图之文，惟福基之凭固；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152683_comment'></div>拟鸡园之舍，邈壮栋以迭隆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152683_comment'></div>金绳禅院者，旧号龙华院。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152683_comment'></div>唐天复，有禅月大师贯休者，通内外之学，为道俗所宗，风什研精，名声籍甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1152683_comment'></div>当土德之季，戎车竞逐，侯王起于无种，云雷以之遘屯，拊剑顾盼以称豪，专阃福威而自出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1152683_comment'></div>燕开碣石之馆，市骏骨以翘林；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1152683_comment'></div>秦筑逍遥之园，演贝文而重道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1152683_comment'></div>纁玉更荐，簦笈四臻，而师方游所洎，久寓荆渚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1152683_comment'></div>藩牧致礼，邑子倾向。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1152683_comment'></div>时王氏掩据蜀土，将为西帝，延致千里之客，弥丰四时之供。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1152683_comment'></div>师乃遐冒重阻，往干典谒，叩以空寂之理，嗣以篇题之贽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1152683_comment'></div>虞卿既见，殆蒙白璧之颁；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1152683_comment'></div>汤休能诗，迥继碧云之妙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1152683_comment'></div>锡之紫服，待以宾友，请住兹院，极其礼遇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1152683_comment'></div>师自壬戌游蜀，至丙寅定居，比壬申入灭，凡岁星一周于天矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1152683_comment'></div>上足惠光大师昙域，克绍遗躅，弗忘肯构。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1152683_comment'></div>其后有正觉、法忍、法宝、演教四大师，继承世系，无废先烈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1152683_comment'></div>今住持赐紫释惠聪者，自咸平辛丑始掌院事，迥悟宗谛，焕发觉明，愿力攸资，信施弥博。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1152683_comment'></div>远者来而迩者悦，输货沓臻；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1152683_comment'></div>即其旧而图其新，胥宇尤盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1152683_comment'></div>凡作佛殿、斋厅、僧堂、浴室及众舍二百五十馀间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1152683_comment'></div>砻密石以庀材，丁丁毕取；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1152683_comment'></div>侧紫金而布地，昈昈有华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1152683_comment'></div>侔天界之庄严，为众园之依止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1152683_comment'></div>香象蹴踏，并辏霞祴之修禅；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1152683_comment'></div>灵鹫飞翔，无异果唇之住世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1152683_comment'></div>大中祥符之祀，诏赐今名，揭彫榜于楣门，烛霄辉于海会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1152683_comment'></div>陈跮有焕，名香歇而复熏；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1152683_comment'></div>惠命增延，祖燄续而无尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1152683_comment'></div>善利之绩，畴可儗哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1152683_comment'></div>聪师藉予虚名，谓窥秘典，丐词纪实，远不及让。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1152683_comment'></div>蜀冥烦之未祛，颇灭裂而为愧耳。</div><div id='poem_sentence_35_1152683_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1008&endYear=1008')">1008年</a>　约于本年，荐张士逊为监察御史。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1009&endYear=1009')">1009年1月</a>　御史中丞王嗣宗言：杨亿、钱惟演、刘筠唱和《宣曲》诗，词涉浮靡。乃下诏风励学者，戒其流宕。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1009&endYear=1009')">1009年1月24日</a>　与李维等刊定僧道原所编《传灯录》三十卷成，上之。亿并序。作品：景德传灯录序。<div id='poem_1152670' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152670' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152670?labeling=true' target='_blank'>景德传灯录序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1009年1月24日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152670")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152670_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152670'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152670'>昔释迦文以受然灯之夙记，当贤劫之次补，降神演化四十九年，开权实顿渐之门，垂半满偏圆之教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152670_comment'></div>随机悟理，爰有三乘之差；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152670_comment'></div>接物利生，乃度无边之众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152670_comment'></div>其悲济广大矣，其轨式备具矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152670_comment'></div>而双林入灭，独顾于饮光；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152670_comment'></div>屈眴相传，首从于达磨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152670_comment'></div>不立文字，直指心源；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152670_comment'></div>不践阶梯，径登佛地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1152670_comment'></div>逮五叶而始盛，分千灯而益繁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1152670_comment'></div>达宝所者盖多，转法轮者非一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1152670_comment'></div>盖大雄付嘱之旨，正眼流通之道，教外别行，不可思议者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1152670_comment'></div>圣宋启运，人灵幽赞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1152670_comment'></div>太祖以神武戡乱，而崇净刹，辟度门；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1152670_comment'></div>太宗以钦明御辩，而述秘诠，畅真谛；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1152670_comment'></div>皇上以睿文继志，而序圣教，绎宗风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1152670_comment'></div>焕云章于义天，振金声于觉苑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1152670_comment'></div>莲藏之言密契，竺乾之绪克昌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1152670_comment'></div>殖众善者滋多，传了义者间出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1152670_comment'></div>圆顿之化，流于区域。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1152670_comment'></div>有东吴僧道原者，冥心禅悦，索隐空宗，披奕世之祖图，采诸方之语录，次序其源派，错综其辞句。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1152670_comment'></div>由七佛以至大法眼之嗣，凡五十二世，一千七百一人，成三十卷，目之曰《景德传灯录》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1152670_comment'></div>诣阙奉进，冀于流布。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1152670_comment'></div>皇上为佛法之外护，嘉释子之勤业，载怀重慎，思致远久，乃诏翰林学士、左司谏、知制诰臣杨亿，兵部员外郎、知制诰臣李维，太常丞臣王曙等，同加刊削，俾之裁定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1152670_comment'></div>臣等昧三学之旨，迷五性之方，乏临川翻译之能，懵毗邪语默之要。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1152670_comment'></div>恭承严命，不敢牢让，窃用探索，匪遑宁居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1152670_comment'></div>考其论撰之意，盖以真空为本，将以述曩圣入道之因，标昔人契理之说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1152670_comment'></div>机缘交激，若拄于箭锋；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1152670_comment'></div>智藏发光，旁资于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_27_1152670", 1152670, "Clauses/84/Comments/0")'>鞭影</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1152670_comment'></div>诱导后学，敷畅玄猷，而捃摭之来，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_28_1152670", 1152670, "Clauses/88/Comments/0")'>徵引</span>所出，糟粕多在，油素可寻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1152670_comment'></div>其有大士示徒，以一音而开演；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1152670_comment'></div>含灵耸听，乃千圣之證明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1152670_comment'></div>属概举之是资，取少分而斯可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1152670_comment'></div>若乃别加润色，失其指归，既非华竺之殊言，颇近错雕之伤宝，如此之类，悉仍其旧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1152670_comment'></div>况又事资纪实，必由于善叙；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1152670_comment'></div>言以行远，非可以无文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1152670_comment'></div>其有标录事缘，缕详轨迹，或辞条之纷纠，或言筌之猥俗，并从刊削，俾之纶贯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1152670_comment'></div>至有儒臣居士之问答，爵位姓氏之著明，校岁历以愆殊，约史籍而差谬，咸用删去，以资传信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1152670_comment'></div>自非启投针之玄趣，驰激电之迅机，开示妙明之真心，祖述苦空之深理，即何以契传灯之喻，施刮膜之功？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1152670_comment'></div>若乃但述感应之徵符，专叙参游之辙迹，此已标于僧史，亦奚取于禅诠？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1152670_comment'></div>聊存世系之名，庶纪师承之自。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1152670_comment'></div>然而旧录所载，或掇粗而遗精；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1152670_comment'></div>别集具存，当寻文而补阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1152670_comment'></div>率加采撷，爰从附益。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1152670_comment'></div>逮于序论之作，或非古德之文，间厕编联，徒增楦酿，亦用简别，多所屏去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1152670_comment'></div>汔兹周岁，方遂终篇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1152670_comment'></div>臣等性识愧于冥烦，学问惭于涉猎，天机素浅，文力无馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1152670_comment'></div>妙道在人，虽刳心而斯久；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1152670_comment'></div>玄言绝俗，固面墙以居多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1152670_comment'></div>滥膺推择之私，靡著发挥之效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1152670_comment'></div>已克终于䌷绎，将仰奉于清间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1152670_comment'></div>莫副宸襟，空尘睿览。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1152670_comment'></div>谨上。</div><div id='poem_sentence_51_1152670_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1152670'><span class='label'>按：</span>《景德传灯录》卷首，四部丛刊三编本。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1152670_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1009&endYear=1009')">1009年4月</a>　种放得告归终南山，帝作诗赐之，并命群臣皆赋，亿制序，时宰评以为优。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1009&endYear=1009')">1009年5月1日</a>　诏追封孔子及其弟子等，命宰相以下群臣撰赞。亿撰司马耕等三赞。作品：司马耕字子牛宋人赠向伯今进封楚丘侯赞。樊须字子迟齐人赠樊伯今进封益都侯赞。秦博士伏胜今封乘氏伯赞。<div id='poem_1152686' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152686' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152686?labeling=true' target='_blank'>司马耕字子牛宋人赠向伯今进封楚丘侯赞</a><span class='authorDate'>（1009年5月1日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152686")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>四言诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_1152686_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152686'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152686'>仁远乎哉，其言也讱。<div id='poem_sentence_0_1152686_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_1152686'>虚德实归，耽思旁讯。<div id='poem_sentence_1_1152686_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_1152686'>违难迷邦，奚虞悔吝？<div id='poem_sentence_2_1152686_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_1152686'>疏爵丁辰，宠名以峻。<div id='poem_sentence_3_1152686_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_1152686'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1152686_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1152687' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152687' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152687?labeling=true' target='_blank'>樊须字子迟齐人赠樊伯今进封益都侯赞</a><span class='authorDate'>（1009年5月1日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152687")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>四言诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_1152687_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152687'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152687'>学优乃仕，齿于家陪。<div id='poem_sentence_0_1152687_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_1152687'>戎车为右，誓众靡回。<div id='poem_sentence_1_1152687_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_1152687'>质疑辩问，仁智既该。<div id='poem_sentence_2_1152687_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_1152687'>建侯追荣，垂裕方来。<div id='poem_sentence_3_1152687_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_1152687'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1152687_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1152688' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152688' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152688?labeling=true' target='_blank'>秦博士伏胜今封乘氏伯赞</a><span class='authorDate'>（1009年5月1日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152688")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>四言诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_1152688_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152688'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152688'>伏生明经，为秦博士。<div id='poem_sentence_0_1152688_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_1152688'>祖习微言，流离耄齿。<div id='poem_sentence_1_1152688_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_1152688'>壁藏其文，口授厥旨。<div id='poem_sentence_2_1152688_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_1152688'>建号旌儒，锡封仁里。<div id='poem_sentence_3_1152688_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_1152688'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1152688_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1009&endYear=1009')">1009年11月17日</a>　受命撰天贶殿碑铭。作品：大宋天贶殿碑铭并序。<div id='poem_1152694' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152694' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152694?labeling=true' target='_blank'>大宋天贶殿碑铭<span class='inlineComment2'>（并序大中祥符二年十一月十七日）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1009年11月17日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152694")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152694_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152694'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152694'>臣闻玄天之覆物也，阴骘而无私；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152694_comment'></div>上帝之临下也，高明而有赫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152694_comment'></div>倬昭回而成体，其听孔卑；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152694_comment'></div>杳寂寞以希声，厥应如响。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152694_comment'></div>故《周书》纪其「辅德」，羲《易》载其「益谦」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152694_comment'></div>百禄咸宜，于以隆其永命；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152694_comment'></div>庶徵时若，于以降乎嘉生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152694_comment'></div>斯皆自我民而聪明，表其道之贞观者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1152694_comment'></div>至乃秉阳而健，垂象于日星；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1152694_comment'></div>得一以清，成章于云汉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1152694_comment'></div>东壁列位，主图书之秘文；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1152694_comment'></div>魄宝沦精，握河洛之命纪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1152694_comment'></div>盖乾之缊至赜矣，天之文有烂矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1152694_comment'></div>眇觌太古，铺观往牒，三五之世，德化醇茂，故伏牺受龙图以作八卦，轩辕得龟篆以朝万灵，放勋获玉泥青绳之文，帝舜膺赤文绿错之瑞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1152694_comment'></div>夏商以降，绩用昭明，故大禹梦苍水之符，帝乙拜玄玉之字，西伯之赤雀止户，武王之白鱼入舟，皆盛烈通于神祇，茂勋格于穹厚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1152694_comment'></div>繇是奇物谲诡以效质，珍图炳焕以告休，宣纯禧而奋景炎，形宝训而示灵眷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1152694_comment'></div>斯固殊尤绝迹，旷千载而罕逢；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1152694_comment'></div>卓异倜傥，为百祥之称首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1152694_comment'></div>不然者，又何以运契于中和之极，兆发乎至治之期，杂霸已还，寂寥而无纪，合符之盛，启迪而必先者哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1152694_comment'></div>崇文广武仪天尊道宝应章感圣明仁孝皇帝陛下之御天下，十有二载也，纂二圣之丕基，揽八纮之鸿绪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1152694_comment'></div>中道底定，庶邦协和，玉烛阳明，珠躔轨道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1152694_comment'></div>颂声载路，协气横流，百工维时，五兵不试。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1152694_comment'></div>仁风衍于无外，洪化驰而若神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1152694_comment'></div>品物茂遂而由仪，群黎富庶而知教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1152694_comment'></div>徽纆之刑几错，弦诵之声相闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1152694_comment'></div>人自谓于羲皇，家悉为于邹鲁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1152694_comment'></div>行苇勿践，忠厚之性成；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1152694_comment'></div>天网弥疏，宽大之德著。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1152694_comment'></div>淳源载复，治具毕张。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1152694_comment'></div>皇上方端居穆清之中，独运陶甄之表，执粹精而思道，宅清明而在躬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1152694_comment'></div>极深研几，渊默雷震，扬蕤绚景，辉光日新，固已浚哲之懿升闻，憯怛之爱敦洽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1152694_comment'></div>金玉其度，追琢而惟精；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1152694_comment'></div>云日之表，就望而无极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1152694_comment'></div>当其爱景长至，阴魄下弦，斗城靓深，虎闱䆗窱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1152694_comment'></div>建章万户，筦籥之有严；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1152694_comment'></div>卫尉千屯，谁何而载肃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1152694_comment'></div>银汉左界，玉绳西倾，挈壶之漏屡移，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_36_1152694", 1152694, "Clauses/108/Comments/0")'>膝席</span>之对云罢，方将凝神于蠖濩，宁体于清閒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1152694_comment'></div>静虑合于希夷，嘉应通于肸蚃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1152694_comment'></div>俯及乙夜，阒乎严扃，焕发灵光，皎若白昼，乃有真灵降于霄极，胪语示乎休徵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1152694_comment'></div>将求衣而趋对，忽乘飙而灭迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1152694_comment'></div>天子于是申以斋戒，致其精明，爰及献岁发春之初，祗受大中祥符之锡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1152694_comment'></div>九宾宿设，亲拜于广庭；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1152694_comment'></div>八神前驱，奉引于黄道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1152694_comment'></div>寘之恭馆，藏于东序。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1152694_comment'></div>乃复肆眚于绵县，易号于初元。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1152694_comment'></div>惠赉浃于五管，爵秩加乎群后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1152694_comment'></div>均合饮之泽以尚齿，推给复之典以贵农。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1152694_comment'></div>皇明诞敷，纯嘏均被。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1152694_comment'></div>繇是徇东人之勤请，考乾封之旧章，将以陟介丘，禅社首，奉符而行事，刻号以告成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1152694_comment'></div>扬二圣之休光，为天下之壮观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1152694_comment'></div>列城除道，有司讲仪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1152694_comment'></div>龟策告犹，云气呈瑞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1152694_comment'></div>宜象物之咸若，徯我后以来苏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1152694_comment'></div>三神眷怀，万邦和会，而灵心昭答，玄应沓臻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1152694_comment'></div>以为庶人靡常，犹毕星之好雨；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1152694_comment'></div>群小多辟，或夏虫之疑冰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1152694_comment'></div>虽况施之殊伦，舆情之成口，犹复先甲而申告，以儆于清衷，方将应期而绍至，以彰乎绝瑞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1152694_comment'></div>惟元年仲夏既望之后夕，上复梦神人谕以谆谆之意，期以来月锡符于泰山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1152694_comment'></div>于是浚发德音，申儆执事，有依类托寓之异，当疾置飞驰以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1152694_comment'></div>粤勒钟纪铭，铸浑叶度，肇自初吉，以及生明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1152694_comment'></div>惟兹岩岩之峰，荐发穰穰之瑞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1152694_comment'></div>祥光夜烛，成十煇之姿；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1152694_comment'></div>卿霭朝跻，结九葩之状。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1152694_comment'></div>是月之六日也，粤有梓匠，晨诣灵液亭，给升斸之役。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1152694_comment'></div>草露方渥，人迹罕至，忽得黄素于灌莽之上，其文有「皇帝崇孝育民，寿历遐岁」之言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1152694_comment'></div>周章震骇，魂思飞越，亟白引进使曹利用，宣政使李神福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1152694_comment'></div>即共捧持，以诣封禅经度制置使臣钦若、臣安仁，缄縢载严，骑置来献。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1152694_comment'></div>皇上周旋钦翼，夙夜斋明，醰粹内充，典章兼举，命廊庙之元宰，暨左右之信臣，分授使前，奉导灵贶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1152694_comment'></div>驿传云至，诏跸出迎，羽卫星陈，官师景从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1152694_comment'></div>弁冕端委，亲拜受于苑中；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1152694_comment'></div>玄图秘文，复遍示于群下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1152694_comment'></div>先是，阴云待族，大雨濯枝，需泥治道之是艰，沾服废礼之为惧；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1152694_comment'></div>是日也，悬县澄霁，佳气郁葱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1152694_comment'></div>杲杲之驭上跻，光华在旦；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1152694_comment'></div>丛丛之姿迭媚，纷郁垂文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1152694_comment'></div>五弦之风载薰，九光之霞成绮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1152694_comment'></div>神人胥悦，戬谷来同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1152694_comment'></div>矧乃绵蕞之仪，素已草具；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1152694_comment'></div>翠葆之驾，乃先启行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1152694_comment'></div>既备物以吉蠲，俾有司而翊卫，载以威辂，入于应门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1152694_comment'></div>星旄先驱，金奏并作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1152694_comment'></div>天子方复弭鸾旗而税龙驭，抚毡案而坐帷宫，穆穆皇皇，以俟夫玄符之至也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1152694_comment'></div>既而步自阊阖，率先群司，纳之殊庭，是为秘宝，且复讨论前载，追求遗范。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1152694_comment'></div>煇景下烛，秦既作畤；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1152694_comment'></div>珍瑞云获，汉亦起宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1152694_comment'></div>其后因轨迹而增崇，建名称而不朽者，非可以悉数也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1152694_comment'></div>乃诏鲁郡，申饬攸司，爰就灵区，茂建清宇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1152694_comment'></div>授规于哲匠，董役以廷臣，朴斲前施，塈涂咸备，法《大壮》而取象，曾不日以克成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1152694_comment'></div>直寒门□□之庭，镇阿阁神房之麓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1152694_comment'></div>云封崛起，回对于轩檐；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1152694_comment'></div>泉流冽清，载环于阶墄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1152694_comment'></div>祗若天贶，表以徽名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1152694_comment'></div>既而慎择灵辰，揭之题榜，乃有玄鹤，集于雕甍，清唳引之，坠羽而去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1152694_comment'></div>斯又九皋之仙质，千岁之纯精，挺胎化之姿，告寿昌之兆者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1152694_comment'></div>及夫亲封泥检，载扬槱燎，降自阴道，禅于方丘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1152694_comment'></div>会朝明堂，肆觐东后，灵泽及于四海，神化驰于六幽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1152694_comment'></div>天子乃抚节盘桓，凭轼游豫，周爰溥览，以届于兹，瞻堂构以改容，临清流而发叹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1152694_comment'></div>金炉朱火，修潜德以升闻；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1152694_comment'></div>羽盖清尘，彰健行之不息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1152694_comment'></div>旋轸饮至，天成地平，因时计功，金相玉振。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1152694_comment'></div>且以为古之哲后，褒纪瑞命，方牍所述，踵武可徵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1152694_comment'></div>至若甘露黄龙，标于年历；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1152694_comment'></div>芝房朱雁，播于乐章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1152694_comment'></div>或作绘以彰施，或缉经以论著，皆所以昭答报降，垂示方来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1152694_comment'></div>爰诏下臣，颂兹徽烈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1152694_comment'></div>恭惟紫书秘牒，荐锡于玉晨，福应之大者也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1152694_comment'></div>灵宫真宇，列峙于坰野，制作之盛者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1152694_comment'></div>非有迁、雄之博物通达，崔、蔡之发挥清丽，邹、枚之论辨，曹、王之气质，又曷能敷陈景铄，述宣鸿明，著之金石之刻，流乎亿万之祀？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1152694_comment'></div>如臣肤浅，岂能演畅？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1152694_comment'></div>拜命之下，燥吻惟勤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1152694_comment'></div>颂叹游扬，虽豁于素蕴；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1152694_comment'></div>博约温润，宁企于前修。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1152694_comment'></div>伏纸<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_112_1152694", 1152694, "Clauses/346/Comments/0")'>怔忡</span>，将□□□。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1152694_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_113_1152694'>太始权舆，邃古之初。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1152694_comment'></div>结绳而治，斯文阙如。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1152694_comment'></div>三五迭兴，受命合祛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1152694_comment'></div>河洛开奥，乃出图书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1152694_comment'></div>岐周发祥，凤止高冈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1152694_comment'></div>火流于屋，鱼跃于航。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1152694_comment'></div>灵眷谆谆，赤文煌煌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1152694_comment'></div>金策之赐，剪殷启疆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1152694_comment'></div>卯刀之撰，□□□□。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1152694_comment'></div>秘图玄契，旷绝靡常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1152694_comment'></div>惟皇建极，与天合德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1152694_comment'></div>有开必先，神休叵测。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1152694_comment'></div>清夜戒期，圣容斯觌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1152694_comment'></div>旭日朝跻，真符云获。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1152694_comment'></div>节彼崇巘，天帝之孙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1152694_comment'></div>刺经定议，发祉闿□。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1152694_comment'></div>泉流毖涌，和景晏温。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1152694_comment'></div>□玄申锡，明灵有赫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1152694_comment'></div>云篆腾晶，冰纨襞积。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1152694_comment'></div>殊类响答，奇应山沓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1152694_comment'></div>樵蒸礼成，蓼萧庆洽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1152694_comment'></div>邃宇翚飞，揭榜雕楣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1152694_comment'></div>建兹显号，式昭鸿禧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1152694_comment'></div>□□□□，翠旄扬蕤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1152694_comment'></div>福应之盛，煇光在兹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1152694_comment'></div>鲁邦奕奕，秦观巍巍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1152694_comment'></div>封云荟蔚，浪井涟漪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1152694_comment'></div>岿然宏构，永镇方祇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1152694_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_141_1152694'>大中祥符二年十一月十七日。</div><div id='poem_sentence_141_1152694_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1010&endYear=1010')">1010年8月4日</a>　受命与晁迥等详定《祀汾阴仪注》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1011&endYear=1011')">1011年</a>　京府狱空，有诗寄府尹。作品：京府狱空降诏因寄大尹学士。<div id='poem_129151' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_129151' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/129151?labeling=true' target='_blank'>京府狱空降诏因寄大尹学士</a><span class='authorDate'>（1011年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_129151")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_129151_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_129151'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_129151'>长安恶少罢探丸，桴鼓声沉禁网宽。<div id='poem_sentence_0_129151_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_129151'>三尺旧章闲玉律，八行优诏下金銮。<div id='poem_sentence_1_129151_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_129151'>帝临宣室方前席，民值唐年耻画冠。<div id='poem_sentence_2_129151_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_129151'>终日讼庭无一事，早调伊鼎佐汤盘。<div id='poem_sentence_3_129151_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_129151'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_129151_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1011&endYear=1011')">1011年</a>　国史院进《太祖纪》，帝指出其中有义例未当者，王钦若诿过于杨亿等。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1011&endYear=1011')">1011年12月</a>　奉敕撰《石公（兴保）神道碑铭》作品：大宋故棣州防御使光大夫检校□□□持节棣州诸军事行棣州刺史兼御史大夫上柱国西平郡开国公食邑三千四百户食实封二百户赠贝州观察使石公神道碑铭。<div id='poem_1152699' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152699' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152699?labeling=true' target='_blank'>大宋故棣州防御使光禄大夫检校□□□持节棣州诸军事行棣州刺史兼御史大夫上柱国西平郡开国公食邑三千四百户食实封二百户赠贝州观察使石公神道碑铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1011年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152699")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152699_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152699'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152699'>夫功加于时，《周官》藏于盟府；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152699_comment'></div>忠以奉上，马史列于世家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152699_comment'></div>盖智勇之诞生，必在乎将相之族；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152699_comment'></div>庆灵之回复，允钟乎公侯之门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152699_comment'></div>若乃冯厚于德基，济美于勋阀，若季孙之仕鲁，是为世卿，条侯之仕汉，继掌兵柄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152699_comment'></div>□□馀比光弗□人见之于西□公矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152699_comment'></div>公讳□□，字□□，其先□□周之胄，盛于淇卫之邦，《春秋》所记，官族甚盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152699_comment'></div>孝谨之誉，既符于西京；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1152699_comment'></div>伟丽之姿，实显于晋室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1152699_comment'></div>积累深远，蕃衍扶疏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1152699_comment'></div>今为大梁人也，惟烈考讳守信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1152699_comment'></div>以河目龟文之表，通龙韬鹖冠之学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1152699_comment'></div>□□祖以光启王业，奉□宗以四征。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1152699_comment'></div>□□握兵星□□□□□□□太祖宣戡乱之功，佐佑<span class='inlineComment2'>（下阙）</span>太宗极常尊之数，周旋无悔，高朗令终。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1152699_comment'></div>凡节制五镇，而一保釐西都，历位守中书令、追册为尚书令、卫王，累封秦王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1152699_comment'></div>而曾王父讳锐，累赠太保，兼侍中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1152699_comment'></div>曾祖妣王氏，追封赵国太夫人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1152699_comment'></div>王父□，累赠太师，兼中书令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1152699_comment'></div>祖妣王氏，追封魏国太夫人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1152699_comment'></div>皆由□□之贵□□□王之□□母曰秦国太夫人魏氏，蕴积善庆，诞生畯良。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1152699_comment'></div>公始在孩提，居然颖秀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1152699_comment'></div>歧嶷之表，本乎天资；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1152699_comment'></div>偏伍之容，彰于儿戏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1152699_comment'></div>先王见而异之，拊其背曰：「军旅之事，仲尼辞以未闻；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1152699_comment'></div>《诗》《礼》之资，郤縠由之登用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1152699_comment'></div>不学墙面，古典所非；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1152699_comment'></div>遗子金籯，昔人不取」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1152699_comment'></div>因遣就外傅，俾之讲习□□□□并晓□□□而不遗，多识前言，博通大义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1152699_comment'></div>建隆初，以任子之令，补东头供奉官，始年十四。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1152699_comment'></div>□□尚食副使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1152699_comment'></div>太祖方创业垂统，训师阜财。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1152699_comment'></div>丕昭皇灵，式遏乱略；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1152699_comment'></div>寤寐人杰，讲求武经。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1152699_comment'></div>成汤之日新是图，文王之朝食靡暇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1152699_comment'></div>每东□延访之□西清□□之□必□□□□□□□□□其能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1152699_comment'></div>或质之以烦挐，俾剖释其槃结；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1152699_comment'></div>或叩之以疑似，俾弹射其否臧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1152699_comment'></div>咫尺不违，□机攸慎，公应对明辩，风义甚高，太祖奇之，即拜如京使，且有意于进用也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1152699_comment'></div>属紫坛苍璧，将事于亲□，毡案帷□，□严于宿寝，命公为御营四面都巡检。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1152699_comment'></div>□□□□□□□□□道□□□居岑寂，群灵受职而咸洎，至尊高枕而攸宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1152699_comment'></div>未几，领顺州刺史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1152699_comment'></div>专域之重，荐启于侯封；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1152699_comment'></div>两绶之荣，仍参于内侍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1152699_comment'></div>太宗皇帝天飞在运，帝箓升名，四夷奉珍，诸侯辑瑞，闽越举□而宿卫，勾吴献□于有司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1152699_comment'></div>九州攸同，三乘澈□。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1152699_comment'></div>□□□□□□□□□□□□□□□靡怀，秉武节而躬讨，公从容进对，慷慨请讨，愿得执殳，以备前驱，□抡而当一队，太宗嘉之，以为御寨四面都巡检。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1152699_comment'></div>罙入之举，止诛于元恶；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1152699_comment'></div>干棷之寄，允赖于□□。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1152699_comment'></div>帝□无□□之虞，群下□□□之罚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1152699_comment'></div>太原平，录其劳，加实封。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1152699_comment'></div>太宗益知其有驭众之略，将付以治戎之任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1152699_comment'></div>天街之北，祲氛未消，引弓之民，仍岁为寇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1152699_comment'></div>自晋人失幽陵之地，周室复三关之壤，列鄣相望，盛兵□□。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1152699_comment'></div>□有李□守□之能，□□□□防□之□。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1152699_comment'></div>□□命公为□阳关驻泊都监。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1152699_comment'></div>公内□□□，外□□□，□□□□□□□□容□生养威，怀必胜之略。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1152699_comment'></div>单醪所及，绝甘而悉周；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1152699_comment'></div>爟火斯传，对博而无废。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1152699_comment'></div>威名以震，纪律用张。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1152699_comment'></div>会先王捐馆宛丘，公即见星而往，行哭孺慕，哀感路人，倚庐绝浆，仅成死孝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1152699_comment'></div>有诏起复□□将军、顺州团练使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1152699_comment'></div>□世之赏□□于元□□墨之□乃□□□□雍熙□□□□□□□□□□□支之生羌，连党项之杂种，犯关纵扰，以干灵诛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1152699_comment'></div>命公为银、夏、绥、麟、府州故关都巡检使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1152699_comment'></div>秋气始至，塞外早寒，□□□□，胶折弓劲，公因率麾下以□戎索由罨□众，并黑□□，□□中，戎人数千骑安义于□□，立分精骑二千，持短兵伏于□侧，戎人□□□□□□□以□□□急击，斩首百馀级，逐北数十里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1152699_comment'></div>鼓儳泓水，吻合于沉机；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1152699_comment'></div>献馘泮宫，聿腾于善颂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1152699_comment'></div>□诏褒谕，英声著闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1152699_comment'></div>俄丁内艰，殆将灭性，中旨抑夺，急于用才，出为澶州驻泊都监，以绥军政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1152699_comment'></div>朔方犹□□车未□□□银、夏缴巡之寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1152699_comment'></div>两河□□，佳兵未戢，复□高阳□□□□□□□知□□军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1152699_comment'></div>未几，知莫州军州事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1152699_comment'></div>涿鹿之野，百雉□制惟雄；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1152699_comment'></div>文□之邦，九合之□所出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1152699_comment'></div>公缓带为治，雅歌自娱，疆事益修，条□咸叙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1152699_comment'></div>太宗念服戎之斯久，属乘塞之甫宁，□□□□□□修觐，俄为西京水南北都巡检使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1152699_comment'></div>实先王□守之地，多□□去□之人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1152699_comment'></div>□□□□，素□□□第，美槚成列，俯迩于茔阡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1152699_comment'></div>慰勤孝之□怀，多□公之清宴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1152699_comment'></div>时星□犹朗，□□方驰，公慨然叹曰：「金革未息，吾恐不得久居此矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1152699_comment'></div>月馀，真拜蕲州团练使、京兆府驻泊兵马钤辖，兼管华□□商巡检兵马捕□等事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1152699_comment'></div>戎酋假息，□□于恢疏；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1152699_comment'></div>边垒戒严，不忘于备□。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1152699_comment'></div>□□□镇□□所集，兼总数道，以当一面，徙公为延州路钤辖，兼管界都巡检使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1152699_comment'></div>至道中，命范廷召为都部署，俾公副之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1152699_comment'></div>总万旅以□征，□五□而□会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1152699_comment'></div>山川聚米，虏已见于成擒；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1152699_comment'></div>甲胄起□，才皆思于贾勇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1152699_comment'></div>既致千□之□，乃为绝漠之行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1152699_comment'></div>锡□□□容□□金鼓之□□□□有□□□□□□□拒王师，公以其蠢蠢之妖，无假堂堂之阵，选敢死士数百人，衔枚夜袭，尽灭其族，无有噍类。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1152699_comment'></div>自是吴移、越移等□公□□□恩，望风来归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1152699_comment'></div>适与贼遇□□池，彼既□□公□□□□出□□□□□□□中流矢而踣，公挺立□□□□敢向□□□□□□□□□□□□□□□□□□我，而我武益奋，凶党遂奔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1152699_comment'></div>左轮朱丹，岂尝言□；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1152699_comment'></div>□书月至，安敢宁居？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1152699_comment'></div>朝命班师，不获穷讨，公蓄锐气以克壮，恨渠魁之未歼，谓军吏曰：「彼朝□者，非临阵先遁，将擒□□下矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1152699_comment'></div>□太宗□□□□，公□□□□皇帝□任旧人，慎重边寄，命公知威虏军事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1152699_comment'></div>明年，单于万骑，长围孤堞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1152699_comment'></div>云梯并进，术尽于九攻；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1152699_comment'></div>赪壤仅存，危极于三版。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1152699_comment'></div>公以众寡既悬，利于坚壁，激劝斯在，莫如挥金，大发官帑以□□士□□□执□□□□之□□□□□□□□□事宁□□□□□□□□既□□□□□矢石雨下，杀伤甚多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1152699_comment'></div>乌乌声乐，宿夕皆遁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1152699_comment'></div>完守之绩，帝用嘉之，就拜棣州防御使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1152699_comment'></div>俄以足疾，移知邢州，又改知澶州事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1152699_comment'></div>众潦并集，洪河暴涨，激竹箭之迅浪，溢金堤之□防，公洗心以斋□□致□考古制以沉□□□□□□□□□□□冀于弭患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1152699_comment'></div>□□□水□攸□是□□苗亦有秋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1152699_comment'></div>乐和之声，腾于里谚；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1152699_comment'></div>保鄣之效，简于天衷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1152699_comment'></div>而美珍有加，削章荐至，亦既受代，肩舆而归，赐告家居，以便颐养。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1152699_comment'></div>王人太医，晨夕诊问。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1152699_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1152699_comment'></div>不幸以□□□年秋八月十一日启手足于□义坊之第，享年五十□。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1152699_comment'></div>□□闻讣，嗟悼□久，□□□□□□□□守□监护丧事，凡百费用，悉从官给。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1152699_comment'></div>以明年秋八月甲午，归葬于河南洛阳县平乐乡宣武村梓泽原之先茔，举夫人弘农县君杨氏祔焉，礼也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1152699_comment'></div>夫人即故保大军节度使廷璋之□女，□□□德，仪于通门，先公而亡，不□□□□□□□□□崇仪□□□□□□□□□□□□内朝，尝为小相，角巾东道，方庇大宗，实华胄之恭人，钟高闳之积庆；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1152699_comment'></div>次曰懿孙，西头供奉官，温良自守，淑慎靡渝，俯及胜冠，已彰肯构。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1152699_comment'></div>五女：长适西头供奉官、閤门祗候程继忠，故□州团练使□元之子；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1152699_comment'></div>次适侍禁□永崇，故镇□将军、节度使廷□之子；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1152699_comment'></div>次适□□子□□□政；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1152699_comment'></div>□适供奉官曹伸，今殿前都指挥使宿肺㻮之子；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1152699_comment'></div>次在室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1152699_comment'></div>惟程氏、李氏及幼女皆夭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1152699_comment'></div>孙二人：长宗道，右班殿直；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1152699_comment'></div>次尚幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1152699_comment'></div>孙女一人，亦幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1152699_comment'></div>母弟，故镇安军节度使、检校太师、同中书门下平章事、驸马都尉、□中书令讳保吉，□□□□□□□□□□□□□□□□□□□□□□□伟望冠于友邦，胡不永年，兹用太息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1152699_comment'></div>季弟保从，东头供奉官、閤门祗候，夙负美材，未跻膴仕，亦悲早世，莫申永图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1152699_comment'></div>中书之二子，曰贻孙，崇仪副使；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1152699_comment'></div>孝孙，礼宾副使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1152699_comment'></div>咸挺英概，无忝贻谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1152699_comment'></div>□下之徵□大□□公之历官□□□□□□□□□□□□□□□□□□□□□□□。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1152699_comment'></div>公菜邑累千室，其禄位之盛矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1152699_comment'></div>五典郡政，八司戎律，屡驰使传，三护大营，斯倚任之重矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1152699_comment'></div>公至性纯孝，勤于致养，先王、太夫人或晦明微疹，息偃弗康，冠带侍旁，□调自手，药先尝而乃进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1152699_comment'></div>□宿露以□□出于诚心，未遑卜□而□□□□□□□□□□□□□□□□□□□□美，闺门称悌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1152699_comment'></div>至于击剑之妙，饮羽之能，绝出辈流，莫可伦儗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1152699_comment'></div>穰苴兵法，孔明阵图，臾匠之占，圯桥之略，悉探其赜，必索其精。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1152699_comment'></div>加以涉猎史传，应答无滞，吟咏情性，叩课特工。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1152699_comment'></div>莅澶渊日，作《言怀》诗一篇，叙止足之意，得比兴之体。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1152699_comment'></div>传□人□作□□□□□□□□□□□□□□□汉籍攸记，翁归兼文武之才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1152699_comment'></div>惟四美之难偕，于公斯无阙矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1152699_comment'></div>矧又体貌魁杰，志怀沉毅，重夫然诺，兼金是轻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1152699_comment'></div>嫉彼回邪，过门必骋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1152699_comment'></div>善保基绪，重世而莫京；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1152699_comment'></div>谨守廉隅，历官而无过。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1152699_comment'></div>咨所谓八伦之□子，王国之吉士者□。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1152699_comment'></div>大中祥符□年□□□□之□□□流根之□贝州观察使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1152699_comment'></div>贻燕之祉，久而益光；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1152699_comment'></div>褒命之数，兹焉为异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1152699_comment'></div>公本名贞，太祖改赐今讳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_147_1152699_comment'></div>允协充闾之庆，以成知臣之美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_148_1152699_comment'></div>公亦拜君之赐，退思而有光；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_149_1152699_comment'></div>裕父之蛊，聿修而无忝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_150_1152699_comment'></div>载德之盛，良可述焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_151_1152699_comment'></div>诸孤等以窀穸即安，岁月增逝，□□□□□□□□□□□□□□□□□刊贞琰，猥颁俞旨，属于下臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_152_1152699_comment'></div>顾惭空疏，谬当论撰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_153_1152699_comment'></div>九原可作，方恻于宸襟；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_154_1152699_comment'></div>一字之褒，虔遵于直笔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_155_1152699_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_156_1152699'>先民有言，立功不朽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_156_1152699_comment'></div>公于出征，屡折戎丑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_157_1152699_comment'></div>大《易》之训，积善庆馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_158_1152699_comment'></div>公之肯构，克昌门闾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_159_1152699_comment'></div>紫禁承荣，伦侯列爵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_160_1152699_comment'></div>印兮累累，绶兮若若。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_161_1152699_comment'></div>通都列城，居官有恪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_162_1152699_comment'></div>二矛重弓，从军信乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_163_1152699_comment'></div>击鼓其镗，我□□□。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_164_1152699_comment'></div>□□□□，□□□□。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_165_1152699_comment'></div>□□□□，威名日彰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_166_1152699_comment'></div>呜呼不吊，今也云亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_167_1152699_comment'></div>曲洛东流，维嵩南峙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_168_1152699_comment'></div>巩树苍茫，周原沵迤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_169_1152699_comment'></div>逝者如斯，人生到此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_170_1152699_comment'></div>真宅言归，新阡郁起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_171_1152699_comment'></div>日车奔兮风驷驰，□舟趋兮灰琯移。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_172_1152699_comment'></div>夜漫漫兮佳城闭，露瀼瀼兮宿草滋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_173_1152699_comment'></div>□□□□□□，□□德兮□□。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_174_1152699_comment'></div>□□□□□□，欲报德兮无期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_175_1152699_comment'></div>托斯文兮篆刻，尉终天之孝思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_176_1152699_comment'></div>砻密石兮表幽域，亘方来兮无愧辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_177_1152699_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_178_1152699'>大中祥符四年，岁次辛亥，十二月庚子朔、十一日庚戌建。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_178_1152699_comment'></div>翟询、翟文□刻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_179_1152699_comment'></div>勾当人张罗<span class='inlineComment2'>（《金石萃编》卷一二九。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_180_1152699_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_181_1152699'>题下原署：「翰林学士、通奉大夫、行尚书户部郎中、知制诰、同修国史、□史馆事、上柱国、南阳郡开国侯、食邑一千一百户、赐紫金鱼袋臣杨亿奉敕撰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_181_1152699_comment'></div>翰林待诏、朝散大夫、守太府少卿同正、骑都尉、赐紫金鱼袋臣尹熙古奉敕书并篆额」。</div><div id='poem_sentence_182_1152699_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1011&endYear=1011')">1011年</a>　为译经院润文官，奉诏与赵安仁同编修《元正造录》、《大藏目录》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1012&endYear=1012')">1012年3？</a>　三月或稍后，进士蒋堂携文来谒，杨亿以为极可喜，与宰相王旦书称之。作品：与王魏公书。<div id='poem_1152635' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152635' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152635?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与王魏公书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1012年3？）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1152635'><span class='label'>按：</span>《春卿遗稿》附录，光绪武进盛氏重刊本。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1152635_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1012&endYear=1012')">1012年9月28日</a>　以疾在告，帝遣中使挟太医疗之，亿拜章为谢，帝作诗慰之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1012&endYear=1012')">1012年9月</a>　以疾未愈，奏权免起居。寻以久疾求解近职。优诏不许，但权免朝直。作品：望权免十数日起居奏。<div id='poem_1152579' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152579' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152579?labeling=true' target='_blank'>望权免十数日起居奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（大中祥符五年九月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152579'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152579'>疾疹稍痊，虚羸尚甚，望许权免十数日起居。</div><div id='poem_sentence_0_1152579_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1012&endYear=1012')">1012年12月24日</a>　立刘皇后。先是，帝命亿草答辽人诏，帝有所改，亿乃引咎求罢；及议立刘氏皇后，帝欲得亿草制，使丁谓谕旨，亿难之，且言不愿苟得富贵。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1012&endYear=1012')">1012年</a>　陈越卒，亿与杜镐、陈彭年奏延恩，其后赐越兄咸同《三传》出身。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1013&endYear=1013')">1013年5月2日</a>　杨亿母亲往视阳翟别墅，得疾；亿闻之，请归省。五月二日不待报而行。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1013&endYear=1013')">1013年</a>　杨亿母亲在阳翟得疾；亿请归省，不待报而行。行前，以手简上二相，望察以微诚，宽其谴责。作品：上二相手简。<span class='inlineComment2'>（二相即王旦、向敏中。）</span><div id='poem_1152630' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152630' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152630?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上二相手简</a><span class='authorDate'>（1013年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152630")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152630_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152630'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152630'>某辄有血诚，上干台听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152630_comment'></div>某顷于许州阳翟县买得少薄田，并有一小宅子，自来舍弟倚一房在彼居止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152630_comment'></div>前月中老亲往彼看觑，忽于今日得家信，知老母风疾发动，不安至甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152630_comment'></div>已具状奏闻，暂乞假往彼看省医疗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152630_comment'></div>才候痊损，扶迎归阙就养。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152630_comment'></div>忝居近列，合候报音。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152630_comment'></div>缘某方寸已乱，顷刻难安，已一面径马连夜往彼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152630_comment'></div>伏望特垂台念，曲赐敷扬，察以危诚，宽其谴责。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1152630_comment'></div>情意陨迫，不避烦黩，伏望深垂悯恻。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1152630_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1152630'><span class='label'>按：</span>《永乐大典》卷二三六八引《杨公文集·手简》。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1152630_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1013&endYear=1013')">1013年6月11日</a>　宪官劾杨亿不俟命而去；王旦以为亿有过错，但不至于讥谤朝政。六月十一日，以亿为太常少卿，分司西京。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='efb78908a1c14d3e8c6547705a191360_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("efb78908a1c14d3e8c6547705a191360");'><span id='efb78908a1c14d3e8c6547705a191360_link'
