href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1015&endYear=1015')">1015年</a>　约本年冬，自汝州代还，知礼仪院，判秘阁、太常寺。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1015&endYear=1015')">1015年</a>　到阙，真宗以诗赐之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1016&endYear=1016')">1016年2月12日</a>　王旦上杨亿等预修之太祖、太宗两朝国史，优诏答之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1016&endYear=1016')">1016年9月</a>　杨亿以秘书监判秘阁。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1016&endYear=1016')">1016年11月23日</a>　应召预观书龙图阁，帝作诗赐之，受命赋诗。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1016&endYear=1016')">1016年11月</a>　以宰相王旦荐，礼部郎中李及出知秦州。王旦言其之所以荐及，亿益服王旦之识度。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1016&endYear=1016')">1016年</a>　入内都知秦翰卒后，于本年重赠彰国军节度，诏亿撰碑文。亿表辞所贽物，时论美之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1016&endYear=1016')">1016年</a>　约于本年，石霜楚圆禅师来访，亿与李遵勖、楚圆以为法友。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1017&endYear=1017')">1017年1月1日</a>　改元天禧，帝奉天书行荐献礼。杨亿作赋颂之。作品：天禧观礼赋。<div id='poem_1152428' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152428' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152428?labeling=true' target='_blank'>天禧观礼赋</a><span class='authorDate'>（1017年1月1日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152428")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152428_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152428'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152428'>客有嘲臣曰：「夫飘飘之气能赋，可为于大夫；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152428_comment'></div>荡荡之道不谈，见嗤于樵采。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152428_comment'></div>当今景炎震赫，休嘉翕习，礼有同节，会无后至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152428_comment'></div>容典寖盛，讴谣载路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152428_comment'></div>子尝奏伎于玉堂之署，方司籍于道家之山，智效乎官联，隶业乎雅颂，乌可后渊、云之杼叹，怯游、夏之措辞哉」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152428_comment'></div>臣应之曰：「大明升中，萤燐息照，广乐合变，巴歈绝响。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152428_comment'></div>皇上躬浚明之德，探述作之奥，尧文惟焕，禹声为律。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152428_comment'></div>三变以至于妙道，群臣绝望于清光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1152428_comment'></div>而敢饰枯槁之姿，呈露于仁寿，持瓴甋之质，唐突于玙璠？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1152428_comment'></div>斯固不知量而任其责矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1152428_comment'></div>客曰：「不然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1152428_comment'></div>海以善下，故号为谷王；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1152428_comment'></div>山匪护尘，爰配于天极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1152428_comment'></div>兜离杂奏，亦升于乐府；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1152428_comment'></div>沼沚纤植，尚参于庙荐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1152428_comment'></div>稗官之说，列于广内之藏；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1152428_comment'></div>游董之讴，备于清夜之诵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1152428_comment'></div>盖各言志，斯为乐职，亦奚畏于咎耳」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1152428_comment'></div>臣应曰：「唯唯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1152428_comment'></div>皇上御天下之二十载也，守宇嘉靖，斯民乐和，边庭卧鼓，武库包戈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1152428_comment'></div>讲万枢而俾人，序彝伦而可歌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1152428_comment'></div>南踰铜柱，西亘金河，北弥狼望，东越鳀波。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1152428_comment'></div>四表之德咸被，崇朝之泽匪颇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1152428_comment'></div>锡嘉生于庶士，均善养于中何。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1152428_comment'></div>张旃驾牡兮笃邻好，徇铎舞干兮脩国教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1152428_comment'></div>恤人隐兮如纳于隍，握道枢兮以观其妙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1152428_comment'></div>弛罟之惠兮洽于怀生，非黍之馨兮升于有昊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1152428_comment'></div>交感兮惟微，盖高兮必报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1152428_comment'></div>先是，景德之夕也，宸关靖冥，齐居洁清，脩令乃慎，观书中程。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1152428_comment'></div>息偃宁处，希微告徵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1152428_comment'></div>犹苍水之感禹梦，同金人之翔汉庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1152428_comment'></div>戒期晤语，锡瑞幽经。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1152428_comment'></div>专洗心而淳濯，果颁文于紫清。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1152428_comment'></div>逖览舆议，属国封事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1152428_comment'></div>旄头先驱，玉牒不秘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1152428_comment'></div>采倪宽之节文，述夷吾之所记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1152428_comment'></div>陟阿阁之神房，追纵乎七十有二。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1152428_comment'></div>承统得天，勒崇高世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1152428_comment'></div>复以嗣岁，诏跸中冀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1152428_comment'></div>荣河发光，灵坤制位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1152428_comment'></div>西宾相欢，簉车宿戒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1152428_comment'></div>八奏升祗，贰觞遗味。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1152428_comment'></div>醰粹格于清宁，恩霈沦乎骨髓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1152428_comment'></div>伊明祭之并脩兮，弥小心而抑畏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1152428_comment'></div>罄宇多欢，西清燕间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1152428_comment'></div>窅忘怀于赤水，邈驰想于姑山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1152428_comment'></div>至灵不测，秘感无间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1152428_comment'></div>同传岩之梦寐兮，驻列御以盘桓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1152428_comment'></div>先期之庚甲申戒，太一之威神下观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1152428_comment'></div>坐乙帐兮岑寂，望殊庭兮太息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1152428_comment'></div>倏御气以旁戾，恍排云而绝迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1152428_comment'></div>浆柘滑甘，旌霓骆驿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1152428_comment'></div>述百世之璿源，系九清之霄极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1152428_comment'></div>垂诲谆谆，厥灵赫赫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1152428_comment'></div>语秘兮珠囊，事传兮金策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1152428_comment'></div>稽尊祖之丕宪兮，享自天之纯锡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1152428_comment'></div>祗遹洪应，介福甚盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1152428_comment'></div>稽群言，建徽称，达渊衷，昭默定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1152428_comment'></div>答报贶之惟几，择元辰而申命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1152428_comment'></div>历吉习祥，首祚居正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1152428_comment'></div>讲仪物而有容，励斋明而执竞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1152428_comment'></div>若夫紫虚定位，星机宅粹，典诸神之秘图，主九阳之生气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1152428_comment'></div>象先之赜兮，至寂而谁知？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1152428_comment'></div>魄宝之精兮，常明而绝异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1152428_comment'></div>总御人灵，握可命纪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1152428_comment'></div>强为之名，尊无与二。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1152428_comment'></div>惟繠简绿文兮，于以宣其音旨；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1152428_comment'></div>惟琳阙绛房兮，于以象其奥秘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1152428_comment'></div>谓天载之无声兮，其言大备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1152428_comment'></div>谓帝居之既邈兮，其应孔迩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1152428_comment'></div>皇哉监观，屑然戾止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1152428_comment'></div>伊虚皇之锡祚兮，瑞如山兮交委。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1152428_comment'></div>又如人皇兴世，天历允归，诞生刑马之麓，财成分土□□。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1152428_comment'></div>螾彰应玉，理标奇乘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1152428_comment'></div>五精之雄运流，三百之英威升。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1152428_comment'></div>神翊化穷，变通微奄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1152428_comment'></div>九天而受职，主赤符之始基。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1152428_comment'></div>期九垓之汗漫兮，友千年之令威。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1152428_comment'></div>挹浮丘之霞袂兮，赓西母之云辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1152428_comment'></div>乘飙车于空漠，提生籍于太微。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1152428_comment'></div>右序皇历，输姓本支。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1152428_comment'></div>唯灵神之垂裕兮，应如响而弗违。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1152428_comment'></div>非夫合德之淳懿，凝祯之蕃炽，积累之凭厚，怀监之尤异，即何以恢恢大圆，讫寓以昭夫顾諟？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1152428_comment'></div>颙颙高真，降格以敷乎明晦？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1152428_comment'></div>休徵叶景福同，贞期启精虑通。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1152428_comment'></div>包众志而惟一，保大盈而若冲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1152428_comment'></div>清心而钦翼，锡类以丰融。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1152428_comment'></div>乃度建乎真阙，以萃乎子民之劝功；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1152428_comment'></div>乃增饰乎寿壤，以昭夫灵命之所从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1152428_comment'></div>乃范金而攻玉，侔睟像以致恭；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1152428_comment'></div>乃荐馨而陈信，载令甲以无穷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1152428_comment'></div>稽枢电之腾精，式表乎号荣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1152428_comment'></div>罄舆域之所括，咸列乎闬闳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1152428_comment'></div>置官局而寅奉，著节物而有经。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1152428_comment'></div>恭默以忘，玩众妙而无极；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1152428_comment'></div>吉蠲用享，监二代而作程。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1152428_comment'></div>味道之腴，配天合符。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1152428_comment'></div>念美报之斯在，必鸿名而与俱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1152428_comment'></div>内以尽其志，当罄其称谓；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1152428_comment'></div>动以观其变，必包其美善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1152428_comment'></div>夫天之称有九，曷尝不处其厚；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1152428_comment'></div>道之大居四，曷尝不极其挚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1152428_comment'></div>总清襟，考宏议，抽大猷，研秘思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1152428_comment'></div>疏瀹以虚心，登闳而立制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1152428_comment'></div>粤若疑始混天，盘古开先，判一气而有象，裁万灵而既甄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1152428_comment'></div>肇司符契，翊宣统纪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1152428_comment'></div>郁彼苍之正色，宅中黄而定位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1152428_comment'></div>蕴妙朴以无名，袭气母而不匮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1152428_comment'></div>绵绵若存，皇皇而帝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1152428_comment'></div>乘六龙以御天，首庶物而出类。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1152428_comment'></div>盖宵晨之凝命也，兹可以撰德而比义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1152428_comment'></div>又如濯濯炳灵，窈窈储精，周游罔象，出入淩兢，翊帝宸而御辨，宅天极以扬明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1152428_comment'></div>乘于至正，司人之命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1152428_comment'></div>冒九域以顾临，保群生之安定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1152428_comment'></div>大庇皇图，丕昭有庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1152428_comment'></div>冠众真之上阶，祚卜世而惟永。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1152428_comment'></div>斯灵尊之蕴道也，固可以漱芳而摛景。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1152428_comment'></div>于是建显号，司至奥，方底奉将，杨庭诞告：含生之听惟新，经礼之文再造。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1152428_comment'></div>刊以美瑜，藉之采缫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1152428_comment'></div>升龙绣裳，回鸾篆宝，备物惟精，奉珍咸造。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1152428_comment'></div>先时，易纪元之称，顺更端之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1152428_comment'></div>以天禧之告朔，遵上辛之明教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1152428_comment'></div>宿寝燕宁，京室密清。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1152428_comment'></div>属车九九，以诣夫丛宵之庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1152428_comment'></div>苾芬既荐，纯嘏具膺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1152428_comment'></div>回辕弭节，历重闉而径五城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1152428_comment'></div>还憩乎恭馆，谒隶乎上灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1152428_comment'></div>官师相规，徒御不惊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1152428_comment'></div>蔼曾宙而丕覆，淡淑气而惟清。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1152428_comment'></div>天行弥健，国容以成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1152428_comment'></div>浃欢康于庶品，腾英茂而莫京。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1152428_comment'></div>乃揆次辛，习于肇禋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1152428_comment'></div>追怀贻厥之盛，奉承如在之神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1152428_comment'></div>悟仙源之夐远，属景舆之下臻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1152428_comment'></div>述宣乎懿铄，昭报乎恩勤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1152428_comment'></div>节壹惠以增号，荐六室而同寅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1152428_comment'></div>镂秦玺，琢荆珉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1152428_comment'></div>龙旂耳耳，鹭序振振。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1152428_comment'></div>上公奉璋以恭肃，列圣在天而顾存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1152428_comment'></div>殆斋辂之息驾，饰壶人而警夜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1152428_comment'></div>祗见宗祊，躬奠樽斝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1152428_comment'></div>僾然永怀，礼无违者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1152428_comment'></div>卜郊大报，于国之阳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1152428_comment'></div>樵蒸具设，牲角无伤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1152428_comment'></div>九宾之列济济，六变之音洋洋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1152428_comment'></div>百灵受于瑞记，五畤烛于神光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1152428_comment'></div>官象物而罔忒，天明畏而孔彰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1152428_comment'></div>唯圣能享，唯德能让。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_147_1152428_comment'></div>扢嘉坛之嶕峣，外高烟于沆砀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_148_1152428_comment'></div>对越之容有孚，奔走之工无旷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_149_1152428_comment'></div>谅克诚之在兹，垂亿兆之攸仰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_150_1152428_comment'></div>旋雕轸，御端闱，俨天临于两观，纵堵观于九逵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_151_1152428_comment'></div>法鸡星而肆赦，漏蝇笔之先知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_152_1152428_comment'></div>云油然而泽布，萧蓼被而露垂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_153_1152428_comment'></div>厩置之马沃若，圜土之牢阒其。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_154_1152428_comment'></div>固室家之无外，威相庆以惟熙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_155_1152428_comment'></div>凝辰旒，负法扆，呼鞭出乎东房，委佩森乎文陆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_156_1152428_comment'></div>镂金版以扬蕤，会紫庭而成礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_157_1152428_comment'></div>就如日兮方中，戴如天兮仰止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_158_1152428_comment'></div>执万玉以相趋，植九旗而有炜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_159_1152428_comment'></div>殆鸟兽之异类，亦率舞而交至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_160_1152428_comment'></div>观夫八狄六蛮之述职，四海九州之献力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_161_1152428_comment'></div>荆楚谨包茅之供，鲜虞给守燎之役。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_162_1152428_comment'></div>走计车而相望，旅庭实而惟百。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_163_1152428_comment'></div>列三恪而有容，包十伦而为式：其助祭之尤盛也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_164_1152428_comment'></div>博士礼官之总领，执秩司仪之辨等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_165_1152428_comment'></div>素青因革以或殊，绵蕝讨论而先定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_166_1152428_comment'></div>金玉条贯兮总宸衷，粉泽彰施兮参国政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_167_1152428_comment'></div>制上下以咸秩，与天地而相并：其讲礼之得正也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_168_1152428_comment'></div>凤盖棽丽，狼狐逞威。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_169_1152428_comment'></div>前清尘兮天罼，密扶路兮雷辎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_170_1152428_comment'></div>六骏駮兮沛艾，万虎贲兮髬髵，抚皇舆而进辙，遵大道以甚夷：此容卫之多仪也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_171_1152428_comment'></div>瑄玉温泽，斋牺博硕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_172_1152428_comment'></div>沛兰之齐甘良，󵭓萧之馨充格。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_173_1152428_comment'></div>品百笾而既丰，列奇鼎而有翼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_174_1152428_comment'></div>嘉荐普淖以尽恭，至神盻蚃而辅德：此奠献之成式也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_175_1152428_comment'></div>傅御咸暨，官司靡劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_176_1152428_comment'></div>或累叶珥貂而内侍，或有客卓马而来朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_177_1152428_comment'></div>拱于著而匪懈，寘彼行而勿嚣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_178_1152428_comment'></div>戬谷之锡攸洽，陟降之容孔昭：此庶工之不佻也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_179_1152428_comment'></div>藻衮象夫，雷声默渊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_180_1152428_comment'></div>俟张弧而登举，中采茨以周旋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_181_1152428_comment'></div>奉迥酌而沃酹，步容佩以呜鋗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_182_1152428_comment'></div>躬接神于紫幄之次，如坐拜于交门之前：此宸心之至虔也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_183_1152428_comment'></div>帷宫靓深，釐庭赫敞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_184_1152428_comment'></div>受祭膰而在兹，翕天祺而专享。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_185_1152428_comment'></div>卿底日以叙徵，嘏告慈而克广。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_186_1152428_comment'></div>介南山之寿臧，跻大庭之怡畅：兹福应之不爽也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_187_1152428_comment'></div>恩典庞鸿，庆赍均被，沉贯索之星辉，遍班觞于耆指。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_188_1152428_comment'></div>室无幽而不烛，民有瘼而皆弭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_189_1152428_comment'></div>涤蒙士之瑕疵，纳群伦于物轨：此渥惠之兼济也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_190_1152428_comment'></div>原夫历祚之永，推炎汉以洎前唐；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_191_1152428_comment'></div>载祀之久，惟孝武逮于明皇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_192_1152428_comment'></div>当元鼎之际，幸甘泉而祠泰畤，奉郊以致礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_193_1152428_comment'></div>且元符绝闻，曷以昭夫天意？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_194_1152428_comment'></div>洎天宝之岁，尊金阙而造曲里，惇宗而考瑞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_195_1152428_comment'></div>然真游匪接，奚以贞乎道契？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_196_1152428_comment'></div>自馀屑屑之习仪，区区而脩废，或增置于巫史，或但益于圭币。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_197_1152428_comment'></div>或祠官之所奉，不可胜谈；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_198_1152428_comment'></div>或祀典之罔载，成乎谄祭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_199_1152428_comment'></div>稽方册以遐观，曾无足以拟议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_200_1152428_comment'></div>儒臣司礼，祗承己事，觇德容而悉同，裁颂声而弗坠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_201_1152428_comment'></div>系曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_202_1152428'>皇天上帝宅高穹兮，巍乎真祖序太宗兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_202_1152428_comment'></div>剥璋错宝施尊名兮，丽牲㪺水享众灵兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_203_1152428_comment'></div>铿钟舞籥神降格兮，燔柴通火志渊塞兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_204_1152428_comment'></div>纡轸旋衡泽𭰘濊兮，备物典册德明类兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_205_1152428_comment'></div>深居蠖濩膺眷祐兮，丕冒方国跻富寿兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_206_1152428_comment'></div>清净致治臻无为兮，亿万斯年咸保宜兮。</div><div id='poem_sentence_207_1152428_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1017&endYear=1017')">1017年4月14日</a>　从弟伟赐进士及第。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1017&endYear=1017')">1017年9月</a>　宰相王旦卒。临终前，亿受请为撰遗表上之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1017&endYear=1017')">1017年</a>　有诗送高绅出知越州。作品：送高学士知越。<span class='inlineComment2'>（薛映、钱惟演、张士逊、陈知微、刘筠等均有送诗。高绅仕历史无载。）</span><div id='poem_129231' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_129231' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/129231?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送高学士知越</a><span class='authorDate'>（1017年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_129231")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_129231_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_129231'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_129231'>万壑千岩古剡中，锦旗朱毂此临戎。<div id='poem_sentence_0_129231_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_129231'>酒厨岁取公田秫，樵舸朝分射的风。<div id='poem_sentence_1_129231_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_129231'>阁吏蒸青藏史牍，席宾簪玳奉谈丛。<div id='poem_sentence_2_129231_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_129231'>海邦讼息多幽赏，禹穴奇书为一空。<div id='poem_sentence_3_129231_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_129231'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_129231_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1017&endYear=1017')">1017年</a>　四明知礼法师晚结十僧，以修忏法三年烧身为约，冬，亿致书请留住世；又致书杭州僧遵式、明州太守李夷庚共劝知礼留世。作品：致四明知礼法师请留住世书。致释遵式托劝四明知礼法师留世书。上太守李夷庚同请释知礼住世书。<div id='poem_1152641' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152641' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152641?labeling=true' target='_blank'>致四明知礼法师请留住世书</a><span class='authorDate'>（天禧元年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152641")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152641_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152641'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152641'>亿钦闻修千日之忏，焚四大之躯，结净行之十僧，生乐邦之九品。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152641_comment'></div>窃尝具请，冀徇群情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152641_comment'></div>乞住世以为期，希传持而兴利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152641_comment'></div>愿垂许可，庶获瞻风。</div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1152641_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1152646' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152646' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152646?labeling=true' target='_blank'>致释遵式托劝四明知礼法师留世书</a><span class='authorDate'>（天禧元年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152646")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152646_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152646'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152646'>昨为明州礼座主宏发愿心，精修忏法，期以三年，并趋火化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152646_comment'></div>况此僧传持大教，为世导师，得其久住，利益甚多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152646_comment'></div>诚怀景重，窃欲劝留，罄叙克诚，遂形恳请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152646_comment'></div>得其报音，确乎不拔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152646_comment'></div>窃知忏主与之同禀，并化东南，可涉浙江之巨浸，造鄞水之净居，善说谏言，宜久住世。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1152646_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1152648' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152648' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152648?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上太守李夷庚同请释知礼住世书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1017年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152648")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152648_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152648'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152648'>亿启：违阔己来，倾凝何极！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152648_comment'></div>辄有闻白，不避渎烦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152648_comment'></div>顷者贵郡天台教主礼大师精修忏仪，前约岁纪将趋火化以泯身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152648_comment'></div>缘亿素闻其风，辄伸首劝，以其通赤城之秘典，启浙水之度门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152648_comment'></div>迥传止观之妙机，尤续能仁之慧命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152648_comment'></div>实经论之龙虎，作黑暗之明灯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152648_comment'></div>傥住世之久如，固利生之寖广。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152648_comment'></div>函封沓委，志愿确坚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1152648_comment'></div>率和四众之情，叩端不已；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1152648_comment'></div>度越重江之阻，驰讯继臻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1152648_comment'></div>得其来音，颇似相许。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1152648_comment'></div>尚虑持于宿誓，或匪顾于幻躯，望敦外护之心，共延住寿之数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1152648_comment'></div>叶宣大教，克树胜因。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1152648_comment'></div>遐祝在兹，繁述为此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1152648_comment'></div>凛冬冠序，精摄是宜。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1152648_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1018&endYear=1018')">1018年8月16日</a>　受命为撰皇太子册文。九月八日，册立皇太子。作品：册皇太子文。<div id='poem_1152429' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152429' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152429?labeling=true' target='_blank'>册皇太子文</a><span class='authorDate'>（天禧二年九月八日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152429")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152429_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152429'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152429'>维天禧二年，岁次戊午，九月庚申朔，八日丁卯，皇帝若曰：夫以天下为家者，三王之通制；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152429_comment'></div>居正体之贰者，万世之大本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152429_comment'></div>明嫡之建，爰主于宗器；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152429_comment'></div>元良之重，以正乎庶邦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152429_comment'></div>国家德源深长，孙谋锡羡，丕承积累之庆，保定储副之位，所以经大猷而畅淳烈也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152429_comment'></div>咨尔皇子、崇仁保运宣德守正功臣、建康军节度、管内观察处置等使、开府仪同三司、守太保、兼中书令、行江宁尹、上柱国、升王、食邑五千户、食实封三百户某，冲粹居质，聪哲成性，钟清宁之孚佑，表徇齐于羁贯，生而知于孝爱，天攸纵于艺能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152429_comment'></div>奇智夙彰，英声外发，书社南纪，毓德少阳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152429_comment'></div>勤至寝门，乐游讲肄，资弦诵以崇术，仪星海而昭象。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1152429_comment'></div>宝极凝祐，官师率和，公言亟飏，舆咏胥洽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1152429_comment'></div>永惟长发之懿，慎固守成之业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1152429_comment'></div>明两攸属，佥谋大同，式阐承华，以旌上嗣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1152429_comment'></div>今册尔为皇太子，仍改名某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1152429_comment'></div>于戏！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1152429_comment'></div>体仁而不违，于以济众；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1152429_comment'></div>好谦而自牧，乃能服民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1152429_comment'></div>惟正人之务亲，惟前言之多识。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1152429_comment'></div>师俭而固，介祉于无疆；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1152429_comment'></div>宝慈以持，锡善而不匮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1152429_comment'></div>一乃心而祗肃，永来誉之广渊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1152429_comment'></div>往钦哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1152429_comment'></div>勤宣令图，以对越我祖宗之景命，不其韪欤！</div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1152429_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1018&endYear=1018')">1018年</a>　冬，拜工部侍郎。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1018&endYear=1018')">1018年</a>　本年前后，荐谢绛文章。召试，谢绛擢秘阁校理、同判太常礼院。又教仲简诗赋。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1019&endYear=1019')">1019年1月9日</a>　与钱惟演等同知贡举。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1019&endYear=1019')">1019年3月26日</a>　权同知贡举，坐考较差谬，二十六日降授秘书监。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1019&endYear=1019')">1019年6月</a>　王钦若出判杭州，真宗及臣下皆有诗送，独亿不作，盖嫉其为人倾巧也。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1019&endYear=1019')">1019年10月3日</a>　丁母忧。值行郊礼，未卒丧，起复工部侍郎。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1019&endYear=1019')">1019年</a>　约于本年，致书袁州守黄宗旦，请楚圆禅师出世说法。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1019&endYear=1019')">1019年</a>　约于本年，手书《遗教经》万余言，为后人所宝藏，多有题跋。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1020&endYear=1020')">1020年4月9日</a>　起复为翰林学士。钱惟演请序班在己上，降诰从之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1020&endYear=1020')">1020年</a>　四明高僧知礼再约焚身期已届满，亿致书恳请时知永兴军寇准劝其留世。适马知节、李遵勖亦奏请赐知礼法号。乃有诏赐知礼号法智大师。亿以《启》贺之。作品：贺法智受命服启。<div id='poem_1152637' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152637' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152637?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺法智受命服启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1020年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152637")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152637_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152637'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152637'>亿启：夙陪清侣，因熟高名，闻传教于赤城，久领徒于鄞水。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152637_comment'></div>达契经之旨，叶彼重宣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152637_comment'></div>精修忏之规，臻乎本净。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152637_comment'></div>机缘胥应，真俗焉依。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152637_comment'></div>顷更值于严凝，常奉陪于枢弼，辄求论荐，式冀褒扬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152637_comment'></div>俄遇疾以归田，殆解麾而趋阙，涉乎累岁，绝望报音。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152637_comment'></div>暖席未遑，飞邮遽至，前言克践，私愿允谐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152637_comment'></div>事虽自于乞邻，道弥光于出世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1152637_comment'></div>所有大师赐衣敕命，已于本州递角内附去，必垂领受。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1152637_comment'></div>谨奉状咨问，兼伸陈贺，伏惟照察。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1152637_comment'></div>谨状。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1152637_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1020&endYear=1020')">1020年</a>　法智以书贺亿起复翰林学士，亿有书谢之。又三致书问法义。作品：谢法智贺书。<span class='inlineComment2'>（法智即僧知礼。）</span>致法智三问书。<span class='inlineComment2'>（法智即僧知礼。）</span>谢法智答三问启。<span class='inlineComment2'>（法智即僧知礼。）</span>谢法智答义书启。<span class='inlineComment2'>（法智即僧知礼。）</span><div id='poem_1152636' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152636' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152636?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢法智贺书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1020年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152636")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152636_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152636'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152636'>亿启：近者起于苫庐，荐膺纶检，复尘内署，仍冠迩班。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152636_comment'></div>属创钜之痛除，固杌枯之才尽，猥承甄录，罔克避辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152636_comment'></div>徒僶勉以从公，益支离而取诮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152636_comment'></div>教主大师迥敦道眷，遐枉贺笺，仰窥勤渥之私，但切感惭之抱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152636_comment'></div>谨修状陈谢。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1152636_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1152638' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152638' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152638?labeling=true' target='_blank'>致法智三问书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1020年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152638")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152638_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152638'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152638'>亿启：远寄示长书为答，重复窥玩，但钦渊奥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152638_comment'></div>俗学肤浅，何以奉酬？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152638_comment'></div>辄缘来意，虔致三问，具于别纸，请赐见答。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152638_comment'></div>傥契卑心，别具咨报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152638_comment'></div>然希取證于泥日，亦冀专修于末供也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152638_comment'></div>亿白。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1152638_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1152639' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152639' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152639?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢法智答三问启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1020年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152639")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152639_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152639'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152639'>亿启：近致问端，远承答诲，恭闻了义，尤涤蒙襟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152639_comment'></div>盖龙象之极谈，续云雷之雄韵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152639_comment'></div>依而领解，奉以遵行，足照了于色空，乃混同于心境。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152639_comment'></div>往生随愿，福智并严，受顶记以何赊，得法乳之正味。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152639_comment'></div>然而陋闻所及，结舌匪容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152639_comment'></div>有疑须争，罔关于人我；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152639_comment'></div>觌面相示，期达于本源。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152639_comment'></div>若乃谷响随声，动彰于答应；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1152639_comment'></div>镜火立照，随显于形规。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1152639_comment'></div>如理而言，表枢机之迅发；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1152639_comment'></div>依经以解，味糟粕以沉研。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1152639_comment'></div>其如离句绝非，终焉杳邈；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1152639_comment'></div>丧词忘虑，曷取攀缘？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1152639_comment'></div>惟少室之宗风，本灵山之笑视。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1152639_comment'></div>瞥然起念，已蹉西天之程；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1152639_comment'></div>兀尔忘情，正坐山鬼之窟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1152639_comment'></div>有修有證，虑剜肉以成疮；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1152639_comment'></div>以心传心，乃标指而为月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1152639_comment'></div>自他路绝，生佛道齐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1152639_comment'></div>纵直下以承当，已未来而丧失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1152639_comment'></div>故黄檗痛杖于临济，至再三而自知；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1152639_comment'></div>船子挥楫于夹山，一刹那而顿悟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1152639_comment'></div>傥全无扣激，遂泯于宗风；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1152639_comment'></div>然少室机锋，为求于道契。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1152639_comment'></div>恭承旨喻，但积钦隆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1152639_comment'></div>谅惟领众之馀，允获深禅之乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1152639_comment'></div>未期瞻拜，但积倾依。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1152639_comment'></div>谨奉状起居谢。</div><div id='poem_sentence_27_1152639_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1152640' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152640' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152640?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢法智答义书启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1020年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152640")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152640_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152640'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152640'>亿启：近于公邮，获披芳翰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152640_comment'></div>承法裕以增胜，享净乐以无涯，景仰尤深，感叙奚罄？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152640_comment'></div>属拘公局，夐阻句筵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152640_comment'></div>驰系于兹，敷宣宁既。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152640_comment'></div>谨修状谢。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1152640_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1020&endYear=1020')">1020年6月14日</a>　受诏注释真宗御集。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1020&endYear=1020')">1020年6月22日</a>　以翰林学士充考试官，试礼部下第特奏名举人。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1020&endYear=1020')">1020年6月</a>　真宗疾，亿受宰相寇准密令，草表请太子监国，亿屏左右为之辞。既而以寇准被酒事泄。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1020&endYear=1020')">1020年7月</a>　以请太子监国，寇准受谴，亿几受责，丁谓爱其才而护之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1020&endYear=1020')">1020年7月</a>　授冯振枢密使，亿为草制。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1020&endYear=1020')">1020年8月4日</a>　准诏举陈诂、王宗道，充崇文院检讨。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1020&endYear=1020')">1020年</a>　亿以章得象有公辅器，约于本年，荐之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1020&endYear=1020')">1020年11月21日</a>　丁谓罢相，亿草制，以为“不道之诛，难逃于汉法”。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1020&endYear=1020')">1020年</a>　约于卒前，李遵勖绘杨亿、刘筠、李遵勖、环禅师等人像，为《禅会图》。后为宋庠所得，有诗记其事。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1020&endYear=1020')">1020年</a>　微恙，临卒，戒家人勿哭；卒前作偈一首遗李遵勖。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1020&endYear=1020')">1020年12月1日</a>　卒。赵德文有诗悼挽。门人郑戬倍道至许州会葬。<br /></div>
-----end

武夷山（崇安）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='7c01532ed6184185820e40c6675a2a2b_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("7c01532ed6184185820e40c6675a2a2b");'><span id='7c01532ed6184185820e40c6675a2a2b_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=994&endYear=994')">994年</a>，21岁</div><div id='7c01532ed6184185820e40c6675a2a2b' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=994&endYear=994')">994年</a>　游武夷山，姻亲彭悦、张彝宪等款留之，为张赋诗题壁。作品：赠张季常。<div id='poem_129297' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_129297' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/129297?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赠张季常</a><span class='authorDate'>（994年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_129297")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_129297_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_129297'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_129297'>叠巘参差翠绕门，雕梁贺燕自成群。<div id='poem_sentence_0_129297_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_129297'>杀鸡日夕期嘉客，种竹寒暄对此君。<div id='poem_sentence_1_129297_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_129297'>且向东皋输黍稷，便应北阙降玄纁。<div id='poem_sentence_2_129297_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_129297'>子真漫说耕岩石，不奈声名四远闻。<div id='poem_sentence_3_129297_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_129297'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_129297_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>

-----title
丽水
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='6d4755fedbb94fe38675462369474a5a_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("6d4755fedbb94fe38675462369474a5a");'><span id='6d4755fedbb94fe38675462369474a5a_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=998&endYear=1000')">998-1000年</a>，25-27岁</div><div id='6d4755fedbb94fe38675462369474a5a' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=998&endYear=998')">998年12月3日</a>　到处州任，上谢表。作品：知处州谢到任表。<div id='poem_1152443' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152443' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152443?labeling=true' target='_blank'>知处州谢到任表</a><span class='authorDate'>（998年12月3日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152443")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152443_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152443'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152443'>臣某言：臣昨奉敕差知处州军州事，已于今月三日赴本任讫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152443_comment'></div>远辞螭陛，权剖使符，百城之任既优，五䌽之荣斯极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152443_comment'></div>臣某<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>臣早自孤平，获逢开泰，徒以雕虫之伎，遂尘汗简之司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152443_comment'></div>皇帝陛下夤奉宗祧，旁求俊乂，谓臣处于群萃，窃画饼之名，知臣耻于进趋，挺素丝之节，度越伦辈，超践掖垣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152443_comment'></div>复误赐于选抡，获同司于笔削。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152443_comment'></div>家徒四壁，贫方甚于临邛；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152443_comment'></div>字赏千金，书未悬于秦市。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152443_comment'></div>特推恩于陋巷，俾将命于列藩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1152443_comment'></div>既克就于国书，又骤加于勋籍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1152443_comment'></div>未出瀛州之署，尚参文石之班。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1152443_comment'></div>盖以臣早奉庭闱，久栖辇毂，离邦寖远，怀土滋深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1152443_comment'></div>乌鸟之情，实巢南之是切，刍荛之恳，须伏阁以自陈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1152443_comment'></div>封章才黩于冕旒，俞诏已颁于蓬荜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1152443_comment'></div>幸一麾之甚便，复再疏以请行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1152443_comment'></div>陛下察以寸心，恕其九死，许扶携于老幼，令密迩于乡闾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1152443_comment'></div>况浙右奥区，缙云善地，闾阎蕃庶，土壤膏腴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1152443_comment'></div>声教所覃，俗知礼让；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1152443_comment'></div>耕桑甚广，民少惰游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1152443_comment'></div>今岁虽罹旱暵之灾，尚多溉灌之利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1152443_comment'></div>人无菜色，亩有馀粮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1152443_comment'></div>属邻郡之不登，故谷籴之微贵，提封之内，安堵如常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1152443_comment'></div>前春已来，不至乏绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1152443_comment'></div>一境偶无于疲瘵，九重望减于焦劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1152443_comment'></div>臣谨当恭守诏条，恪居官次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1152443_comment'></div>裤襦服政，岂期月之敢期；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1152443_comment'></div>冰檗检身，固生平之所履。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1152443_comment'></div>傥渝素守，是速灵诛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1152443_comment'></div>臣又念朝辞日，得面圣颜，亲承睿旨，以俯邻于桑梓，又获奉于甘旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1152443_comment'></div>推从欲之仁，广听卑之造，特许终于考秩，且未议于替移。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1152443_comment'></div>即臣举族知归，杀身莫报！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1152443_comment'></div>况丘园甚近，鸡犬相闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1152443_comment'></div>乡里亲姻，或谐于聚首；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1152443_comment'></div>弟妹婚嫁，免至于失时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1152443_comment'></div>上以慰慈母之心，次以了私门之事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1152443_comment'></div>而臣齿发方盛，驽蹇未衰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1152443_comment'></div>抱椠怀铅，终预诸儒之末；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1152443_comment'></div>摩顶至踵，须酬万乘之知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1152443_comment'></div>冒昧上言，陨越无措，臣无任云云。</div><div id='poem_sentence_37_1152443_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=998&endYear=998')">998年12月</a>　初至处州，累旬恶风，有诗忧之。作品：至郡累旬恶风。<div id='poem_129117'
