ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=999&endYear=999')">999年</a>　监缙云县茶盐酒税韩永锡任满归阙，作诗送。作品：送韩永锡归阙，奉举韩永锡状。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=999&endYear=999')">999年</a>　以状荐举韩永锡。作品：奉举韩永锡状。<div id='poem_1152508' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152508' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152508?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏举韩永锡状<span class='inlineComment2'>（自后出知处州。）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（999年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152508")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152508_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152508'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152508'>臣忝封朝寄，获总郡符。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152508_comment'></div>官吏之间，合知其能否；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152508_comment'></div>阙庭之远，敢避于荐论！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152508_comment'></div>臣伏见前监本州缙云县茶盐酒税、三班借职韩永锡，早以明经，曾干场屋；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152508_comment'></div>晚不择禄，遂齿班行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152508_comment'></div>一自监临，六迁寒燠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152508_comment'></div>检身奉上，挺夙夜匪懈之诚；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152508_comment'></div>守道安贫，励风雨弗渝之操。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1152508_comment'></div>士流推慕，名迹蔼然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1152508_comment'></div>臣询于群伦，备知行实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1152508_comment'></div>筦榷之任，不足尽才；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1152508_comment'></div>州县之间，可使从政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1152508_comment'></div>傥预字人之选，必成循吏之名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1152508_comment'></div>臣窃睹淳化四年选进士诸科，举人充班行，曾降宣命，如两任六考无遗阙，许与文资安排。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1152508_comment'></div>永锡考秩之间，与诏书而未应；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1152508_comment'></div>临涖之际，实官业之甚优。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1152508_comment'></div>伏望圣慈，特与文资升奖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1152508_comment'></div>徇私黩货，保其不为；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1152508_comment'></div>茍罹此愆，臣甘当连坐之典云云。</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1152508_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=999&endYear=999')">999年5月20日</a>　乞减龙泉县三处酒坊税额。作品：论龙泉县三处酒坊乞减额状。<div id='poem_1152509' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152509' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152509?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论龙泉县三处酒坊乞减额状</a><span class='authorDate'>（999年5月20日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152509")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152509_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152509'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152509'>臣获领郡符，合求民瘼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152509_comment'></div>苟自图于缄默，是上负于忧勤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152509_comment'></div>傥有救于疮痍，亦无辞于鼎镬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152509_comment'></div>臣窃见龙泉县松瞿、小梅、松源三处酒坊，一年共趁办额钱一千九贯八百一十九文足，并是勾当人自备曲米、本柄，酝造沽卖，收趁上件净利钱数纳官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152509_comment'></div>自来州司枷项差勒人员军将，须管甘认。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152509_comment'></div>勾当并皆破卖家业及身命偿官，并均摊干系人填纳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152509_comment'></div>臣自到任所，深访其由，盖是往年王师讨伐江南，龙泉乃其境上，钱俶多调发卒士防遏边陲，此时榷酤，甚获其利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152509_comment'></div>县民张延熙，贪婪无识，遂入状添起虚额，买扑勾当。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1152509_comment'></div>自江南平定，钱俶进纳土疆，书轨既同，幅员无外，所遣丁卒，皆已罢归，遂致酤卖不行，课利亏失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1152509_comment'></div>元买扑户，并尽底破卖家产，填纳不足，只有身命偿官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1152509_comment'></div>州司又不敢陷失旧额，须至差勒平民，以至籍人家财，通纳身命，蠹伤和气，流患生民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1152509_comment'></div>百姓亦尝诣阙披陈，诏下三司相度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1152509_comment'></div>虽行刺问，寻便共申。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1152509_comment'></div>所司惟聚敛是图，陆沉无报，疮痍益甚，冤痛弥深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1152509_comment'></div>又况龙泉县连接七闽，弥亘千里，山川险绝，闾舍稀疏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1152509_comment'></div>所有三处酒坊，并皆越在草莽，数间小屋，仅庇风霜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1152509_comment'></div>虽有榷酤之名，全无酝酿之具。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1152509_comment'></div>盖是勾当人相承败阙，兴创不成，须至破败田园，遭离刑辟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1152509_comment'></div>见今勾当人并系徵欠司枷项徵督，每三数日，一度就科。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1152509_comment'></div>盖省司之益峻课程，官吏之惧于书罚，纵加决责，何以徵填？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1152509_comment'></div>挤沟壑而可期，扣阊阖而无路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1152509_comment'></div>臣备见此事，深究其由。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1152509_comment'></div>自以受两朝之圣知，忝百城之忧寄，有所闻见，岂敢缄藏？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1152509_comment'></div>虽获罪以犹言，庶期死而得请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1152509_comment'></div>伏望皇帝陛下念远民之涂炭，采微臣之刍荛，更询相府之吁谟，勿令计司之关决。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1152509_comment'></div>傥谓狂瞽之有实，所侵功利以非多，旧额之中，减其大半，人乃受赐，天实听卑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1152509_comment'></div>茍事下于有司，必谨守于旧制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1152509_comment'></div>王泽既壅，民病愈滋，虽龚、黄临之，亦不能为理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1152509_comment'></div>臣复见陛下践祚之始，尽放天下逋欠，寰海之内，歌舞太平，虽甚盛德，无以加此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1152509_comment'></div>又自守郡之后，寅奉诏书，莫不以优恤为先，未尝以课利为急。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1152509_comment'></div>百姓既足，长府自然有馀；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1152509_comment'></div>一人向隅，满堂为之不乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1152509_comment'></div>臣忝称谏列，获佩郡符，早受特达之知，敢辞进越之罪！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1152509_comment'></div>祈天俟命，伏切愚衷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1152509_comment'></div>干犯宸严，无任兢惶激切之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_34_1152509_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1152509'><span class='label'>按：</span>二年五月二十日发，九月二十三日敕差命官专监，取一年收到钱为额。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1152509_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=999&endYear=999')">999年5月</a>　处州旱，遣人于宣阳观祈雨。作品：宣阳观祈雨文。<div id='poem_1152717' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152717' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152717?labeling=true' target='_blank'>宣阳观祈雨文</a><span class='authorDate'>（999年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152717")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152717_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152717'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152717'>咸平二年月日，知军州事杨某，谨遣丽水县尉侯俨，以香茶酒纸之奠，致祷于宣阳观叶天师之神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152717_comment'></div>卉物具腓，骄阳为患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152717_comment'></div>倬彼云汉，昭回于天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152717_comment'></div>畏景载炎，膏泽靡降。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152717_comment'></div>川原将竭，稼穑卒瘏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152717_comment'></div>比屋嗷嗷，大命将止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152717_comment'></div>去岁小歉，斯民荐饥，贫者不厌于糟糠，富室亦空于担石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152717_comment'></div>羹藜啜菽，力耕数耘，期乎有秋，以续其命；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1152717_comment'></div>而朱夏将半，溽暑方隆，肥𧔥兴妖，旱魃为虐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1152717_comment'></div>人亦劳止，天其忍诸？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1152717_comment'></div>唯神佐佑化工，惠绥兹土。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1152717_comment'></div>庙貌载肃，阴隙孔昭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1152717_comment'></div>乃眷含生，讵可无意？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1152717_comment'></div>人者神之主，食者民之天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1152717_comment'></div>民失其天，遂至于死；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1152717_comment'></div>神乏其主，复将畴依？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1152717_comment'></div>神其鉴兹下诚，请于上帝，使龙起沮泽，蜧跃层波；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1152717_comment'></div>电鞭一挥，雨足散洒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1152717_comment'></div>沟塍流溢，溪谷沸腾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1152717_comment'></div>藁然善苗，如揠而长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1152717_comment'></div>年谷大稔，厉鬼不行，家获仓箱之储，人免涂炭之患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1152717_comment'></div>当洁祀典，以答神休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1152717_comment'></div>若分野缠炎，阴阳作沴，凡有殃咎，宜加守土者之身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1152717_comment'></div>百姓无辜，庶可以免。</div><div id='poem_sentence_23_1152717_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=999&endYear=999')">999年</a>　夏，致仕李寅自洪州寄诗，次韵。作品：次韵和致仕李殿丞寅见寄之什因以纪赠。<div id='poem_129328' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_129328' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/129328?labeling=true' target='_blank'>次韵和致仕李殿丞寅见寄之什因以纪赠<span class='inlineComment2'>（李公寓居历阳，近徙于洪井）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（999年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_129328")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_129328_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_129328'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_129328'>乡国驰名几十春，鸣皋一旦九天闻。<div id='poem_sentence_0_129328_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_129328'>翔鸾栖棘曾为吏，金鼎调梅未致君。<div id='poem_sentence_1_129328_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_129328'>百里象雷嫌碌碌<span class='inlineComment2'>（公尝权历阳县政）</span>，片言折狱厌云云<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：公任三衢司理数考。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_2_129328_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_129328'>诗名已是齐康乐，笔力何曾减右军。<div id='poem_sentence_3_129328_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_129328'>抗表忽然干凤扆，拂衣殊欲谢人群。<div id='poem_sentence_4_129328_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_129328'>都缘梁苑慵为赋，且免钟山被勒文。<div id='poem_sentence_5_129328_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_129328'>清夜独吟牛渚月，高秋时望帝乡云。<div id='poem_sentence_6_129328_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_129328'>鲤庭禀训门逾盛，兰畹传芳气益薰。<div id='poem_sentence_7_129328_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_129328'>尽室远依洪井侧，直钩犹钓楚江濆。<div id='poem_sentence_8_129328_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_129328'>西山有药应须饵，待看蜺旌入紫氛。<div id='poem_sentence_9_129328_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_129328'></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_129328_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=999&endYear=999')">999年</a>　久旱得雨，有诗记之。作品：己亥年郡中夏旱遍祷群望喜有甘泽之应。<div id='poem_129307' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_129307' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/129307?labeling=true' target='_blank'>己亥年郡中夏旱遍祷群望喜有甘泽之应</a><span class='authorDate'>（999年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_129307")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_129307_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_129307'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_129307'>旱魃偏为虐，阳乌益以骄。<div id='poem_sentence_0_129307_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_129307'>何曾柱础润，惟恐土山焦。<div id='poem_sentence_1_129307_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_129307'>请祷弥增洁，阴灵亦孔昭。<div id='poem_sentence_2_129307_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_129307'>云兴不待族，风细欲鸣条。<div id='poem_sentence_3_129307_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_129307'>隐辚雷车转，霏微雨足飘。<div id='poem_sentence_4_129307_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_129307'>层阴低匝野，鸿霈近连宵。<div id='poem_sentence_5_129307_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_129307'>庭树含佳色，村田长善苗。<div id='poem_sentence_6_129307_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_129307'>藓痕缘屋壁，泉脉吐山椒。<div id='poem_sentence_7_129307_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_129307'>辙鲋那忧涸，园蔬岂待浇。<div id='poem_sentence_8_129307_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_129307'>官渠逗水急，客路裛尘销。<div id='poem_sentence_9_129307_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_129307'>掾吏阶前贺，耕夫垄上谣。<div id='poem_sentence_10_129307_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_129307'>秋成知有幸，岁欲近玄枵。<div id='poem_sentence_11_129307_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_129307'></div><div id='poem_sentence_12_129307_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=999&endYear=999')">999年</a>　夏，于郡斋东北建凝霜阁，撰文记之。作品：处州郡斋凝霜阁记。<div id='poem_1152673' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152673' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152673?labeling=true' target='_blank'>处州郡斋凝霜阁记</a><span class='authorDate'>（999年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152673")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152673_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152673'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152673'>夫谈仁义者，必就閒宴；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152673_comment'></div>避炎酷者，必登高明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152673_comment'></div>故鲁史述其三宫，诗人咏夫百堵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152673_comment'></div>中堂湫隘，妇姑由是勃溪；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152673_comment'></div>大夏穹崇，燕雀以之相贺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152673_comment'></div>若乃叔孙之葺墙屋，陆抗之治庐舍，去如始至，后无以加。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152673_comment'></div>贤者用心，岂徒然耳！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152673_comment'></div>兹郡唐季之乱，王泽弗流，大姓名豪，窃据其地，腹背受敌，兵戈日寻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1152673_comment'></div>假息朝晡，迁保岩险。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1152673_comment'></div>迄今郡署，冠西山之颠，高出千岑，俯窥万井。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1152673_comment'></div>徼道迂曲，何翅乎七盘；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1152673_comment'></div>峰顶坦夷，不过乎数亩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1152673_comment'></div>厩库之外，参以吏舍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1152673_comment'></div>向之平田，占其半矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1152673_comment'></div>堂庑之制，因而偪下；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1152673_comment'></div>亭榭之设，率以乘危。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1152673_comment'></div>每温风勃兴，畏景流烁，如临炽炭，若游沸鼎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1152673_comment'></div>冰壶屡挹，内热靡蠲；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1152673_comment'></div>羽扇失挥，流汗相属。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1152673_comment'></div>俄顷之际，燋烂可期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1152673_comment'></div>盖由乎改筑之初，面势素定，因重岗之回抱，且四垂之斗绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1152673_comment'></div>堂涂迫窄，不开南荣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1152673_comment'></div>栋宇胶葛，无有北户。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1152673_comment'></div>故郁蒸之戒候，必薰灼之是忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1152673_comment'></div>自国朝已来，领郡者仅以十数，率困簿领，未暇经营。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1152673_comment'></div>及余之涖是邦也，承数贤之馀，庶务修举，曹无巧诋之吏，下无失职之民，清心处之，期月而治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1152673_comment'></div>适离暵热，殆将委顿，因创飞阁于东北隅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1152673_comment'></div>运甓累土以成基，斩木陶瓦而备用，仅及旬浃，层构岿然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1152673_comment'></div>轩窗洞开，景象辐凑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1152673_comment'></div>峰峦掩映，杂火云之嵯峨；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1152673_comment'></div>沟塍糺纷，涨时雨以澎濞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1152673_comment'></div>闾阎森以相错，竹树翠而成帷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1152673_comment'></div>百里虽迥，不隐于秋毫；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1152673_comment'></div>万象实繁，如在于指掌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1152673_comment'></div>固可胸中荡于鄙吝，眸子极于泬寥，披襟以当雄风，岸帻以度永昼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1152673_comment'></div>凭高望远，式动能赋之心；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1152673_comment'></div>置酒娱宾，便为逃暑之饮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1152673_comment'></div>夫如是，乃体宁虑澹，心和气平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1152673_comment'></div>庄室弥虚，神明所以来舍；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1152673_comment'></div>孔堂不坏，丝竹期乎有闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1152673_comment'></div>岂但逶迤退食之馀，从容案吏而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1152673_comment'></div>阁既成，命之曰「凝霜」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1152673_comment'></div>将使来者无执热之烦，登者有解愠之适。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1152673_comment'></div>亦犹《抱朴子》所谓玄冰丸、飞雪散，用以却暑，兼取夫相胜之义云耳。</div><div id='poem_sentence_43_1152673_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=999&endYear=999')">999年7月</a>　以雨未足，复求于宣阳观。作品：宣阳观赛雨文。<div id='poem_1152718' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152718' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152718?labeling=true' target='_blank'>宣阳观赛雨文</a><span class='authorDate'>（999年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152718")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152718_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152718'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152718'>近以愆伏之气，沴于阴阳；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152718_comment'></div>旱暵之灾，延于稼穑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152718_comment'></div>某忝守兹土，不敢遑宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152718_comment'></div>虽天灾流行，厥有冥数；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152718_comment'></div>而神道正直，享于至诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152718_comment'></div>惟天师敷佑一方，历祀浸远，功济万类，化驰九幽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152718_comment'></div>惨舒天吏之权，陟降上帝之右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152718_comment'></div>肇建真宇，聿为殊庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1152718_comment'></div>尸祝具陈，若亢仓之居㟪𡾊；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1152718_comment'></div>祭祀不绝，犹朱邑之在桐乡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1152718_comment'></div>灵贶孔昭，斯民攸赖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1152718_comment'></div>是用备菲薄之奠，陈危苦之辞，愿以一介之躯，少赎百姓之命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1152718_comment'></div>精意恳祷，冥感玄通，山川出云，天地交泰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1152718_comment'></div>祁祁甘泽，濡涸辙而有馀；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1152718_comment'></div>莓莓原田，取嘉谷而可冀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1152718_comment'></div>明神无乏祀之愧，农夫慰望岁之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1152718_comment'></div>夫如是，神之降祥至矣，民之受赐深矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1152718_comment'></div>当与周弃播种百谷，勾龙平易水土，功德相若，社而稷之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1152718_comment'></div>虽肸蚃无方，高明不宰，然豺獭有祭，亦出于自然；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1152718_comment'></div>黍稷非馨，岂资于备物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1152718_comment'></div>爰洁祀典，以答神休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1152718_comment'></div>适因昭报之辰，更露虔祈之恳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1152718_comment'></div>以畏日流毒，多稼向荣，水泉枯乾，山田硗埆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1152718_comment'></div>民非稻不食，稻非雨不滋，秋孟以来，浸润恐竭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1152718_comment'></div>岂昔也如响之斯答，而今也为惠之不终？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1152718_comment'></div>一篑之功，傥或中辍，一溉之益，亦必后枯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1152718_comment'></div>神其鉴兹下诚，终乃前烈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1152718_comment'></div>殒越颠沛，罔敢自安？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1152718_comment'></div>洗心沥肝，仰冀冥助。</div><div id='poem_sentence_28_1152718_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=999&endYear=999')">999年9月</a>　辽南侵，宋高阳路先锋田绍斌率众破契丹于保州境。亿在处州得报，上表贺之。作品：贺高阳关路破贼表。<div id='poem_1152446' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152446' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152446?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺高阳关路破贼表</a><span class='authorDate'>（999年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152446")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152446_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152446'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152446'>臣某言：得进奏院报，前月二十四日，镇定高阳关马步军都部署傅潜等，差侍禁郭筠赍到状奏，称九月十七日，先锋使田绍斌差人报杨嗣、石普杀下蕃贼二千馀人，斫到贼头五百个，夺到马五百疋，衣甲器械不少者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152446_comment'></div>蠢尔凶渠，敢犯边境，灵诛所及，丑类以歼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152446_comment'></div>克传三捷之音，实赖一人之庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152446_comment'></div>臣某<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>臣闻疆埸之事，用备不虞，金革之兴，盖非获巳，而况并建万国，守在四夷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152446_comment'></div>崇山之阿，或蚁壤之斯漏；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152446_comment'></div>隆车之辙，犹螳臂之敢张。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152446_comment'></div>舞干虽示于怀徕，祝网岂容于越逸！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152446_comment'></div>是用西蕃命将，北落徵师，授以庙谋，龚行天讨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1152446_comment'></div>兵锋未接，豺狼尚肆于无厌；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1152446_comment'></div>汤沐既陈，虮虱果闻于相吊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1152446_comment'></div>渠魁折北，馀党稿原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1152446_comment'></div>斩馘擒俘，已倍云中之级；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1152446_comment'></div>投戈弃甲，更齐熊耳之山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1152446_comment'></div>获冀马以谷量，表胡庭之运尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1152446_comment'></div>此盖皇帝陛下道符天锡，化比神驰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1152446_comment'></div>樽俎折冲，悬知于千里；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1152446_comment'></div>边陲息警，将自于一戎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1152446_comment'></div>伫收督亢之图，便勒燕然之石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1152446_comment'></div>克清朔漠，永洽承平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1152446_comment'></div>臣忝备谏垣，远分忧寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1152446_comment'></div>明庭献捷，阻闻振凯之音，宣室策勋，不在称觞之列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1152446_comment'></div>歌时恋圣，倍万常情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1152446_comment'></div>臣无任欢欣激切。</div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1152446_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=999&endYear=999')">999年</a>　秋，温州从事聂茂先赴阙过处州，以诗送之。作品：送温州聂从事赴阙。<div id='poem_129356' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_129356' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/129356?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送温州聂从事赴阙<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup></a><span class='authorDate'>（999年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_129356")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_129356_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_129356_0'>① 原作闽，据祝刻本改　从事先自此郡移任永嘉</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_129356'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_129356'>佩鞬来海上，七见岁星移。<div id='poem_sentence_0_129356_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_129356'>务剧操刀割，书成插羽驰。<div id='poem_sentence_1_129356_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_129356'>诗传百越遍，诏下九霄迟。<div id='poem_sentence_2_129356_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_129356'>束带朝阊阖，归艎汎渺㳽。<div id='poem_sentence_3_129356_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_129356'>旧游聊税驾，雅饮且轩眉。<div id='poem_sentence_4_129356_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_129356'>郑驿欢相接，牙弦辱所知。<div id='poem_sentence_5_129356_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_129356'>病惊琼树瘦，醉露玉峰奇。<div id='poem_sentence_6_129356_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_129356'>上马便西笑，何须诉酒卮。<div id='poem_sentence_7_129356_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_129356'></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_129356_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=999&endYear=999')">999年</a>　聂茂先以其为吏处州日所作诗《云堂集》及从事温州日所作诗《永嘉集》，求亿为序。作品：温州聂从事云堂集序。温州聂从事永嘉集序。<div id='poem_1152655' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152655' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152655?labeling=true' target='_blank'>温州聂从事云堂集序</a><span class='authorDate'>（999年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152655")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152655_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152655'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152655'>《云堂集》者，永嘉从事聂君茂先试吏括苍日所赋诗也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152655_comment'></div>君雍熙三年举进士，策名乙科，由一命随牒兹郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152655_comment'></div>属仍岁大稔，比户小康，赋舆先期，狱讼滋少。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152655_comment'></div>盘牙悉解，郡阁鲜簿领之勤；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152655_comment'></div>爟火不惊，幕府无书檄之事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152655_comment'></div>婉画勿用，善政已成，飘飘然其于游刃固有馀地矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152655_comment'></div>于是占胜选奇，寻幽览古。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152655_comment'></div>名山福地，必命驾以游；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1152655_comment'></div>美景良辰，乃登高而赋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1152655_comment'></div>精骛八极，智周万物，触类有得，少选成章，信所谓造次颠沛必于是者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1152655_comment'></div>其或心将化驰，意与境会，闻箫韶者不知肉味，逃虚空者蔑闻人声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1152655_comment'></div>追鸿濛而与游，抟扶摇而上击。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1152655_comment'></div>其探赜也，若求玄珠于赤水，索金简于丹台；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1152655_comment'></div>其得隽也，如纵涸鲋于西江，骋归鸿于碣石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1152655_comment'></div>故再岁之内，所赋凡二百篇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1152655_comment'></div>东瓯山水之清丽，缙云谣俗之朴古，佛刹玄祠之标槩，讼庭官舍之形胜，见于题咏之什矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1152655_comment'></div>一郡人物之选，一时寮佐之盛，林谷高蹈之士，吴楚薄游之贤，备于赠答之作矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1152655_comment'></div>名邦风物之美，通人吏隐之适，齐氓富寿之乐，居上神明之化，形于倡和之篇矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1152655_comment'></div>若乃《国风》之作，骚人之辞，风刺之所生，忧思之所积，犹防决川泄流，荡而忘返，弦急柱促，掩抑而不平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1152655_comment'></div>今夫聂君之诗，恬愉优柔，无有怨谤，吟咏情性，宣导王泽，其所谓越《风》《骚》而追二《雅》，若西汉《中和》、《乐职》之作者乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1152655_comment'></div>君素工于诗，及载笔从军，又得兹壤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1152655_comment'></div>前后左右，陟降俯仰，皆青山白云，茂林脩竹，嗜欲之物，旦暮在前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1152655_comment'></div>矧又旁睨石门，谢公游历之所；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1152655_comment'></div>却瞻东阳，隐侯赋咏之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1152655_comment'></div>精爽未泯，风流尚存，宜乎聂君之于诗弥所感发，岂二子之风期吻合，潜有佽助欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1152655_comment'></div>而此都之灵粹閟蓄，将有散越欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1152655_comment'></div>不然，何其得之多也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1152655_comment'></div>去年，予假守是邦；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1152655_comment'></div>今年，通理虞曹，外郎常公，将命赋民盐于邻郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1152655_comment'></div>既饮至，且达聂君之命，以集为贶，而序是求。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1152655_comment'></div>雅意甚勤，饰让非礼，聊叙梗概，以塞其请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1152655_comment'></div>若夫咏歌嗟叹之不足，识者开卷而尽见也，岂仆倦谈者所能一二乎！</div><div id='poem_sentence_31_1152655_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1152657' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152657' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152657?labeling=true' target='_blank'>温州聂从事永嘉集序</a><span class='authorDate'>（999年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152657")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152657_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152657'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152657'>河东聂君，昔从事缙云日，赋诗二百篇，予既序之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152657_comment'></div>及随牒永嘉，再见闰月，所得弥广，凡七百章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152657_comment'></div>会秩满北归，假道敝邑，又示予以新集，且徵辞焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152657_comment'></div>予才非患多，学素不足，已尝僶勉从命，狂简成文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152657_comment'></div>运族庖之刀，一割犹可；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152657_comment'></div>殴市人而战，再鼓必衰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152657_comment'></div>深病未能，岂足以辱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152657_comment'></div>而君之请弥笃，且予之让莫谐，固不暇扬搉而言，但撮其梗槩而已。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1152657_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=999&endYear=999')">999年</a>　进士陈在中自闽赴京选调，过处州谒亿，亿作序送之。作品：送进士陈在中序。<div id='poem_1152649' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152649' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152649?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送进士陈在中序</a><span class='authorDate'>（999年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152649")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152649_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152649'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152649'>昔孔子五十而读《易》，以至韦编三绝，然后知天命之终始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152649_comment'></div>自卫反鲁，删《诗》定《书》正《乐》，《雅》《颂》各得其所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152649_comment'></div>六籍既立，百王由是取法焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152649_comment'></div>盖夫《易》者，世历三古，人更三圣，达性命之际，通神明之德，探赜索隐，钩深致远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152649_comment'></div>故曰：《易》不可见，即乾坤之道几乎息矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152649_comment'></div>若乃《春秋》、《诗》、《书》、《礼》、《乐》，犹五行之更用事，而《易》之为原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152649_comment'></div>古者十有五而志于学，既耕且养，三年而通一艺，三十而五经立也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152649_comment'></div>至于学《易》，必俟夫四五十。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1152649_comment'></div>岂非心志未定，不可以参阴阳之变；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1152649_comment'></div>涉猎未博，不可以睹圣哲之奥？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1152649_comment'></div>至有唇腐齿落，块然面墙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1152649_comment'></div>其或沿波讨源，剪焉先觉，黜章句异端之说，研《彖》《象》极深之言，不俟知命之岁，不求一卷之师，天人之占，鬼神之变，消息盈虚之理，吉凶悔吝之徵，自明而诚，若指诸掌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1152649_comment'></div>非夫禀人伦之上智，得天下之至精，其孰能与于此乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1152649_comment'></div>颍川陈君，世家瓯闽，寝处坟索，少好《易》象，洞达其要。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1152649_comment'></div>尝慷慨发愤，以学者传授失其宗本，去圣逾远，亡羊多岐，大惧夫羲、文之微言将坠于地，乃铺衍遗意，发挥成文，作赋六十四篇，篇演一卦之义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1152649_comment'></div>前年从赋南安郡，薄游上都，扣门造予，以赋为贽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1152649_comment'></div>予一见而甚骇之也，深者厉之，坚者钻之，高者跂而望之，幽者俯而探之，汗漫无际者凌厉以求之，窈冥无状者罔象以索之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1152649_comment'></div>隐几弥旬，恍然有得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1152649_comment'></div>或谈于台阁僚友，或语于场屋流辈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1152649_comment'></div>闻善如响，争取以观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1152649_comment'></div>于是陈君之名，一旦籍甚，所谓《易赋》者，亦盛行于时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1152649_comment'></div>既观艺泽宫，不利攸往，盖聿来下国，剿无先容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1152649_comment'></div>新羁之足，争据于要津；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1152649_comment'></div>寒谷之苗，不沾于暖律。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1152649_comment'></div>非战之罪也，其势所然乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1152649_comment'></div>退居旧庐，高卧环堵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1152649_comment'></div>今年，予典郡瓯越，命驾爰来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1152649_comment'></div>乘桴浮海，冒风涛之险；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1152649_comment'></div>杖策徒步，越岭峤之阻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1152649_comment'></div>将以生平素业，伸于知己。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1152649_comment'></div>若予之孤陋迂阔，何足以当之哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1152649_comment'></div>陈君其亟随乡书，便卜西笑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1152649_comment'></div>有司方选擢寒隽，牢笼英杰，以副万乘虚左侧席之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1152649_comment'></div>君博综文史，详练经术，词彩奋发，学殖坚深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1152649_comment'></div>取片玉于昆冈之颠，彯华缨于文石之陛，可以俯拾，未足为难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1152649_comment'></div>矧乃行有馀力，深穷《系》《象》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1152649_comment'></div>天子方复三代之制，开庠序，聚生徒，选经明行脩之士列于学官，以教胄子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1152649_comment'></div>如君醇儒，当中兹选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1152649_comment'></div>仆谓君明圣人之道，将有以及乎生民，扬于王庭，宜取显位，一博士之任，岂足为君辱哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1152649_comment'></div>勉哉西游，努力加饭！</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_39_1152649'></div><div id='poem_sentence_39_1152649_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=999&endYear=999')">999年</a>　秋晚，有诗发功名未立、鬓发先凋之叹。<div id='poem_129351' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_129351' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/129351?labeling=true' target='_blank'>秋晚</a><span class='authorDate'>（999年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_129351")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_129351_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_129351'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_129351'>秋晚弥岑寂，天空见泬寥。<div id='poem_sentence_0_129351_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_129351'>溪流拖白练，树叶剪红绡。<div id='poem_sentence_1_129351_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_129351'>露菊英初吐，霜钟韵渐调。<div id='poem_sentence_2_129351_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_129351'>清光开旭旦，爽气逐惊飙。<div id='poem_sentence_3_129351_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_129351'>鹰击秦原迥，鸿归楚水遥。<div id='poem_sentence_4_129351_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_129351'>星高汉将出，胶折虏兵骄。<div id='poem_sentence_5_129351_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_129351'>元亮田多废，安仁鬓恐凋。<div id='poem_sentence_6_129351_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_129351'>功名殊未立，对景自无憀。<div id='poem_sentence_7_129351_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_129351'></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_129351_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=999&endYear=999')">999年10月</a>　上赐冬衣，表谢之。作品：谢赐衣表。<div id='poem_1152451' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152451' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152451?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢赐衣表</a><span class='authorDate'>（999年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152451")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152451_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152451'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152451'>臣某言：今月十六日，翰林艺学郤俊至，伏蒙圣慈赐臣敕书一道，紫绮纯绵旋襕一领，并赐屯驻本城诸军员僚初冬衣袄者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152451_comment'></div>解衣之赐，猥及于下臣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152451_comment'></div>挟纩之仁，更均于列校。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152451_comment'></div>光生郡邸，喜动辕门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152451_comment'></div>臣某<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>伏以崇文广武圣明仁孝皇帝陛下诞膺元符，恭临大宝，惠必先于逮下，志惟在于爱人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152451_comment'></div>鸟兽氄毛，甫及严凝之候；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152451_comment'></div>衣裳在笥，爰推赐予之恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152451_comment'></div>在涣汗之所沾，虽容光而必照。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1152451_comment'></div>如臣者，任叨符竹，地僻瓯吴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1152451_comment'></div>奉汉诏之六条，方深祗畏；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1152451_comment'></div>分齐官之三服，忽荷颁宣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1152451_comment'></div>纂组极于纤华，纯绵加于丽密。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1152451_comment'></div>玺书下降，窃窥云汉之文；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1152451_comment'></div>驿骑来临，更重皇华之命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1152451_comment'></div>但曳履而增惕，实被服以难胜，矧于戎行，亦膺天宠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1152451_comment'></div>干城虽久，曾无汗马之劳；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1152451_comment'></div>守土何功，独惧濡鹈之刺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1152451_comment'></div>仰瞻宸极，唯誓糜捐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1152451_comment'></div>臣与军校等无任感天荷圣、欢呼蹈舞、激切屏营之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1152451_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1152451'><span class='label'>按：</span>《武夷新集》卷一二。又见《皇朝文鉴》卷六三，《文翰类选大成》卷一四二，《宋四六选》卷九等。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1152451_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=999&endYear=999')">999年10月10日</a>　子云堂生。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=999&endYear=999')">999年10月</a>　州田稻再熟，上表贺之。作品：贺再熟稻表。<div id='poem_1152445' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152445' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152445?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺再熟稻表</a><span class='authorDate'>（999年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152445")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152445_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152445'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152445'>臣某言：据本州丽水等县状申，今年人户所种早稻，自秋初刈后，为雨水调适，元根再发青苗，结实成熟，共得两收，已具州司，别状闻奏者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152445_comment'></div>多稼并熟，所谓有年；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152445_comment'></div>嘉谷再登，斯为上端。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152445_comment'></div>臣某<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>臣闻昔者后稷之功既著，一稃二米显其祥；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152445_comment'></div>成周之道方隆，异亩同颖昭其应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152445_comment'></div>贡交趾者曾闻于再熟，取甫田者爰及于十千。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152445_comment'></div>盖以玄德升闻，至诚昭格。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152445_comment'></div>天地䜣合，百嘉由是而生；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1152445_comment'></div>风雨弗迷，三时以之无害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1152445_comment'></div>允钟上圣，克协灵符。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1152445_comment'></div>窃以山越之乡，多乏膏腴之产。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1152445_comment'></div>火耕水耨，获地利以甚微；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1152445_comment'></div>食稻与鱼，习土风而惟旧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1152445_comment'></div>去岁因罹于小歉，今春遂至于荐饥，力穑虽勤，糇粮殆绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1152445_comment'></div>参以五种之利，救其二釜之艰，俯及秋成，仅无菜色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1152445_comment'></div>皇帝陛下乃眷东顾，阴骘下民，临遣使臣，循行县道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1152445_comment'></div>虑赋舆之不集，尽赐田租；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1152445_comment'></div>念饥馑之可哀，大发仓粟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1152445_comment'></div>城邑聚人之地，为设淖糜；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1152445_comment'></div>山川血食之神，必祈膏泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1152445_comment'></div>道路之敚攘者，贷其枯木之毙；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1152445_comment'></div>沟隍之填委者，推以掩骼之仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1152445_comment'></div>明诏诞敷，和气斯应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1152445_comment'></div>如臣所领之郡，近接海隅，一千里之封陲，三万家之生聚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1152445_comment'></div>自蚕事载饬，厥篚之获颇多；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1152445_comment'></div>及麦秋俯临，两岐之谣斯洽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1152445_comment'></div>菽粟流衍，黍稷丰穰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1152445_comment'></div>绝无螟螣之灾，率有钟釜之蓄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1152445_comment'></div>矧早稻既获，陈根尚存，大雨时行，土膏脉起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1152445_comment'></div>芃芃发秀，薿薿垂芒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1152445_comment'></div>同枯杨之再生，异靡草之先死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1152445_comment'></div>结实栖亩，敛穧盈车。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1152445_comment'></div>至于晚田，又收数倍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1152445_comment'></div>遗秉滞穗，既寡妇之是资；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1152445_comment'></div>千仓万箱，顾老农而何幸！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1152445_comment'></div>臣忝膺郡寄，获睹年丰，亲逢五谷之祥，同赖一人之庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1152445_comment'></div>周原膴膴，犹咏曾孙之诗；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1152445_comment'></div>尧民熙熙，敢迷上帝之力！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1152445_comment'></div>休徵斯在，纯锡昭然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1152445_comment'></div>伏望宣付史官，书之简策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1152445_comment'></div>干冒宸扆，弥切兢惶。</div><div id='poem_sentence_40_1152445_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=999&endYear=999')">999年10月17日</a>　有诗咏大雪。作品：己亥年十月十七日大雪。<div id='poem_129306' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_129306' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_sentence_8_129306_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=999&endYear=999')">999年10月</a>　闻婺州太守陈靖改官计司判官，作诗寄之。作品：闻道卿途中授计司判官。<div id='poem_title_129362_0'>① 罢东阳得告归泉州宁觐，行至建安而有是命</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_129362'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_129362'>几年华省冠名曹，归棹夤缘入海涛。<div
