id='poem_sentence_6_129362_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=999&endYear=999')">999年10？</a>　十月或稍早，进奉贺南郊礼物，有状。作品：进奉南郊礼物状。<div id='poem_1152512' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152512' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152512?labeling=true' target='_blank'>进奉南郊礼物状</a><span class='authorDate'>（999年10？）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152512")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152512_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152512'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152512'>进奉贺南郊大礼绢一千匹者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152512_comment'></div>伏以衮冕祀天，百神述职，玉帛助祭，万国骏奔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152512_comment'></div>合陈任土之宜，式备克庭之实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152512_comment'></div>前件绢，实惟方物，出自地征。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152512_comment'></div>敢致贡于有司，庶获归于长府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152512_comment'></div>岂足称于厥篚，盖用表于献芹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152512_comment'></div>干冒宸严，伏增战汗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152512_comment'></div>谨差摄司马应霸押领上进。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1152512_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=999&endYear=999')">999年11月8日</a>　加勋上骑都尉，有谢表。作品：谢加勋表。<div id='poem_1152448' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152448' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152448?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢加勋表</a><span class='authorDate'>（999年11月8日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152448")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152448_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152448'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152448'>臣某言：今月二十五日，进奏院递到官诰一通、敕牒一道，蒙恩加上骑都尉，馀如故，仍放朝谢者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152448_comment'></div>在宥之恩，方覃于率土；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152448_comment'></div>册勋之典，俄及于具僚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152448_comment'></div>祗荷宠灵，伏增悚惕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152448_comment'></div>臣某<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>伏以唐制勋官，十有二等，克遵班爵之序，备存律令之文，所以褒赏忠劳，甄明品秩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152448_comment'></div>不称其职，羊胃之谤乃兴；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152448_comment'></div>或旷厥官，鹈翼之讥斯起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152448_comment'></div>如臣者，谬尘禄仕，蔑著声猷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1152448_comment'></div>束带立朝，已愧诤臣之任；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1152448_comment'></div>一麾出守，猥惭循吏之称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1152448_comment'></div>属燔柴荐鬯之辰，无除地给薪之效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1152448_comment'></div>爰因大庆，亦被鸿私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1152448_comment'></div>谏垣未削于姓名，勋籍骤迁于等级。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1152448_comment'></div>天威所及，盖咫尺之不违；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1152448_comment'></div>官箴有常，但颠沛而于是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1152448_comment'></div>弥勤职守，用报宠光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1152448_comment'></div>仰荷天慈，臣无任云云。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1152448_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=999&endYear=999')">999年11月8日</a>　又有状论加勋制错误，未进。作品：论郊禋加勋制书错误状。<div id='poem_1152515' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152515' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152515?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论郊禋加勋制书错误状<span class='inlineComment2'>（不曾进）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（999年11月8日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152515")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152515_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152515'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152515'>右，臣近者蒙恩加勋，已奉表称谢讫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152515_comment'></div>臣伏读制命，窃佩训词。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152515_comment'></div>以臣有奉册从祀之劳，于以用舍爵策勋之典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152515_comment'></div>退自循省，罔敢遑宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152515_comment'></div>盖以臣出领使符，远违文陛，职当奉引，既阻属车之尘；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152515_comment'></div>位列常参，莫厕大夫之后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152515_comment'></div>籍虽连于近署，礼不睹于严禋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152515_comment'></div>猥窥明诏之文，实越下臣之分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1152515_comment'></div>然而恩覃具位，庆洽普天，或参表著之馀，曾微内外之隔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1152515_comment'></div>如臣者，既官常之未改，荷宠泽以无辞；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1152515_comment'></div>至敦奖之所云，实凌兢而非据。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1152515_comment'></div>盖虑司言之任，罔遵书命之方，或恐诏旨稽留，茍图简易；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1152515_comment'></div>或因除目填委，不暇甄明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1152515_comment'></div>致涣汗之已行，类朱紫之无别。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1152515_comment'></div>窃以四禁之设，妄误为尤；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1152515_comment'></div>八柄所施，僭滥非可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1152515_comment'></div>故王者之出令，示人不欺；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1152515_comment'></div>有司之守官，失职乃死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1152515_comment'></div>虽小事而必慎，恐大体之或亏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1152515_comment'></div>治本是资，政典攸系。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1152515_comment'></div>臣尝披载籍，幸置周行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1152515_comment'></div>括囊不言，惧罹出位之罚；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1152515_comment'></div>扣阍有请，实怀犯上之忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1152515_comment'></div>然乃朝廷之纪纲，固非下臣之拟议，辄兹披露，诚属僭踰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1152515_comment'></div>伏乞圣慈覆验臣所受告身制词，即知臣所陈非谬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1152515_comment'></div>臣无任云云。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_1152515'></div><div id='poem_sentence_25_1152515_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=999&endYear=999')">999年11月</a>　南郊推恩，追赠其父大理评事。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=999&endYear=999')">999年11月</a>　表进贺真宗生辰礼物。作品：进奉承天节礼物表。<div id='poem_1152514' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152514' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152514?labeling=true' target='_blank'>进奉承天节礼物表</a><span class='authorDate'>（999年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152514")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152514_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152514'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152514'>进奉贺承天节绢一千匹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152514_comment'></div>右，伏以六龙出震，适逢华渚之祥；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152514_comment'></div>万国奉琛，竞奏涂山之会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152514_comment'></div>祝后天而斯切，陈任土以攸同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152514_comment'></div>前件绢，鲛杼非工，茧丝乏丽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152514_comment'></div>什一之取，盖出于地征；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152514_comment'></div>旅百之馀，愿充于庭实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152514_comment'></div>表封人之善颂，同野老之荐诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1152514_comment'></div>干犯宸严，伏增陨越。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1152514_comment'></div>谨差教练使陈昭简押领上进。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1152514_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=999&endYear=999')">999年</a>　作《偶兴》诗，发斥邪扶正意。<div id='poem_129424' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_129424' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/129424?labeling=true' target='_blank'>偶兴</a><span class='authorDate'>（999年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_129424")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_129424_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_129424'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_129424'>芳兰滋九畹，萧蒿亦旁植。<div id='poem_sentence_0_129424_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_129424'>威凤翔丹山，鸱枭犹接翼。<div id='poem_sentence_1_129424_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_129424'>雅琴歌南风，蛙鸣不容息。<div id='poem_sentence_2_129424_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_129424'>骊珠媚清川，鱼目光激射。<div id='poem_sentence_3_129424_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_129424'>薰莸岂同器，云壤自悬隔。<div id='poem_sentence_4_129424_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_129424'>咄咄来逼人，薨薨止于棘。<div id='poem_sentence_5_129424_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_129424'>发迹由屠沽，操心希桀蹠。<div id='poem_sentence_6_129424_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_129424'>天形固残毁，吏曹尝摈斥。<div id='poem_sentence_7_129424_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_129424'>狠羊远刀杌，黠马委衔策。<div id='poem_sentence_8_129424_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_129424'>心同溪壑险，恶比邱山积。<div id='poem_sentence_9_129424_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_129424'>天听本聪明，神道尤正直。<div id='poem_sentence_10_129424_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_129424'>当用御魑魅，岂令为鬼蜮。<div id='poem_sentence_11_129424_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_129424'>舂喉鲁阳戈，钩颈子云戟。<div id='poem_sentence_12_129424_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_129424'>肉委饿虎蹊，尸投穷发北。<div id='poem_sentence_13_129424_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_129424'>饥鹰砺吻啄，猰貐磨牙食。<div id='poem_sentence_14_129424_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_129424'>魂气絷酆都，膏血涂荒碛。<div id='poem_sentence_15_129424_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_129424'>去草绝本根，决疽恣针石。<div id='poem_sentence_16_129424_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_129424'>所居必污潴，遗种尽刳剔。<div id='poem_sentence_17_129424_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_129424'>渠魁已歼殄，非类弥怵惕。<div id='poem_sentence_18_129424_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_129424'>稂莠既芟夷，善苗渐滋殖。<div id='poem_sentence_19_129424_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_129424'>君子益知命，视履如<span class='inlineComment2'>（祝刻本作加）</span>平昔。<div id='poem_sentence_20_129424_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_129424'>小人竞革音，灭身在漏刻。<div id='poem_sentence_21_129424_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_129424'>尧民率可封，汤网从此释。<div id='poem_sentence_22_129424_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_129424'>永跻仁寿期，共造华胥域。<div id='poem_sentence_23_129424_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_129424'></div><div id='poem_sentence_24_129424_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=999&endYear=999')">999年</a>　处州任满，作诗抒怀自遣。作品：到郡满岁自遣。<div id='poem_129338' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_129338' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/129338?labeling=true' target='_blank'>到郡满岁自遣</a><span class='authorDate'>（999年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_129338")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_129338_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_129338'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_129338'>迢递分符竹，因循度岁华。<div id='poem_sentence_0_129338_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_129338'>地将<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_129338", 129338, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>鲸海</span>接，路与凤城赊。<div id='poem_sentence_1_129338_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_129338'>触石云频起，衔山日易斜。<div id='poem_sentence_2_129338_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_129338'>潮平聚渔市，水落见人家。<div id='poem_sentence_3_129338_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_129338'>吏隐偏知幸，民谣岂敢誇。<div id='poem_sentence_4_129338_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_129338'>无嫌<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_129338", 129338, "Clauses/10/Comments/0")'>勾漏</span>僻，且得养丹砂。<div id='poem_sentence_5_129338_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_129338'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_129338_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=999&endYear=999')">999年</a>　寄诗贺扬州守柴成务晚年得子。作品：闻扬州柴给事有弄璋之庆寄诗贺之。<div id='poem_129243' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_129243' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/129243?labeling=true' target='_blank'>闻扬州柴给事有弄璋之庆寄诗贺之<span class='inlineComment2'>（给事年六十六始有嗣子）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（999年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_129243")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_129243_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_129243'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_129243'>华堂何夕梦熊罴，卫氏如今有一儿。<div id='poem_sentence_0_129243_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_129243'>三日悬弧应是喜，十年结实未为迟。<div id='poem_sentence_1_129243_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_129243'>预知驷马门闾盛，暗想天麟骨法奇。<div id='poem_sentence_2_129243_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_129243'>曾忝门墙摄齐者，待看孔鲤学闻诗。<div id='poem_sentence_3_129243_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_129243'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_129243_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=999&endYear=999')">999年</a>　龙泉县造金沙塔院，郡名士周启明致书求记，撰《处州龙泉县金沙塔院记》<div id='poem_1152672' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152672' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152672?labeling=true' target='_blank'>处州龙泉县金沙塔院记</a><span class='authorDate'>（999年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152672")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152672_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152672'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152672'>金仙氏之教，有自来矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152672_comment'></div>天毒之国，实纪于《山经》；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152672_comment'></div>竺乾之师，尝闻于柱史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152672_comment'></div>西京名将，得休屠天祭之人；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152672_comment'></div>东汉诸王，为蒲塞桑门之馔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152672_comment'></div>道之行也，源远乎哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152672_comment'></div>三吴奥区，控带闽粤，鱼盐所出，生齿实繁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152672_comment'></div>昔仲雍之剪发文身，参以殊俗；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1152672_comment'></div>刘濞之即山煮海，放于末游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1152672_comment'></div>加以勾践之好兵，民性犷悍；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1152672_comment'></div>益之东瓯之事鬼，土风妖讹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1152672_comment'></div>自像法西来，渐被诸夏，此方士庶，佞佛尤谨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1152672_comment'></div>毁形变服，竞为苾刍之饰；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1152672_comment'></div>倾财破产，争修浮屠之舍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1152672_comment'></div>含福畏祸，革音迁善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1152672_comment'></div>水火或蹈，徽纆罔惧，而怵报应之说，坚信向之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1152672_comment'></div>奸轨用衰，民德归厚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1152672_comment'></div>《易》所云「神道设教」者，其是之谓乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1152672_comment'></div>缙云西鄙之邑曰龙泉，实瓯冶子淬剑之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1152672_comment'></div>土田膏腴，居人杂错，山谷环合，习俗豪举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1152672_comment'></div>版图所载，提封万井；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1152672_comment'></div>舟楫仅通，悬流千仞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1152672_comment'></div>县之南有精舍曰金沙，林岭襟束，烟霞亏蔽，地形四塞，靡通鸟道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1152672_comment'></div>石门中豁，迥非人境，香火不绝，钟呗相闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1152672_comment'></div>聿为道场，多历年所，徒众弥盛，堂构益隆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1152672_comment'></div>求之东隅，盖有隙地，邑人李文进施财百万，造塔七层。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1152672_comment'></div>货泉之费已殚，土木之功未毕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1152672_comment'></div>桑门延通，与其徒鸿显，暨大姓李仁禄，共倡其事，薄歛于人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1152672_comment'></div>经斯营斯，载朴载斲，基扃环回而固护，堂陛崛起以穹崇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1152672_comment'></div>斲材也必取山木之良，砻之以密石；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1152672_comment'></div>购匠也必择云梯之巧，赏之以兼金。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1152672_comment'></div>极剞劂之工，加丹雘之饰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1152672_comment'></div>筑室斯广，盖百堵之有馀；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1152672_comment'></div>为台甚高，非三休而能诣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1152672_comment'></div>鸟鼠攸去，燕雀是依。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1152672_comment'></div>名翚轩而欲飞，巨鳌兀以方抃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1152672_comment'></div>由余谓之使鬼，士茁疑其胜人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1152672_comment'></div>殆岁星之周天，始祇园之讫役。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1152672_comment'></div>凡堂以陈宾主之次，室以备晏息之所，高门洞启，回廊翼舒，庖厨载严，井榭攸设，举其成数，凡四十间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1152672_comment'></div>涌塔屹于中庭，反宇耸于天半。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1152672_comment'></div>泛朝日以增丽，蒙夕霭而如失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1152672_comment'></div>作镇兹壤，垂厥方来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1152672_comment'></div>且以岳阳王感应舍利，李长者《华严合论》，匮而藏之，目之曰华严宝塔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1152672_comment'></div>举其一而称焉，亦取夫百宝庄严之义也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1152672_comment'></div>夫诚不果者物不应，志不笃者事不集。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1152672_comment'></div>故霜陨燕地，风击齐台，诚之谓也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1152672_comment'></div>精卫填海，愚公移山，志之谓也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1152672_comment'></div>若通师者，奋空拳，创曾构。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1152672_comment'></div>秉心固，必异石席之卷转；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1152672_comment'></div>致功微，渐同水索之钻锯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1152672_comment'></div>于是名豪居士，捐千金而不疑；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1152672_comment'></div>织妇贩夫，拔一毫而无惜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1152672_comment'></div>聚财致用，积日累劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1152672_comment'></div>物力告穷，形势总萃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1152672_comment'></div>非夫挺鸡鸣不已之操，用蚍蜉时术之功，磨涅靡渝，颠沛于是，固将九年治水，厥功弗成，一篑为山，中道而止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1152672_comment'></div>迹其所自，夫岂偶然！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1152672_comment'></div>予乃知夫西方之言，有益于化，大雄之教，不虚其传。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1152672_comment'></div>矧于海隅，崇尚尤笃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1152672_comment'></div>以通师之善诱，以邑人之悦随，譬诸灵台，既克成于不日，将比棠树，永见爱于斯民，岂只轩丘之独神，孔堂之不坏而已！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1152672_comment'></div>汝南周启明者，郡之造秀，占数是邦，致书于予，恳请为记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1152672_comment'></div>聊叙始末，以附诸地志焉。</div><div id='poem_sentence_60_1152672_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=999&endYear=999')">999年</a>　知丽水县甄旦修葺县斋毕，亿撰文记之，榜于厅壁。作品：处州丽水县厅壁记。<div id='poem_1152671' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152671' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152671?labeling=true' target='_blank'>处州丽水县厅壁记</a><span class='authorDate'>（咸平二年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152671")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152671_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152671'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152671'>丽水，古括苍县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152671_comment'></div>唐大历末，避德宗讳，并郡改焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152671_comment'></div>地亘婺女之区，俗盖东瓯之旧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152671_comment'></div>提封之广袤，仅十万井；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152671_comment'></div>生齿之富庶，几八千室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152671_comment'></div>自钱氏窃据之际，头会箕歛，民不堪命；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152671_comment'></div>及圣朝混一之后，生聚教诲，日不暇给。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152671_comment'></div>县署湫隘，仅庇风雨，偪下已甚，陋如之何！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1152671_comment'></div>前此宰邑者，皆鞅掌王事，沉迷簿领，盘错游刃之不暇，栋宇改作之未遑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1152671_comment'></div>至道初，天子以古者郎官出宰百里，申命廷尉评甄侯旦，以六百石秩来涖是邑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1152671_comment'></div>侯，孔门之达者也，吏道详敏而饰以文学，天资高朗而辅以经术，清白以率下，明察以照奸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1152671_comment'></div>狱讼滋彰，必片言以折；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1152671_comment'></div>赋调倥偬，皆先时而办。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1152671_comment'></div>曾未期月，县政大成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1152671_comment'></div>天子嘉之，凡再降玺书，进爵朝大夫，总殿中六尚之职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1152671_comment'></div>不改其任，恐夺民贤君，增秩以留，用西汉故事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1152671_comment'></div>侯既五月报政，休声著闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1152671_comment'></div>终日清谈，庶务自治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1152671_comment'></div>从容暇豫，周览县斋，苫盖不完，梁木将坏，慨然愤发，经之营之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1152671_comment'></div>度山取材，悬金购匠，因农务之隙，募子来之徒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1152671_comment'></div>运斤成风，挥汗为雨，皆曰：「吾侪小人，犹有阖庐以避燥湿寒暑，岂我贤宰君筑室而不速成乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1152671_comment'></div>曾未浃旬，层构云毕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1152671_comment'></div>恍若神化，焕乎惟新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1152671_comment'></div>凡楼以藏诏书，厅以决政事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1152671_comment'></div>楼之南，敞重关可入方轨；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1152671_comment'></div>厅之北，辟回廊仅容宴豆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1152671_comment'></div>通而计之，共十有一间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1152671_comment'></div>丽谯渠渠，治象之法在焉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1152671_comment'></div>堂皇峨峨，神明之化出焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1152671_comment'></div>侯陟降以之，造次于是，职修事举，体宁神王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1152671_comment'></div>使虚室生白，高门容车，后来之人，坐享其利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1152671_comment'></div>侯之规模，信宏远矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1152671_comment'></div>昔者一日必葺，《春秋》称叔孙之贤；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1152671_comment'></div>百堵皆作，诗人著《斯干》之咏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1152671_comment'></div>鄙夫不佞，假守方州，每行春棠郊，摄齐偃室，目是轮奂，饱其风声，爰勒贞珉，以志盛事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1152671_comment'></div>异日甄侯弃去下邑，扬于王庭，此邦之人，谁无遗爱？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1152671_comment'></div>即陵迁邑改，斯宇也比灵光而独存；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1152671_comment'></div>石泐金销，斯文也与岘首以同致。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1152671_comment'></div>后之君子，善似续之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1152671_comment'></div>咸平二年记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_39_1152671_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=999&endYear=999')">999年</a>　岁暮，聂茂先赋诗纪处州善政，亿以诗谢之。作品：郡民以岁稔刑清相率为斋以报善政永嘉聂从事赋诗纪其事因依韵足成一百言以谢之。<div id='poem_129358' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_129358' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/129358?labeling=true' target='_blank'>郡民以岁稔刑清相率为斋以报善政永嘉聂从事赋诗纪其事因依韵足成一百言以谢之</a><span class='authorDate'>（999年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_129358")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_129358_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_129358'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_129358'>为郡临瓯越，云泉兴未乖。<div id='poem_sentence_0_129358_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_129358'>欢谣乏襦裤，归思满荆柴。<div id='poem_sentence_1_129358_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_129358'>偶遂丰年望，潜将乐土偕。<div id='poem_sentence_2_129358_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_129358'>流民争襁负，凶党绝椎埋。<div id='poem_sentence_3_129358_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_129358'>精力奸多露，清心政自谐。<div id='poem_sentence_4_129358_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_129358'>群生不疵疠，比屋已绥怀。<div id='poem_sentence_5_129358_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_129358'>辄诣金人宇，同修香积斋。<div id='poem_sentence_6_129358_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_129358'>漫劳歌邵父，方待拍洪崖。<div id='poem_sentence_7_129358_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_129358'>治行非尤异，传闻及等侪。<div id='poem_sentence_8_129358_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_129358'>雕章忽垂赠，属和愧淫哇。<div id='poem_sentence_9_129358_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_129358'></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_129358_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=999&endYear=999')">999年</a>　和聂茂先除夜诗。作品：次韵和酬永嘉聂从事除夜之什。<div id='poem_129111' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_129111' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/129111?labeling=true' target='_blank'>次韵和酬永嘉聂从事除夜之什</a><span class='authorDate'>（999年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_129111")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_129111_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_129111'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_129111'>三百六旬今夜尽，寥寥虚室独凝神。<div id='poem_sentence_0_129111_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_129111'>莲城五鼓欲催晓<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>，梅岭一枝先报春。<div id='poem_sentence_1_129111_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_129111'>邹律渐吹阴谷暖，尧蓂看傍土阶新。<div id='poem_sentence_2_129111_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_129111'>海隅留滞年华长，坐对寒釭浩叹频。<div id='poem_sentence_3_129111_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_129111'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_129111_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_129111'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_1_129111_0'>⑴ 自注：按《图记》，郡城号莲华城。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_129111_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=999&endYear=999')">999年</a>　年中，得痔漏下血之疾。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1000&endYear=1000')">1000年</a>　约本年初，以百姓婚姻事，奏请依淳化敕命施行。作品：奏依淳化二年七月敕命施行状。<div id='poem_1152513' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152513' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152513?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏乞依淳化二年七月敕命施行状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1000年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152513")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152513_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152513'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152513'>右，据本州州院司理院勘到龙泉县百姓吴宝、遂昌县百姓叶清，各是开宝九年已前吴越国王钱俶任内婚娶小妻，准律文，虽会赦并合离异者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152513_comment'></div>臣窃见淳化二年七月四日敕文，诸军州应有百姓及诸色人，伪命日已前曾娶次妻者，并以免罪，或有论讼，官不为理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152513_comment'></div>又，准新降《删定编敕》，即无此上件敕条。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152513_comment'></div>窃以遐远之民，各承僭伪之化，不被声教，罔识宪章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152513_comment'></div>先朝深究下情，浚发明命，怜其或有子息，多已长成，一旦仳离，无所归往，恐伤和气，俾至困穷，遂降德音，悉令如故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152513_comment'></div>奉行已久，恩贷实隆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152513_comment'></div>无赖之徒，狱讼稍息；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152513_comment'></div>旧染之俗，反侧自安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1152513_comment'></div>今来删定敕条，无此一件，盖从简易，有所削除。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1152513_comment'></div>然恩施于前，法变于后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1152513_comment'></div>昔被宽大之诏，伉俪如初；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1152513_comment'></div>今由律令之文，告讦兹始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1152513_comment'></div>率皆垂白，多或抱孙，须至分携，有足哀悯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1152513_comment'></div>伏望特降敕命，许依淳化二年七月内条贯施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1152513_comment'></div>所冀侧隐之仁，克符于先旨；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1152513_comment'></div>画一之法，永守于国章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1152513_comment'></div>山越之民，实受其赐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1152513_comment'></div>无任僭越兢惶之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1152513_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1000&endYear=1000')">1000年1月23日</a>　从祖徽之卒。约于本年为撰《行状》作品：故翰林侍读学士正奉大夫尚书兵部侍郎兼秘书监上柱国江陵郡开国侯食邑一千三百户实封三百户赐紫金鱼袋赠兵部尚书杨公行状。<div id='poem_1152690' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152690' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152690?labeling=true' target='_blank'>故翰林侍读学士正奉大夫尚书兵部侍郎兼秘书监上柱国江陵郡开国侯食邑一千三百户食实封三百户赐紫金鱼袋赠兵部尚书杨公行状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1000年1月23日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152690")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152690_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152690'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152690'>曾祖式皇，不仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152690_comment'></div>祖郜皇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152690_comment'></div>父澄皇，累赠礼部侍郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152690_comment'></div>建州浦城县乾封乡长乐里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152690_comment'></div>杨徽之，字仲猷，年八十。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152690_comment'></div>公之先，华阴人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152690_comment'></div>永嘉之乱，流寓江表，占籍上饶郡，凡十馀世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152690_comment'></div>唐上元中，刘展叛涣，吴会骚然，公之六代祖遂举族避地于建安之吴兴，因为著姓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1152690_comment'></div>自高、曾以来，用财力雄于州里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1152690_comment'></div>唐季俶扰，乃祖鸠合义旅几乎千人，保境亢宗，一邑是赖，受署义军指挥使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1152690_comment'></div>烈考博通文史，为乡党所称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1152690_comment'></div>王氏之据有闽隅也，物色异人，寤寐豪杰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1152690_comment'></div>首画奇策，请见牙门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1152690_comment'></div>忠懿王奇之，即日解褐，置之幕府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1152690_comment'></div>未几，赐五品服，拜本县令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1152690_comment'></div>弦歌之化，流于桑梓；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1152690_comment'></div>蕃衍之祥，钟于燕翼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1152690_comment'></div>公即其次子也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1152690_comment'></div>始在童丱，卓然不群；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1152690_comment'></div>结发从师，刻苦为学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1152690_comment'></div>群从兄弟，率以豪侠相尚，驰骋狗马，被服轻煖，使酒难近，结客报仇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1152690_comment'></div>而公杜门端居，偃仰图籍，躬亲布素之行，深为宗党所服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1152690_comment'></div>邑人江文蔚善赋，江为能诗，公皆延于客馆之中，伸以师事之礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1152690_comment'></div>曾未期岁，与之齐名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1152690_comment'></div>寻阳庐山学舍甚盛，四方髦俊，辐辏其间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1152690_comment'></div>公既终二亲之丧，即与从父弟参，蹑屩担簦，不远千里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1152690_comment'></div>亦既至止，名声蔼然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1152690_comment'></div>先生钜儒，咸共叹服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1152690_comment'></div>凡再罹寒暑，其业大成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1152690_comment'></div>参适有怀土之心，公即遣归省视坟墓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1152690_comment'></div>时李氏建国，奄有淮淝，贽币不通，边关甚急。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1152690_comment'></div>公不居一国，有志四方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1152690_comment'></div>思树勋于中原，耻怀安于故土。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1152690_comment'></div>杖策径去，潜伏间行，聿来上都，憩于逆旅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1152690_comment'></div>适及秋赋，假籍河南，首冠荐书，时誉愈出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1152690_comment'></div>时翰林学士窦公仪，枢密直学士王公朴，皆负公望，为一代龙门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1152690_comment'></div>公遍投以文，窦公倒屣相迎，王公置书为谢，待以奇士，名动一时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1152690_comment'></div>明年，礼部侍郎刘公温叟实掌文衡，擢于殊等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1152690_comment'></div>同时登第者，凡十有六人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1152690_comment'></div>周世宗申命近臣，再加考覆，唯公及李覃、何曮、赵邻几，得预其选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1152690_comment'></div>是年秋，授秘书省校书郎、集贤校理，迁著作郎，升朝为右拾遗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1152690_comment'></div>皇朝革命，以周室旧臣不宜在侍从之列，出监唐州方城商税。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1152690_comment'></div>太祖多遣近臣，廉访谣俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1152690_comment'></div>使者即公之故旧，公因言应天顺人，海内宁一，所宜崇儒术以厚民风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1152690_comment'></div>使还，具白其语，太祖怒，以其讪上，左迁凤翔天兴令；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1152690_comment'></div>未几，又移嘉州峨眉令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1152690_comment'></div>公文学之外，长于吟咏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1152690_comment'></div>历宰二邑，周旋数载，凡游赏宴集，良辰美景，必有彫章丽句，传诵人口。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1152690_comment'></div>或刊于琬琰，或被于筦弦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1152690_comment'></div>岐陇巴蜀之间，盖金相而玉振矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1152690_comment'></div>开宝初，复为著作佐郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1152690_comment'></div>散民盐、掌仓谷者四五年，僶俛从事，曾无愠色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1152690_comment'></div>未几，知全州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1152690_comment'></div>属太宗御极，拜左拾遗；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1152690_comment'></div>归朝，迁右补阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1152690_comment'></div>及受代归阙，见于内朝，太宗顾左右曰：「朕在藩邸，尝闻其能诗」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1152690_comment'></div>因尽索公生平所著。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1152690_comment'></div>公搜于箧笥，凡得数百篇，悉以奏御，且献诗称谢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1152690_comment'></div>其断章曰：「十年流落今何幸，叨遇皇王问姓名」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1152690_comment'></div>太宗览之甚喜，和以赐之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1152690_comment'></div>自是黄屋间宴，翠华游豫，宸章焕发，天言下布，宣示近臣之外，必以别本赐公，琼蕴瑶编，充盈箧笥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1152690_comment'></div>未几，拜侍御史，历库部员外郎，赐金紫，受诏与诸公编《文苑英华》一千卷，皆前贤之词赋诗章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1152690_comment'></div>分别部类，柬求菁英。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1152690_comment'></div>先朝以公专精风骚，特命编诗为二百卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1152690_comment'></div>公孜孜采掇，矻矻服勤，非风雅之言，未尝取也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1152690_comment'></div>迁刑部、兵部二郎中，同知京朝官考课。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1152690_comment'></div>端拱初，拜左谏议大夫；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1152690_comment'></div>明年，知许州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1152690_comment'></div>公久奉外朝，不乐吏役。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1152690_comment'></div>许昌地接京辅，当四通五达之郊，邮传交驰，冠盖相望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1152690_comment'></div>公励精为治，尽公无私，饯劳之勤，日不暇给。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1152690_comment'></div>才二岁，太宗召升殿，慰劳数四，即以本官判史馆事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1152690_comment'></div>中谢日，上顾侍臣曰：「杨某，儒雅之士，置于馆殿，正得其宜矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1152690_comment'></div>数日，加史馆修撰，仍判馆事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1152690_comment'></div>会张洎以翰林学士判史馆，即以公判集贤院。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1152690_comment'></div>时刘昌言掌机务，张洎在翰林。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1152690_comment'></div>昌言固恩宠，洎希进用，有以公常评议二人者语于昌言，昌言又以语洎，因共诬公，以飞语中伤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1152690_comment'></div>近臣闻于上，上恶之，不复问状，即以公检校右散骑常侍，充山南东道节度行军司马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1152690_comment'></div>未行，改镇安军行军司马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1152690_comment'></div>数月，以今上出领京邑，慎择府僚，驿召公，拜左谏议大夫，与今兵部侍郎毕公士安，同授开封府判官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1152690_comment'></div>明年，肇建承华，分置众职，以公兼太子左庶子，判官如故，进位给事中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1152690_comment'></div>上即位，拜工部侍郎，充枢密直学士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1152690_comment'></div>咸平初，转礼部侍郎，学士如故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1152690_comment'></div>俄以衰疾，求解近职，拜兵部侍郎、兼秘书监。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1152690_comment'></div>数月，上优奖耆德，图任旧人，且欲亲近老成，讲论经义，遂诏置翰林侍读、侍讲学士，以公为翰林侍讲学士，秘书监如故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1152690_comment'></div>与户部侍郎夏侯公峤，国子祭酒邢公炳，工部郎中吕公文仲并命焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1152690_comment'></div>公侍讲金华，分直麟阁，执经待问，前席畴咨，上从容言天下事甚众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1152690_comment'></div>借箸之画，莫非沃心；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1152690_comment'></div>更仆之谈，或至移晷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1152690_comment'></div>然奏稿多削，温树不言，其慎密也如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1152690_comment'></div>俄以足疾请告，太医诊视，中使劳问，上自取名药封以赐之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1152690_comment'></div>适会郊禋，不及扈从，上特命加锡，如侍祠之例。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1152690_comment'></div>銮舆北幸，力疾辞于苑中，涕泗沾襟，备述忠恳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1152690_comment'></div>上谓之曰：「卿勉进医药，当不日相见」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1152690_comment'></div>及驻跸大名，特降手诏存问，公每上表疏，皆自为之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1152690_comment'></div>三年正月二十二日，车驾还都，上特遣中贵人慰谕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1152690_comment'></div>即日，疾遂革；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1152690_comment'></div>二十三日，以不起闻，上轸悼者久之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1152690_comment'></div>诏赠兵部尚书，降内司宾至其第，以钱五十万、绢五百疋赐其家，仍命中使监护丧事，缘葬所须，并从官给。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1152690_comment'></div>以其子婿、太常丞宋皋直集贤院，外孙宋绶为太常寺太祝，才十岁侄孙偃集，皆同学究出身，奖旧臣而示优典也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1152690_comment'></div>公先娶王氏，生宋氏女；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1152690_comment'></div>后娶王氏，封太原郡君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1152690_comment'></div>公天性纯懿，无有矫饰，履行端谨，未尝放佚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1152690_comment'></div>以俭约自律，奉养甚薄；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1152690_comment'></div>以名教为务，颠沛不违。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1152690_comment'></div>接士以谦卑，检身以清白。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1152690_comment'></div>好谈名理，多识典故，自唐朝已来，士族人物，风流雅俗，悉能记之，亹亹可听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1152690_comment'></div>素好吟咏，遂臻其极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1152690_comment'></div>每对客论诗，终日不倦，此所以垂名，亦几乎成癖也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1152690_comment'></div>崇奉释典，酷信因果。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1152690_comment'></div>每五鼓即起，盥漱诵《金刚经》，如是者三十年，未尝暂废，所诵亦十数万过矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1152690_comment'></div>公无男子，亦不养子姓为嗣，琴书素业，并以付外孙焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1152690_comment'></div>公自结发筮仕，彯缨登朝，中外荐更，夷险一致。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1152690_comment'></div>精力极思，能成其名；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1152690_comment'></div>劳形啬神，用跻乎寿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1152690_comment'></div>夫子所谓「善人，吾不得而见之矣」，又云「未见好学者也」，公之谓欤！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1152690_comment'></div>其馀十年在官，徐防无过；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1152690_comment'></div>一裘不易，晏子能贫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1152690_comment'></div>周旋累朝，名节保于终始；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1152690_comment'></div>遭遇明主，存殁极于哀荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1152690_comment'></div>亦人伦之羽仪，士类之标准也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1152690_comment'></div>纪述之际，有直笔在焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1152690_comment'></div>聊叙遗芬，以咨史氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1152690_comment'></div>谨状。</div><div id='poem_sentence_123_1152690_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1000&endYear=1000')">1000年</a>　正月，官军破王均乱军于剑门，亿表贺之。作品：贺剑门破贼表。<div id='poem_1152453' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152453' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152453?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺剑门破贼表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1000年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152453")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152453_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152453'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152453'>臣某言：今月二十七日，得本道进奏院状报，近有西川驻泊神卫右第三军第二都虞候王均等，为恶作乱，奔冲剑门，已据剑门都监裴臻与知州李士衡同共杀败者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152453_comment'></div>虿毒甚微，敢行称乱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152453_comment'></div>鸱张未几，已睹成擒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152453_comment'></div>凶丑既歼，朝野相庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152453_comment'></div>臣某<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>窃以王者之谨关梁，所以备他盗；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152453_comment'></div>用鈇钺，所以诛叛臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152453_comment'></div>如王均等，身率戎行，地亲藩卫，禄廪优厚，赐予便蕃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152453_comment'></div>餍饫膏粱，被服轻煖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1152453_comment'></div>出荷干城之寄，曾无汗马之劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1152453_comment'></div>乃敢结搆异端，胁从群小，茍图不轨，辄负大恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1152453_comment'></div>挺狼贪羊狠之谋，为鼠窃狗偷之计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1152453_comment'></div>天设之险，爰肆凭凌；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1152453_comment'></div>鬼得而诛，岂容越轶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1152453_comment'></div>裴臻等任当要害，职在谁何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1152453_comment'></div>属蛇豕之兴妖，乘貔貅之鼓怒，遂摧锋而奋击，未旋踵以剪除。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1152453_comment'></div>元恶既就于枭悬，馀党更无于噍类。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1152453_comment'></div>寝皮食肉，式快忠义之心；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1152453_comment'></div>犯门斩关，永破奸邪之胆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1152453_comment'></div>天威所被，井络载宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1152453_comment'></div>赏典聿行，舆诵斯惬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1152453_comment'></div>臣忝分忧寄，幸睹捷音。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1152453_comment'></div>庆抃之诚，实万常品。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1152453_comment'></div>无任云云。</div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1152453_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1000&endYear=1000')">1000年</a>　闻帝幸河北视师，亿奉表问起居。作品：驾幸河北起居表。<div id='poem_1152449' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152449' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152449?labeling=true' target='_blank'>驾幸河北起居表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1000年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152449")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152449_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152449'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152449'>臣某言：今月八日，得进奏院状报去年十二月三日御札，取五日车驾暂幸河北者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152449_comment'></div>毳幕稽诛，銮舆顺动，羽卫方离于象魏，天威已震于龙荒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152449_comment'></div>慰边氓徯后之心，增壮士平戎之气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152449_comment'></div>臣某<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>臣闻涿鹿之野，轩皇所以亲征；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152449_comment'></div>单于之台，汉帝因之耀武。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152449_comment'></div>用歼夷于凶丑，遂底定于边陲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152449_comment'></div>五材并陈，盖去兵之未可；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152449_comment'></div>六龙时迈，固犯顺以必诛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1152449_comment'></div>矧朔漠馀妖，腥膻杂类，敢因<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_1152449", 1152449, "Clauses/22/Comments/0")'>胶折</span>之候，辄为鸟举之谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1152449_comment'></div>固已命将出师，擒俘献馘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1152449_comment'></div>虽达名王之帐，未焚老上之庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1152449_comment'></div>是用亲御戎车，躬行天讨，劳军细柳之壁，巡狩常山之阳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1152449_comment'></div>师人多寒，感恩而皆同挟纩；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1152449_comment'></div>匈奴未灭，受命而孰不忘家？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1152449_comment'></div>行当肃静塞垣，削平夷落，枭冒顿之首，收督亢之图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1152449_comment'></div>使辽阳八州之民，专闻声教；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1152449_comment'></div>榆关千里之地，尽入提封。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1152449_comment'></div>蛇豕之穴悉除，干戈之事永戢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1152449_comment'></div>然后登临瀚海，刻石以铭功；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1152449_comment'></div>陟降云亭，泥金而展礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1152449_comment'></div>远追八九之迹，永垂亿万之年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1152449_comment'></div>臣忝守方州，莫参法从，空励请缨之志，惭无扈跸之劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1152449_comment'></div>唯聆三捷之音，远同百兽之舞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1152449_comment'></div>臣无任云云<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_1152449'></div><div id='poem_sentence_23_1152449_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1152449'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_23_1152449_0'>⑴ 《武夷新集》卷一二。又见《皇朝文鉴》卷六三，《文翰类选大成》卷一四二，《三续古文奇赏》卷一○等。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1152449_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1000&endYear=1000')">1000年</a>　闻北师克捷，喜而成咏。作品：闻北师克捷喜而成咏。<div id='poem_129361' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_129361' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/129361?labeling=true' target='_blank'>闻北师克捷喜而成咏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1000年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_129361")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_129361_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_129361'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_129361'>岁晏增冰合，烟尘起羯<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>陲。<div id='poem_sentence_0_129361_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_129361'>文昌先命将，羽檄便徵师。<div id='poem_sentence_1_129361_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_129361'>天迥星狼灭，宵寒月魄亏。<div id='poem_sentence_2_129361_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_129361'>前军临瀚海，后骑缚阏氏。<div id='poem_sentence_3_129361_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_129361'>蓟北胡<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑵</sup>沙静，河南露版驰。<div id='poem_sentence_4_129361_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_129361'>辽阳诸父老，重睹汉官仪。<div id='poem_sentence_5_129361_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_129361'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_129361_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_129361'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_0_129361_0'>⑴ 原作朔，据祝刻本改</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_4_129361_0'>⑵ 原作飞，据祝刻本改</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_129361_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1000&endYear=1000')">1000年2月27日</a>　得报车驾还京，上贺表，并进奉贺表。作品：贺车驾还京表。<div id='poem_1152452' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152452' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152452?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺车驾还京表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1000年2月27日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152452")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152452_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152452'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152452'>臣某言：今月廿七日，得本州进奏院状，称前月廿二日车驾还京者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152452_comment'></div>戎索巳清，宸游乃复，凡在臣子，庆抃同深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152452_comment'></div>臣某<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>伏以五载四巡，《虞书》所纪；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152452_comment'></div>一月三捷，周《雅》攸称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152452_comment'></div>商汤乃致讨于鬼方，汉文亦亲临于细柳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152452_comment'></div>东征西怨，用慰徯后之心；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152452_comment'></div>春蒐夏苗，爰示治兵之典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152452_comment'></div>顾惟时迈，允谓国章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1152452_comment'></div>崇文广武圣明仁孝皇帝陛下诞膺元符，奉若古训，垂衣裳而致治，百度惟贞；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1152452_comment'></div>舞干羽以怀柔，五兵载戢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1152452_comment'></div>然燕南尚屯于虎旅，漠北犹立于王庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1152452_comment'></div>辄率引弓之民，敢肆穿窬之盗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1152452_comment'></div>虽九天命将，六月出师，日献稿街之俘，行案榆溪之塞，而陛下方欲劳军于壁，责战于边，亲御戎车，躬秉武节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1152452_comment'></div>貔貅奋怒，将食肉以寝皮；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1152452_comment'></div>毡毳馀妖，悉稿原而涂地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1152452_comment'></div>胡尘永息，冀北克清。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1152452_comment'></div>出观民风，既省方而展义；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1152452_comment'></div>人数军实，爰舍爵以策勋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1152452_comment'></div>举群臣之寿觞，献九庙之戎捷，欢娱载洽，庆赐遂行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1152452_comment'></div>固与夫瑶池之滨，空疲于八骏；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1152452_comment'></div>有洛之表，遂至于十旬，不可同日而语也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1152452_comment'></div>臣参守使符，僻在裔壤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1152452_comment'></div>六龙顺动，独远属车之尘；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1152452_comment'></div>百辟欢呼，莫厕大夫之后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1152452_comment'></div>瞻恋之极，抃蹈无涯<span class='inlineComment2'>（《武夷新集》卷一二。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1152452_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_1152452'>参：疑当作「忝」。</div><div id='poem_sentence_25_1152452_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1000&endYear=1000')">1000年</a>　仲春喜雨，有诗吟之。作品：中春喜雨。<div id='poem_129309' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_129309' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/129309?labeling=true' target='_blank'>中春喜雨</a><span class='authorDate'>（1000年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_129309")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_129309_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_129309'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_129309'>土膏初脉起，东作向农时。<div id='poem_sentence_0_129309_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_129309'>隐辚雷车转，霏微雨足垂。<div id='poem_sentence_1_129309_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_129309'>龙蛇争奋跃，桃李渐离披。<div id='poem_sentence_2_129309_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_129309'>流润先从叶，馀波更及私。<div id='poem_sentence_3_129309_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_129309'>讴谣耕父喜，渗漉稻畦滋。<div id='poem_sentence_4_129309_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_129309'>连夜空阶滴，愁吟水部诗。<div id='poem_sentence_5_129309_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_129309'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_129309_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1000&endYear=1000')">1000年</a>　春，李宗讷、孙何相继使浙西。宗讷到处州，以孙何诗三首示杨亿，亿酬和之。作品：太常李博士史馆孙秘丞相继奉使浙右博士至郡以孙侯诗三章示予且以致意因次韵和酬。<div id='poem_129030' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_129030' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/129030?labeling=true' target='_blank'>太常李博士史馆孙秘丞相继奉使浙右博士至郡以孙侯诗三章示予且以致意因次韵和酬<span class='inlineComment2'>（时孙不来）</span><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1000年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_129030")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_129030_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_129030'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_129030'>迅濑拖舟上，危梯蹑屐登。<div id='poem_sentence_0_129030_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_129030'>山光翠欲滴，水气热如蒸。<div id='poem_sentence_1_129030_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_129030'>路转藤萝暗，天开物象澄。<div id='poem_sentence_2_129030_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_129030'>丘园足逋客，应得荐贤能。<div id='poem_sentence_3_129030_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_129030'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_129030_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_129028' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_129028' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/129028?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1000年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_129028_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_129028'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_129028'>分忧从汉殿，捧诏出萧墙。<div id='poem_sentence_0_129028_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_129028'>路入三吴远，舟浮一水长。<div id='poem_sentence_1_129028_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_129028'>诗题石门侧，梦彻斗城傍。<div id='poem_sentence_2_129028_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_129028'>清晓见云物，依依认帝乡。<div id='poem_sentence_3_129028_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_129028'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_129028_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_129029' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_129029' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_title_129029_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_129029'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_129029'>北极分忧瞩，东瓯布惠和。<div id='poem_sentence_0_129029_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_129029'>曾蒙倾盖分，偶得枉帆过。<div id='poem_sentence_1_129029_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1000&endYear=1000')">1000年</a>　春，丽水县丞甄旦赠朱李实，感而赋诗。作品：丽水甄殿丞手植朱李繁实盈枝折以贶予感而成咏。<span class='inlineComment2'>（诗题“甄殿丞”，谱云“县丞”显误。）</span><div id='poem_129119' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_129119' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/129119?labeling=true' target='_blank'>丽水甄殿丞手植朱李繁实盈枝折以贶予感而成咏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1000年）</span><span id='poem_sentence_0_129119'>五年为邑鬓霜侵，吏隐由来得趣深。<div id='poem_sentence_0_129119_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_129119'>不独弦歌长满耳，兼闻桃李已成阴。<div id='poem_sentence_1_129119_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_129119'>晨昏我有南陔恋，江海君怀北阙心。<div id='poem_sentence_2_129119_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_129119'>早晚飞沉俱遂志，愿将初服敌华簪。<div id='poem_sentence_3_129119_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_129119'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_129119_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1000&endYear=1000')">1000年4月</a>　太夫人偕一家大小自处州归建安吴兴别墅。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1000&endYear=1000')">1000年</a>　在处州任，曾状举下属李翔。作品：奏举李翔状。<div id='poem_1152517' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152517' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152517?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏举李翔状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1000年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152517")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152517_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152517'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152517'>右，臣忝分朝寄，获领郡符，总官属以颇多，在吏能而毕见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152517_comment'></div>合伸论荐，敢避僭踰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152517_comment'></div>臣窃见前知本州青田县事李翔，元是御前试中进士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152517_comment'></div>植性耿介，临事强明，不染脂膏，自甘藜藿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152517_comment'></div>当州龙泉县山深地险，俗薄民顽，岁有逋租，狱多滞讼，号为难治，非止一朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152517_comment'></div>翔权知一考有馀，庶事办集，刑清讼息，民不敢欺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152517_comment'></div>又权本州判官、推官两厅公事，仅及半年，甚彰才干。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152517_comment'></div>勤恪匪懈，洁白无私，求之辈流，不可多得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1152517_comment'></div>伏望圣慈擢授京官，别加任使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1152517_comment'></div>傥犯赃罪，臣甘当连坐之文。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1152517_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>

-----title
金华
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='6bfcbdf06618497b9167dfcf04a16773_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("6bfcbdf06618497b9167dfcf04a16773");'><span id='6bfcbdf06618497b9167dfcf04a16773_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1000&endYear=1000')">1000年</a>，27岁</div><div id='6bfcbdf06618497b9167dfcf04a16773' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1000&endYear=1000')">1000年</a>　赴阙道出婺州，州人求为大藏经楼作记。作品：婺州开元寺新建大藏经楼记。<div id='poem_1152678' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152678' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152678?labeling=true' target='_blank'>婺州开元寺新建大藏经楼记</a><span class='authorDate'>（景德二年十二月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152678")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152678_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152678'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152678'>昔如来登菩提坐，为天人师，万德庄严，十号其足，大千世界，以愿力而摄受；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152678_comment'></div>十二部经，自悲心而流出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152678_comment'></div>所以宣畅了义，提拯群迷，开方便门，示真实相。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152678_comment'></div>有条不紊，譬以线而贯花；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152678_comment'></div>得象忘言，如标指之见月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152678_comment'></div>自鹤林示灭，大教方行，并龙宫秘藏，所传无几。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152678_comment'></div>爰暨像法之运，乃流震旦之区。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152678_comment'></div>大士继生，广绎五天之语；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1152678_comment'></div>精庐错峙，并缄三藏之文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1152678_comment'></div>于是大雄之法音，雷震于兹土矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1152678_comment'></div>勾吴之域，介于海隅；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1152678_comment'></div>东阳之墟，上直婺女。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1152678_comment'></div>蒙太伯至德之化，俗敦廉让之风；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1152678_comment'></div>渐初平好道之馀，人禀清真之气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1152678_comment'></div>有耻且格，见善乃迁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1152678_comment'></div>邑居相望，悉奉竺乾之教；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1152678_comment'></div>弦诵之隙，必阅贝多之言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1152678_comment'></div>繇是弃尘劳而为苾刍者，实繁有徒；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1152678_comment'></div>辟净土而崇塔庙者，比比而是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1152678_comment'></div>开元寺者，兹郡之大招提也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1152678_comment'></div>前临九逵，旁接万井。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1152678_comment'></div>金碧绚彩，上拟天宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1152678_comment'></div>钟梵交音，居然福地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1152678_comment'></div>土木壮且丽矣，岁祀寖以远矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1152678_comment'></div>龙象六和之众，禅律交修；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1152678_comment'></div>香灯四事之供，檀施总萃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1152678_comment'></div>而琅函宝揭，有所缺然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1152678_comment'></div>乃有本寺僧文靖，与本州都知兵马使曹维旭，同发志诚，共营胜利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1152678_comment'></div>爰以淳化中，相率诣阙，击登闻鼓，求借方版，摹印真文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1152678_comment'></div>奏牍上闻，帝俞其请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1152678_comment'></div>逮至道初，维旭等始共辇置楮墨之直，聿来京都。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1152678_comment'></div>诏免关市之征，授以要券。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1152678_comment'></div>缮造既毕，护持而归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1152678_comment'></div>特给上计之回舟，俾达金华之本郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1152678_comment'></div>维旭等又相与刻轴以文木，织绦以色丝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1152678_comment'></div>香芸染签，丹漆涂匣，崇饰既以备矣，誓愿既已圆矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1152678_comment'></div>而经台旧基，圮毁滋久，轩庑摧挠，墁绘舛駮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1152678_comment'></div>维旭等遂请于郡阁，躬诣属城，遍募有情，共成众善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1152678_comment'></div>鸠工度费，即旧谋新，建重楼，开法藏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1152678_comment'></div>其上级置卢舍那、文殊、普贤及十六大阿罗汉之像；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1152678_comment'></div>中级设虎座，作八神王箕踞捧持；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1152678_comment'></div>其下象七金山，法四大海。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1152678_comment'></div>宝地平布，祥云周绕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1152678_comment'></div>缔构雕镂，殚匠石之精能；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1152678_comment'></div>像设焚修，见天龙之护卫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1152678_comment'></div>固使黑白之众有所归依，利钝之根因而起发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1152678_comment'></div>皮纸骨笔，学道者靡涉于艰辛；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1152678_comment'></div>宝藏金言，开卷者并谐于悟入。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1152678_comment'></div>广大利益，岂胜言哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1152678_comment'></div>维旭又尝于雍熙中，募众缘累甓为浮屠，凡七级，直经楼之南十数步。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1152678_comment'></div>讫役之日，白光烛天，晴空泬寥，久之始灭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1152678_comment'></div>行路瞻睹，道俗嗟叹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1152678_comment'></div>斯亦树善之冥感，殖福之昭报也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1152678_comment'></div>予咸平中罢守缙云，道出兹郡，维旭者捧持事状，拜于道周，求得片文，以刻贞石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1152678_comment'></div>会予入掌书命，不遑官次，而勤请弥笃，践言是冀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1152678_comment'></div>予固从事于空宗者也，随喜称赞，岂有吝焉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1152678_comment'></div>削简含毫，兹用无愧云耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1152678_comment'></div>时景德二年，岁次乙巳，十二月朔日记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_57_1152678_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end
