-----title
禹州（阳翟）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='f40732cffa244237bbce152c0f1fd44a_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("f40732cffa244237bbce152c0f1fd44a");'><span id='f40732cffa244237bbce152c0f1fd44a_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1013&endYear=1014')">1013-1014年</a>，40-41岁</div><div id='f40732cffa244237bbce152c0f1fd44a' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1013&endYear=1013')">1013年</a>　亿居阳翟，因受毁訾，作《君可思赋》以抒忠愤。<div id='poem_1152427' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152427' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152427?labeling=true' target='_blank'>君可思赋</a><span class='authorDate'>（1013年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152427")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152427_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152427'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152427'>夫民生在世兮，事之攸同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152427_comment'></div>子之能仕兮，父教之忠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152427_comment'></div>念委质而勿贰兮，本陈力以首公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152427_comment'></div>虽代耕而徯禄兮，曷期侈以图丰？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152427_comment'></div>亦怀材而<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_1152427", 1152427, "Clauses/8/Comments/0")'>待试</span>兮，将乘时而奋庸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152427_comment'></div>夫何直谅不回，孤坚寡偶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152427_comment'></div>贯岁寒而勿改兮，濯江汉而无垢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152427_comment'></div>中履洁以好修兮，外葆光而虚受。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1152427_comment'></div>筮仕逢亨，奏技承平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1152427_comment'></div>濯鳞禁沼，拊翼丹楹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1152427_comment'></div>尧文载郁，禹律惟精。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1152427_comment'></div>荷紫囊而舐笔兮，从单于之勤兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1152427_comment'></div>霜飙刮骨，流尘满缨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1152427_comment'></div>自此研精藻翰，局影天扃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1152427_comment'></div>毫残鸡管，香消<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_14_1152427", 1152427, "Clauses/29/Comments/0")'>鹤绫</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1152427_comment'></div>鬓凋屋帻，心悬閤铃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1152427_comment'></div>矧乃郢坊酒醇，武都泥紫，版急<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_16_1152427", 1152427, "Clauses/34/Comments/0")'>鹄头</span>，书详马尾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1152427_comment'></div>石屋䌷书，鸿都约史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1152427_comment'></div>捃摭阙遗，发明统纪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1152427_comment'></div>窃企迹于前修，庶同风于古始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1152427_comment'></div>虑罔越思，身亦勤止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1152427_comment'></div>宣汉德于无穷，纳舜《韶》于尽美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1152427_comment'></div>志本勿矜，言乎有凭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1152427_comment'></div>非施劳而伐善，岂扬己而害能！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1152427_comment'></div>每燥吻而踯躅，屡抚心而屏营。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1152427_comment'></div>敷谈泉而载涸，鼓思风而弗兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1152427_comment'></div>感外邪而遘厉，殆五日之沈冥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1152427_comment'></div>怅官事之孰了，泪劳府而靡宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1152427_comment'></div>岂望夫连城之报？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1152427_comment'></div>岂爱乎画饼之名？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1152427_comment'></div>嗟民生之朴忠，希在昔之遐踪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1152427_comment'></div>思不出位，罔贪天功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1152427_comment'></div>慕台骀之业官，肯有二事；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1152427_comment'></div>念犁弥之辞赏，愈激厥衷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1152427_comment'></div>庶克终于雅尚，聊有裨于素风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1152427_comment'></div>奈何虺心昌炽，锦言萋斐，蝇薨薨以交乱，犬狺狺而迎吠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1152427_comment'></div>贤登朝而共嫉，女入门而各媚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1152427_comment'></div>乍缉缉以翩翩，竞翕翕而訾訾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1152427_comment'></div>结合阴邪，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_38_1152427", 1152427, "Clauses/79/Comments/0")'>缔造</span>疑似。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1152427_comment'></div>俾朕师之震惊，恣星箕之华哆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1152427_comment'></div>幸大度之不校，专巧言而纵毁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1152427_comment'></div>胡能伤君德之巍巍，徒以动贤心之惴惴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1152427_comment'></div>然后饰卫鹤之华轩，衒黔驴之短技。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1152427_comment'></div>窃名器以晏居，绝上下之愧畏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1152427_comment'></div>俟贯恶之既盈，将幽神而共弃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1152427_comment'></div>若夫睟穆东房，奚望清光？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1152427_comment'></div>定心服物，伟量包荒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1152427_comment'></div>耿求贤兮不及，慎乃宪而惟康。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1152427_comment'></div>延登体貌，义问覃详。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1152427_comment'></div>伊蓬心之受惠，怜橘性之有常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1152427_comment'></div>置之近署，采其寸长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1152427_comment'></div>遇忠见察，浸润无伤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1152427_comment'></div>犯四禁而多恕，缓千编而不遑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1152427_comment'></div>丁宁一札，在宥三章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1152427_comment'></div>践丹涂而乃春，宴华林而釂觞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1152427_comment'></div>动群伦之耸羡，曷丹心之弭忘？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1152427_comment'></div>盛宪多忧，长卿沉疾，退迹东阁之陂，举首长安之日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1152427_comment'></div>色变愁鬓，谗消病骨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1152427_comment'></div>周田食粟，聊强饭于数升；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1152427_comment'></div>江径诛茅，姑却扫于一室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1152427_comment'></div>岂不念悲哀作主，圳亩思君？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1152427_comment'></div>羁心檗苦，别绪丝棼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1152427_comment'></div>岷江一廛，幸天畿之接畛；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1152427_comment'></div>成周五世，庶宰树以参云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1152427_comment'></div>感骚人之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_64_1152427", 1152427, "Clauses/132/Comments/0")'>遗韵</span>，聊抒意于斯文。</div><div id='poem_sentence_64_1152427_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1013&endYear=1013')">1013年8月13日</a>　王钦若等上新修《历代君臣事迹》，真宗亲制序，赐名《册府元龟》。亿因预修，进秩秘书监。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1013&endYear=1013')">1013年</a>　亿居阳翟，编辑近作为《别集》十二卷。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1013&endYear=1013')">1013年</a>　辇下江吴僧闻杨亿集当代名公诗，竟以诗为贽；亿择其善者，写入《笔苑时文录》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1013&endYear=1013')">1013年</a>　约本年，门生黄鉴等记录亿平日语谈，汇编为《南阳谈薮》。后经宋庠删订，名《杨文公谈苑》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1013&endYear=1013')">1013年</a>　族人杨玮将赴举，求赀粮而行，亿以钱百千贷之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1014&endYear=1014')">1014年</a>　居阳翟逾年，致书亲友见意。作品：介推母子，愿归绵上之田；伯夷兄弟，甘受首阳之饿。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1014&endYear=1014')">1014年8月15日</a>　复以病愈求入朝，起知汝州。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
临汝（梁县）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='19bbbdce8f61416a970425940f6e690b_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("19bbbdce8f61416a970425940f6e690b");'><span id='19bbbdce8f61416a970425940f6e690b_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1014&endYear=1015')">1014-1015年</a>，41-42岁</div><div id='19bbbdce8f61416a970425940f6e690b' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1014&endYear=1014')">1014年</a>　到汝州任，有谢表。作品：汝州谢上表。<div id='poem_1152578' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152578' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152578?labeling=true' target='_blank'>汝州谢上表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1014年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152578")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152578_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152578'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152578'>沉疴初释，宠寄荐臻，祇命惟寅，饬装靡暇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152578_comment'></div>初临郡閤，获见吏民，揣己若惊，戴恩罔措。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152578_comment'></div>伏念臣本由单弱，特禀方愚，以童刻之微能，际帝图之亨会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152578_comment'></div>骤参纶掖，获草芝函，属以尧德弥文，汉辞尔雅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152578_comment'></div>云章有烂，谅黼黻以何施；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152578_comment'></div>天律惟精，亦哇咬之罔弃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152578_comment'></div>居常摩厉，徒益空疏；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152578_comment'></div>俄践内庭，预司密命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1152578_comment'></div>值皇闱之有庆，扈清跸以多欢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1152578_comment'></div>窥云瑞于封中，听棹歌于汾曲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1152578_comment'></div>四巡第颂，诚辨丽之绝闻；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1152578_comment'></div>二竖兴妖，致冥顽之坐遘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1152578_comment'></div>偶婴沉痼，遂剧支离，因请急以归宁，遽迷魂而不复。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1152578_comment'></div>率由蹇否，自抵困穷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1152578_comment'></div>矧以蕞尔之躯，茕然去职；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1152578_comment'></div>羁孤至甚，毁嫉居多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1152578_comment'></div>啧有烦言，实盈庭之可畏；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1152578_comment'></div>豁然大度，终如地以见容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1152578_comment'></div>比及痊平，果蒙齿叙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1152578_comment'></div>此盖尊号皇帝陛下仁深惨怛，德茂钦明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1152578_comment'></div>轸旧故以兴怀，俾肖翘之遂性，特加采录，令获便安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1152578_comment'></div>伏况临汝旧邦，陪京近辅，姬文之化所及，首载声诗；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1152578_comment'></div>地官之籍攸分，实繁兵赋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1152578_comment'></div>土多岩险，民或惰游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1152578_comment'></div>置使劭农，抑惟令典；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1152578_comment'></div>分条察俗，盖有新书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1152578_comment'></div>臣亦夙侍凝严，僭窥律度，敢忘瘁尽，以奉化成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1152578_comment'></div>然念臣早以断断之薄材，获齿振振之近列，典司训诰，就望威颜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1152578_comment'></div>读铭字于汤盘，时瞻景式；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1152578_comment'></div>载史言于董笔，获次旧闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1152578_comment'></div>舛命遘屯，荣阶绝迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1152578_comment'></div>酒泉素愿，敢望于生归；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1152578_comment'></div>丽正残编，几成于死恨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1152578_comment'></div>今者星畿接畛，竹使长人，预方国之颁书，禀天台之布宪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1152578_comment'></div>水深土厚，足养于槁骸；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1152578_comment'></div>昼访夕修，冀无于秕政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1152578_comment'></div>亲末光而弥阻，感再造以难胜。</div><div id='poem_sentence_36_1152578_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1014&endYear=1014')">1014年</a>　有书与王旦，多谈禅理；又寄栗一秤，以表心意。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1014&endYear=1014')">1014年</a>　汾州大中寺太子禅院僧善昭缀刊无德禅师语录成，遣僧求序于亿，乃序之。作品：汾阳无德禅师语录序。<div id='poem_1152669' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152669' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152669?labeling=true' target='_blank'>汾阳无德禅师语录序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1014年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152669")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152669_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152669'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152669'>昔者白象降生，教兴于权实；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152669_comment'></div>青莲视瞬，义著于师承。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152669_comment'></div>厥后只履西归，一花东布，世系联续，开悟寖广，然而根器各异，宗致迭举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152669_comment'></div>少林之嗣，既分皮髓之浅深；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152669_comment'></div>大寂之徒，亦著心眉之阶级。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152669_comment'></div>虽搅为一呼，匪酥酪醍醐之殊；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152669_comment'></div>然列彼三车，推羊鹿大牛之别。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152669_comment'></div>趋觉城而固有淹速，非智眼而孰克炤明？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1152669_comment'></div>汾州大中寺，太子禅院长老释善昭者，本太原人，积习闻薰，孤贞绝俗，自去饰受具，即杖策巡方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1152669_comment'></div>所至少留，随机叩发，历参知识七十一员，最后受印于汝州南院省念，遂法裔念。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1152669_comment'></div>出风穴沼，沼嗣先南院颙，颙嗣兴化奖，奖嗣临际玄，玄嗣黄檗运，运嗣百丈海，海出马祖，祖出南岳让，让为曹溪嫡子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1152669_comment'></div>自曹溪至师，凡十一世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1152669_comment'></div>师既投针临汝，分灯摩竭，衣珠内炳，潮音尚秘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1152669_comment'></div>薄言湘楚，依止林樾，道俗归慕，名声普闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1152669_comment'></div>长沙守张侯茂宗以四大寺命师择居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1152669_comment'></div>北抵襄沔，止白马山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1152669_comment'></div>郡牧刘公昌言躬诣顶谒延住兰若，前后八请皆不之诺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1152669_comment'></div>淳化四年，西河缁素千馀人，协心削牍，遣沙门契聪诣白马山，迎至其郡，遂尔留憩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1152669_comment'></div>摄伽梨而登席，挥犀柄以谈空，毗耶净名，宴坐罔离于空室；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1152669_comment'></div>庐峰慧远，送迎不越于虎溪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1152669_comment'></div>净众骈臻，法韵雄震。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1152669_comment'></div>而师愿力勇猛，学解淹博，周游湖岭，探索筌蹄，效遍参于善财，同多闻于庆喜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1152669_comment'></div>若乃江西即心之诲，而归于无物；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1152669_comment'></div>石头全提之句，而谓之真吼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1152669_comment'></div>南泉捭阖而自得，引发上机；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1152669_comment'></div>赵州纵夺而有端，摧伏异见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1152669_comment'></div>洞山之建立五位，回互以彰；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1152669_comment'></div>仰山之分列诸势，游戏无碍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1152669_comment'></div>雪峰应接之眼，啐啄同时；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1152669_comment'></div>云门扬攉之言，药石苦口。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1152669_comment'></div>咸达其要，悉举其纲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1152669_comment'></div>至如大用现前，纤尘不立，诸法皆泯，四句迥超，盖有黄檗之迅机，临际之妙脉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1152669_comment'></div>三玄三要，在掌握之所施；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1152669_comment'></div>二主二宾，与盲瞑而何异？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1152669_comment'></div>是为正路，直造上乘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1152669_comment'></div>师之所證，踰于格量，非齐肩于佛慧，曷染指于禅味哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1152669_comment'></div>予刳心弥久，感疾无损，静虑冥默，世缘纷染。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1152669_comment'></div>守郡楚北，恪居官次，而师遐遣清侣，躬裁尺讯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1152669_comment'></div>谓广内集录，载师之辞句，既参于刊缀；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1152669_comment'></div>汝海答问，陪师之法属，且联其宗派。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1152669_comment'></div>邈同风于千里，遽授书之一编。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1152669_comment'></div>法兴、智深，二上人飞锡实勤，巽床甚谨，述邑子之意，愿永南宗之旨，属图镂版，邈求冠篇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1152669_comment'></div>赏音相从，重胝忘苦，幸烦襟之微释，因濡翰以塞请云尔。</div><div id='poem_sentence_42_1152669_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1152669'><span class='label'>按：</span>《汾阳无德禅师语录》卷首，日本大正新修大藏经卷四七。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1152669_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1014&endYear=1014')">1014年</a>　杨亿受命知汝州，宪官姜遵弹而请罢之。诏中书召遵谕之。亿在州，有书与亲友，述忧谗畏讥意。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1015&endYear=1015')">1015年</a>　在汝州任。去年冬暮与今年春半，两致书张咏，述心中郁虑；咏移书宽解之，时咏知陈州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1015&endYear=1015')">1015年</a>　在汝州常礼佛。有书寄李维，叙其学佛始末师承。作品：与李维内翰书。<div id='poem_1152634' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1152634' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1152634?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与李维内翰书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1015年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27871, "北宋", "杨亿", "poem_title_1152634")'>杨亿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1152634_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1152634'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1152634'>病夫夙以顽惷，获受奖顾，预闻南宗之旨，久陪上国之游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1152634_comment'></div>动静咨询，周旋策发，俾其刳心之有诣，面墙之无惭者，诚出于席间床下矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1152634_comment'></div>矧又故安公大师每垂诱导，自双林灭影，只履西归，中心浩然，罔知所止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1152634_comment'></div>仍岁沉痼，神虑迷恍，殆及小间，再辨方位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1152634_comment'></div>又得云门谅公大士见顾蓬蒿，谅之旨趣，正与安公同辙，并自庐山归宗云居而来，皆是法眼之流裔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1152634_comment'></div>去年假守兹郡，适会广惠禅伯，实承嗣南院念，念嗣风穴，风穴嗣先南院，南院嗣兴化，兴化嗣临济，临济嗣黄檗，黄檗嗣先百丈海，海嗣马祖，马祖出让和尚，让即曹溪之长嫡也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1152634_comment'></div>斋中务简，退食多暇，或坐邀而至，或命驾从之，请叩无方，蒙滞顿释。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1152634_comment'></div>半岁之后，旷然弗疑，如忘忽记，如睡忽觉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1152634_comment'></div>平昔碍膺之物，曝然自落；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1152634_comment'></div>积劫未明之事，㸌尔现前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1152634_comment'></div>固亦决择之洞分，应接之无蹇矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1152634_comment'></div>重念先德，率多参寻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1152634_comment'></div>如雪峰九度上洞山，三度上投子，遂嗣德山；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1152634_comment'></div>临济得法于大愚，终承黄檗；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1152634_comment'></div>云岩多蒙道吾训诱，乃为药山之子；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1152634_comment'></div>丹霞亲承马祖印可，而作石头之裔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1152634_comment'></div>在古多有，于理无嫌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1152634_comment'></div>病夫今继绍之缘，实属于广惠；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1152634_comment'></div>而提激之自，良出于鳌峰也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1152634_comment'></div>忻幸忻幸<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1152634_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_1152634'>原前有「翰林学士、工部侍郎、赠礼部尚书文公杨亿，任秘书监知汝州日，尝有书寄李维内翰，叙其始末师承」。</div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1152634_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1152634'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_19_1152634_0'>⑴ 《天圣广灯录》卷一八，续藏经第二编乙第八套第四册。又见《佛祖纲目》卷三五，《五灯会元》卷一二，《人天宝鉴》。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1152634_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1015&endYear=1015')">1015年</a>　在汝州，数谒广慧禅师，尝置一百问，请广慧答。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1015&endYear=1015')">1015年8月13日</a>　上章言部内秋稼甚盛。真宗览章，赞其词笔冠映当世；宰相王旦以为杨亿以后，刘筠、晏殊相继为文，宋文有贞元、元和之风格者，自亿始也。<br /></div>
